## Part 1: 照片描述 (Q1 - Q6)

### Q1 (正确答案：A)

![Page 43](images/listen_page_43.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) She's guiding the cart. (她正在推手推车。)
- (B) She's ready to cross the road. (她准备过马路。)
- (C) She's loading a box onto the cart. (她正在把一个箱子装到手推车上。)
- (D) She's sweeping the sidewalk. (她正在清扫人行道。)

**其他可能表达：**
- She's transporting the cart. (她正在运送手推车。)
- She's moving the cart. (她正在移动手推车。)
- She's pushing the cart. (她正在推手推车。)


### Q2 (正确答案：C)

![Page 43](images/listen_page_43.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) The people are moving the seats. (那些人正在移动座位。)
- (B) They are waiting to board the plane. (他们正在等待登机。)
- (C) Most of them are concentrating on reading. (他们中的大多数人正在聚精会神地读书。)
- (D) The travelers are looking in the same direction. (旅行者们正在朝同一个方向看。)

**其他可能表达：**
- They are reading something on the bench. (他们正在长椅上读书。)
- The people are absorbed in reading. (那些人专心致志地读书。)
- The people are looking at reading materials. (那些人正在看阅读材料。)


### Q3 (正确答案：D)

![Page 43](images/listen_page_43.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) The fruit is displayed on the stand. (水果被放在架子上展示。)
- (B) Some food is being cooked in the kitchen. (厨房里正在烹饪一些食物。)
- (C) The apples are being picked. (苹果正在被采摘。)
- (D) There is a basket full of fruit on the table. (桌子上有一个装满水果的篮子。)

**其他可能表达：**
- Some fruits have been placed in a basket. (一些水果已经被放到篮子里了。)
- An assortment of fruit has been put in a basket. (各式各样的水果被放到一个篮子里了。)
- Various types of fruits are in a basket. (篮子里有各种水果。)


### Q4 (正确答案：A)

![Page 44](images/listen_page_44.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) There is a microphone near the speaker. (演讲者旁边有一个麦克风。)
- (B) They're speaking to one another. (他们正在互相交谈。)
- (C) He's ready to take off his shirt. (他准备脱掉衬衫。)
- (D) He's admiring the picture on the wall. (他正在欣赏墙上的画。)

**其他可能表达：**
- The speaker is standing at the podium. (演讲者正站在讲台上。)
- The speaker is talking into the microphone. (演讲者正在对着麦克风讲话。)
- The speaker is using the microphone. (演讲者正在使用麦克风。)


### Q5 (正确答案：A)

![Page 44](images/listen_page_44.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) They're playing the same musical instrument. (他们在演奏同一种乐器。)
- (B) The musicians are performing in front of an audience. (乐师正在观众面前表演。)
- (C) They are about to finish their performance. (他们的表演快要结束了。)
- (D) They are walking off the stage. (他们正往舞台下走。)

**其他可能表达：**
- They are performing together. (他们正在一起表演。)
- The musicians are performing indoors. (乐师正在室内表演。)
- They're making music together. (他们正在一起演奏音乐。)


### Q6 (正确答案：B)

![Page 45](images/listen_page_45.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) They have all taken seats outside. (他们都已经在外面入座了。)
- (B) They have assembled together outdoors. (他们已经在室外聚在了一起。)
- (C) The people are enjoying a game together. (大家正在一起欣赏比赛。)
- (D) The people are laughing at a joke. (大家因为一个笑话正在大笑。)

**其他可能表达：**
- The people have gathered outdoors. (大家已经聚到了室外。)
- Many of the people have taken seats outdoors. (许多人已经在外面坐下了。)
- There are parasols set up outdoors. (室外架起了遮阳伞。)
- 注：在Part 1中，每道试题都添加了3种可能的正确表达方式，考生可
- 以了解对于同样的照片可能出现的不同表达。


## Part 2: 应答测试 (Q7 - Q31)

### Q7 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** When are you leaving for Paris? (你什么时候出发去巴黎？)
- **A:** That depends on when I can book a seat on the plane. (那要看我什么时候能订到机票了。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** When will you take off for Paris? (你什么时候飞往巴黎？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) No, she left a while ago. (不，她刚走一会儿。)
  - (B) I'd rather go to London. (我更愿意去伦敦。)
  - (C) On Tuesday afternoon. (星期二下午。)


### Q8 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Where do they sell raincoats around here? (这附近有卖雨衣的吗？)
- **A:** Try the neighborhood mall. (试试附近的商场。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Where can I pick up a raincoat? (我在哪里能买到雨衣？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, it might be all right. (是的，没问题。)
  - (B) Around three o'clock. (3 点左右。)
  - (C) Probably at the mall. (商场里很可能有。)


### Q9 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Didn't you find the speech a bit dull? (你不觉得这个演讲有点儿枯燥吗？)
- **A:** Yes, I couldn't keep myself awake. (是的，我无法让自己保持清醒。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Didn't you think the speech was a bit slow? (你不觉得这个演讲的节奏有点儿慢吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) No, I found it to be quite stimulating. (不，我觉得这个演讲很令人兴奋。)
  - (B) It's quite a distance from here. (那儿离这儿很远。)
  - (C) All right, I think it's a good idea. (好吧，我觉得这是个好主意。)


### Q10 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Good afternoon. I was wondering if there is a single room available for this weekend? (下午好，我想问本周末有没有单间？)
- **A:** Sure, may I have your name, please? (当然有，请问您叫什么名字？)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Hello, I'd like to book a single room for this weekend. (你好，我想预订一个单间，这周末住。)
- **选项：**
  - (A) The bookstore is down the street. (书店就在这条街上。)
  - (B) You should have made a reservation. (你本来应该预约的。)
  - (C) Sure, will this be for one night? (没问题，是住一晚吗？)


### Q11 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** When did I last talk to Jack? (我上次和杰克谈话是在什么时候？)
- **A:** The day before yesterday. (前天。注：在Part 2中，为帮助考生提高听懂题目的能力，添加了和试题相同或相似的表达方法。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Do you recall which day I spoke to Jack? (你记得我是哪天和杰克谈话的吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, it was a day before you left for New York. (记得，是在你出发去纽约的前一天。)
  - (B) Tuesday would be a good day to meet. (星期二见面挺好的。)
  - (C) No, I am not sure what it is called. (不，我不确定它叫什么。)


### Q12 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How would you like to try on a pair of these sneakers instead? (试试这双运动鞋怎么样？)
- **A:** They seem a bit too small. (这双鞋看起来有点儿小。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Would you be interested in trying a pair of these sneakers here instead? (你有没有兴趣试试这边的一双运动鞋？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I saw it on the news, too. (我也在新闻里看到它了。)
  - (B) Yes, it is quite interesting. (是的，这很有意思。)
  - (C) Don't you think they're a bit too small? (你不觉得这双鞋有点儿太小了吗？)


### Q13 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How did you ever manage to get those tickets? (你怎么弄到那些票的？)
- **A:** I know someone who works at the theater. (我认识一个在剧院工作的人。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Where did you ever get a hold of those tickets? (你在哪儿弄到那些票的？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, I got in touch with him. (是的，我联系到他了。)
  - (B) They're for the three o'clock show. (这是 3 点钟演出的票。)
  - (C) From a friend who works at the theater. (从一个在剧院工作的朋友那里。)


### Q14 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Do you want sugar or cream with your coffee? (你的咖啡里加糖还是奶油？)
- **A:** Neither. I like mine black. (都不加。我喜欢喝清咖啡。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Would you prefer sugar with your tea or just cream? (你想在茶里加糖还是奶油？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I'll take both please. (我想两个都加。)
  - (B) Yes, I will do just that. (是的，我想那样做。)
  - (C) No, he likes it that way. (不，他喜欢那样。)


### Q15 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Is there a reason why you show up to work so early in the morning? (为什么你今天早上这么早来上班？)
- **A:** I come early to avoid the morning rush hour traffic. (我早来是为了避开早上的交通高峰期。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Why do you show up to work at such an early hour? (为什么你这么早来上班？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I did call her this morning. (我今天早上的确给她打电话了。)
  - (B) No, she is working at home today. (不，她今天在家里工作。)
  - (C) I hate being caught in traffic. (我讨厌堵车。)


### Q16 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How did you manage to meet the deadline? (你是怎样赶在最后期限之前完成的？)
- **A:** I've been working really hard. (我一直工作得非常努力。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** How did you manage to get the project done on time? (你是怎样做到按时完成那个项目的？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) It might be a little too late. (可能有点儿太迟了。)
  - (B) I work with a great staff. (我和一个很棒的团队一起工作。)
  - (C) Let's do it tomorrow instead. (咱们明天再做吧。)


### Q17 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Could you lower the volume of the music just a bit? (你能把音乐的音量调小一点儿吗？)
- **A:** No problem. I'll take care of it right away. (没问题。我这就调一下。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Could you turn down the music just a notch? (你能把音乐声调小点儿吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I'm sorry. I didn't know it was bothering you. (对不起。我不知道打扰到你了。)
  - (B) Please turn it in as soon as possible. (请尽快把它交上来。)
  - (C) Yes, right around the corner from here. (是的，就在前面拐弯的地方。)


### Q18 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Why don't you finish this work by three and go home for the day? (你为什么不在3点之前完成工作，然后下班回家呢？)
- **A:** Yes, I was planning on doing that. (是的，我正计划那样做。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** If you get this work done by three, I think you should call it a day. (如果你 3 点前能把这项工作完成，你就可以下班了。)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I will go home and get them. (我会回家取它们。)
  - (B) I'll call him back later. (我稍后会给他回电话。)
  - (C) That's what I am planning to do. (那正是我计划的。)


### Q19 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Who is in charge of arranging the tables and chairs for the meeting? (谁负责给会议安排桌椅？)
- **A:** The maintenance staff. (维护人员。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Who's responsible for setting up the tables and chairs for the meeting? (谁负责为会议摆放桌椅？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) There are plenty of tables. (有很多桌子。)
  - (B) It is scheduled to start at ten. (会议定于 10 点开始。)
  - (C) The Facilities Department, why? (设备部门，怎么了？)


### Q20 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Did you get a chance to get the tax sheets ready? (你有可能把税单准备好吗？)
- **A:** Yes, I left them on your desk. (是的，我已经把它们放在你桌上了。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Aren't the tax sheets ready yet? (税单还没有准备好吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, they are just about ready. (不，刚刚准备好。)
  - (B) I didn't call a taxi yet. (我还没有叫出租车。)
  - (C) It might be two sheets actually. (事实上可能是有两张单子。)


### Q21 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Maybe it would be more personal if I wrote the letter by hand. (如果我的信件是手写的话，那会更私人化。)
- **A:** Yes, that would definitely be more personal. (是的，那肯定会更私人化。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** I could always handwrite the letter. (我通常会手写信件。)
- **选项：**
  - (A) That would seem more personal. (那会显得更私人化。)
  - (B) Mary wrote the letter this morning. (玛丽今天早上写信了。)
  - (C) I will hand it to her when I get there. (我到那里后会把这个给她。)


### Q22 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How would you like to grab some lunch after we finish here? (你觉得我们完工后去吃午饭怎么样？)
- **A:** Okay, I'll take you to a South Korean restaurant. (好，我带你去一家韩国餐馆。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Would you be interested in having lunch after we are done here? (你愿意在我们干完活儿之后去吃午餐吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, let's check out a South Korean restaurant. (好的，咱们去一家韩国餐馆看看吧。)
  - (B) Sorry, I have never been interested in it. (对不起，我对此来从不感兴趣。)
  - (C) Yes, I went there a few days ago. (是的，我几天前去过那儿。)


### Q23 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How can I get the reception desk from here? (我怎么从这儿和服务台通电话？)
- **A:** Just dial 34. (拨34就行。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** What do I press to get the reception desk? (我按什么能和服务台通电话？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Try extension 34. (试试分机号 34 。)
  - (B) She's the receptionist. (她就是服务员。)
  - (C) I will get it. (我会拿到它。)


### Q24 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Why did Mr. Lee cancel this morning's meeting? (为什么李先生取消了今天早上的会议？)
- **A:** He had something important to take care of. (他有重要的事要办。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Do you know why Mr. Lee called off the meeting this morning? (你知道李先生为什么取消今天早上的会议吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Something urgent came up. (发生了紧急的事。)
  - (B) He will be back by then. (他到时候会回来。)
  - (C) No, I forgot to call him. (不知道，我忘记给他打电话了。)


### Q25 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** It's sizzling outside. (外面热极了。)
- **A:** Yes, it's really a hot day today. (是的，今天真是炎热的一天。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** It's really hot out there. (外面真的很热。)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, the humidity level is unbelievable. (是的，湿度高得让人难以相信。)
  - (B) He went over there an hour ago. (他一小时前去那儿了。)
  - (C) Why don't you turn down the heat then? (你为什么不把暖气调小一点儿？)


### Q26 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Who will fill in for Leslie when she takes her leave of absence? (谁会在莱斯莉请假期间接替她？)
- **A:** They're searching for someone now. (他们现在正在寻找人选。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Do you know who will be taking over Leslie's position while she takes her leave of absence? (你知不知道莱斯莉请假期间谁来接替她的工作？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, she will be taking it with her. (是的，她会随身带着。)
  - (B) Mr. Lee has not made up his mind yet. (李先生还没有决定好。)
  - (C) To a little island in the Pacific somewhere. (去太平洋上的一个小岛。)


### Q27 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Jenny was asked to forward this invoice to the home office, wasn't she? (珍妮被要求把这张发票转寄到总公司，是吗？)
- **A:** Yes, Mr. Smith asked her to do that. (是的，史密斯先生让她这么做的。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Jenny's got to mail this invoice to the head office, doesn't she? (珍妮必须把这张发票寄到总公司，是吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, she does have a nice voice. (是的，她的嗓音确实很好。)
  - (B) It's not very far from where she lives. (那儿离她住的地方不太远。)
  - (C) I don't think she is required to do that this time. (我认为她这次不需要那样做。)


### Q28 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Where is a good place to get some great Greek food near here? (这附近哪儿有好吃的希腊菜？)
- **A:** Try Mr. Greeks on Pape Road. (试试佩普路的希腊先生饭店。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Where do you recommend I go to have some good Greek food around here? (你推荐我到附近哪家饭店吃好吃的希腊菜？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, the service there is really good. (是的，那儿的服务的确很好。)
  - (B) I heard the food is quite tasty there. (我听说那儿的菜很好吃。)
  - (C) I always go to George's on Pape Road. (我经常去佩普路的乔治饭店。)


### Q29 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Didn't we update this program a while ago? (我们此前没有给这个程序升级吗？)
- **A:** We were supposed to. (我们本来应该这么做的。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Isn't there an updated version of this program? (这个程序没有升级版吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Not that I am aware of. (据我所知，没有。)
  - (B) Yes, it is a great program. (是的，它是一个很棒的程序。)
  - (C) Let's do it another day. (咱们改天再做。)


### Q30 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How is the new guy on your team doing? (你组里那个新来的小伙子干得怎么样？)
- **A:** He's coming along fine. (他干得不错。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Is the new guy on your team doing okay? (你组里那个新来的小伙子干得好吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I might join the team as well. (我也会加入这个组。)
  - (B) No, I don't know him that well. (不，我不太了解他。)
  - (C) Yes, he's just becoming used to his job now. (是的，他现在越来越习惯他的工作了。)


### Q31 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Do you want me to send the papers, or are you going to come and get them? (你想让我把文件给你送过去，还是你来取？)
- **A:** I will stop by later today. (我今天晚些时候过去。Questions 32 through 34 refer to the following conversation.M:I really need to get a new computer.（34）W: Why？ What's the problem？M: Well，I've had this computer for eight years. It's so slow to downloadanything， it drives me crazy.（)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Should I get one of my staff members to bring you the papers, or are you planning to make a trip out here? (我是找一个员工把文件带给你，还是你来这边一趟？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) No, my plane takes off at nine. (不，我的飞机 9 点起飞。)
  - (B) I'll drop by this afternoon. (我今天下午顺路过去。)
  - (C) I had a great vacation, thanks. (我度过了一个愉快的假期，谢谢。)


## Part 3: 简短对话 (Q32 - Q70)

### Questions 32 - 34

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** I really need to get a new computer. (34)
**W:** Why? What's the problem?
**M:** Well, I've had this computer for eight years. It's so slow to download anything, it drives me crazy. (32) And it often freezes completely, and then I have to restart it. I really need a faster computer, so I can work more efficiently.
**W:** Why don't you go to A&T Computers? I've used them for years. They use quality components, and they really know how to set up systems properly. I've always found their technicians friendly and helpful. (33)

**中文对照：**
> **M：**我真的需要买一台新电脑了。
> **W：**怎么了？出了什么问题？
> **M：**哦，这台电脑我用了8年了。它下载东西太慢了，我快疯了。它还经常彻底死机，然后我就得重启。我真的需要一台速度更快的电脑，这样我能更有效率地工作。
> **W：**为什么不试试A&T电脑？我用这个品牌的电脑好多年了。他们用的是高质量的配件，而且他们很懂得如何恰当地搭建系统。我发现他们的技术员挺友好，而且乐于助人。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **drive ~ crazy**：使发疯，逼疯
- **freeze**：（电脑）死机
- **restart**：重启（电脑）
- **efficiently**：效率高地，有效地
- **component**：元件，组件
- **set up**：安装（电脑系统），建立
- **properly**：适当地
- **helpful**：有帮助的，乐于助人的
- **access**：访问，使用
- **be frustrated with**：因为而感到沮丧，烦恼
- **have a sale**：促销

#### Q32 (正确答案：C)
**问题：**  (出了什么问题？)
- (A) The man can't access something on his computer. (男士无法访问他电脑上的某个文档了。)
- (B) The woman does not know how to use the program. (女士不知道怎样使用程序。)
- (C) The man is frustrated with his computer. (男士的电脑让他很烦恼。)
- (D) The woman's work is not going very efficiently. (女士的工作效率不太高。)

#### Q33 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Why does the woman recommend A&T store? (女士为什么推荐 A&T 商店？)
- (A) She has known the owner for years. (她好多年前就认识这家店的店主。)
- (B) It provides great service. (它提供很好的服务。)
- (C) The technician is her brother. (技术员是她的兄弟。)
- (D) The store is having a sale now. (商店现在正在促销。)

#### Q34 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What are they talking about? (她们在谈论什么？)
- (A) The man's company. (男士的公司。)
- (B) The woman's job. (女士的工作。)
- (C) The man's computer. (男士的电脑。)
- (D) The woman's car. (女士的汽车。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **get a computer = buy a computer = purchase a computer = pick up a computer** (买一台电脑)
  - *例句：I need to get a new computer soon.* (我需要尽快买一台新电脑。)
- **What's the problem? = What's the matter? = Is something wrong?** (出什么问题了？出什么事了吗？)
- **It drives me crazy. = It makes me mad.** (这件事把我逼疯了。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：It is so frustrating. It drives me crazy to see how slow the work is progressing.* (这件事很令人沮丧。看到工作进展得如此慢，我快疯了。)

### Questions 35 - 37

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Lucy, a client of mine is arriving in a few minutes for a consultation, but Mr. Woods just requested to see me immediately. (35)
**W:** What's the name of the person coming to visit?
**M:** Alexander Sullivan. Would you mind talking to him for a few minutes? (36) I should be back by a quarter after eleven.
**W:** Okay, but please be sure the meeting doesn't run too long. Derrick and I are going to the Watertown facility, and we're planning to leave at half past eleven. (37)
**M:** I'm positive I'll be done before then.
**W:** In that case, I'll speak with Mr. Sullivan until you return.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**露西，我的一个客户几分钟后要过来咨询事情，但是伍兹先生刚刚要求马上见我。
> **W：**来访的客户叫什么？
> **M：**亚历山大·沙利文。你介意跟他谈几分钟吗？我应该会在11点15分回来。
> **W：**没问题，但是请确保会议不要持续太长时间。德里克和我要去沃特顿工厂，我们计划11点半出发。
> **M：**我确定在那之前会结束的。
> **W：**那样的话，在你回来之前，我会跟沙利文先生谈的。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **client**：客户
- **consultation**：咨询
- **request**：请求，要求
- **immediately**：立即，立刻
- **facility**：设备；场所
- **plan to**：计划，打算
- **positive**：确信的，肯定的
- **in that case**：如果那样的话

#### Q35 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What is the man's problem? (男士遇到的问题是什么？)
- (A) He is unable to visit Watertown before noon. (他无法在中午之前访问沃特顿。)
- (B) He scheduled two meetings for the same time. (他同时安排了两个会议。)
- (C) He is unprepared for his meeting with his supervisor. (对于跟主管的会议，他毫无准备。)
- (D) He cannot meet a person at an appointed time. (他无法在约定好的时间见一个人。)

#### Q36 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the man request the woman to do? (男士请求女士做什么？)
- (A) Speak with his client. (和他的客户交谈。)
- (B) Look over a form for him. (为他检查一份表格。)
- (C) Speak to Derrick. (跟德里克谈话。)
- (D) Give him some documents. (给他一些文件。)

#### Q37 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What will the woman do at 11:30? (女士打算在 11 点半做什么？)
- (A) Go to another location. (去另一个地方。)
- (B) Conduct a consultation. (进行一次咨询。)
- (C) Meet a client for lunch. (与一个客户见面共进午餐。)
- (D) Speak with Mr. Sullivan. (跟沙利文先生谈话。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **would you mind~ = do you mind~** (（用于委婉请求）你介意…吗？)
  - *例句：Would you mind my opening the window?* (你介意我打开窗户吗？)
- **be sure = be certain** (肯定扩展表达：)
  - *例句：make sure Can we be sure that she's honest?* (查明；弄清楚；设法确保我们能确保她是诚实的吗？)

### Questions 38 - 40

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** I've just heard on the radio that all flights from the domestic air terminal will be delayed by two hours. (38) There's been a security alert and they're searching all the bags. (39)
**W:** Oh, no! That's going to cause us a serious problem. Our clients are expecting us and we won't be able to make it for the meeting.
**M:** That shouldn't be a big problem. I am expecting a call from them this afternoon to talk about the seminar. I'll see if I can postpone the meeting until tomorrow morning. (40)

**中文对照：**
> **M：**我刚才听广播说国内航站的所有航班将被延迟两个小时。刚才拉响了安全警报，他们正在搜查所有的行李。
> **W：**哦，不！那会给我们带来严重的问题。客户在等我们呢，我们没法参加会议了。
> **M：**那不算是个大问题。我在等他们的电话，今天下午他们会和我谈研讨会的事情。我看看能不能把会议推迟到明天上午。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **flight**：航班
- **domestic**：国内的
- **delay**：推迟，延后
- **security alert**：安全警报
- **postpone**：推迟
- **condition**：条件；情况
- **security**：安全
- **complication**：难题，困难
- **occur**：发生
- **make a mistake**：出错
- **booking**：（机票）预订

#### Q38 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** How long has the flight been delayed? (航班被推迟了多长时间？)
- (A) 1 hour. (一个小时。)
- (B) 2 hours. (两个小时。)
- (C) 3 hours. (三个小时。)
- (D) 4 hours. (四个小时。)

#### Q39 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What is the reason for the delay? (推迟的原因是什么？)
- (A) The weather condition is bad. (天气情况很差。)
- (B) There's a security complication. (出现了一个安全问题。)
- (C) An engine problem has occurred. (发动机出了问题。)
- (D) The airline staff made a booking mistake. (航空公司的工作人员在预订机票时出错了。)

#### Q40 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the man mean when he says,“That shouldn't be a big problem”? (男士说 “ 那不算是个大问题 ” 时是什么意思？)
- (A) He will use another mode of transportation. (他将使用另一种交通工具。)
- (B) He will ask the client to come to the office. (他将让客户来办公室。)
- (C) He will schedule the meeting for a later time. (他将把会议安排在晚一点的时间。)
- (D) He will attend the seminar a little early. (他将早一点参加研讨会。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **be delayed by two hours = be postponed for two hours = be held up for two hours** (被推迟了两个小时)
  - *例句：The meeting will be delayed by two hours because some of the guests have not arrived.* (因为有一些客人还没到，所以会议将推迟两个小时。)
- **make it for the meeting = get to the meeting = attend the meeting** (参加会议)
  - *例句：John said he might not be able to make it for the meeting.* (约翰说他也许不能参加会议了。)

### Questions 41 - 43

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Good afternoon. I'm from Waldorf Taxi Trucks with the items you requested.
**W:** Oh, really? I wasn't aware that we were expecting any deliveries. Who did you speak to?
**M:** Her name was Sylvie James. She called us just before lunch today and requested a special order. (41) Let's see I should have the phone order form here somewhere. Ah. Here it is.
**W:** Okay, but Sylvie's out showing some of our clients around our plant site (42) and is not due back for another two hours. (43) Why don't you leave the boxes here and I will sign for it?

**中文对照：**
> **M：**下午好。我是瓦尔多夫出租卡车公司的，来送你们需要的东西。
> **W：**哦，是吗？我不知道有人在等送货。你和谁通的电话？
> **M：**塞尔维·詹姆斯。她今天午饭前给我们打电话，下了一个特殊订单。我看看，我应该把电话订单表放在什么地方了。啊，在这儿。
> **W：**好的，但是塞尔维带我们的一些客户到工厂参观去了，而且两小时之内不会回来。你把箱子放在这儿吧，我来签收。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **be aware that**：意识到，知道
- **delivery**：交货
- **lunch**：午饭
- **order**：订单
- **site**：地方，场所
- **be due back**：（到时间）回来

#### Q41 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What has Sylvie done this morning? (塞尔维今天上午做什么了？)
- (A) Placed an order. (下了一个订单。)
- (B) Ordered lunch. (订了午饭。)
- (C) Met with a client. (会见了一个客户。)
- (D) Paid her phone bill. (支付了她的电话费。)

#### Q42 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Where is Sylvie? (塞尔维在哪儿？)
- (A) At lunch. (在吃午餐。)
- (B) At the factory. (在工厂。)
- (C) In a meeting. (在开会。)
- (D) In her office. (在她的办公室。)

#### Q43 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** When is Sylvie expected to return? (塞尔维预计什么时候回来？)
- (A) In an hour. (一个小时之后。)
- (B) In two hours. (两个小时之后。)
- (C) In three hours. (三个小时之后。)
- (D) In four hours. (四个小时之后。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I wasn't aware that (of) ~ = I was not informed about ~ = I didn't know about ~** (我不知道…)
  - *例句：I wasn't aware of the fact that some parts of the company policy had changed.* (我不知道公司政策有一部分已经变化了。)
- **be due back = return = come back** (回来)
  - *例句：He is due back the day after tomorrow.* (他后天回来。)

### Questions 44 - 46

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** I've got some outstanding news. The inspector gave my new café a passing grade, so now I have permission to open it for business. (44)
**M:** I'm so happy for you. When is the grand opening scheduled for?
**W:** This Friday. Why don't you stop by if you have some time? (45) Drinks will be half off, and there will be live entertainment all day long.
**M:** Okay. I'll visit sometime after work. Where exactly is it located? (46)
**W:** It's on the corner of Macon Street and Bedford Drive. It's right beside the big drugstore.
**M:** Oh, I know exactly where it is.

**中文对照：**
> **W：**我有个特别好的消息告诉你。督察员给我新开的咖啡馆打了及格分，所以现在我得到开门营业的许可了。
> **M：**真心为你感到高兴。正式营业安排在什么时候？
> **W：**本周五。你有时间的话，为什么不顺便过来坐坐？那天饮料全部五折，而且全天都有现场表演可以看。
> **M：**好的。我下班后过去。具体地址在哪里？
> **W：**在梅肯大街和贝德福德大道的拐角处，就在那个大药房的旁边。
> **M：**哦，我知道它的确切位置了。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **outstanding**：杰出的，优秀的
- **inspector**：督察员
- **café**：咖啡馆
- **passing grade**：及格分数
- **permission**：许可，允许
- **grand opening**：盛大开业，正式开业
- **schedule**：安排，计划
- **stop by**：顺便访问，偶然拜访
- **live entertainment**：现场表演
- **locate**：坐落于，位于
- **Drive**：大道

#### Q44 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Why is the woman pleased? (女士为什么很高兴？)
- (A) A contract was signed. (签署了一份合同。)
- (B) A business was opened. (公司开业了。)
- (C) An inspection was passed. (通过审查了。)
- (D) A profit was made. (获得利润了。)

#### Q45 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What does the woman advise the man to do? (女士建议男士做什么？)
- (A) Speak with her friend. (和她的朋友交谈。)
- (B) Contact a supplier. (联系一位供货商。)
- (C) Perform at a venue. (在一个地方表演。)
- (D) Visit a café. (到一家咖啡馆去。)

#### Q46 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the man ask about? (男士问了什么？)
- (A) The type of entertainment. (表演类型。)
- (B) The location of a business. (店铺的地址。)
- (C) The discounts on beverages. (饮料的折扣。)
- (D) The hours of operation. (营业时间。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **Why don't you~ = Why not~** (（表示建议）你为什么不…？)
  - *例句：Why don't you join us for lunch?* (你何不跟我们一起吃午餐呢？)
- **all day long = a whole day** (一整天)
  - *例句：They chatted and enjoyed themselves at the party all day long.* (在派对上，他们一整天都在攀谈，玩得很尽兴。)
- **right beside = right near** (紧挨)
  - *例句：I was standing right beside her at the time.* (当时，我正好站在她的身边。)

### Questions 47 - 49

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Is this the right counter for opening a new account? （ 47, 48 ）
**W:** Sure, I can do that for you right here. What kind of account were you thinking of?
**M:** I need to open a checking account. (48) I already have a savings account here. (47)
**W:** Great, in that case we can open a checking account for you very quickly. Would you do me a favor and fill out this form? I will also need your identification card with a picture. (49)

**中文对照：**
> **M：**在这个柜台可以开新账户吗？
> **W：**当然可以，我在这儿就能给您办理。您想开什么账户？
> **M：**我想开一个活期存款账户。我在这儿已经开过一个储蓄存款账户了。
> **W：**太好了，那样的话我们就能很快为您开一个活期账户了。您能帮忙填一下这张表格吗？我还需要您带照片的身份证。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **counter**：柜台
- **open**：开，办理
- **checking account**：活期存款账户
- **savings account**：储蓄存款账户
- **fill out**：填写
- **identification card**：身份证
- **write out**：写出，开出
- **cash**：现金

#### Q47 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Where is the conversation taking place? (对话发生在哪儿？)
- (A) In a bank. (银行。)
- (B) At a photo studio. (照相馆。)
- (C) In an accounting office. (会计办公室。)
- (D) At a store opening. (商店开业仪式上。)

#### Q48 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the man want to do? (男士想做什么？)
- (A) Write out a check. (开一张支票。)
- (B) Make an ID card. (制作一张身份证。)
- (C) Open a bank account. (开一个银行账户。)
- (D) Take a picture. (照一张照片。)

#### Q49 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the woman request from the man? (女士向男士要什么东西？)
- (A) Some cash. (一些现金。)
- (B) A discount coupon. (一张打折券。)
- (C) A picture ID. (一张带照片的身份证。)
- (D) Some forms. (一些表格。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **What kind of account were you thinking of? = What type of account do you want to open? = What kind of account are you thinking of opening up?** (您想要开哪种账户？)
- **in that case = if that's the situation = if that's what's happening** (如果是那样的话)
  - *例句：In that case, why don't you take over the job?* (如果是那样的话，你为什么不接手那份工作？)

### Questions 50 - 52

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Hi, Suzie. I'm just ringing to see if you got the job.
**W:** Oh, hi John. Well, actually, I'm not sure. But I do have to go for a second interview this afternoon. (50)
**M:** That's great! I guess you must be excited. Where is your second meeting supposed to happen anyway?
**W:** At the big building next to the art gallery downtown. Hey, do you think we can meet up for lunch today before I go to my interview? (51) I really could use some inside information about your supervisor. (52) He is going to interview me today.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**嗨，苏茜，我打电话来看看你是否找到工作了。
> **W：**哦，嗨，约翰。嗯，事实上，我不太确定。不过我今天下午确实要去参加第二次面试。
> **M：**太好了！我猜你一定很兴奋。你的第二场面试在哪里呢？
> **W：**在市中心艺术馆旁边的大楼。嘿，咱们今天在我去面试前一起吃午饭，你觉得怎么样？我真能用上一些关于你的上司的内部信息。他今天将对我进行面试。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **ring**：打电话
- **be supposed to do ~**：应该，被期望做
- **meet up ~**：会见，与见面
- **inside information**：内部信息
- **infer**：推测
- **apply to**：申请
- **avid**：渴望的，热切的
- **get along with**：与相处得好

#### Q50 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What will the woman most likely do today? (女士今天最有可能做什么？)
- (A) Go for a job interview. (去参加一个工作面试。)
- (B) Visit the art gallery. (参观艺术馆。)
- (C) Ring up an old friend. (给一位老朋友打电话。)
- (D) Meet with her brother. (见她的兄弟。)

#### Q51 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** On which part of the day is the conversation most likely taking place? (这篇对话最有可能发生在一天中的哪段时间？)
- (A) In the morning. (上午。)
- (B) During lunch. (午饭时。)
- (C) In the afternoon. (下午。)
- (D) In the evening. (晚上。)

#### Q52 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What can be inferred about the man? (关于男士可以推断出什么？)
- (A) He works at the company the woman is applying to. (他在女士应聘的公司上班。)
- (B) He is an avid art lover. (他是一个热忱的艺术爱好者。)
- (C) He doesn't get along with his supervisor. (他与上司相处得不好。)
- (D) He is looking for a better opportunity. (他在寻找更好的机会。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I'm ringing to see ~ = I'm calling to find out ~ = I'm phoning to ask ~** (我打电话来看看…)
  - *例句：I'm ringing to see if you would be interested in having lunch together.* (我打电话来看看你想不想一起吃午饭。)
- **Where is your second meeting supposed to happen anyway? = Where will the next meeting take place?** (你的第二次面试到底在什么地方？)
- **meet up for lunch = get together for lunch = gather for lunch** (见面一起吃午饭)
  - *例句：Let's meet up for lunch this week.* (咱们这周见个面一起吃午饭吧。)

### Questions 53 - 55

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Hi, Susan. This is Mike. Listen, could you do me a huge favor? (53)
**W:** Well, I'll try. What is it?
**M:** I have an appointment with a new client this afternoon, but I can't make it. Could you do it for me? (53) Another important client has called me in for an emergency meeting. (54) I really have to be out of the office this afternoon, and I can't get back here before 3:00 p.m.
**W:** Well, in that case, of course I'll be happy to take over for you. Why don't you drop by the office later so I can tell you how it went? (55)

**中文对照：**
> **M：**嗨，苏珊，我是迈克。你能不能帮我一个大忙？
> **W：**好，我试试吧。什么忙？
> **M：**我今天下午约见了一个新客户，但是我不能去了。你能替我去吗？另一个重要客户叫我去参加一个紧急会议。我今天下午确实不能在办公室，而且我三点之前回不来。
> **W：**好吧，如果是那样，我当然很乐意替你。你晚些时顺道来办公室一趟，我给你讲讲事情的进展如何。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **favor**：恩惠，帮助
- **emergency**：紧急情况，突发事件
- **out of ~**：在外面
- **get back**：返回
- **take over**：接管，接收
- **drop by**：顺路拜访
- **on one's behalf**：为的利益，代表
- **take care of**：负责；处理
- **tie up**：占用，阻碍
- **attend to**：处理，注意

#### Q53 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the man ask the woman to do? (男士要女士做什么？)
- (A) Attend a meeting on his behalf. (代表他参加一次会面。)
- (B) Take care of an existing client. (负责一位现有的客户。)
- (C) Drive him to his client's office. (开车带他去他客户的办公室。)
- (D) Pick him at 5 o'clock. (5 点时去接他。)

#### Q54 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Why is the man asking for a favor? (男士为什么要人帮忙？)
- (A) He is tied up at his office. (他在办公室走不开。)
- (B) He has to attend to something else. (他得去处理别的事。)
- (C) He doesn't like working alone. (他不喜欢一个人工作。)
- (D) He has a family emergency to take care of. (他家里有急事要办。)

#### Q55 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** When will Susan meet with Mike? (苏珊什么时候与迈克见面？)
- (A) Before she goes on her appointment. (在她去会见客户之前。)
- (B) After she meets with the new client. (在她会见新客户之后。)
- (C) At three o'clock in the afternoon. (在今天下午 3 点。)
- (D) After she finishes with the emergency meeting. (在她开完紧急会议之后。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **Could you do me a huge favor?** (你能帮我一个大忙吗？扩展表达：)
  - *例句：Can I ask you to do something for me? = Can you do something for me?* (你能帮我做件事情吗？)
- **take over for ~ = take one's place = fill in for ~** (接管，顶替…)
  - *例句：I will take over for you while you are away.* (我会在你不在的时候接替你工作。)
- **Why don't you drop by ~? = Why don't you stop by ~? = Why don't you come by ~?** (你顺道来…怎么样？)
  - *例句：Why don't you drop by on your way back from work today?* (你何不在下班路上顺道来一下？)

### Questions 56 - 58

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** I was just informed we'll be getting a new assignment. We're scheduled to go to 83 Lambert Street.
**M1:** What kind of work will we be doing there?
**W:** We've got to take care of the lawn and plant some trees and flowers. (56) The job starts tomorrow. (57)
**M1:** Okay, but I heard it's supposed to rain then. Mr. Myers, can we delay the work next week if it rains?
**M2:** In that case, you'll have the day off, but you'll need to come on the weekend to handle the job. (58) It's for a new client, and we don't want to lose him. (57) Is that okay, Tim?
**M1:** I sure hope it doesn't rain. I'm planning to visit my parents. (58)

**中文对照：**
> **W：**我刚接到通知，我们将有一个新任务。我们计划去兰伯特街83号。
> **M1：**我们将在那里做什么工作？
> **W：**我们要在那里打理草坪，种植一些树和花。明天开始工作。
> **M1：**好吧。但我听说明天可能会下雨。梅尔斯先生，如果下雨，我们可以把工作推迟到下周吗？
> **M2：**如果那样的话，你可以休息一天，但是你需要周末过来处理这项工作。这是一位新客户，我们不想失去他。这样可以吗，提姆？
> **M1：**我真希望明天不要下雨。我打算去看望我的父母。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **inform**：通知，告知（某人）
- **assignment**：（分配的）任务
- **take care of**：打理；照顾
- **lawn**：草坪，草地
- **delay**：推迟
- **handle**：处理（工作）
- **client**：客户，顾客

#### Q56 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Where do the speakers most likely work? (讲话者们最可能在哪里工作？)
- (A) At a landscaping firm. (在一家园林绿化公司。)
- (B) At a construction company. (在一家建筑公司。)
- (C) At an interior design company. (在一家室内设计公司。)
- (D) At a city park. (在一个城市公园。)

#### Q57 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What are the speakers supposed to do tomorrow? (讲话者们明天应该做什么？)
- (A) Submit some documents. (提交一些文件。)
- (B) Provide an estimate to a customer. (向顾客提供报价。)
- (C) Purchase some supplies. (购买一些必需品。)
- (D) Do some work for a new client. (为新客户做些工作。)

#### Q58 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What most likely does Tim mean when he says, “I sure hope it doesn't rain”? (当提姆说 “ 我真希望明天不要下雨 ” 的时候，最有可能意味着什么？)
- (A) He plans to go to the beach tomorrow. (他计划明天去海滩。)
- (B) He forgot to bring his umbrella to work. (他忘记带雨伞去上班了。)
- (C) He does not want to work on the weekend. (他不想周末上班。)
- (D) He wants to do some yardwork at home. (他想在家做些庭院杂活。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **We're scheduled to go to 83 Lambert Street. = We plan to go to 83 Lambert Street.** (我们计划去兰伯特街83号。)
  - *例句：We're scheduled to meet the reporter this afternoon.* (我们计划今天下午与记者见面。)
- **be supposed to do/be sth.** (应该做某事/是某事)
  - *例句：We're supposed to check out of the hotel by 11o'clock.* (我们应该11点半从酒店退房。)
- **In that case, you'll have the day off. = If that happens, you'll have the day off. = In that case, you'll take the day.** (如果那样的话，你可以休息一天。)
  - *例句：In that case, we won't wait any longer.* (如果那样的话，我们就不再等了。)
- **I sure hope it doesn't rain. = I really wish it doesn't rain.** (我真希望明天不要下雨。)
  - *例句：I sure hope you can help me.* (我真希望你可以帮助我。)

### Questions 59 - 61

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Have you been to any good restaurants lately? I'm looking for somewhere special to take my wife on her birthday. (59)
**W:** Well...My fiancé and I tried Clancy's Seafood Bar last weekend.
**M:** Oh, really? I read in the local paper (60) last week that the food and atmosphere there are superb but the price is a bit on the steep side.
**W:** It's true that the food is really very good, (61) and the price is a bit on the expensive side. However, the place is a bit too formal for my liking: I couldn't really relax there.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**你最近去过不错的饭店吗？我正在找一个能带我妻子过生日的特别的饭店。
> **W：**哦…我和未婚夫上周末到克兰西海鲜酒吧了。
> **M：**噢，真的吗？我上周在本地报纸上看到，那里的饭菜和气氛都是一流的，但是价格有点儿贵。
> **W：**是的，那里的菜确实很好吃，价格稍贵一点儿。可是，那里的气氛对我来说太正式了：在那儿我没法放松。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **lately**：最近，近来
- **look for**：寻找
- **fiancé**：未婚夫
- **atmosphere**：气氛，氛围
- **superb**：极好的，超级棒的
- **a bit**：有点儿，稍微
- **steep**：（价格）过高的
- **formal**：正式的，正规的
- **liking**：爱好，嗜好
- **propose**：求婚
- **affordable**：可支付得起的，价廉的
- **rather**：相当地，非常

#### Q59 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What are they talking about? (他们在谈论什么？)
- (A) An article the woman read in the local newspaper. (女士在当地报纸上看到的一篇文章。)
- (B) A plan for a surprise birthday party of a co-worker. (为同事举办一个惊喜生日派对的计划。)
- (C) A place where the man can take his wife on a special day. (男士可以在特殊的日子带妻子去的一个地方。)
- (D) How the woman was proposed by her fiancé. (女士的未婚夫是如何向她求婚的。)

#### Q60 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** How does the man know of the place the woman had gone over the weekend? (男士怎么知道女士周末去过的饭店？)
- (A) He read it in the local paper. (他在当地报纸上看到过。)
- (B) His friend had mentioned it. (他的朋友提到过。)
- (C) He went there before. (他以前去过。)
- (D) He lives nearby. (他住在那家饭店附近。)

#### Q61 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Which of the following does the woman mention about the place? (关于这个饭店，女士提到了下面哪条？)
- (A) The price is very affordable. (价格低廉。)
- (B) The food is rather good. (饭菜很好。)
- (C) It has a relaxing atmosphere. (气氛轻松。)
- (D) It is her favorite restaurant. (这是她最喜欢的饭店。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **The price is a bit on the steep side. = The price is a little high. = The price is a bit ridiculous.** (价格有一点儿贵。)
- **The place is a bit too formal for my liking.** (这个地方对于我来说太正式了。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：I don't like the place because there is a dress code. I didn't like the atmosphere there.* (我不喜欢这个地方，因为这里有穿衣规则。我不喜欢那儿的气氛。)

### Questions 62 - 64

![Page 52](images/listen_page_52.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Ms. Hutchinson, here are the blueprints for the Desmond Building. Catie and I finished them a moment ago. (62) We hope you like them.
**W:** I'm glad you finished, but you're running way behind schedule, Hans. (63) The final design is due a week from today, and we've only completed the second stage.
**M:** I'm terribly sorry. I'm sure that if we work hard, we can finish on schedule though.
**W:** Well, it's my job to examine the plans, but I'm flying to Toronto on business tomorrow. (64) I have no choice but to call the client to request an extension.
**M:** When are you returning?
**W:** Three days from now. So we can't initiate the next step until then.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**哈钦森女士，这是我和凯蒂刚刚完成的德斯蒙德大厦的设计蓝图，希望您能满意。
> **W：**我很高兴你们完成了，但是汉斯，你们的进度还是落后于计划。一周后的今天要完成最终的设计，我们只完成了第二阶段。
> **M：**非常抱歉。我相信如果我们努力工作，我们能按时完成任务。
> **W：**嗯，检查计划是我的工作，但我明天要飞往多伦多出差。我别无选择，只能打电话给客户请求延期。
> **M：**您什么时候回来？
> **W：**三天以后。所以只能等我回来，我们才能开始下一步。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **blueprint**：蓝图，设计图；计划
- **schedule**：进度表，计划表
- **due**：到期的
- **extension**：延期
- **initiate**：开始，创始；发起

#### Q62 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Which step in the schedule was just completed? (请看图表，计划表中的哪一步刚被完成？)
- (A) Design. (设计。)
- (B) Review. (检查。)
- (C) Adjustments. (调整。)
- (D) Final Design. (最终设计。)

#### Q63 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the woman say about the man? (对话中的女士对男士说什么？)
- (A) He should call Mr. Desmond. (他应该给德斯蒙德先生打电话。)
- (B) He is late with his assignment. (他的任务完成得晚了。)
- (C) He is in charge of the project. (他负责这个项目。)
- (D) He needs to work harder. (他需要更努力地工作。)

#### Q64 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What is the woman doing tomorrow? (对话中的女士明天要去做什么？)
- (A) Going on vacation. (去度假。)
- (B) Visiting her family. (去看望她的家人。)
- (C) Taking a business trip. (去出差。)
- (D) Attending a marketing conference. (去参加一个市场营销会议。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **on schedule = to schedule** (按照预定时间；按时)
  - *例句：Once the program starts, the producer makes sure it stays on schedule.* (一旦节目开播，制作人要确保节目按照预定时间进行。)

### Questions 65 - 67

![Page 53](images/listen_page_53.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Max, I received a telephone call from Justin Weathers this morning. He wants to see me next Tuesday instead of next Wednesday. (66)
**M:** I'm pretty sure you have some open space in your sche-dule then. (65) Why don't you request that he visit at 3p.m.?
**W:** Okay, I'll send an e-mail to inform him of that. Would you make the adjustment to my calendar, please?
**M:** Of course. Is there anything else you'd like me to do?
**W:** Three people from Accounting are visiting my office in ten minutes. How about preparing some drinks and snacks for us? (67)
**M:** I'll get right on it. Diane Foster's Weekly Calendar

**中文对照：**
> **W：**马克斯，今天早上贾斯汀·韦瑟斯给我打电话。他想下周二而不是下周三见我。
> **M：**我很确定您的日程安排中有一些空闲时间。您为什么不要求他下午3点过来呢？
> **W：**好的，我会发邮件通知他的。请你调整一下我的日程安排好吗？
> **M：**当然可以。您还有其他事情要我做吗？
> **W：**十分钟后会计部有三位同事要来我的办公室，给我们准备些饮料和点心吧。
> **M：**我马上去办。黛安·福斯特每周日程表

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **receive**：收到；接收
- **pretty**：相当地；很
- **inform**：通知；告诉
- **adjustment**：调整，调节
- **calendar**：日程表
- **snack**：小吃，点心

#### Q65 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What most likely is the man's job? (对话中的男士最有可能做什么工作？)
- (A) Secretary. (秘书。)
- (B) Computer specialist. (电脑专家。)
- (C) Technician. (技术员。)
- (D) Accountant. (会计。)

#### Q66 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Who is Justin Weathers? (请看图表，贾斯汀 · 韦瑟斯是谁？)
- (A) A CEO. (首席执行官。)
- (B) The head of the Marketing Department. (市场营销主管。)
- (C) A representative of PTR, Inc. (中石油公司代表。)
- (D) A job applicant. (求职者。)

#### Q67 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What will the man most likely do next? (对话中的男士接下来最有可能做什么？)
- (A) Reserve a room. (预订房间。)
- (B) Go to the Accounting Department. (去会计部。)
- (C) Get some refreshments. (拿一些点心。)
- (D) Prepare some documents. (准备一些文件。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **make the adjustment to = adjust to = take some changes** (调整；适应于)
  - *例句：Some institutions have begun to make the adjustment to the new age.* (一些机构开始调整以适应新时代。)

### Questions 68 - 70

![Page 54](images/listen_page_54.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Samantha, you're running a bit late this morning. (68)
**W:** I had trouble driving here. I normally do a U-turn at the intersection of Maple Street and Forest Avenue, but there was a sign indicating it's not permitted anymore. (69)
**M:** Oh, yeah, the city put it up because several accidents have happened at that intersection in the past few months.
**W:** I wasn't aware of that, so I had to drive straight until I could find a place to turn around, and that was when traffic got bad.
**M:** Well, it's okay to be late today since you didn't know about the sign, but make sure that it doesn't happen again. （ 68, 70 ）
**W:** Thanks for understanding.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**萨曼莎，你今天早上来得有点晚了。
> **W：**我开车遇到点麻烦。平时我在枫树街和森林大道的交叉口掉头，但今天放了一个指示牌写着不让在这里掉头了。
> **M：**噢，对，因为过去几个月那个十字路口发生了好几起交通事故，所以市里在那里搭建了一个指示牌。
> **W：**我没注意到这一点，所以我不得不一直开，直到我能找到一个掉头的地方，那时候交通变得很堵。
> **M：**嗯，今天晚到没关系，因为你不知道那个标志，但要确保以后不会再发生。
> **W：**谢谢您的理解。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **intersection**：交叉；十字路口
- **sign**：指示牌
- **indicate**：表明；指出
- **permit**：许可；允许
- **aware**：意识到的；知道的
- **turn around**：转向反方向

#### Q68 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Who most likely is the man? (对话中的男士最有可能是谁？)
- (A) The woman's client. (女士的客户。)
- (B) The woman's intern. (女士的实习生。)
- (C) The woman's boss. (女士的上司。)
- (D) The woman's assistant. (女士的助理。)

#### Q69 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Which sign did the woman see? (请看图表，对话中的女士看到的是哪个指示牌？)
- (A) Sign 1. (指示牌 1 。)
- (B) Sign 2. (指示牌 2 。)
- (C) Sign 3. (指示牌 3 。)
- (D) Sign 4. (指示牌 4 。)

#### Q70 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the man tell the woman to do? (对话中的男士告诉女士要做什么？)
- (A) Arrive on time at work. (准时上班。)
- (B) Carpool to the office. (拼车来上班。)
- (C) Take public transportation. (乘坐公交车。)
- (D) Park in the company's lot. (把车停在公司停车场。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **be running a bit late = arrived a little late = be a little late** (晚到一会)
  - *例句：He might be running a bit late, but he'll be here soon.* (他可能会晚到一会儿，但是他很快会到的。)
- **have trouble = get into trouble = be in trouble** (遇到麻烦)
  - *例句：I have trouble understanding it.* (我理解起来有困难。)
- **be not permitted = be prohibited** (被禁止)
  - *例句：Knotted rope or tape slings shall not be permitted.* (打结的绳环或扁带环是禁止使用的。)
- **put it up = build/construct it** (建造)
  - *例句：Protesters have been putting up barricades across a number of major intersections.* (抗议者们已在许多主要十字路口搭建了路障。)

## Part 4: 简短独白 (Q71 - Q100)

### Questions 71 - 73

![Page 55](images/listen_page_55.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Hello, Ms. Brown, my name is Mike Lee and I'm calling from Burma Airways London office about your missing baggage. (71) I just want to let you know that we have located the whereabouts of your lost baggage, (72) and we can have it delivered to your house tomorrow. Or if you prefer, you can come into our office at the airport anytime between 9:00 a.m. and 6:00 p.m. to pick it up. Could you please contact me at 777-2213, during office hours today? (73) Please let us know as soon as possible, so that we can make the best arrangement for you. And please accept our apologies for the mix-up.

**中文对照：**
> 您好，布朗女士，我叫迈克·李，是缅甸航空公司伦敦办事处的工作人员，想谈谈有关您丢失行李的事。我想告诉您我们找到您丢失的行李了，而且我们明天就可以请人把它递送到您家。或者如果您愿意，您也可以在上午9∶00到下午6∶00之间的任何时间来我们的机场办公室领取。请您今天在办公时间给我回电话，号码是777-2213。请尽快告知我们，以便我们为您做最合适的安排。并请接受我们对这个失误的道歉。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **missing/lost baggage**：丢失的行李
- **whereabouts**：下落，所在之处
- **locate whereabouts**：找到的下落
- **make arrangements**：做安排
- **accept**：接受
- **apology**：道歉
- **mix-up**：混乱，失误
- **notify**：通知
- **confirm a reservation**：确认一个预订
- **apologize**：道歉

#### Q71 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Who is Mike Lee? (迈克 · 李是谁？)
- (A) A travel agent. (旅行代理人。)
- (B) An airline employee. (航空公司职员。)
- (C) A passenger. (乘客。)
- (D) A delivery person. (快递公司的工作人员。)

#### Q72 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Why is the caller leaving the message? (打电话者为什么留言？)
- (A) To notify of a found luggage. (告知找到行李。)
- (B) To confirm a flight reservation. (确认预订的航班。)
- (C) To report a missing item. (报告一件丢失的物品。)
- (D) To apologize for a mix-up. (为一个失误道歉。)

#### Q73 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the speaker request from the listener? (讲话者向听话者提出什么要求？)
- (A) To call him back. (给他回电话。)
- (B) To pick up the bag. (领取包裹。)
- (C) To pay for the tickets. (付机票钱。)
- (D) To provide more information. (提供更多信息。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **pick it up = get it = come and take it** (过来领取)
  - *例句：You should come by my place to pick it up.* (你应该到我这里来领取。)
- **during office hours = during business hours = between 9:00 a.m. and 6:00 p.m.** (在办公时间)
  - *例句：You may pick it up during office hours.* (你可以在办公时间来领取。)
- **mix-up = confusion = screw-up** (混乱)
  - *例句：The mix-up will be cleared up soon.* (混乱马上会被消除。)

### Questions 74 - 76

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Attention all shoppers. We will be closing in thirty minutes time (74) so please finalize your purchases. We'd also like to advise you about some very special closing time prices. All meat in the fresh meat department must be sold tonight, before we close. Make your way to the meat department for some fabulous specials. (75) Here's just a sample of what's on offer: T-bone and fillet steak, only ten dollars a kilo; 100% beef mince for only four dollars a kilo; a selection of quality Europeanstyle sausages for only five dollars a kilo. (76) Be quick, customers! You'll be able to fill up your freezers.

**中文对照：**
> 所有的顾客请注意。我们再过30分钟就要闭店了，所以请结束您的购物。我们还想向您推荐一些非常特殊的闭店优惠价格。鲜肉区的肉今晚闭店前必须全部卖掉。到鲜肉区看一看吧，有很棒的特价商品。出售的商品包括：丁骨牛排和里脊牛排每公斤仅售10美元；100%纯牛肉馅每公斤仅售4美元；精选的优质欧洲风味香肠每公斤仅售5美元。顾客们，抓紧时间吧。您一定会满载而归的。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **finalize**：结束
- **closing time**：下班时间，闭店时间
- **make one's way to ~**：前往，向走
- **fabulous**：绝妙的，很棒的
- **special**：特价商品
- **be on offer**：待出售
- **fillet**：里脊肉（片）
- **mince**：肉馅
- **fill up**：装满
- **freezer**：冰箱
- **vegetable**：蔬菜
- **counter**：柜台

#### Q74 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What is the main purpose of the announcement? (通知的主要目的是什么？)
- (A) To tell the shoppers that the store will close soon. (告知顾客商店马上要关门了。)
- (B) To announce tomorrow's specials to the customers. (向顾客通告明天的特价商品。)
- (C) To thank the customers for shopping at the store. (感谢顾客在商店购物。)
- (D) To notify a change in the store hours to the customers. (向顾客通告营业时间的变化。)

#### Q75 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** Where should those interested in the special go? (那些对特价商品感兴趣的人应该去哪里？)
- (A) To the vegetable section. (去蔬菜区。)
- (B) To the checkout counter. (去收银台。)
- (C) To the manager's office. (去经理办公室。)
- (D) To the meat department. (去鲜肉区。)

#### Q76 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** How much is one kilogram of the European sausages? (一公斤欧洲香肠卖多少钱？)
- (A) Two dollars. (2 美元。)
- (B) Four dollars. (4 美元。)
- (C) Five dollars. (5 美元。)
- (D) Ten dollars. (10 美元。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **Please finalize your purchases. = Please make your last minute purchases. = Please finish your shopping soon.** (请（尽快）结束您的购物。)
  - *例句：Please finalize your purchases because the store will close in five minutes.* (请尽快结束您的购物，因为商店5分钟后就要关门了。)
- **fill up = stock up = pack up** (装满，存满)
  - *例句：I need to fill up the shelves.* (我需要装满这些架子。)

### Questions 77 - 79

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Good evening, and welcome to The Bay View Restaurant. I'm Richard, and I'll be looking after you this evening. (77) I should tell you that you may dine àla carte, or choose from our range of special set meals. The set meals have been designed by our head chef to provide an exquisite dining experience. Starters, all main courses come with a choice of our finest desserts and wines. (78) Set A is for lovers of red meats, and rich red wine for a low price of fifteen dollars; Set B is for those who are fond of fish and white wine for a price of twelve dollars. (79) For dessert, you may choose from our cake selection. Oh, and fresh filtered coffee is also included in these meals. (78)

**中文对照：**
> 晚上好，欢迎来到海景饭店。我叫理查德，今晚由我来为大家服务。我想告诉大家，你们可以按照菜单点菜，或者选择我们的特价套餐。所有套餐均由我们的厨师长设计，希望大家能有一次美好的用餐体验。开胃菜和所有主菜都配有各种精美的甜点和葡萄酒。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **A**：套餐只有美元，适合喜欢红肉和香浓红葡萄酒的客人；
- **B**：套餐美元，适合喜欢鱼肉和白葡萄酒的客人。甜点可以从我们的蛋糕里选。哦，这些套餐还包括新鲜的过滤咖啡。
- **look after**：照看，服务
- **dine à la carte**：按照菜单点菜
- **chef**：厨师
- **exquisite**：精致的，制作精良的
- **starter**：开胃菜
- **lover**：爱好者
- **be fond of**：喜欢
- **filtered coffee**：过滤咖啡
- **waitperson**：侍者，服务员

#### Q77 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Who is Richard? (理查德是谁？)
- (A) A chef. (厨师。)
- (B) A waitperson. (服务员。)
- (C) A customer. (顾客。)
- (D) A baker. (面包师。)

#### Q78 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Which of the following is NOT part of the set meals? (下面哪个不是套餐的一部分？)
- (A) Wine. (葡萄酒。)
- (B) Ice cream. (冰激凌。)
- (C) Coffee. (咖啡。)
- (D) Cake. (蛋糕。)

#### Q79 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** How much does fish dinner cost? (鱼肉套餐多少钱？)
- (A) Five dollars. (5 美元。)
- (B) Twelve dollars. (12 美元。)
- (C) Fifteen dollars. (15 美元。)
- (D) Twenty dollars. (20 美元。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **look after = take care of = serve** (为…服务，照顾)
  - *例句：The manager will be looking after you.* (经理会为您服务。)
- **be fond of = like = be into** (喜欢)
  - *例句：He is fond of fish.* (他喜欢鱼肉。)

### Questions 80 - 82

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Hello, everyone. As CEO of this company, I am happy to make this great announcement. (80) I have been informed by the sales manager this morning that the sales division has just reported on its sales figures for the first half of the year, and they are well beyond expectations. (81) They have also surveyed customer satisfaction, and, there again, the results are excellent. The combination of lower costs and higher sales means that we are heading for the highest profit figures ever. So, what does all this mean? Yes, you guessed it. This means that you guys are due for a fat bonus at the end of this year. (82) All you have to do is just continue doing what you have been doing so far.

**中文对照：**
> 大家好，作为本公司的CEO，我很高兴做这次发言。今天早上销售经理告诉我，销售部刚刚上报了上半年的销量，比预期销量要好得多。他们还调查了消费者满意度，结果同样出色。更低的成本和更大的销量说明我们正向最大的利润额迈进。那么，这些意味着什么？是的，你们猜对了。这意味着你们今年年底将会获得丰厚的奖金。你们唯一需要做的就是把现在的状态保持下去。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **figure**：数字
- **the first half of the year**：上半年
- **beyond**：超过，超越
- **expectation**：预料，预期
- **survey**：调查
- **customer**：顾客
- **satisfaction**：满意
- **combination**：组合
- **head for**：出发，前往
- **profit**：利润
- **due**：应得的
- **fat**：丰厚的
- **so far**：到目前为止
- **surpass**：超越
- **quota**：定额；指标
- **be satisfied with ~**：对满意
- **promotion**：升职

#### Q80 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Who is speaking? (谁在讲话？)
- (A) The company president. (公司总裁。)
- (B) The sales manager. (销售经理。)
- (C) A satisfied customer. (一位满意的顾客。)
- (D) An accountant. (一名会计。)

#### Q81 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** According to the speaker, what did the sales manager say? (根据讲话者所说，销售经理说了什么？)
- (A) The sales have surpassed everyone's expectation. (销售量超过了所有人的预期。)
- (B) The sales reps are working hard to meet their quotas. (销售代表们正在努力工作，以完成他们的定额。)
- (C) The customers are not very satisfied with their service. (顾客对他们的服务不太满意。)
- (D) They need to increase the price of their products. (他们需要提高产品的价格。)

#### Q82 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What does the speaker imply when he says,“Yes, you guessed it”? (讲话者说 “ 是的，你猜对了 ” ，他在暗示什么？)
- (A) The company will introduce a new product. (公司会引进一种新产品。)
- (B) The sales manager will get a promotion. (销售经理会得到晋升。)
- (C) They will get the result of the survey. (他们会得到调查结果。)
- (D) The workers will receive a big bonus. (员工会得到一笔不菲的奖金。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **CEO** (首席执行官)
  - *例句：president boss Mr. Lee is the CEO of our company.* (总裁老板李先生是我们公司的首席执行官。)
- **the first half of the year = the first six months of the year = from January until June** (上半年)
  - *例句：We need to make a lot of sales in the first half of the year.* (我们需要在上半年完成很多销售额。)
- **be due for a fat bonus = be due for a big bonus = expect a large bonus** (即将获得一笔丰厚的奖金)
  - *例句：I think we are due for a fat bonus at the end of this year.* (我认为我们今年年底会获得一笔丰厚的奖金。)

### Questions 83 - 85

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Good evening, Radio National listeners, and welcome to “Your Live Concert Hour” with Jill Boothby. (83) Tonight we have something very special in store for you—a two-part program featuring two of Asia's premier folk music acts performing live for you in our studio. In the first part of the program we'll be listening to the Young Asia Ensemble. This is one of Asia's most innovative groups, with performers from four different Asian countries who blend a variety of folk styles. (84) In the second half, we'll hear the Japanese ensemble, Kaito, who specialize in natural acoustic sounds. And don't forget that both of these groups will be performing this weekend at the World Folk Festival. (85)

**中文对照：**
> 国家广播电台的听众们，晚上好，欢迎收听由吉尔·布思比主持的“你的现场音乐会”节目。今晚我们为您准备了非常特别的节目——这个节目由两段组成，包含两场亚洲最著名的民乐表演，我们将在演播室里为您现场直播。在节目的上半段，我们将听到亚洲青年乐团的演奏，这是亚洲最富创意的乐团，成员来自四个不同的亚洲国家，他们在表演中融合了多种民乐风格。在节目的下半段，我们会听到日本乐团Kaito的演奏，他们擅长演奏自然原声态音乐。还有，别忘了这两个乐团都会于本周末在世界民歌节上演出。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **feature**：以为特色
- **premier**：最著名的
- **folk**：民间的
- **act**：幕，场
- **perform**：表演，演出
- **ensemble**：乐团
- **innovative**：有创意的
- **performer**：表演者，演奏者
- **blend**：混合，融合
- **a variety of**：各种各样的
- **specialize in ~**：以为专长，擅长
- **acoustic**：声音的；音响的
- **host**：主持人
- **conductor**：（乐队）指挥
- **put together**：把组合在一起
- **nationality**：国籍
- **tour**：旅行，巡回演出

#### Q83 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Who is Ms. Boothby? (布思比女士是谁？)
- (A) A folk singer. (民歌歌手。)
- (B) The host. (节目主持人。)
- (C) An engineer. (工程师。)
- (D) A conductor. (乐队指挥。)

#### Q84 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Which of the following is mentioned about the Young Asia Ensemble? (关于亚洲青年乐团广播中，提到了下面的哪一条内容？)
- (A) The musical group was put together only recently. (乐队只是最近才组建的。)
- (B) All the members do not share the same nationality. (成员的国籍不都一样。)
- (C) The group is currently on a tour around Asia. (乐队目前正在亚洲巡回演出。)
- (D) They specialize in natural acoustic sounds. (他们擅长自然原声态的音乐。)

#### Q85 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** When will the mentioned groups perform at the festival? (提到的两个乐队何时会在音乐节上表演？)
- (A) Today. (今天。)
- (B) This weekend. (本周末。)
- (C) Next week. (下周。)
- (D) Next month. (下个月。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **in store for you = coming your way = waiting for you …** (等着你)
  - *例句：We have something very special in store for you.* (我们为您准备了非常特别的东西。)
- **a two-part program = a two-part series program** (两集节目，上下集节目)
  - *例句：This documentary will be aired as a two-part program with the first program being telecast this evening.* (这个纪录片会作为一个上下集的节目播出，上集将在今晚播出。)

### Questions 86 - 88

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Good evening, ladies and gentlemen, and welcome to the biennial Shipbuilding Research Convention. (86) I'm very pleased and proud, as the convener of this convention, to introduce to you one of the world's leading research scientists in the field of shipbuilding, Professor Nathan Davidson. (87) Professor Davidson's speech, entitled “Shipbuilding: the next twenty years”, will form the basis of a book to be published later this year. (88) I'm sure that you're all aware that whatever Professor Davidson has to say is not only fascinating and original, but also extremely pertinent. So, please welcome Professor Davidson.

**中文对照：**
> 女士们先生们，晚上好，欢迎参加两年一届的船舶制造研究大会。作为大会的召集人，我非常高兴和自豪地向大家介绍船舶制造领域的一位世界顶级科学家——内森·戴维森教授。戴维森教授演讲的题目是“船舶制造：下一个二十年”。以此演讲内容为基础的一本著作将在今年晚些时候出版。我肯定你们都会意识到，戴维森教授演讲的内容不但引人入胜、见解独到，而且同时也极为切题。因此，请大家欢迎戴维森教授演讲。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **biennial**：两年一次的
- **shipbuilding**：造船业
- **convention**：大会，集会
- **convener**：会议召集人
- **leading**：处于领先地位的
- **entitle**：把命名为
- **be aware that ~**：意识到，明白
- **whatever**：无论什么
- **original**：新颖的，有独创性的
- **pertinent**：切题的，贴切的
- **shipbuilder**：造船者，造船公司

#### Q86 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** How often is the event held? (该会议多久举办一次？)
- (A) Once a year. (一年一次。)
- (B) Once every two years. (两年一次。)
- (C) Once every five years. (五年一次。)
- (D) Once every ten years. (十年一次。)

#### Q87 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Who is Nathan Davidson? (内森 · 戴维森是谁？)
- (A) A shipbuilder. (造船者。)
- (B) A scientist. (科学家。)
- (C) The convener. (会议召集人。)
- (D) A publisher. (出版商。)

#### Q88 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** According to the speaker, what is expected to happen toward the end of the year? (根据讲话者所说，今年年底会有什么事发生？)
- (A) Another seminar will take place. (将会举行另一个研讨会。)
- (B) The research project will be completed. (这个研究计划将完成。)
- (C) A book will be published. (一本书将出版。)
- (D) The world's largest ship will be built. (世界上最大的船将造好。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **biennial = every two years = every second year** (每两年，两年一次的)
  - *例句：This is a biennial meeting.* (这是一个两年一届的会议。)
- **You're all aware ~ = You all know ~ = You are all familiar with ~** (你们都知道…)
  - *例句：I'm sure that you're all aware of the next guest I am going to introduce to you.* (我肯定你们都知道我将介绍给你们的下一位来宾。)

### Questions 89 - 91

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Welcome to tonight's “At the Movies”. My name is Michael Sanderson, (89) and it's my great pleasure to bring you all the latest movie news, plus previews of this week's blockbuster movie releases. And, if you're an action movie fan, this is going to be a great week. The long-awaited sequel to Dangerous Mission, starring Danny Jackson, will finally be released this week. The movie, which is called Dangerous Mission II: In Enemy Territory, is expected to break all box-office records. (90) We'll be showing an extended interview with Danny Jackson and the director, Jacky Lee. But first, let's have a look at some of the incredible action scenes, plus some of the action on the set during the making of In Enemy Territory. (91)

**中文对照：**
> 欢迎收看今晚的“看电影”。我是迈克尔·桑德森，很高兴为大家带来所有最新的电影资讯，还有本周上映的票房大片的预告片。另外，如果您是动作片迷，本周将是激动人心的一周，因为期待已久的由丹尼·杰克逊主演的《危险任务》续集终于将在本周上映了。这部名为《危险任务2敌占区》的电影将有望打破所有票房纪录。我们还会播放一段对丹尼·杰克逊和导演杰克·李的专访。不过，我们首先还是来看一下部分精彩的电影片断，以及《敌占区》拍摄现场的一些动作画面。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **preview**：〈美〉预告片
- **release**：发行，（电影）上映
- **sequel**：续集，续篇
- **star**：由主演
- **enemy**：敌人，敌军
- **territory**：领地，领土
- **have a look at**：看一看
- **incredible**：难以置信的；极妙的
- **host**：主持人
- **critic**：评论家
- **air**：播出
- **commercial break**：插播广告
- **behind the scene**：幕后

#### Q89 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Who is Michael Sanderson? (迈克尔 · 桑德森是谁？)
- (A) An actor. (演员。)
- (B) The host. (主持人。)
- (C) A critic. (评论家。)
- (D) The director. (导演。)

#### Q90 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What is Dangerous Mission? (《危险任务》是什么？)
- (A) A radio show. (一个广播节目。)
- (B) A film. (一部电影。)
- (C) A book. (一本书。)
- (D) A play. (一部戏剧。)

#### Q91 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What will be aired first? (最先播出的将是什么？)
- (A) An interview with the stars. (对明星的专访。)
- (B) Commercial breaks. (插播广告。)
- (C) Behind the scene stories. (幕后故事。)
- (D) The critic's opinion. (评论家的观点。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **break all box-office records** (打破所有票房纪录扩展表达：)
  - *例句：record the highest sales make the most profits The newly released movie is expected to break all box-office records.* (创最高的销售纪录创造最大利润新发行的影片预计能打破所有票房纪录。)
- **Let's have a look at ~ = Let's take a look at ~** (我们来看一看…)
  - *例句：Let's take a look at the problem together.* (我们一起来看一看这个问题。)

### Questions 92 - 94

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Audio World is opening a new store and we're celebrating. (92) Yes, it's party time at Audio World, and you're invited! Come on down for the opening of the spacious new store in exciting downtown George St. Festivities will begin at 9:00 a.m. on Saturday morning, (93) with free performances, balloons and face- painting for your children. And of course, there'll be some incredible opening specials. (94) Here's an example: complete hi-fi sound systems for as little as $500. (92) At last you can get that surround sound system you've been dreaming of! And that's not all: all day there will be specials, with discounts of as much as 50%. See you all on Saturday morning, at our new George St. superstore!

**中文对照：**
> 音响世界的新店铺就要开张了，我们将为此举办庆祝活动。是的，这是音响世界的欢聚时刻，我们邀请您来参加！请到市中心热闹的乔治大街来参加我们宽敞的新店铺的开张典礼。庆祝活动将于星期六上午9点开始。我们给孩子们准备了免费演出、气球、还有脸部油彩。当然，还会有令人难以置信的开张特价商品等着您。比如，完全高保真音响系统只卖五百美元。您终于可以得到梦寐以求的环绕音响系统了！这还不是全部，全天都会有特价商品，折扣低至五折。周六上午在乔治大街我们的新店见吧！

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **come on down**：（快点儿）到
- **spacious**：宽敞的
- **downtown**：城里，市中心
- **free**：免费的
- **performance**：表演，演出
- **balloon**：气球
- **incredible**：难以置信的
- **special**：特价商品
- **at last**：终于
- **surround sound system**：环绕音响系统
- **superstore**：超市
- **giveaway**：赠品

#### Q92 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What is being advertised? (这个广告是关于什么的？)
- (A) Electronics store. (电子产品商店。)
- (B) Supermarket. (超市。)
- (C) Record shop. (唱片商店。)
- (D) Painting store. (绘画商店。)

#### Q93 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** When will the event take place? (活动在什么时候举行？)
- (A) Today. (今天。)
- (B) This weekend. (本周末。)
- (C) Next week. (下周。)
- (D) Next month. (下个月。)

#### Q94 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** Which of the following will NOT be part of the day's event? (当天活动不包括下面的哪一项？)
- (A) Price discounts. (打折。)
- (B) Face paintings. (脸部油彩。)
- (C) Performances. (演出。)
- (D) Free giveaways. (发放赠品。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **You've been dreaming of ~ = You've been hoping for ~ = You've been aching for ~** (你一直梦寐以求得到…)
  - *例句：I know how much you've been dreaming of buying your own home.* (我知道你多么梦想买自己的房子。)
- **And that's not all. = And there is more. = And to top it off.** (而且不止如此。)
  - *例句：And that's not all, folks! We have something special for you next.* (朋友们，不止这些！我们下面还有特别的东西带给你们。)

### Questions 95 - 97

![Page 59](images/listen_page_59.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
It's come to my attention that our latest advertising campaign isn't doing well. In fact, sales of several of our items declined right after our newest TV commercials started airing. (95) According to customer feedback, the ads are extremely unappealing and make people not want to purchase our products. As such, I'm canceling the ad campaign and firing Walters Media. (96) We need to start a new media campaign to make up for the damage that has been done at once. I've decided to use Pembroke Advertising. (97) Janet, I want you to contact the company at once and request that a representative be sent here. Ideally, someone should arrive tomorrow morning.

**中文对照：**
> 我注意到我们最近的广告宣传活动做得不好。实际上，自从最新的电视广告片播出之后，我们几种货品的销量都下降了。根据顾客的反馈，我们的广告非常没有吸引力，看了之后不想购买我们的商品。基于此种情况，我取消了这次广告宣传活动并与沃尔斯特传媒解约。我们需要立即开展一场新的媒体宣传活动来弥补已经造成的损失。我已经决定与彭波洛克广告公司合作。珍妮特，请你迅速联系这家公司并要求其派一名代表过来。如果理想的话，明天一早应该有人过来。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **advertising campaign**：广告宣传活动
- **in fact**：实际上，事实上
- **commercial**：（商业）广告
- **feedback**：反馈，回馈
- **purchase**：购买
- **cancel**：取消；消除
- **make up for**：补偿，弥补
- **representative**：代表；典型

#### Q95 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What is the problem? (（讲话中的）问题是什么？)
- (A) Sales have decreased. (销量下降了。)
- (B) A company is behind schedule. (一家公司落后于预定计划。)
- (C) A budget has been exceeded. (超过预算了。)
- (D) Some stores have closed. (一些商店关门了。)

#### Q96 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the woman say about Walters Media? (女士说了沃尔斯特传媒公司的什么信息？)
- (A) She likes the work it does. (她欣赏这家公司所做的工作。)
- (B) She thinks it charges too much. (她认为这家公司收费太高。)
- (C) She will no longer use its services. (她不会再使用这家公司的服务了。)
- (D) She is unfamiliar with its work. (她不熟悉这家公司的工作内容。)

#### Q97 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. What number will Janet most likely call? (请看图表。珍妮特最可能拨打哪个电话？)
- (A) 290-4837 (290-4837)
- (B) 381-0274 (381-0274)
- (C) 582-1275 (582-1275)
- (D) 259-4783 (259-4783)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **It's come to my attention that ~ = I notice that ~** (我注意到…)
  - *例句：It's come to my attention that autumn is coming.* (我注意到秋天来了。)
- **I've decided to ~ = I've made my mind to ~** (我决定…)
  - *例句：I've decided to go travelling tomorrow.* (我已经决定明天去旅行了。)

### Questions 98 - 100

![Page 59](images/listen_page_59.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Good morning, Mr. Stewart. This is Chuck Pierson from Holloway Housewares calling. We received the order form which you mailed to us and are currently working on filling it. (98) Unfortunately, we no longer stock item number TR394. (99) If you want, we can give you your money back, or we can replace it with a similar item. If you look at page 38 of your catalog, you can see several items which are nearly identical to it. (100) They are roughly the same price, too. Why don't you call me back at 493-9373 to let me know what you decide to do? Thanks. Goodbye.

**中文对照：**
> 斯图尔特先生，早上好。我是霍洛威家居用品的查克·皮尔森。我们收到了您邮寄过来的订单，目前正在给您配货。不巧的是，我们目前没有TR394这一货品的存货了。如果您同意，我们可以将钱款退还给您，或者我们用一件类似的货品代替。如果您方便查看目录的38页，就可以看到几种跟TR394几乎相同的货品。它们的价格也基本一致。请致电493-9373告知我们您的决定。非常感谢。再见。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **houseware**：家居用品
- **order form**：订（购）单
- **no longer**：不再
- **stock**：库存；股票
- **catalog**：目录
- **identical**：同一的；完全相同的
- **roughly**：粗野地；大致上

#### Q98 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** How did Mr. Stewart place his order? (斯图尔特先生是用什么方式下的订单？)
- (A) By visiting a store. (通过拜访门店。)
- (B) By phone. (通过电话。)
- (C) By mail. (通过邮寄。)
- (D) By fax. (通过传真。)

#### Q99 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Which item is no longer available? (请看图表。哪些货品已经没有了？)
- (A) Porcelain dinnerplate. (陶瓷餐盘。)
- (B) Crystal wineglass. (水晶葡萄酒杯。)
- (C) Glass salad bowl. (玻璃沙拉碗。)
- (D) Champagne glass. (香槟酒杯。)

#### Q100 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the speaker suggest Mr. Stewart do? (讲话者建议斯图尔特先生做什么？)
- (A) Cancel his order. (取消他的订单。)
- (B) Look at a catalog. (看一看目录。)
- (C) Buy an item on sale. (买一件打折商品。)
- (D) Pay for express shipping. (支付快递费用。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **no longer = not any longer = not any more** (不再/再也不)
  - *例句：She was no longer a child.* (她不再是个孩子了。)
- **give ~ back = return ~ back** (将…归还/返还)
  - *例句：Please give the book back to him when he comes back.* (他回来时请把这本书还给他。)

## Part 1: 照片描述 (Q1 - Q6)

### Q1 (正确答案：B)

![Page 61](images/listen_page_61.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) They're clapping their hands. (他们正在鼓掌。)
- (B) They're facing one another. (他们正面对着面。)
- (C) They're waving their hands. (他们正在挥手。)
- (D) They're pacing around the place. (他们正在附近慢慢地走着。)

**其他可能表达：**
- They are shaking hands. (他们正在握手。)
- The men are looking at each other. (两个人在相互看着对方。)
- They are greeting one another. (他们在相互问候。)


### Q2 (正确答案：B)

![Page 61](images/listen_page_61.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) A piece of furniture is being repaired. (一件家具正在被修理。)
- (B) A machine is being worked on. (一台机器正在被修理。)
- (C) A toolbox is being opened. (一个工具箱正在被打开。)
- (D) A desk drawer is being closed. (一个书桌抽屉正在被关上。)

**其他可能表达：**
- The machine has been taken
- apart. (机器已经被拆开了。)
- The machine is being fixed. (机器正在被修理。)
- The machine is being put together. (机器正在被组装。)


### Q3 (正确答案：C)

![Page 61](images/listen_page_61.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) She has finished talking on the phone. (她已经打完电话了。)
- (B) A notice is being posted on the door. (一张通知正被人往门上贴。)
- (C) She has the receiver held up to her ear. (她把听筒举到耳朵边。)
- (D) A coin is being placed into the slot. (一枚硬币正被放进投币口。)

**其他可能表达：**
- She's speaking into a phone. (她正在打电话。)
- She's involved in a phone conversation. (她正在通话当中。)
- A public phone is in use. (一部公用电话正在被使用。)


### Q4 (正确答案：C)

![Page 62](images/listen_page_62.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) Some people are sunbathing near the lake. (一些人正在湖边沐日光浴。)
- (B) Some people are ready to go for a swim. (一些人准备好了去游泳。)
- (C) Some people are strolling near the water. (一些人正在水边闲逛。)
- (D) Some people have put their feet in the water. (一些人已经把脚放入了水中。)

**其他可能表达：**
- Some men are walking along the water. (几个人正在水边散步。)
- The people are walking toward a bridge. (人们正朝一座桥走去。)
- There are no swimmers in the water. (水中没有人在游泳。)


### Q5 (正确答案：D)

![Page 62](images/listen_page_62.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) He's serving food to the others. (他正在为别人上菜。)
- (B) He's holding a plastic cup in his hand. (他的手中正拿着一个塑料杯。)
- (C) He's arranging the plates on the table. (他正往桌上摆放盘子。)
- (D) He's helping himself to some food. (他正在随便吃些东西。)

**其他可能表达：**
- A man is putting food onto his plate. (男士正在把食物放到自己的盘子里。)
- A variety of food has been laid out on the table. (各种食物已经被摆在桌子上了。)
- Some food has been prepared on the table. (一些食物已经准备好了，放在)
- 桌子上。


### Q6 (正确答案：C)

![Page 62](images/listen_page_62.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) The house is undergoing renovations. (房子正在被整修。)
- (B) The bushes are being trimmed. (小树丛正在被修剪。)
- (C) Some furniture has been set out in the yard. (一些家具已经被放到院子里了。)
- (D) People are relaxing in the backyard. (人们正在后院里放松。)

**其他可能表达：**
- A portion of the area has been shaded. (一部分地方被树荫遮住了。)
- The seats have been positioned in the shaded area. (座椅已经被放在了阴凉处。)
- The grass has been neatly trimmed. (草坪已经被整齐地修剪过了。)
- 注：在Part 1中，每道试题都添加了3种可能的正确表达方式，考生可
- 以了解对于同样的照片可能出现的不同表达。


## Part 2: 应答测试 (Q7 - Q31)

### Q7 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Who is going to write the letter? (谁将会写这封信？)
- **A:** Jane will. (简。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Who will draft the letter? (谁将会起草这封信？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) He will come by later. (他会晚一点来。)
  - (B) Yes, he left it there. (是的，他把它留在那儿了。)
  - (C) Jane is working on it now. (简正在写。)


### Q8 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** When will they announce the result of the report? (他们什么时候会宣布报告结果？)
- **A:** Before the end of the day. (今天下班之前。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** When are they going to release the report? (他们什么时候发布这个报告？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) By fax. (用传真。)
  - (B) At two o'clock. (在 2 点。)
  - (C) In Room 15. (在 15 号房间。)


### Q9 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Where is the bus stop for the bus to downtown? (到市中心的公交车站在哪儿？)
- **A:** Across the street. (街对面。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Do you know where I can catch a bus to downtown? (你知道在哪儿能坐公交车去市中心吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) He just left a minute ago. (他一分钟前刚走。)
  - (B) Sure, I will catch you later. (当然，我晚点儿再跟你谈。)
  - (C) Try the stop over there. (去那边的车站看看。)


### Q10 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Did you manage to find the books you were looking for? (你找到你一直在找的书了吗？)
- **A:** No, they didn't have them in stock. (没有，这些书他们没货了。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Were you able to pick up the books you need? (你买到需要的书了吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I booked it this morning. (我今天上午预订了。)
  - (B) No, they were all sold out. (没有，都卖完了。)
  - (C) Can you pick me up at 5? (你能 5 点来接我吗？)


### Q11 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How long will you be gone for today? (你今天要离开多久？)
- **A:** I should be back by noon. (我应该中午之前回来。注：在Part 2中，为帮助考生提高听懂题目的能力，添加了和试题相同或相似的表达方法。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** How long will you be on the road today? (你今天在路上会花多长时间？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I'll be back around three. (我会在三点左右回来。)
  - (B) Roughly an hour ago. (大约一个小时之前。)
  - (C) Yes, I will be driving there. (是的，我会开车去那儿。)


### Q12 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Were you able to get through to him, or do you want me to try calling him? (你能打通他的电话吗，还是你想让我试着给他打电话？)
- **A:** Could you try calling him again? (你能给他再打一遍试试吗？)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Did you get in touch with him, or should I try calling? (你和他联系上了没有，要我打电话试试看吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I just got off the phone with him. (我刚和他讲完电话。)
  - (B) He is sitting on the couch. (他正在长椅上坐着。)
  - (C) I'll get it for you later. (我过一会儿把它带给你。)


### Q13 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Shouldn't you be leaving for your appointment with your lawyer now? (你不是应该出发去见你的律师了吗？)
- **A:** No, I am seeing him later today. (不，我今天晚些时候见他。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Don't you have to go to your appointment with your lawyer soon? (你不是马上就得去见你的律师吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) To discuss some legal matters. (去讨论一些法律事宜。)
  - (B) Yes, right after I am done with this. (是的，我做完这个马上就去。)
  - (C) No, he made a point not to do that. (不，他强调不能那样做。)


### Q14 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Who is going to drive you to the software exhibition? (谁将开车带你去软件展览？)
- **A:** I'm supposed to go with Mr. Smith later. (我稍后应该会和史密斯先生一起去。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Who's planning to take you to the software exhibition? (谁计划带你去软件展览？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) He will take his car. (他会用他的车。)
  - (B) Jack said he will. (杰克说他会。)
  - (C) To get some information. (去获得一些信息。)


### Q15 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**

- **A:** She wants to study more. (她想学习更多的知识。)

**听力原文与选项：**

- **选项：**
  - (A) She decided to go back to school. (她决定重返校园。)
  - (B) Sure, just leave it right here. (当然，就把它放在这儿吧。)
  - (C) Yes, she doesn't get along with her boss. (是的，她和老板相处得不好。)


### Q16 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** David Wells gave a great speech today, didn't he? (戴维·韦尔斯今天做了一个很棒的演讲，是吧？)
- **A:** Yes, it was one of his best speeches ever. (是的，这次是他最好的演讲之一。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** David Wells did a good job delivering his speech today, didn't he? (戴维 · 韦尔斯今天的演讲做得很好，是吧？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) He took it to a wrong address. (他把它送到了错误的地址。)
  - (B) No, the job is quite interesting. (不，这个工作很有趣。)
  - (C) Yes, he did a great job. (是的，他表现得非常好。)


### Q17 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Isn't it a bit cold with the air conditioner on? (空调开着不冷吗？)
- **A:** It is a bit chilly, isn't it? (有点儿冷，是吧？)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Don't you feel a bit chilly with the air conditioner on? (你不觉得开着空调有点儿冷吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, it's freezing in here. (是的，这里非常冷。)
  - (B) No, I don't feel too well. (不，我感觉不太好。)
  - (C) He is a bit silly. (他有点儿蠢。)


### Q18 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Where do you think I can buy the things on the list? (你认为我在哪儿能买到清单上的东西？)
- **A:** Probably in that supermarket over there. (在那边的超市可能会买到。)

  - (B) It's too heavy to pick it up alone. (它太沉了，我一个人拿不起来。)
  - (C) Yes, I think you can do it. (是的，我认为你能行。)

### Q21 (正确答案：B)

### Q22 (正确答案：A)

- **A:** No, there is no difference in the price. (不，价格没有区别。)

**听力原文与选项：**

  - (B) I will charge it on my credit card. (我要用信用卡付费。)
  - (C) Yes, there will be a couple more people. (是的，还会再来几个人。)


### Q23 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**

- **A:** Please sign on the last page. (请在最后一页签字。)

**听力原文与选项：**

- **选项：**
  - (A) I already told you his name. (我已经告诉你他的名字了。)
  - (B) Just sign the last one. (只需在最后一页签。)
  - (C) The sign is rather noticeable. (标记很明显。)


### Q24 (正确答案：B)

- **A:** I received his phone call this morning. (我今天上午接到他的电话了。)

**听力原文与选项：**

- **选项：**
  - (A) I will finish it by then. (我到时候就会完成。)
  - (B) He said sometime in May. (他说五月份的某个时候。)
  - (C) He will make the suggestion. (他会提出建议。)


### Q25 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Don't you think we need to work on this design a bit more? (你不觉得我们需要把这个设计再加工一下吗？)
- **A:** Yes, I was thinking the same thing. (是的，我正是这么想的。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Don't you think this design could be improved more? (你不认为这个设计还可以再改进吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) To the designated area. (去指定的区域。)
  - (B) Why? Don't you think it looks nice? (为什么？你不认为它看起来很漂亮吗？)
  - (C) Yes, we decided to proofread it again. (是的，我们决定再校对一遍。)


### Q26 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**

- **A:** I'm meeting someone for lunch today. (我今天要和一个人共进午餐。)

**听力原文与选项：**

- **选项：**
  - (A) That sounds fine by me. (我觉得那听起来不错。)
  - (B) I have to meet a client at noon. (我中午得见一个客户。)
  - (C) How is the Italian place? (意大利风味的地方怎么样？)


### Q27 (正确答案：C)

- **A:** Sure, I'll be with you in a second. (当然可以，我一会儿就来帮你。)

**听力原文与选项：**

- **选项：**
  - (A) To the second floor. (到二层去。)
  - (B) That is a great offer. (那是一个很好的提议。)
  - (C) Sure, give me a second first. (当然可以，稍等我一会儿。)


### Q28 (正确答案：B)

- **A:** I submitted the form yesterday. (我昨天提交了申请表。)

**听力原文与选项：**

- **选项：**
  - (A) I live about twenty minutes from here. (我住在离这儿二十分钟远的地方。)
  - (B) Yes, I was planning on doing that. (是的，我正打算那样做。)
  - (C) Two of my friends live there. (我的两个朋友住在那儿。)


### Q29 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**

- **A:** He went to see a client. (他去见客户了。)

- **选项：**
  - (A) Mr. Sellers is coming this morning. (塞勒斯先生今天上午要来。)
  - (B) I've been hearing it a lot lately, too. (关于这件事，我最近也听说了很多。)
  - (C) No, but Judy should know where he is. (不知道，但是朱迪应该知道他在哪儿。)


### Q30 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**

- **A:** It will be our best project ever. (这将是我们有史以来最好的项目。)

**听力原文与选项：**
