- **选项：**
  - (A) It is going to be very profitable. (它会非常赚钱的。)
  - (B) Yes, John will be here today. (是的，约翰今天会来。)
  - (C) Sure, I will put you in charge of it. (当然，我会让你来负责它。)


### Q31 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How about having our meeting here, or is this room already taken? (在这里开会怎么样，还是这个房间已经被预订了？)
- **A:** I'll go and check with Sarah. (我去找萨拉核实一下。Questions 32 through 34 refer to the following conversation.W:Pardon me， but are you giving any more tours of the gallery thisafternoon？（)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Shall we get together here, or is this room already reserved? (我们在这里聚会吗，还是这个房间已经被预订了？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) There should still be some room. (应该还有地方。)
  - (B) I'll call the restaurant later. (我过一会儿给饭店打电话。)
  - (C) It's available as far as I know. (据我所知，它可以用。)


## Part 3: 简短对话 (Q32 - Q70)

### Questions 32 - 34

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Pardon me, but are you giving any more tours of the gallery this afternoon? (32)
**M:** Yes, there's one more, but it won't start until twenty minutes from now. Would you like to go on it?
**W:** Definitely. I guess I can browse around the gift shop while I wait for it to start. Where do I need to be when the tour begins?
**M:** Come right back here. Would you please sign your name on the sheet so that you can reserve a spot on the tour? (33)
**W:** I need to do that? How come?
**M:** This tour is limited to twenty people since it's being given by the curator. He doesn't often do that. (34)

**中文对照：**
> **W：**对不起，请问你今天下午会再安排参观美术馆吗？
> **M：**是的，还有一次游览，但是20分钟之后开始。你想继续参加吗？
> **W：**当然。我想我在等待的这段时间可以随意逛逛礼品店。游览开始时，我需要在哪里集合呢？
> **M：**回到这里就行。请在表格上签名好吗？这样就可以为此次游览预订一个名额。
> **W：**需要这样做吗？为什么？
> **M：**游览只限20人，因为这次是由美术馆馆长当向导。他平时很少这样做。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **tour**：游览
- **gallery**：美术馆；画廊
- **go on**：继续
- **browse around**：闲逛
- **gift shop**：礼品店
- **sign one's name**：签某人的名字
- **reserve**：预订
- **curator**：（美术馆、博物馆）馆长

#### Q32 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Where does the conversation most likely take place? (对话最有可能发生在哪儿？)
- (A) In a gift shop. (在礼品店。)
- (B) In a museum. (在博物馆。)
- (C) In a gallery. (在美术馆。)
- (D) In a palace. (在宫殿。)

#### Q33 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the man ask the woman to do? (男士要求女士做什么？)
- (A) Sign her name. (签下她的名字。)
- (B) Pay a fee. (支付费用。)
- (C) Show an ID card. (出示身份证。)
- (D) Wait by a store. (在一家商店旁边等候。)

#### Q34 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What is suggested about the tour? (关于此次游览，文章暗示了什么？)
- (A) It will last around twenty minutes. (它将持续 20 分钟左右。)
- (B) It only covers the first two floors. (它只参观一二层楼。)
- (C) It will have a different guide than normal. (与平常相比，它将有一位不同的导游。)
- (D) It will be conducted in a foreign language. (它将使用外语解说。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **pardon me = excuse me** (对不起，打扰一下)
  - *例句：Pardon me, could you tell me where the super market is?* (打扰一下，您能告诉我超市在哪里吗？)
- **Would you please = Could you please** (（用于礼貌的请求）能否麻烦您…？)
  - *例句：Would you please lend me your bike?* (能借用一下你的自行车吗？)
- **so that = in order that** (以便，为了)
  - *例句：Please write down your phone number so that we can inform you of latest information.* (请写下您的手机号码，以便我们可以通知您最新消息。)
- **How come (~)? = How does/did it happen （ that ）** (？（口语）…怎么回事？)
  - *例句：How come you never visit me any more?* (你究竟为什么总不来看我呢？)

### Questions 35 - 37

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Hi, is there anything I can help you with today, sir?
**M:** Yes, I was told by a shopkeeper down the road that you specialize in clothes for big people. (35) I've been looking around this entire area for the last hour, but I have not had any luck yet. I really do hope you have what I am looking for.
**W:** Yes, I think we may be able to help you out. In fact, the entire second floor completely caters to people who are considered big. (36) If you walk up to the second floor, (37) you will see there are many fashionable clothes to choose from at very reasonable prices.
**M:** Wow, this is wonderful. I don't understand why I've never heard of this place before.

**中文对照：**
> **W：**您好，先生，我能帮您什么吗？
> **M：**是的，街那头的一个店主告诉我，你们这里专营为身材高大的顾客设计的服装。我在这一带已经找了一个小时了，可是一点儿也不走运。我真希望你这里有我要找的东西。
> **W：**是的，我想我们也许能帮上忙。事实上，整个二层完全都是为身材高大的顾客准备的。您上了二楼，就会看到有很多时髦的衣服可供选择，而且价格实惠。
> **M：**哇，太好了。我真不明白为什么我以前没听说过这个地方。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **shopkeeper**：店主，老板
- **down**：沿着往前，顺着
- **specialize in**：专门从事
- **look around**：在附近查看，寻找
- **entire**：完整的，整个的
- **cater to someone**：满足某人的需要
- **walk up to ~**：走上
- **fashionable**：时尚的
- **at a reasonable price**：以合理的价格
- **ad advertisement**：）广告
- **close**：紧密的，亲近的
- **refer**：指点，使求助于
- **carry**：备有（货品），有出售
- **conveniently**：方便地，便利地
- **be known**：知名，闻名
- **try on**：穿上试一试

#### Q35 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** How did the man learn of this place? (男士如何知道这个地方的？)
- (A) He saw an ad in the paper. (他在报纸上看到了广告。)
- (B) He was told about it by a close friend. (一个好朋友告诉他的。)
- (C) He was referred there by someone. (有人告诉他去那儿。)
- (D) He found it by luck. (他靠运气找到的。)

#### Q36 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the woman mention is special about this place? (女士提到，这个地方的特别之处是什么？)
- (A) They carry clothes for heavy people. (他们有适合体重较重的顾客穿的衣服。)
- (B) They are very conveniently located. (他们所处的位置交通便利。)
- (C) They sell the cheapest clothing in town. (他们卖的衣服是城里最便宜的。)
- (D) They are very well known in the area. (他们在这个地区非常有名。)

#### Q37 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What will the man do next? (男士下一步会做什么？)
- (A) Pay for his purchase. (为所购商品付账。)
- (B) Go to another store. (去另一家商店。)
- (C) Walk up to the next floor. (到二楼去。)
- (D) Try on some clothes. (试几件衣服。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **look around = search around** (在附近查看，寻找)
  - *例句：I've been looking around the place for an hour.* (我已经在这附近寻找了一个小时了。)
- **I have not had any luck yet.** (我一点儿也不走运。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：I have not found it yet. I have not been successful yet.* (我还没找到它。我还没有成功。)
- **look for = search for = try to find** (寻找，搜寻)
  - *例句：I've been looking for your place for an hour.* (我找你家找了一个小时了。)
- **cater to** (满足…的需要)
  - *例句：The new boss caters to every need of his staff members.* (新老板尽量满足员工的每一个需要。)
- **reasonable prices = affordable prices = low prices** (合理的、实惠的价格)
  - *例句：The items on the list had reasonable prices.* (清单上的物品价格实惠。)

### Questions 38 - 40

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Jane, can you spare an hour this afternoon? I need you to explain some of the figures you put down on the report I got from you last week. （ 38, 39 ）
**W:** I'm terribly sorry, Jack, but could that wait until tomorrow? I have to step out of the office right after lunch to meet with a very important client downtown. I have a great chance to land a big contract today.
**M:** Oh, is that right? I really do hope you get it. Anyway, could you do me a favor and drop by my office first thing tomorrow morning? (40) I really need you to explain some of the parts I don't understand in the report.
**W:** Sure thing, Jack. I will be in your office at 9 o'clock sharp. (40)

**中文对照：**
> **M：**简，你今天下午能抽出一个小时的时间吗？我需要你解释一下你上周交给我的那份报告里的一些数据。
> **W：**非常抱歉，杰克。这事能等到明天吗？我午饭后得马上出门，去市中心见一个非常重要的客户。我今天很有可能签下一个大合同。
> **M：**哦，真的吗？我真希望你能成功。不管怎样，你能帮我这个忙吗，明天早上顺道先来我办公室一趟？我非常需要你解释一下报告里我不太明白的几个地方。
> **W：**没问题，杰克。我九点准时到你的办公室。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **spare**：抽出（时间）
- **figure**：数字
- **put down**：记下，写下
- **step out of ~**：从出去
- **land**：赢得，获得
- **favor**：恩惠，好意
- **drop by**：顺便拜访
- **sharp**：（用于表时间的词后）整
- **clarify**：澄清，阐明
- **personal**：个人的，私人的

#### Q38 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** When was the report submitted? (报告是什么时间提交的？)
- (A) Today. (今天。)
- (B) Yesterday. (昨天。)
- (C) Last week. (上周。)
- (D) Two weeks ago. (两周以前。)

#### Q39 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Why does the man want to meet with the woman? (男士为什么要约见女士？)
- (A) To ask her to clarify something he does not understand. (让她解释一些他不明白的问题。)
- (B) To ask for her help in preparing for the presentation. (让她帮忙准备报告。)
- (C) To discuss a personal problem with her. (和她商讨一个私人问题。)
- (D) To ask her to talk to his client. (让她和他的客户谈谈。)

#### Q40 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** When will the speakers most likely meet? (对话双方最有可能在什么时候见面？)
- (A) This afternoon. (今天下午。)
- (B) This evening. (今天晚上。)
- (C) Tomorrow morning. (明天早上。)
- (D) Tomorrow afternoon. (明天下午。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **Can you spare an hour? = Can I have an hour of your time? = Are you free for an hour?** (你能抽出一个小时吗？)
- **step out of ~ = go out of ~ = walk out of ~** (从…出去)
  - *例句：I need to step out of the office for a little bit.* (我需要离开办公室出去一会儿。)
- **land a big contract = sign a big deal = finalize a huge contract** (赢得一个大合同，签下一笔大买卖)
  - *例句：I am going to land a big contract soon.* (我快要签下一笔大买卖了。)
- **drop by = stop by = swing by** (顺道拜访)
  - *例句：Let's drop by the office first.* (咱们先顺道去一趟办公室。)

### Questions 41 - 43

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Aren't you ready yet? We have to take off soon, you know. The rain out there is starting to really come down hard, and the traffic on the road is probably going to be chaotic. (41)
**M:** I know. Just give me a second. I have to take this paper up to Mr. Kim's office before we take off. (42) Tell you what: why don't I meet you in the lobby in five minutes? This way, I can go back to my office to get my coat as well.
**W:** All right, Bob, but hurry up, please. This is our first meeting with Mr. Rowe, and I don't want to give him the wrong impression by being late.
**M:** Don't worry. We still have plenty of time. Besides, we are going to take the subway, so you don't have to worry about getting stuck in traffic. (43)

**中文对照：**
> **W：**你还没准备好吗？我们得马上出发。外面雨越下越大了，路上的交通很可能会变得很混乱。
> **M：**我知道。就等我一小会儿。我得在出发前把这份材料送到金先生的办公室。我跟你说，我五分钟后在大厅和你见面。这样，我还能回办公室去拿我的外套。
> **W：**好吧，鲍勃，不过请抓紧时间。这是我们第一次见罗先生，我不想因为迟到给他留下不好的印象。
> **M：**别担心。我们还有很多时间。另外，我们坐地铁去，所以你不用担心交通堵塞。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **take off**：出发，离开
- **come down**：落下，降落
- **traffic**：交通
- **chaotic**：混乱的，无秩序的
- **tell you what**：我跟你说
- **impression**：印象
- **plenty of**：很多
- **get stuck in traffic**：堵车
- **congested**：堵塞的
- **get a lift**：搭车

#### Q41 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** According to the woman, what will most likely cause the traffic to be congested? (根据女士所说，什么最有可能造成交通堵塞？)
- (A) Rush hour. (高峰时间。)
- (B) Bad weather. (坏天气。)
- (C) Accidents. (事故。)
- (D) Road construction. (修路。)

#### Q42 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What will the man do first? (男士首先要做什么？)
- (A) Walk down to the lobby. (走到大厅。)
- (B) Drop by Mr. Kim's office. (顺道去金先生办公室。)
- (C) Put on his coat. (穿上外套。)
- (D) Buy a train ticket. (买一张火车票。)

#### Q43 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** How will they get to Mr. Rowe's office? (他们怎么去罗先生的办公室？)
- (A) They will drive there. (他们会开车去。)
- (B) They will use public transportation. (他们会乘坐公共交通工具。)
- (C) They will get a lift from the woman. (他们会搭女士的车。)
- (D) They will walk there. (他们会走过去。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **The rain out there is starting to really come down hard. = The rain is pouring outside. = It's soaking wet outside.** (外面雨下得越来越大。)
- **be stuck in traffic = be caught in traffic = be held up in traffic** (堵车)
  - *例句：John is stuck in traffic and will be late to work.* (约翰遇到交通堵塞，上班要迟到了。)

### Questions 44 - 46

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Is there anything else I can get you, ma'am?
**W:** Yes, I would like to have this coffee refilled. Also, could you bring me the menu again? (44) I want to take a look at your choice of pies. (45) I overheard a couple saying how good your pies are here.
**M:** You must be from out of town if you don't know about our pies. In fact, most of our customers come here for our apple pie. (46) Of course that doesn't mean that our food is not good, it's just that our pies are out of this world. You have to try it.
**W:** Is that right? I guess you leave me no choice but to try it. I'll have the apple pie, please. (45)

**中文对照：**
> **M：**您还想点些什么，女士？
> **W：**好的，我想加满这杯咖啡。还有，你能再把菜单拿过来吗？我想看一下你们有哪些可选择的派。我无意中听到一对夫妇说你们这里的派特别好吃。
> **M：**如果您不知道我们的派，您肯定是从外地来的。事实上，大部分的顾客都是冲着我们的苹果派来这里的。当然，并不是说我们的菜不好吃，只是说我们的派太完美了。您一定要尝一尝。
> **W：**真的吗？我想你让我别无选择，只能尝尝看了。我点苹果派。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **refill**：再装满，补充
- **take a look at**：看一下
- **overhear**：无意中听到
- **out of this world**：十全十美的，无与伦比的
- **regular customer**：老顾客，回头客
- **conveniently**：方便地

#### Q44 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Where is the conversation taking place? (对话发生在哪里？)
- (A) In a copy store. (在一家复印店里。)
- (B) In a restaurant. (在一家饭店里。)
- (C) At an airport. (在机场。)
- (D) At a post office. (在邮局。)

#### Q45 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the woman ask for? (女士要了什么？)
- (A) Extra copies. (额外的复印件。)
- (B) Some dessert. (一些甜点。)
- (C) The receipt. (收据。)
- (D) A few stamps. (几张邮票。)

#### Q46 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the man mean when he says, “most of our customers come here for our apple pie”? (男士说 “ 大部分的顾客都是冲着我们的苹果派来这里的 ” ，是想表达什么意思？)
- (A) The place can hold many people at one time. (该地方一次可以容纳很多人。)
- (B) The place has many regular customers. (该地方有很多老顾客。)
- (C) The place closes early during weekdays. (该地方在工作日关门很早。)
- (D) The place is conveniently located in the center of town. (该地方位于市中心，交通便利。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **Is there anything else I can get you, ma'am? = Would you like something else, ma'am? = Will that be all, ma'am?** (您还想点些什么吗，女士？)
- **Our pies are out of this world.** (我们的派无与伦比。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：Our pies are really good. Our pies are the best in town.* (我们的派真是不错。我们的派是镇上最棒的。)

### Questions 47 - 49

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** As you can see, the kitchen has been redone, and the living room is spacious as well.
**W:** You're right. I really like the large backyard with the swimming pool, too. But what about the price?
**M:** The owner is asking for $220,000. What do you think? Shall I set up a meeting with him? (47)
**W:** I don't think so. That's out of my price range. (48)
**M:** All right, then I can show you something a bit cheaper if you'd like. (49)
**W:** Yes, that would be great. We can go there right now if you have time.
**M:** Sure. It's only about ten minutes away from here by car.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**如您所见，厨房已重新装修，且客厅也很宽敞。
> **W：**你说得对。我真的很喜欢带泳池的宽敞后院。但是价钱怎么样呢？
> **M：**房东要价22万美元。你觉得怎么样？需要我给你们安排会面吗？
> **W：**我认为不用了。这个价格超出了我可以接受的范围。
> **M：**好吧。如果你愿意，我可以带你看稍微便宜一些的。
> **W：**嗯，那真是太好了。如果你有时间的话，我们现在就可以过去。
> **M：**好的。从这里开车过去也就10分钟左右。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **as you can see**：如你所见；你知道的
- **redo**：重做
- **spacious**：宽敞的
- **as well**：也；同样地
- **swimming pool**：游泳池，游泳馆
- **owner**：所有者
- **set up**：安排；建立
- **away from**：距离

#### Q47 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Who most likely is the man? (这个人很有可能是什么身份？)
- (A) An interior decorator. (室内设计师。)
- (B) A home builder. (开发商。)
- (C) A real estate agent. (房产经纪人。)
- (D) An architect. (建筑师。)

#### Q48 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What does the woman most likely mean when she says,“I don't think so”? (当女士说 “ 我认为不用了 ” 的时候，她很有可能是什么意思？)
- (A) She does not have more time today. (她今天没更多时间。)
- (B) She does not want to take a tour. (她不想去旅游。)
- (C) She does not want to make a new offer. (她不想提供新的报价。)
- (D) She does not want to meet a homeowner. (她不想跟房主见面。)

#### Q49 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the man suggest doing? (这位男士建议做什么？)
- (A) Visiting another location. (去另一个地方看看。)
- (B) Going back to his office. (回他的办公室。)
- (C) Swimming in the pool. (在泳池里游泳。)
- (D) Looking at a Web site. (浏览一个网站。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **What about ~? = How about ~? …** (怎么样？)
  - *例句：What about going out for dinner?* (出去吃晚饭怎么样？)
- **out of one's price range = one cannot afford to buy = too expensive to buy I really like that new house, but the thing is, it's out of my price range!** (我很喜欢那栋新房子，但重点是，它超出了我能承受的价格范围！)
- **a bit = a little = a little bit** (一点儿；有点儿)
  - *例句：The weather is a bit unusual these days.* (最近天气有点儿反常。)

### Questions 50 - 52

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** I picked up a cell phone here the other day, but there is something the matter with the screen. It keeps blinking out all the time. I would like an exchange on it, please. (50)
**W:** Of course, sir. Why don't you give that to me, and I can get you a new one from the back room right away?
**M:** Actually, I was wondering if I could take another model instead? I was told that the new X-100 model has far more functions than the one I got. (51) Do you have it in stock today?
**W:** Yes, we do, and I think you have made a wise choice. This particular model was only released a week ago, and they're selling like hot cakes. Of course it is a bit more expensive, （ 51,52 ） and you will have to pay for the difference, but I think it will be well worth your money.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**我前几天在这里买了一部手机，但是屏幕有些问题，它总是在不停地闪。我想换一部。
> **W：**当然可以，先生。您把它给我吧，我马上到里屋给您拿一部新的。
> **M：**其实，我在想我能不能换另一个型号的？有人告诉我X-100型号的新款手机比我买的这个功能更多。这个型号今天有货吗？
> **W：**是的，有货。我想您做了一个明智的选择。这款特别的型号一周前才上市，现在卖得很火。当然它的价格贵一些，您还需要支付差价，不过我认为它物有所值。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **the other day**：几天前
- **blink**：闪烁
- **I was wondering if ~**：我在想，是不是
- **function**：功能
- **have ~ in stock**：有的存货
- **wise**：明智的
- **particular**：特别的，专门的
- **release**：发行，上市
- **be worth ~**：值
- **sell like hot cakes**：十分畅销，卖得很火
- **application**：用途，应用

#### Q50 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the man want to do? (男士想做什么？)
- (A) Get his money back. (拿回他的钱。)
- (B) Take another product. (换另外一款商品。)
- (C) Buy a cellular phone. (买一部手机。)
- (D) Try some cakes. (尝尝蛋糕。)

#### Q51 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What is NOT mentioned about the X-100 model? (关于 X-100 ，哪一点没有提到？)
- (A) Its applications. (它的用途。)
- (B) Its price. (它的价格。)
- (C) Its quality. (它的质量。)
- (D) Its popularity. (它的热销程度。)

#### Q52 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** Who is the man speaking with? (男士在和谁说话？)
- (A) A co-worker. (同事。)
- (B) A bank teller. (银行职员。)
- (C) A baker. (面包师。)
- (D) A salesperson. (售货员。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I picked up a cell phone here the other day. = I bought a mobile phone a few days ago. = I got a portable phone a couple of days ago.** (我几天前在这儿买了一部手机。)
- **Do you have it in stock today? = Do you have it in today?** (你这里今天有货吗？)
- **You have made a wise choice. = You have made a smart choice. = You have made a good choice.** (您做了一个明智的选择。)
- **sell like hot cakes = sell very well = sell like there is no tomorrow** (十分畅销，卖得很火)
  - *例句：The new product is selling like hot cakes.* (这款新产品十分畅销。)

### Questions 53 - 55

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Hi, I saw a for-rent sign on your lobby window. (53) I am looking for a two-bedroom apartment.
**W:** You are in luck. We do have an available apartment for rent on the fifth floor, and I think it may be exactly what you're looking for. It has two bedrooms, and the rent is quite reasonable. In fact, I don't think you will be able to find a place like this for a price this low anywhere near here. (54)
**M:** Really? Do you think I can take a look at it right now? I really am in a hurry to find a place.
**W:** Of course. Just give me a second, and I will get the key. (55)

**中文对照：**
> **M：**你好，我看到你在门厅窗户上贴的出租标志了。我正在找一套两居室的公寓。
> **W：**你真走运。我们在五层的确有一套出租的套间，我想可能就是你想找的。它有两个卧室，房租很便宜。事实上，我认为你在这附近很难以如此的低价找到类似这样的房子了。
> **M：**真的吗？我现在能看看房子吗？我真的着急找房。
> **W：**当然可以。稍等片刻，我去取钥匙。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **for-rent**：出租
- **be in luck**：运气好
- **reasonable**：合理的，（价格）公道的
- **take a look at**：看一看
- **be in a hurry**：匆忙，着急
- **real estate agent**：房地产经纪人，房地产经纪公司
- **affordable**：买得起的，能负担的
- **remove**：移动，撤掉
- **lease**：租赁
- **retrieve**：取回，找回

#### Q53 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** How did the man find this place? (男士如何找到这里的？)
- (A) He read about it in a newspaper ad. (他在报纸的广告上看到的。)
- (B) He heard about it through a person he knows. (他从一个认识的人那儿听说的。)
- (C) It was referred to him by a real estate agent. (一个房地产经纪人告诉他的。)
- (D) He saw an ad posted on the window. (他看到了窗户上贴的广告。)

#### Q54 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** According to the woman, what is special about this place? (根据女士所说，这套房子有什么特别之处？)
- (A) It is conveniently located. (它的位置便利。)
- (B) It has many rooms. (它有很多房间。)
- (C) It is very affordable. (它价格便宜。)
- (D) It opens with a special key. (它的钥匙很特别。)

#### Q55 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What will the woman do first? (女士要先做什么？)
- (A) Remove the for-rent sign. (撤掉出租标志。)
- (B) Walk up to the fifth floor. (走上五楼。)
- (C) Bring out a lease agreement. (拿出一份租赁合同。)
- (D) Retrieve the key. (取钥匙。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I saw a for-rent sign on your lobby window.** (我看到你在门厅窗户上贴的出租标志了。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：I am here to see if there is an apartment available for rent. I'd like to rent a two-bedroom apartment.* (我来看看有没有可租的公寓。我想租一套两居室的公寓。)
- **You are in luck. = It's your lucky day.** (你很幸运。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：I think I can help you out.* (我想我可以帮你解决问题。)

### Questions 56 - 58

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Hey, congratulations. I just heard from Mr. Shaw that the directors have come to a decision regarding the proposal you gave at this morning's meeting. (56)
**W:** Yes, I just heard the news myself, and you wouldn't believe how relieved I am. I mean, considering the number of days and nights the guys on our team worked to prepare for this morning's presentation, I had to get the approval. I was so afraid that I would not be able to convince the directors. But, I guess I did all right.
**M:** Are you kidding? It was perfect. I thought it was one of the best speeches you have ever given. (57) In fact, I wasn't too sure about the possibility of the project myself until I heard your speech. You really did a good job.
**W:** Thanks. I owe it all to my staff. (58) This calls for a celebration.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**嘿，祝贺你。我刚听肖先生说董事们对你今天上午在会议上提出的建议做出决定了。
> **W：**是的，我自己也是刚听说这个消息。你肯定不会相信我有多欣慰。我的意思是，考虑到我们的团队为了准备今天上午的报告而努力工作的日日夜夜，建议就必须获得通过。我特别担心说服不了董事们。不过，我想我表现得不错。
> **M：**你开玩笑吧？表现得很完美。我认为这是你做过的最好的发言了。实际上，我自己最初不太肯定这个项目能否做下去，直到我听了你的发言才相信。你做得真的很不错。
> **W：**谢谢你。这一切都要归功于我的同事。要庆祝一下才行。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **come to**：达成，得出
- **regarding**：关于
- **relieve**：使宽慰，使放心
- **approval**：赞成，通过
- **convince**：说服
- **give a speech**：发言
- **owe ~ to**：把归功于
- **compliment**：称赞，恭维
- **promote**：升职
- **accept**：接纳，接受
- **positive**：积极的，肯定的
- **keynote**：基调，主题

#### Q56 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Why is the woman being complimented? (女士为什么被称赞？)
- (A) She was promoted to the director's position. (她被提升为主管。)
- (B) She convinced Mr. Shaw to sign a contract. (她说服肖先生签了一个合同。)
- (C) Her proposal was accepted by the directors. (她的建议被董事们采纳了。)
- (D) Her co-workers have positive feelings for her. (她的同事对她有积极的评价。)

#### Q57 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the man say? (男士说了什么？)
- (A) She gave a great talk. (她的发言很棒。)
- (B) She should work a bit harder. (她应该更努力地工作。)
- (C) She will have to give a speech. (她将不得不做一个演讲。)
- (D) She won't get the contract. (她将得不到这个合同。)

#### Q58 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Who does the woman say is responsible for the outcome? (女士说这个成果归功于谁？)
- (A) The keynote speaker. (主题发言者。)
- (B) Her team members. (她的团队成员。)
- (C) The directors. (董事们。)
- (D) The man. (男士。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I wasn't too sure about ~ = I was not totally convinced about ~ = I was not totally fixed on ~** (我对…不太确定)
  - *例句：I wasn't too sure about going to New York this weekend.* (我不确定这周末去不去纽约。)

### Questions 59 - 61

![Page 68](images/listen_page_68.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Cindy, did you happen to attend the staff meeting today? I was at the factory in Dunham and got back to the office just now. (59)
**W1:** Sorry, Albert, but I missed it as well.
**M:** That's too bad. I was hoping to find out if next year's budget was discussed. Do you know, Joanie?
**W2:** It wasn't. Mr. Richards said discussions regarding it are still ongoing, but it should be covered at this Friday's meeting.
**M:** Oh, no. I'm scheduled to be in Laredo all day. I'll be giving a speech at a marketing conference there. (60)
**W1:** Don't worry about it. I'll take notes and fill you in on anything important you miss. (61)
**M:** Thanks, Cindy.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**辛迪，今天你碰巧参加了这次员工会议吗？我当时在邓纳姆的工厂，刚刚回到办公室。
> **W1：**对不起，艾伯特，我也错过了这次会议。
> **M：**那太糟糕了。我想知道会议是否讨论了明年的预算。乔安妮，你知道吗？
> **W2：**并没有讨论。理查兹说，关于此事的讨论仍在进行中，但是应该会在本周五的会议中讨论。
> **M：**哦，不！那天我将一整天都在拉雷多。我将在那里的营销会议上发表演讲。
> **W1：**不用担心。我会记下你所错过的任何重要的事并告诉你。
> **M：**谢谢你，辛迪。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **attend**：参加，出席
- **miss**：错过（想去的地方或想做的事情）
- **regard**：关于
- **ongoing**：继续进行的
- **cover**：包含，涉及
- **marketing**：营销；促销
- **conference**：（大型、正式的）会议
- **fill sb. in**：向提供最新消息

#### Q59 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What did the man do today? (这位男士今天做了什么？)
- (A) He attended a meeting. (他参加了一个会议。)
- (B) He delivered a speech. (他发表了一次演说。)
- (C) He visited a factory out of town. (他参观了镇外的一个工厂。)
- (D) He worked on the budget. (他做了预算。)

#### Q60 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the man imply when he says, “I'm scheduled to be in Laredo all day”? (当这位男士说 “ 我将一整天都在拉雷多 ” 时，是在暗示什么？)
- (A) He will miss a scheduled meeting. (他将错过这次安排好的会议。)
- (B) He cannot submit the budget on time. (他不能按时提交预算。)
- (C) He hopes an event will be rescheduled. (他希望重新安排一次活动。)
- (D) He wants the women to accompany him to go to the meeting. (他希望这位女士可以陪他一起参加会议。)

#### Q61 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does Cindy offer to do for the man? (辛迪为这位男士主动提供什么帮助？)
- (A) Contact Mr. Richards. (联系理查兹先生。)
- (B) Provide him with information. (为他提供信息。)
- (C) Review the numbers in the budget. (检查预算中的数据。)
- (D) Help him write a speech. (帮他写演讲稿。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **happen to do sth.** (碰巧（凑巧）做某事)
  - *例句：I happened to see James in town.* (我碰巧在镇上看见了詹姆斯。)
- **I'll be giving a speech at a marketing conference there. = I'll be making/delivering a speech at a marketing conference there.** (我将在那里的营销会议上发表演讲。)
  - *例句：Each child had to give a short speech to the rest of the class.* (每个小孩都必须在班里作一个简短的演讲。)
- **take notes** (做笔记扩展表达：)
  - *例句：take note （ of sth. ） I read the first chapter and take notes.* (注意（到某事），留意（到某事）我阅读了第一章并做了笔记。)

### Questions 62 - 64

![Page 69](images/listen_page_69.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Television sales have increased dramatically recently.
**M:** All the credit for that goes to our newest TV, the HD5000. TV sales reached their lowest point during the month it came out, but they've been going up ever since. (62)
**W:** I had no idea. Are we running any special ads?
**M:** Not really. We're advertising on TV, radio, and the Internet, but we aren't spending more money than usual. (63) Mostly, people are purchasing the HD5000 because it's so well made.
**W:** That's excellent news. Could you copy that sales report for me?
**M:** No problem, but I'll need to run upstairs because our copier is out of toner. (64) TV Sales by Month

**中文对照：**
> **W：**最近电视销量有了很大的增长。
> **M：**所有的功劳都要归功于我们最新型号的电视HD5000。电视销量在HD5000发布当月跌到了最低点，但之后就一直在上升。
> **W：**我不太明白。我们有登什么特别的广告吗？
> **M：**并没有。我们在电视、广播和互联网上做广告，但花的钱并没有比平时多。大多数情况下，人们购买HD5000是因为它制作精良。
> **W：**这是个好消息。你能帮我复印一下那份销售报告吗？
> **M：**没问题，不过我得去楼上，因为我们的复印机没有墨粉了。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **TV Sales by Month**：每月电视销量
- **increase**：增加，增大
- **dramatically**：显著地，剧烈地
- **credit**：信誉；声望；赞扬
- **advertise**：做广告，登广告；作宣传
- **purchase**：购买
- **copier**：复印机
- **toner**：调色剂，增色剂；（打印机等用的）墨粉，色粉

#### Q62 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. When was the HD5000 released? (请看图表， HD5000 是几月份推出的？)
- (A) March. (三月。)
- (B) April. (四月。)
- (C) May. (五月。)
- (D) June. (六月。)

#### Q63 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What does the man say about advertising for the HD5000? (关于 HD5000 的广告，对话中的男士说了什么？)
- (A) A media firm was employed to handle it. (聘请了一家媒体公司来负责广告。)
- (B) It is mostly based on television ads. (主要以电视广告为基础。)
- (C) There are ads being run in newspapers. (报纸上正在刊登广告。)
- (D) The money spent on it is the same as normal. (花在广告上的钱和平常一样多。)

#### Q64 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** Why will the man go upstairs? (对话中的男士为什么去楼上？)
- (A) To request data from the Sales Department. (向销售部要数据资料。)
- (B) To schedule a meeting. (安排一次会议。)
- (C) To attend a conference call. (参加一次电话会议。)
- (D) To make some photocopies. (去复印。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **reach the lowest point = be at rock bottom = tumble to its lowest level** (跌到最低点)
  - *例句：As l struggled through the snowdrifts, l had just about reached the lowest point in my life.* (处在人生低谷的我在暴风雪中艰难地行走着。)
- **be out = run out of** (没有了；用完)
  - *例句：Young people were several times more likely to be out of work than older members of the workforce.* (在劳动人口中，年轻人失业的可能性是年长者的好几倍。)

### Questions 65 - 67

![Page 70](images/listen_page_70.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Hello, Mr. Rutherford. I have some good news for you. A house that fits your requirements has just come on the market.
**M:** Really? What is the asking price for it?
**W:** It's got four bedrooms, and the owners are only asking for $165,000. (65) It's quite a good deal. If you'd like to see it, I can show it to you.
**M:** I've got time right now, so if you let me know the address, I can meet you there. (66)
**W:** It's actually one block away from my office, so how about driving here around 4:00? (67) We can walk there together.
**M:** All right, I'll see you then. Thank you.

**中文对照：**
> **W：**您好，卢瑟福先生。我有个好消息要告诉您，一套符合您的要求的房子正在出售。
> **M：**真的吗？它的要价是多少？
> **W：**它是四居室的，房主只要16.5万美元，很划算。如果您想看房，我可以带您去看看。
> **M：**我现在有时间，所以如果你告诉我地址，我们可以在那里见。
> **W：**那里离我的办公室只有一个街区，您4点左右开车过来怎么样？我们可以一起走过去。
> **M：**好的，到时候见。谢谢你！

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **fit**：符合，适合
- **requirement**：要求
- **asking price**：要价；索价
- **deal**：交易
- **block**：街区；大厦

#### Q65 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. What is the address of the house the woman wants to show the man? (请看图表，对话中的女士想带男士去哪里看房子？)
- (A) 48 Clark Street. (克拉克街道 48 号。)
- (B) 232 Brown Road. (布朗路 232 号。)
- (C) 118 Daisy Lane. (黛西巷 118 号。)
- (D) 75 Marcher Street. (马尔谢街道 75 号。)

#### Q66 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the man express interest in? (对话中的男士对什么感兴趣？)
- (A) Meeting the woman at once. (马上和女士见面。)
- (B) Negotiating about a price. (谈价格。)
- (C) Purchasing a larger house. (买更大的房子。)
- (D) Renting a house for two years. (租两年的房子。)

#### Q67 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the woman request the man to do? (对话中的女士要求男士做什么？)
- (A) Consider an alternative house. (考虑换一个房子。)
- (B) Pay a visit to her office. (去她的办公室。)
- (C) Look at an online listing. (查看在线列表。)
- (D) Make a bid on a house. (出价买房子。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **fit one's requirements = fit one's requests = meet one's demands** (符合某人的需要/请求)
  - *例句：He earns enough to fit his requirements.* (他赚得的钱足够满足他的要求。)
- **come on the market = be on sale** (出售)
  - *例句：This house will probably come on the market next month. Sentry Real Estate Agency Check out our newest available homes.* (这幢房子可能下个月要出售。)

### Questions 68 - 70

![Page 71](images/listen_page_71.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Jennifer, I've been planning to buy a new computer, but there are so many models available. Do you have any advice for me? (68)
**W:** Why don't you check out this Web site called www.computerpurchases.com? All you have to do is explain how you'll use your computer, and it will make suggestions for you. (69)
**M:** That sounds like something I should do at once. How are the prices there?
**W:** They're quite reasonable. Even better, I've got a coupon you can use. But you should wait to make your purchase tomorrow because then you can get 30% off. (70)
**M:** Wow, what a deal. Thanks for the assistance, Jennifer.
**W:** You're welcome.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**珍妮弗，我一直想买一台新电脑，但是现在市面上有很多型号的电脑。你有什么建议吗？
> **W：**你为什么不查一下

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **www.computepurchases.com**：这个网站呢？你只需要说一下你将如何使用你的电脑，它会为你提供建议。
- **M**：：听起来我应该马上去查一下。那里的价格怎么样？
- **W**：：非常合理。更好的是，我有一张优惠券，你可以用。但是你应该等到明天再买，因为明天你就可以享受七折优惠了。
- **M**：：哇，真划算。谢谢你的帮助，珍妮弗。
- **W**：：不用客气。
- **available**：可获得的；可购得的
- **check out**：调查；检查
- **reasonable**：合理的
- **coupon**：优惠券，折价券
- **assistance**：帮助

#### Q68 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What is the man concerned about? (对话中的男士在忧虑什么？)
- (A) What computer programs he needs. (他需要什么电脑程序。)
- (B) Which computer he should buy. (他应该买哪种电脑。)
- (C) When his computer will arrive. (他的电脑什么时候到。)
- (D) How much he should spend on a computer. (他应该花多少钱买一台电脑。)

#### Q69 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the woman say about www.computerpurchases.com? (关于 www.computerpurchases.com 网站，对话中的女士说了什么？)
- (A) It provides free overnight delivery. (它提供免费的隔夜送达服务。)
- (B) It opened around six months ago. (它大约 6 个月前营业。)
- (C) It makes recommendations for buyers. (它为买家提供建议。)
- (D) It guarantees all the items it sells. (它保修所售的所有商品。)

#### Q70 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. What day does the conversation take place on? (请看图表，对话发生在哪一天？)
- (A) Tuesday. (星期二。)
- (B) Wednesday. (星期三。)
- (C) Thursday. (星期四。)
- (D) Friday. (星期五。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **make a purchase = do the shopping** (购物，购买)
  - *例句：Each can make a purchase with the touch of a button.* (只需触摸一个按钮即可进行购物。)
- **what a deal = a real bargain** (好便宜，多合算)
  - *例句：Two meals for the price of one: What a deal!* (花一顿饭的钱吃两顿饭：多合算！)

## Part 4: 简短独白 (Q71 - Q100)

### Questions 71 - 73

**听力独白/对话原文：**
First I want to inform you of the good news that we have doubled our sales over the last 6 months. (72) Yes, we have more than fulfilled our growth target, and it is with great pleasure that I congratulate you for your effort and the care you have taken in making this happen. (71) In order to recognize this achievement and your performance, we have decided to invite all employees and their families to a special thank-you buffet lunch at the Criterion Hotel. Please join us this Saturday for some excellent food and wine. (73) I hope to see you all there!

**中文对照：**
> 首先我想告诉大家一个好消息，在过去的六个月中我们的销量翻了一番。是的，我们超额完成了增长目标，我很高兴地对大家表示祝贺，因为你们的努力和用心，才能有这样的结果。为了表彰你们的成绩和表现，我们决定邀请所有员工及其家属参加一个特别感谢午宴，地点在Criterion饭店。请在本周六与我们一起享用美食和美酒。希望大家都能光临！

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **double**：使加倍
- **sales**：销售，销量
- **fulfill**：完成，实现
- **growth**：增长，成长
- **effort**：努力
- **care**：用心；努力
- **recognize**：表彰；赏识
- **achievement**：成绩，成就
- **performance**：表现
- **publicize**：公开，发布
- **appreciation**：感激；欣赏
- **steadily**：稳定地
- **buy out**：买下
- **luncheon**：午宴

#### Q71 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What is the purpose of the announcement? (本通知的目的是什么？)
- (A) To inform people of a policy change. (告知人们一项政策的变化。)
- (B) To publicize a new product. (发布一个新产品。)
- (C) To introduce the new sales manager. (介绍新任销售经理。)
- (D) To show appreciation for good work. (对出色的工作表示感谢。)

#### Q72 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What has happened in the past six months? (过去的六个月中发生了什么？)
- (A) There was a change in management. (管理部门发生了变动。)
- (B) Sales have steadily increased. (销量稳步增长。)
- (C) The company bought out a hotel. (公司买下了一家酒店。)
- (D) The performance of the workers were evaluated. (员工的表现被考核。)

#### Q73 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What is going to happen this weekend? (本周末会发生什么？)
- (A) A new company sales goal will be set. (将会制定一个新的公司销售目标。)
- (B) The staff members will go on a trip. (工作人员会去旅行。)
- (C) There will be a luncheon party. (会举行一个午宴。)
- (D) A family get together will take place. (会举行一个家庭聚会。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **inform you of ~ = let you know ~ = tell you ~** (通知你们…)
  - *例句：I'd like to inform you of the upcoming party we will be holding for Mr. Smith.* (我想通知大家，我们即将为史密斯先生举行一个聚会。)
- **We have more than fulfilled our growth target. = We have surpassed our growth goal. = We have achieved beyond our growth goal.** (我们超额完成了增长目标。)

### Questions 74 - 76

**听力独白/对话原文：**
It is reported in the business news column today that Susan Bartlett, CEO of Tasty Foods, (74) will leave her position at the end of December. (75) It is well known that the success of Tasty Foods' expansion into Asia was due to Ms. Bartlett's personal dynamism and commitment. A committee, which includes Ms. Bartlett, who will remain with the company as a consultant, is currently searching for the next CEO. (76)

**中文对照：**
> 今天的商业新闻专栏报道说，美味食品公司的首席执行官苏珊·巴特利特将在12月底离职。众所周知，美味食品公司向亚洲的成功进军离不开巴特利特女士个人的推动和投入。巴特利特女士将继续留在公司担任顾问。包括她在内的公司委员会正在寻找下一任首席执行官。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **leave one's position**：离职
- **well known**：知名的，出名的
- **expansion**：扩张，扩大
- **dynamism**：推动力
- **commitment**：奉献，投入
- **consultant**：顾问
- **critic**：评论家

#### Q74 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What is Ms. Bartlett's current position? (巴特利特女士目前的职位是什么？)
- (A) Chief executive officer. (首席执行官。)
- (B) Consultant. (顾问。)
- (C) News reporter. (新闻记者。)
- (D) Food critic. (食品评论家。)

#### Q75 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** When will Susan leave her job? (苏珊会在何时离职？)
- (A) At the end of this week. (本周末。)
- (B) Sometime next month. (下个月的某个时候。)
- (C) Later this year. (今年年末。)
- (D) Early next year. (明年年初。)

#### Q76 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What has the company started doing? (公司已经开始做什么了？)
- (A) Importing food from Asia. (从亚洲进口食品。)
- (B) Seeking a new leader. (寻找新领导。)
- (C) Hiring more consultants. (聘请更多的顾问。)
- (D) Reporting business news. (报道商业新闻。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **leave one's position = quit one's job = resign from one's job** (离职)
  - *例句：Jane will leave her position to go back to school.* (简离职后会回到学校。)
- **remain with the company = stay with the company = don't go to another company** (留在公司)
  - *例句：Ralph will remain with the company for another year.* (拉尔夫会留在公司再工作一年。)
- **search for = look for = seek** (寻找)
  - *例句：We are searching for the right person to take over for Mr. Wang.* (我们在寻找合适的人选接替王先生。)

### Questions 77 - 79

![Page 72](images/listen_page_72.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
I'd like to welcome you all to the annual golf championship, and I hope that you enjoy the week you will be spending with us. (78) I would like to remind you that, due to security arrangements, it is essential to have your press identification cards with you at all times. If you forget your card, you will not be allowed to enter any press area. Press conferences will be held at the end of play every day. All reporters will be able to question the selected competitors in the press room. (77) Please indicate that you have a question by raising your hand. A tournament official will pass you a microphone when it is your turn. And please ensure that your mobile phones are off during question sessions. (79)

**中文对照：**
> 欢迎大家来到年度高尔夫锦标赛，我希望你们能和我们一起度过愉快的一周。我想提醒大家，根据安全措施的要求，您需要把记者证随时带在身上。假如您忘记带记者证，那么将无法进入任何采访区域。新闻发布会将在每天比赛结束后举行，所有的记者都可以在新闻室里选择选手提问。请您在想要提问的时候举手示意。比赛官员会在轮到您的时候向您传递话筒。请您确保手机在提问环节处于关机状态。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **annual**：每年的，年度的
- **championship**：锦标赛
- **security**：安全
- **press**：新闻界，记者
- **identification card**：身份证
- **allow**：允许
- **hold**：举行
- **selected**：选出的
- **indicate**：指出，指示
- **tournament**：比赛，锦标赛
- **turn off**：关闭
- **referee**：裁判
- **take turns**：轮流

#### Q77 (正确答案：A)

- (B) Golfers. (高尔夫球手。)
- (C) Security guards. (保安。)
- (D) Referees. (裁判。)

#### Q78 (正确答案：C)

- (A) One day. (一天。)
- (B) Two days. (两天。)
- (C) Seven days. (七天。)
- (D) Twenty days. (二十天。)

#### Q79 (正确答案：B)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **annual = yearly** (每年一次的，年度的)
  - *例句：The annual meeting will be held this Friday.* (年度会议将在本周五举行。)
- **pass = hand = give** (传递)
  - *例句：Would you please wait until I pass you a microphone?* (您能等我把话筒递给您吗？)
- **mobile phone = cellular phone = portable phone** (手机)
  - *例句：There are various types of mobile phones out on the market today.* (目前市场上有很多种类的手机。)

### Questions 80 - 82

![Page 73](images/listen_page_73.png)

We would like all employees to note that our management has decided to expand the snack bar into a full lunchroom service. (80) There will be several hot main courses, salads, desserts, and hot and cold drinks on offer every day. (81) Prices will be kept to a minimum. We trust that our employees will not only enjoy the food and atmosphere but also the convenience of having healthy and tasty meals available in the building. **核心词汇与短语：**
- **management**：管理人员，管理部门
- **expand**：发展；扩大
- **lunchroom**：午餐厅
- **be on offer**：供应，提供
- **atmosphere**：气氛，氛围
- **convenience**：便利
- **healthy**：健康的
- **tasty**：美味的
- **post**：张贴
- **notice board**：通告栏
- **appreciate**：体会，领会
- **valued**：珍贵的，受到重视的
- **instructor**：教练
- **appetizer**：开胃菜
- **entree**：主菜
- **stand**：摊位

  - *例句：on sale on display There will be many types of sales on offer this weekend.* (出售展示本周末将会有多种降价商品出售。)
- **Prices will be kept to a minimum.** (价格会保持在最低价位。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：Prices will be kept low. Prices will be kept to a minimum to attract more customers into the store.* (价格会保持在低位。价格会保持在最低水平，从而吸引更多顾客来到店里。)

### Questions 83 - 85

**听力独白/对话原文：**
I'm Jack Thompson, presenting another edition of “Tips for Your Trip”. Christmas time is here again, so it's important for all of you making that long drive home to be extra careful on the road. (83) So listen carefully. Firstly, there will be many tired and stressed drivers on the road, so you will need to be extra careful. Secondly, try to share the driving with a friend or relative or two if possible. (84) That way there will always be someone who can take over the steering wheel when you're tired.Thirdly, take a break when you start to notice the effects of drowsiness—drifting, blurry vision, and yawning. (84) And finally, remember that drinking a lot of coffee can only help you fight drowsiness for a short time. Learn to recognize the signs of sleepiness, and stop. (84) Have a good sleep. Don't drive after midnight if you can possibly avoid it. (84) That's all, but please listen again next week for more“Tips for Your Trip”. (85)

**中文对照：**
> 我是杰克·汤普森，为您带来新一期的“旅途小贴士”节目。圣诞节又到了，对每个人都很重要的就是确保在开车回家的漫长旅程中格外小心。所以，请您认真收听。首先，道路上将会有很多疲惫、紧张的司机，所以你需要多加小心。第二，如果可能的话，尽量和一两个亲友共同开车。这样在你疲劳的时候总能有人接过你手中的方向盘。第三，在你开始感觉到睡意的时候，比如摇晃、视线模糊、打哈欠，马上休息一下。最后，记住大量喝咖啡只能帮你在短时间内抵御睡意。要学会识别瞌睡的信号，然后停车。睡个好觉。如果可能的话，就不要后半夜开车。今天的节目就到这儿，请您下周继续收听“旅途小贴士”。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **present**：展示
- **tips**：小贴士，小窍门
- **extra**：额外的
- **share**：分享，分担
- **relative**：亲戚
- **take over**：接替，接管
- **steering wheel**：方向盘
- **take a break**：休息
- **effect**：作用，影响
- **drowsiness**：睡意
- **drift**：晃动
- **blurry**：模糊的
- **vision**：视力
- **yawn**：打哈欠
- **sleepiness**：瞌睡
- **bargain**：便宜货，减价品
- **overcome**：战胜，克服
- **pull over**：（把车）开到路边，靠在路边

#### Q83 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What is the talk mainly about? (这段话主要是关于什么内容？)
- (A) How to get a bargain during Christmas. (圣诞节期间如何买到便宜货。)
- (B) How to overcome stress at a workplace. (如何克服工作压力。)
- (C) How to become closer to family members. (如何与家人变得更加亲密。)
- (D) How to drive safely during the holiday season. (假期里如何安全驾驶。)

#### Q84 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Which of the following is NOT a tip mentioned by the speaker? (下列哪一项不是讲话者提到的旅途小窍门？)
- (A) Don't drive alone. (不要单独驾驶。)
- (B) Pull over when tired. (劳累时就要停车。)
- (C) Drink a lot of coffee. (多喝咖啡。)
- (D) Do not drive too late. (开车不要开到太晚。)

#### Q85 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** How often is the show aired? (这个节目多久播一次？)
- (A) Every day. (每天。)
- (B) Once a week. (一周一次。)
- (C) Twice a week. (一周两次。)
- (D) Only on weekdays. (只在周末播出。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **take over = relieve = substitute for** (接替，接管)
  - *例句：Paul will take over my shift at five o'clock.* (保罗下午5点接我的班。)
- **take a break = rest a little** (休息一会儿)
  - *例句：Why don't you take a break for five minutes?* (为什么不休息5分钟？)

### Questions 86 - 88

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Welcome all of you. And thank you for making the effort to come so promptly. As all of you know, we have to move out of this building by the end of the month （ 86, 87 ） because the owner is asking too much money for rent. And you also know how difficult it is to rent a place in this city at an affordable price. The head chef and I have spent a lot of time trying to find premises that are both in the right location and have the character we need to maintain the tradition of our restaurant. (88) Well, you'll be happy to hear that we've found the ideal location. (86) After weeks of fruitless searching, we heard of a first floor site which was originally a French restaurant near the local theater. We contacted the agents immediately and inspected the site. It's great, and we've signed a 3- year contract. (86) So let's get busy; we have a lot of work to do! Thanks again for your commitment.

**中文对照：**
> 欢迎大家。感谢大家设法如此迅速地赶来。正如大家所知，我们必须在月底之前搬出这栋大楼，因为房东索要的房租太贵了。大家也知道在这个城市很难租到价格合适的房子。我和主厨花了很多时间寻找位置合适又具备我们需要的能够保留我们饭店传统特色的店面。哦，你们听到这个消息会很高兴，我们找到了理想的地方。几周毫无收获的寻找之后，我们听说本地剧院附近的一处店面，在一楼，那里原来是一家法国餐馆。我们马上联系房产经纪人并去看了店面。那里很棒，我们签下了三年的合同。所以我们得忙起来了，有很多工作要做！再次感谢大家的支持。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **effort**：努力
- **promptly**：敏捷地，迅速地
- **affordable price**：负担得起的价格
- **premises**：房产，房屋
- **character**：特征，个性
- **maintain**：保持，维持
- **tradition**：传统
- **fruitless**：没有结果的
- **agent**：经纪人，代理人
- **commitment**：支持
- **alert**：使注意
- **gather**：收集，聚集
- **renegotiate**：重新谈判，再协商

#### Q86 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What is the purpose of the talk? (这个讲话的目的是什么？)
- (A) To alert customers about a new dish. (让消费者注意新添的菜品。)
- (B) To notify the staff about the new location of the restaurant. (通知员工饭店的新址。)
- (C) To gather suggestions about a new menu for the place. (收集关于本店新菜单的建议。)
- (D) To announce a new chef for the restaurant. (宣布饭店来了一位新厨师。)

#### Q87 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What is going to happen at the end of the month? (月底会发生什么？)
- (A) They will move out to a new place. (他们会搬到一个新地方。)
- (B) The chef will renegotiate his contract. (厨师会重新协商合同。)
- (C) A French restaurant will open next door. (一家法国餐馆会在隔壁开业。)
- (D) The theater will hold its first Broadway play. (剧院会首次上演百老汇戏剧。)

#### Q88 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the speaker imply when he says, “maintain the tradition of our restaurant”? (讲话者说 “ 保持我们饭店的传统 ” ，他在暗示什么？)
- (A) The restaurant has recently opened. (该饭店最近才开张。)
- (B) The restaurant has a long history. (该饭店有很悠久的历史。)
- (C) The restaurant has the best food in town. (该饭店的饭菜是城里最好吃的。)
- (D) The restaurant is very busy. (该饭店非常繁忙。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **come so promptly = come right away = come at once** (如此迅速地到来)
  - *例句：I appreciate you making the effort to come so promptly.* (我感谢你们能设法如此迅速地赶到。)
- **after weeks of fruitless searching = after weeks of endless searching = after searching for weeks without having any luck** (经过了几周毫无结果的寻找)
  - *例句：After weeks of fruitless searching, we have finally found the right person for the job.* (经过了几周毫无结果的寻找，我们终于找到了适合这项工作的人。)

### Questions 89 - 91

![Page 74](images/listen_page_74.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Hello, everybody. I'm Wendy Raynford, and I'd like to welcome you to our company's orientation program. (89) Firstly, let me tell you about the schedule for this week's training. One of our personnel officers, Tim O'Brien, (90) will hand out envelopes containing some forms for you as well as company information. We'll look over the forms together, and then you can fill them out. This will be followed by a tea break and a chance to talk informally with members of the personnel staff. At 11:00 a.m. we will break into 3 groups for a tour of the production facilities, (91) with our volunteer guides who are keen to meet you. This will be followed by lunch at 12:30. You will then have free time to visit the grounds before the start of the afternoon program at 1:30 p.m. This will begin with a company promotional and training video, lasting 1 hour.

**中文对照：**
> 大家好，我是温迪·雷恩福德，欢迎大家参加我们公司的“新员工培训计划”。首先，让我来告诉大家本周培训的日程安排。我们的人事专员之一，蒂姆·奥布赖恩，会发给大家装有表格和公司信息的信封。我们将一起浏览这些表格，然后你们要把表格填好。之后是茶点和休息时间，在此期间大家将有机会和人事部的同事进行非正式的交谈。到了11点，我们会分成三组，由志愿导游陪同大家参观生产设施。我们的导游非常想见到大家。12点半是午餐时间。午餐后到下午1点半培训之前是自由活动时间，大家可以参观厂区。培训开始时会播放一段时长为1小时的公司宣传及培训录像。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **orientation**：（任职等前的）培训
- **personnel**：人事部门；员工
- **hand out**：下发，分发
- **look over**：查看，看一遍
- **fill out**：填写
- **tea break**：享用茶点的休息时间
- **volunteer**：志愿者
- **ground**：空地，庭院
- **promotional**：推广的，促销的
- **last**：持续
- **bunch**：束，串，群

#### Q89 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Who is the speaker most likely addressing? (说话者最有可能在对谁讲话？)
- (A) A group of new employees. (一群新员工。)
- (B) A bunch of managers. (一批经理。)
- (C) Some volunteer guides. (一些志愿导游。)
- (D) Cafeteria workers. (咖啡厅员工。)

#### Q90 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Who most likely is Mr. O'Brien? (奥布赖恩先生最有可能是谁？)
- (A) The personnel manager. (人事经理。)
- (B) The keynote speaker. (主题发言人。)
- (C) The company policy maker. (公司的政策制定者。)
- (D) The production manager. (生产经理。)

#### Q91 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** When will the listeners tour the factory floor? (听众会在什么时间参观车间？)
- (A) At 11:00. (11 点。)
- (B) At 12:30. (12 点半。)
- (C) At 1:30. (1 点半。)
- (D) At 3:00. (3 点。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **hand out = distribute = give out** (下发，分发)
  - *例句：We are planning to hand out some business cards at the exhibition.* (我们计划在展会上分发一些名片。)
- **look over = review = go over** (查看，看一遍)
  - *例句：Let's look over the contract once more.* (咱们再查看一遍合同。)
- **be keen to meet = be eager to meet = be anxious to meet** (急切地想见到)
  - *例句：Mr. Miller is keen to meet you.* (米勒先生急切地想见到你。)

### Questions 92 - 94

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Good morning. As I'm sure you're aware, the gallery's management committee has requested an engineering survey of the site and its facilities. The aim of this survey is twofold: first, to find remedies for certain serious problems which have resulted in damage to the building (92) and parts of the collection; secondly, to consider how the facilities can be improved. I have to report to you that the structure of the building requires immediate attention. Neglect has resulted in serious damage. (93) I know that the necessary renovations will be expensive and funding is a problem. But my consultants are certain that, if we act now, far more serious and expensive repairs can be avoided. (94)

**中文对照：**
> 上午好。我相信大家一定知道，美术馆的管理委员会要求针对馆址及其设施进行一次工程勘察。勘察的目的有两方面：一、找到损坏建筑物和部分藏品的严重问题的补救措施；二、考虑如何改善设施。我必须告诉大家，我们需要立即关注这座建筑物的结构。疏忽已经造成了严重的损坏。我知道必要的修缮会很贵，资金是个问题。但是我的顾问们确信，如果我们现在就行动，能免去更多重大而昂贵的维修。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **be aware**：知道，意识到
- **engineering**：工程的
- **survey**：调查，勘察
- **facility**：设施
- **twofold**：两方面的
- **remedy**：补救（法）；纠正（法）
- **damage**：破坏，损坏
- **collection**：收集品，收藏
- **structure**：结构；建筑物
- **immediate attention**：立即关注
- **neglect**：疏忽，玩忽
- **funding**：资金
- **beyond**：超过
- **due**：到期的
- **suitable**：合适的
- **auction**：拍卖会
- **recruit**：招募

#### Q92 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** According to the speaker, what is the goal of the survey? (根据讲话人所说，本次勘察的目的是什么？)
- (A) To see if they can collect more money. (看他们能否募集到更多钱。)
- (B) To find collections of old art. (找到古代艺术藏品。)
- (C) To look into the cause of the damages. (调查损坏的原因。)
- (D) To find ways to fix the damages. (寻找维修的方法。)

#### Q93 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the result of the survey report? (勘察结果是什么？)
- (A) The place is beyond repairs. (那个地方无法维修。)
- (B) The building is in need of repairs. (这座建筑需要维修。)
- (C) The structure is in good condition. (（建筑的）结构状况较好。)
- (D) The gallery is due for paint job. (美术馆该粉刷了。)

#### Q94 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What does the consultant advise? (顾问的建议是什么？)
- (A) To move to another more suitable place. (搬到另一个更合适的地方。)
- (B) To buy more art at the auction. (在拍卖会上购买更多的艺术品。)
- (C) To recruit more volunteers to help out. (招募更多志愿者帮忙。)
- (D) To respond right away to reduce future costs. (立即应对以减少未来的损失。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **twofold = double** (两方面的)
  - *例句：The purpose of today's questionnaire is twofold.* (今天的问卷有两方面的目的。)
- **remedies = solutions = cures** (补救办法)
  - *例句：We need to find remedies for the problems quickly.* (我们需要马上找到这些问题的补救办法。)
- **if we act now = if we do something right now = if we move now** (如果我们现在就行动)
  - *例句：If we act now, we may still be able to fix the problem.* (如果我们现在就行动，或许仍然能够解决问题。)

### Questions 95 - 97

![Page 75](images/listen_page_75.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Hello. This is Ryan Rogers from the Murdoch Corporation. I'm calling to let you know that you have been selected for an interview for the position you applied for. Your interview has been scheduled for next Tuesday morning at 10:30. (95) If this doesn't work for you, please call me back at 874-8432 no later than this Thursday so that we can reschedule it. (96) In addition, you must bring three letters of recommendation from current or previous employers with you. (97) You failed to include those in the application packet you submitted, and we won't be able to hire you without them. Tuesday's Interviews

**中文对照：**
> 您好，我是默多克公司的赖安·罗杰斯。我打电话是想通知您，您已入选了所申请职位的面试。您的面试时间安排在下周二上午10点半。如果这个时间对您来说不方便的话，请于本周四前致电874-8432以便我们能重新安排面试时间。另外，请您务必携带三封当前或者以前雇主的推荐信。您提交的申请信息包中如果没有附上这些推荐信，您将不能被我公司录取。周二的面试

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **corporation**：公司；社团
- **select**：挑选，选拔
- **position**：职位；位置
- **schedule**：安排；时间表
- **reschedule**：重新排定日程
- **recommendation**：推荐（信）；建议
- **current**：现在的，当前的
- **previous**：以前的
- **submit**：提交，递交

#### Q95 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Who is the speaker calling? (请看图表，讲话者在给谁打电话？)
- (A) Rosanna Barnes. (罗莎娜 · 巴尔内斯。)
- (B) Lloyd Kirchner. (罗伊德 · 柯克纳。)
- (C) Anita Wall. (安妮塔 · 沃尔。)
- (D) Penelope Sanderson. (佩内洛普 · 桑德森。)

#### Q96 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Why would the listener call the speaker? (接电话的人为什么会致电讲话者？)
- (A) To set another time to meet. (另外约定面试时间。)
- (B) To accept an offer of employment. (接受录用通知。)
- (C) To confirm an arrival time. (确定到达时间。)
- (D) To ask for directions. (询问（公司）地址。)

#### Q97 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What does the speaker tell the listener to bring? (讲话者要求对方携带什么？)
- (A) An application sheet. (一张申请表。)
- (B) A résumé. (一份简历。)
- (C) A portfolio. (一份作品集。)
- (D) Some documents. (一些文件。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **let ~ know = tell ~** (告知/告诉…)
  - *例句：Please let me know when you will come back.* (请告知我你何时回来。)
- **schedule for = plan for** (为…制定/安排（行程）)
  - *例句：Let's schedule for each goal of this year.* (我们来为今年的每个目标制定计划吧。)

### Questions 98 - 100

![Page 76](images/listen_page_76.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
That's all we have time for today, listeners. Thanks for stopping by Radio 103.4 FM, the top radio station in Arlington County. I hope you enjoyed my interview with Brandon Meyers today. (98) If you have any questions or comments about our city's leading businessman, send them to me, and I'll do my best to have them answered by tomorrow's show. (99) You can get my e- mail address on the radio station's homepage. All right, it's time for me to go off the air. Before you listen to our next program, it's time for a few words from our sponsors. (100) I'll be back at the same time tomorrow with a report on our area's schools. (98) Radio 103.4 FM Schedule

**中文对照：**
> 听众们，以上就是今天全部的放送时间。感谢您锁定收听阿灵顿县一流的无线电台——调频103.4。希望大家喜欢今天我对布兰登·迈耶斯所做的访谈。如果您对本市杰出的企业家有任何问题或者评价，请发送给我，我将尽可能在明天的节目当中回答。您可以在无线电台的主页找到我的电子邮件地址。好了，我今天的播送即将结束。在您收听下面的节目之前，将播放我台赞助商的几句话。我将于明天同一时间与您再会，届时将带来关于本地区学校的报道。调频103.4 节目时间表

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **comment**：评论；意见
- **leading**：主要的；领导的
- **businessman**：企业家，商人
- **e- mail address**：电子邮件地址
- **homepage**：主页
- **program**：节目；项目；程序
- **sponsor**：赞助商；发起者

#### Q98 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Who most likely is the speaker? (请看图表，讲话者很可能是谁？)
- (A) Jeff Martin. (杰夫 · 马丁。)
- (B) Randal Smith. (兰德尔 · 史密斯。)
- (C) Lionel Kendrick. (莱昂内尔 · 肯德里克。)
- (D) Richard Samuels. (理查德 · 塞缪尔斯。)

#### Q99 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the speaker tell listeners to do? (讲话者请听众做什么？)
- (A) Listen to the next show. (收听下一期节目。)
- (B) Send e-mail. (发送电子邮件。)
- (C) Submit questions. (提交问题。)
- (D) Suggest people to interview. (推荐接受采访的人。)

#### Q100 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What will listeners most likely hear next? (听众们接下来最可能听到什么节目？)
- (A) Some music. (一些音乐。)
- (B) A commercial. (一则广告。)
- (C) A weather report. (天气预报。)
- (D) A traffic report. (一份交通报道。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **enjoy = have a good time** (享受；过得愉快)
  - *例句：I enjoyed staying in Canada last summer vacation.* (我享受去年暑假在加拿大的日子。)
- **do my best to ~ = try my best to ~** (尽我最大的努力)
  - *例句：I will do my best to help you.* (我会尽最大的努力帮助你。)
