## Part 1: 照片描述 (Q1 - Q6)

### Q1 (正确答案：C)

![Page 78](images/listen_page_78.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) He's opening the door. (他正在开门。)
- (B) He's sitting upright in a chair. (他正笔直地坐在椅子上。)
- (C) He's working with a tool. (他正在使用一个工具。)
- (D) He's taking off his running shoes. (他正在脱下他的跑鞋。)

**其他可能表达：**
- He's using a hammer. (他正在使用锤子。)
- He's holding a tool. (他正拿着一个工具。)
- He's concentrating on his work. (他正专心于他的工作。)


### Q2 (正确答案：A)

![Page 78](images/listen_page_78.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) He has taken a seat at a workstation. (他已经坐在工作区里了。)
- (B) He is tidying up his work area. (他正在清理他的工作区域。)
- (C) He's turning on the computer. (他正在开电脑。)
- (D) He's about to sit in the chair. (他正要坐到椅子上。)

**其他可能表达：**
- The man is working at the computer. (男士正在使用电脑。)
- He's gathering information from the monitor. (他正在从显示器上收集信息。)
- The man is looking at the computer screen. (男士正看着电脑屏幕。)


### Q3 (正确答案：D)

![Page 78](images/listen_page_78.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) They're entering the gallery. (他们正走进美术馆。)
- (B) They're hanging up some pictures. (他们正在挂几张画。)
- (C) They're sketching some art. (他们正在绘制一些艺术作品。)
- (D) They're closely examining a picture. (他们正在仔细地审视一幅画。)

**其他可能表达：**
- They're admiring the painting
- on the wall. (他们正在欣赏墙上的画。)
- Some paintings are hanging in a gallery. (几幅画正挂在美术馆里。)
- A painting has been hung next to the women. (一幅画已经被挂在了女士的旁边。)


### Q4 (正确答案：C)

![Page 79](images/listen_page_79.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) The people are loading goods onto a truck. (人们正在往卡车上装货物。)
- (B) A man is closing up the storage room. (一位男士正在关闭储物间。)
- (C) One of the people is handling heavy machinery. (他们中的一个人正在操作沉重的机器。)
- (D) One man is directing the other man. (一位男士正在指挥另一个人。)

**其他可能表达：**
- A man is operating heavy machinery. (一位男士正在操作沉重的机器。)
- Heavy machinery is being used. (沉重的机器正在被使用。)
- There is heavy machinery in use at the moment. (现在有一台沉重的机器正)
- 在被使用中。


### Q5 (正确答案：B)

![Page 79](images/listen_page_79.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) A worker is organizing the shelves. (一个工人正在整理书架。)
- (B) The shelves are lined up against one side of the wall. (书架靠着一面墙排成一排。)
- (C) There are books neatly arranged on top of the desk. (书在书桌上整齐地排放着。)
- (D) The map is being taken down at the moment. (地图现在正被取下来。)

**其他可能表达：**
- The shelves are stocked with reading materials. (书架上放满了读物。)
- There are bookshelves against one side of the wall. (一面墙上靠着几个书架。)
- Some books have been filled in the shelves. (一些书已经被放到书架上了。)


### Q6 (正确答案：D)

![Page 79](images/listen_page_79.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) A man is escorting the woman into the car. (男士正在护送女士上汽车。)
- (B) The woman is backing the car out of the driveway. (女士正把车倒出车道。)
- (C) Several passengers are seated in the backseat of the car. (几名乘客坐在汽车的后座上。)
- (D) The door of the vehicle is open. (车门是开着的。)

**其他可能表达：**
- The woman is about to get in the car. (女士正要上车。)
- The passenger door is wide open. (乘客门大开着。)
- They are dressed in formal wear. (他们穿着正装。)
- 注：在Part 1中，每道试题都添加了3种可能的正确表达方式，考生可
- 以了解对于同样的照片可能出现的不同表达。


## Part 2: 应答测试 (Q7 - Q31)

### Q7 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Did you have any difficulties in finding this place? (你找这个地方有没有遇到困难？)
- **A:** No, I've been here several times in the past. (没有，我过去来过这里几次。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Did you have a hard time finding this place? (你觉得这个地方难找吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Why don't you take a look at the map? (你为什么不看一看地图呢？)
  - (B) No, I've been here once before. (不难，我以前来过这里一次。)
  - (C) This job is easier than you think. (这个工作比你想的简单一些。)


### Q8 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** What's the weather going to be like this weekend? (这周末的天气怎么样？)
- **A:** I think rain is in the forecast. (我记得天气预报说有雨。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** What's in the forecast for the weekend? (天气预报说周末的天气怎么样？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I heard it's going to rain. (我听说要下雨。)
  - (B) Probably on Saturday. (很可能在周六。)
  - (C) Yes, at the local park. (是的，在本地公园。)


### Q9 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How did you enjoy the play we just saw? (你觉得我们刚才看的戏剧怎么样？)
- **A:** I really liked it a lot. (我真的很喜欢。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Did you like the play you just saw? (你喜欢刚才看的戏剧吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) No, I saw her today. (不，我今天见到她了。)
  - (B) Yes, it was very nice. (喜欢，非常好。)
  - (C) Yes, all work and no play. (是的，只工作，不娱乐。)


### Q10 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Do you want to let John know that you dropped by today? (你想让约翰知道你今天来过吗？)
- **A:** I will tell him myself later. (晚些时候我自己告诉他吧。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Can I tell John that you came by today? (我能告诉约翰你今天来过吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, I will drop by at six. (是的，我会在 6 点顺道过来。)
  - (B) That won't be necessary. (那没有必要。)
  - (C) No, I forgot to call him. (不，我忘记给他打电话了。)


### Q11 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Why did you come by today? (你今天为什么来？)
- **A:** I am here to meet with Mr. Lee. (我来这儿见李先生。注：在Part 2中，为帮助考生提高听懂题目的能力，添加了和试题相同或相似的表达方法。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** What is the main reason for your visit? (你来访的主要原因是什么？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I'm here on business. (我来这里是因为公事。)
  - (B) This is my third time here. (这是我第三次来这里。)
  - (C) To the third floor office. (到三层的办公室去。)


### Q12 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How much is the total? (总共多少钱？)
- **A:** That will be twenty dollars. (总共是20美元。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** How much does all this come to? (这些一共多少钱？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Twenty dollars. (20 美元。)
  - (B) No, I won't. (不，我不会。)
  - (C) With a credit card. (用信用卡。)


### Q13 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** What are the chances of Mr. Chen showing up tonight? (陈先生今晚出现的可能性有多大？)
- **A:** Next to none. (几乎没有可能。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Is Mr. Chen likely going to show up this evening? (陈先生今晚会出现吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Most likely not. (很可能不会。)
  - (B) Yes, it went up. (是的，增加了。)
  - (C) He will show it to me. (他会把它给我看。)


### Q14 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** When will the test result be announced? (考试成绩什么时候公布？)
- **A:** This Friday at the latest. (最晚本周五。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** When will I get the result of my test? (我什么时候能拿到考试成绩？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I acted it. (我假装的。)
  - (B) By this Friday. (本周五之前。)
  - (C) Yes, I know. (是的，我知道。)


### Q15 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Would you like a ride to the bus station? (你想搭车去公交车站吗？)
- **A:** Thanks. I really appreciate it. (谢谢。真的非常感谢。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Do you want a lift to the bus terminal? (你想要搭车去公交车终点站吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) It's a bit too heavy for me. (它对我来说有点儿太重了。)
  - (B) That would be very nice of you. (你太好了。)
  - (C) To see my in-laws in New York. (去见我纽约的姻亲。)


### Q16 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Do you accept personal checks here, or do I have to pay in cash? (你这里接受个人支票吗，还是我必须交现金？)
- **A:** Either way is fine. (怎么都行。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Can I give you a check, or would you prefer cash? (我可以给你支票吗，还是你更想要现金？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) It doesn't matter to me. (对我来说没关系。)
  - (B) Yes, I checked it twice. (是的，我检查过两遍。)
  - (C) No, I don't have any money on me. (不，我身上没钱。)


### Q17 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** I am curious to know whom the next project is going to be assigned to. (我很好奇下一个项目会分配给谁。)
- **A:** I heard Jake is going to get it. (我听说杰克会承担那个项目。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** I wonder who is going to take on the next project, don't you? (我想知道谁会承担下一个项目，你不想知道吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Sure, I can take it with me today. (当然，我今天能带着它。)
  - (B) Sorry, but I am not going that way. (抱歉，我不走那边。)
  - (C) It will most likely be Jake. (很有可能是杰克。)


### Q18 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Are there any tickets left for this evening's show? (今晚的演出还有剩余的票吗？)
- **A:** Sorry, but all the tickets are sold out. (抱歉，所有的票都卖光了。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Are there any seats left for tonight's performance? (今晚的演出还有剩余的座位吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) It is going to be very expensive. (票会非常贵。)
  - (B) Sorry, but it's a full house today. (抱歉，今天满座了。)
  - (C) Sure, here is my ticket. (当然，这是我的票。)


### Q19 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How far is the hotel you are staying at from here? (你住的宾馆离这里有多远？)
- **A:** It's just around the corner. (就在前面拐角处。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** How far is your hotel from here? (你的宾馆离这里多远？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I'm staying in Room 1204. (我住在 1204 房间。)
  - (B) At the Prince Hotel. (在王子酒店。)
  - (C) About ten minutes on foot. (步行大约 10 分钟。)


### Q20 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Did you not like the talk? (你不喜欢这个讲话吗？)
- **A:** No, it was a little too slow. (不喜欢，有点儿太慢了。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Didn't you enjoy the speech? (你难道不喜欢这个演讲吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) He speaks two languages. (他讲两种语言。)
  - (B) Yes, it's much better. (是的，好多了。)
  - (C) No, it was a bit boring. (不喜欢，有点儿枯燥。)


### Q21 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Were there enough forms to go around for everybody at the workshop? (讨论会上有足够的表格分发给每个人吗？)
- **A:** Yes, I think everyone had a copy. (是的，我想每个人都有一份。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Were there plenty of forms for everyone at the workshop? (有很多表格发给讨论会上的每个人吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) There were just enough. (正好有足够的表格。)
  - (B) He works until six today. (他今天一直工作到 6 点。)
  - (C) I already went shopping. (我已经去购物了。)


### Q22 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Are you up for shopping today, or do you want to do it another time? (你今天打算去买东西吗，还是想改天再去？)
- **A:** I am a bit worn out today. (我今天有点儿累了。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Do you feel like shopping today, or would you prefer going another time? (你想今天购物还是改天？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I bought a T-shirt. (我买了一件 T 恤。)
  - (B) I feel quite good. (我感觉很好。)
  - (C) I'm a bit tired today. (我今天有点儿累。)


### Q23 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Would you happen to know where I could get some good coffee around here? (你知道我在附近哪儿能买到好喝的咖啡？)
- **A:** The café on the second floor is good. (二层的咖啡厅很不错。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Do you know where to go to get a nice cup of coffee around here? (你知道这儿附近哪里能喝到好喝的咖啡吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) They make a great couple. (他们是很棒的一对。)
  - (B) Sure, I could use a cup. (当然，我可以用茶杯。)
  - (C) Try the café on the second floor. (试试看二层的咖啡厅。)


### Q24 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Would you care for a game of tennis after we finish work today? (今天下班后你想一起打一局网球吗？)
- **A:** I'd love to, but I can't today. (我很想去，可是今天去不了。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Do you want to join me for a game of tennis after work? (你想下班后和我一起打一局网球吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Thanks, but I'll pass this time. (谢谢，这次我就不去了。)
  - (B) I learned the game a week ago. (我一周前学了这项运动。)
  - (C) There will be three of us going. (我们会有三个人去。)


### Q25 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** You have a moment to spare this morning, don't you? (你今天上午能抽出一点儿时间，是吧？)
- **A:** Sure, what's up? (当然可以，怎么啦？)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** You have some spare time this morning, don't you? (你今天上午有空，是吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) It is ten o'clock now. (现在 10 点了。)
  - (B) Yes, in my office. (是的，在我的办公室。)
  - (C) I think so. (我想是的。)


### Q26 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Would you by chance know of a good restaurant to take Mr. Lee? (你知道有什么好饭店可以带李先生去吗？)
- **A:** Well, what does he like to eat? (哦，他喜欢吃什么？)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Could you recommend a nice place to take Mr. Lee? (你能推荐一个可以带李先生去的好地方吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I recommended him to the boss. (我向老板推荐了他。)
  - (B) What type of food does he like? (他喜欢哪种食物？)
  - (C) He will be here for a week. (他会在这里待一周。)


### Q27 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Don't you think it would be okay to go over after we finish work first? (你不觉得我们先做完工作之后再过去就行吗？)
- **A:** Yes, let's leave right at five o'clock. (是的，咱们5点整走。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Couldn't we just head over after work? (难道我们下班后再过去不好吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) He works on the first floor. (他在一层工作。)
  - (B) No, let's look it over now. (不，咱们现在就检查。)
  - (C) Sure, let's take off at five. (当然，咱们 5 点出发。)


### Q28 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** The construction work is making a lot of noise. (建筑工作产生了很多噪音。)
- **A:** You should close the windows. (你应当关上窗户。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** The renovation work they're doing is very loud. (他们正在做的修缮工作很吵。)
- **选项：**
  - (A) It will be completed next year. (明年能结束。)
  - (B) Why don't you shut the windows? (你为什么不关上窗户呢？)
  - (C) There will be plenty of work. (会有很多工作。)


### Q29 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Don't you have to set up the tables for this evening's meeting? (你难道不用为今晚的会议安排桌子吗？)
- **A:** I asked Jack to take care of it. (我让杰克负责这件事了。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Don't you have to prepare the tables for the meeting tonight? (你难道不需要为今晚的会议准备桌子吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) A table for four, please. (请准备一张四人桌。)
  - (B) We are meeting today. (我们今天见面。)
  - (C) No, Jack will do it later. (不，过一会儿杰克会准备。)


### Q30 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Why don't you take it easy and take a few days off? (你为什么不放松点儿，休几天假？)
- **A:** I wish I could, but I have to finish this project first. (我也希望这样，但是我得先完成这个项目。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Why don't you take a break and stay home for a few days? (你为什么不休息一下，在家待几天呢？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Thanks, I had a great vacation. (谢谢，我的假期很愉快。)
  - (B) I wish I could, but I have too much work. (我也希望这样，但是我的工作太多了。)
  - (C) The one here is much stronger. (这里的这个强壮多了。)


### Q31 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** You can make the copies tomorrow, can't you? (你可以明天复印，是吧？)
- **A:** Yes, I have time until noon tomorrow. (是的，我到明天中午都有时间。Questions 32 through 34 refer to the following conversation.M:The boss wants me to change the setting of our office before thepresident's visit next month. He wants me to utilize the space here by movingthe furniture around.（)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** You don't have to make copies today, do you? (你今天不必复印，是吧？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I already had two cups, thanks. (我已经喝了两杯了，谢谢。)
  - (B) No, I could do it tomorrow morning. (是的，我可以明天上午做。)
  - (C) I should be able to make it there. (我应该能准时到那儿。)


## Part 3: 简短对话 (Q32 - Q70)

### Questions 32 - 34

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** The boss wants me to change the setting of our office before the president's visit next month. He wants me to utilize the space here by moving the furniture around. (32) I am not very good at this, so I need your expert advice. Can you spare some time to discuss the office layout?
**W:** Well, I am kind of busy today. Let me see... this Thursday or next Monday is good for me. What about you? (33)
**M:** I have to leave town for a week on Friday. (34) I think we'd better get together before I leave. (33) Is that okay with you?
**W:** That will be fine as long as it's in the morning. I have to leave early for a dentist appointment in the afternoon.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**老板想让我在总裁下个月来参观之前改变一下我们办公室的布局。他想让我挪动这些家具，把这里的空间利用起来。我不擅长干这个，所以我需要你这个专家的建议。你能抽点时间和我讨论一下办公室的布局吗？
> **W：**嗯，我今天有点儿忙。我想想…这周四或者下周一我可以。你呢？
> **M：**我周五得去外地，要去一周。我想我们最好在我走之前见面。你方便吗？
> **W：**只要在上午就行。我下午得早走，约好了去看牙医。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **setting**：环境，布置
- **utilize**：利用
- **expert**：专家
- **spare**：抽（时间）
- **layout**：布局
- **get together**：见面
- **rearrange**：重新安排

#### Q32 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the man's boss want him to do? (男士的老板想让他做什么？)
- (A) Cancel his dental appointment. (取消他跟牙医的约会。)
- (B) Move closer to the workplace. (搬到工作地点附近。)
- (C) Rearrange the furniture in the office. (重新安排办公室里的家具。)
- (D) Pick up the president from the airport. (到机场接总裁。)

#### Q33 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** When will they get together to discuss the issue? (他们会在什么时间见面讨论这个问题？)
- (A) Monday. (周一。)
- (B) Tuesday. (周二。)
- (C) Thursday. (周四。)
- (D) Friday. (周五。)

#### Q34 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the man say he will do Friday? (男士说他周五会做什么？)
- (A) Attend a meeting with the boss. (和老板一起参加一个会议。)
- (B) Go on a business trip. (出差。)
- (C) Visit his dentist's office. (去看牙医。)
- (D) Work in his office. (在办公室里工作。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **change the setting of our office** (改变我们办公室的布局扩展表达：)
  - *例句：rearrange the furniture in our office change things around in our office We need to change the setting of our office to make space for the newly hired employees.* (重新布置办公室的家具改变我们办公室的陈设我们需要改变一下办公室的格局，给新来的员工腾出地方。)
- **utilize the space = make （ best ） use of the space** (（充分）利用空间)
  - *例句：We should call a professional to utilize the space we have in the office.* (我们应该找一位专业人士帮我们利用办公室的空间。)
- **get together = meet = gather** (见面)
  - *例句：We should get together to discuss the possibilities.* (我们应该见面讨论各种可能性。)

### Questions 35 - 37

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** I think I am going to have to take a trip to Chicago tomorrow to talk to Mr. Shaw in person. I spoke to him on the phone just now, but he didn't sound too convinced about our offer. (35)
**M:** Well, if that's what's needed, then you'd better get yourself over there. I don't think I have to stress the fact to you again how important it is that we get this deal. Please go out of your way to get this contract. In other words, do what you have to do to get it.
**W:** Yes sir, I will try my best. By the way, can you tell me where the bus station is? I have never gone out of the city, and I am not sure where the bus station is. (36)
**M:** You've got to be kidding me. Tell you what, I will come and pick you up tomorrow and drive you to the station. (37) It's the least I can do to get your day started off right.

**中文对照：**
> **W：**我想我明天要去一趟芝加哥和肖先生当面谈一谈。我刚才和他通过电话了，但是听起来他对我们的报价不太确信。
> **M：**哦，如果需要这样，那你最好设法去那儿一趟。我想我不用再向你强调达成这笔交易有多重要了。请你想方设法拿到合同。换句话说，需要做什么就做什么，把合同拿下。
> **W：**好的，先生，我会尽力的。顺便说一下，你知道公交车站在哪儿吗？我还没离开过这座城市，我不确定公交车站在哪儿。
> **M：**你肯定是在开玩笑。告诉你吧，明天我会开车来接你，送你去车站。为了你明天顺利地动身，这是我最起码能做的事。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **in person**：亲自，当面
- **convinced**：确信的，信服的
- **get over**：克服
- **stress**：强调
- **go out of one's way**：想方设法
- **in other words**：换句话说
- **tell you what**：告诉你吧
- **least**：最少的
- **persuade**：说服
- **travel**：旅行
- **give a lift/ride**：让搭车

#### Q35 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Why is the woman thinking of taking a trip to Chicago? (为什么女士考虑要去芝加哥一趟？)
- (A) To persuade someone. (去说服某个人。)
- (B) To take a vacation. (去度假。)
- (C) To visit a friend. (去看望一个朋友。)
- (D) To accept an offer. (去接受一个报价。)

#### Q36 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** How will the woman travel? (女士会怎么去？)
- (A) By bus. (乘公共汽车。)
- (B) By subway. (乘地铁。)
- (C) By car. (乘汽车。)
- (D) On foot. (步行。)

#### Q37 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the man imply when he says, “You've got to be kidding me”? (男士说 “ 你肯定是在开玩笑 ” ，他在暗示什么？)
- (A) He will buy the woman a ticket. (他会给女士买一张票。)
- (B) He will give the woman a lift to the station. (他会开车送女士去车站。)
- (C) He will go with the woman on her trip. (他会和女士一起去。)
- (D) He will talk to the woman's client. (他会和女士的客户谈话。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **talk to Mr. Shaw in person = see Mr. Shaw face to face** (当面和肖先生谈谈扩展表达：)
  - *例句：discuss it over a cup of coffee with Mr. Shaw In order to resolve this situation, I have to talk to Mr. Shaw in person.* (和肖先生边喝咖啡边讨论为了解决这个问题，我必须和肖先生当面谈谈。)
- **He didn't sound too convinced about our offer.** (听起来他对我们的报价不太确信。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：He didn't seem very interested in our offer. = He didn't show any signs of interest in our offer.* (他对我们的报价不太感兴趣。)
- **I don't think I have to stress the fact to you again.** (我认为我不必再向你强调这个事实了。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：I don't have to tell you again. = I don't have to repeat it to you again. I don't have to stress the fact to you again that it is vital for us to launch this product in August.* (我不用再跟你重复了。我不必再向你强调8月份发布这个产品的重要性了。)

### Questions 38 - 40

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Did you cancel your trip? I thought you were supposed to take off today.
**M:** I was, but I got a great deal on a plane ticket from a friend of mine who works at a travel agency. (40) So I decided to fly to New York next Monday instead. (38)
**W:** Wow! That is great. What about your hotel reservation? Were you able to change it? I heard it's very hard to get any rooms this week because of the film festival there. (39)
**M:** Actually, I ended up canceling it. It turns out that another friend of mine has a condominium there, and he said I could use it while I am staying there. (40) He recently moved out here from New York because of his new job, and he hasn't had enough time to get rid of it yet.

**中文对照：**
> **W：**你取消旅行了吗？我以为你应该今天出发呢。
> **M：**原定是今天出发，但是我从一个在旅行社工作的朋友那里买到一张很值的机票。所以我决定下周一再飞往纽约。
> **W：**哇，太棒了！那你预订的宾馆怎么办？你能调换一下吗？我听说因为那儿正举办电影节，这周很难订到房间。
> **M：**其实，我最后把房间取消了。原来我的另一个朋友在那儿有一套公寓，他说我在那儿时可以住在里面。他近期要搬出纽约，因为他找到了一份新工作，但还没来得及卖掉这套房子。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **be supposed to**：应该，被期望
- **take off**：出发；起飞
- **great deal**：划算的买卖
- **end up**：结果，最后
- **turn out**：结果是，证明是
- **condominium**：公寓
- **get rid of**：摆脱
- **postpone**：推迟
- **on time**：按时
- **strike**：罢工
- **swarm**：聚集，云集
- **deposit**：押金
- **infer**：推测，推断

#### Q38 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Why did the man delay his trip? (男士为什么推迟了旅行？)
- (A) He got a discount on a later flight. (他买到了晚些时候航班的打折机票。)
- (B) His meeting got postponed. (他的会议推迟了。)
- (C) His friend could not make it on time. (他的朋友没能按时出发。)
- (D) He couldn't book a hotel room. (他订不到房间。)

#### Q39 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** According to the woman, why is it hard to reserve a room in New York this week? (根据女士所说，为什么这周在纽约很难订到房间？)
- (A) The hotel workers have gone on a strike. (宾馆员工罢工了。)
- (B) Many visitors have swarmed the city. (很多观光者涌入了这座城市。)
- (C) Some of the hotels aren't accepting bookings. (一些宾馆不接受预订。)
- (D) A large deposit is required for reservations. (预订需要一大笔押金。)

#### Q40 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What can be inferred about the man? (关于男士，可以推测出什么？)
- (A) He is a good businessman. (他是个优秀的商人。)
- (B) He has some good contacts. (他有一些好朋友。)
- (C) He travels a lot. (他经常旅行。)
- (D) He has a lot of money. (他有很多钱。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **Did you cancel your trip? = Did you call off your trip?** (你取消旅行了吗？扩展表达：)
  - *例句：Did you say you have decided not to go away?* (你说你决定不走了吗？)
- **I got a great deal. = I got a great bargain. = I managed to get a good price.** (我得到一个优惠价。)
  - *例句：I got a great deal on a pair of sunglasses.* (我以优惠价买了一副太阳镜。)
- **It turned out that ~ = It ended up that ~ = It worked out that ~** (结果…)
  - *例句：It turned out that Jeff went to the same college as I did.* (结果杰夫和我去了同一所大学。)

### Questions 41 - 43

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Hello. This is Carol Dunning from Huntington Consulting. I need to talk to someone about the order we placed this morning. (41)
**M:** Good afternoon, Ms. Dunning. I can handle that. Do you want to add something to your order?
**W:** That's correct. Would it be possible to double the amount of copy paper we ordered?
**M:** Totally. Should I send you an updated bill by e-mail? (42)
**W:** That won't be necessary. Just attach it to the invoice you send us every month.
**M:** Okay, I can do that. You can expect to receive everything by Friday morning. (43)

**中文对照：**
> **W：**您好。我是亨廷顿咨询公司的卡罗尔·邓宁。我需要和某个人谈一下我们今天早上下的订单。
> **M：**下午好，邓宁女士。我可以处理。您想在您的订单里添加些物品是吗？
> **W：**是的。我们订购的复印纸数量可以增加一倍吗？
> **M：**完全可以。需要我把更新后的账单发到您邮箱吗？
> **W：**不必了。请把它附在你每月寄给我们的发票上就可以了。
> **M：**好的，我能做到。您在星期五早上就能收到所有东西。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **handle**：处理
- **add~to~**：把增加到
- **double**：两倍；加倍
- **order**：订单
- **totally**：完全地
- **attach~to~**：将依附于；附属于

#### Q41 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Why did the woman call the man? (女士为什么给男士打电话？)
- (A) To change an order. (更改订单。)
- (B) To ask for a discount. (要求折扣。)
- (C) To cancel an order. (取消订单。)
- (D) To alter her address. (更改她的地址。)

#### Q42 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Why does the woman say, “That won't be necessary”? (为什么女士说 “ 不必了 ” ？)
- (A) She does not need a new bill. (她不需要一个新账单。)
- (B) She is not interested in a different item. (她对不同的物品不感兴趣。)
- (C) She does not want express delivery. (她不想要快递。)
- (D) She has no need for an itemized list. (她不需要逐项清单。)

#### Q43 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** When will the items be delivered? (物品什么时候可以送达？)
- (A) Later in the day. (当天晚些时候。)
- (B) Tomorrow. (明天。)
- (C) This Friday. (本周五。)
- (D) Next week. (下周。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **Would it be possible to do sth.? = Is there any possibility that~?** (有可能…吗？)
  - *例句：Would it be possible to postpone the party?* (聚会有可能推迟吗？)
- **the amount of = the number of …** (的数量)
  - *例句：The number of pages is set by the amount of advertising space they sell. the number of the amount of* (报纸的页数由他们出售的广告空间来决定的。（知识扩展：一般情况下，用来修饰可数名词，而则用来修饰不可数名词）)
- **send sb. sth. = send sth. to sb.** (送给某人某物)
  - *例句：I will send my mom a purse as her birthday gift.* (我会送我妈妈一个钱包当她的生日礼物。)

### Questions 44 - 46

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** I overheard you mentioning to the sales manager that you and your wife are into watching movies. Will you be seeing one this weekend by any chance?
**M:** Yes, I was thinking of checking out the Sunday matinée at the Imperial Six Cinema. (44) They are playing Mary Poppins there this weekend. You see, I am a real big fan of classical flicks.
**W:** Oh, that's perfect. I got these two complimentary tickets that you can use at that theater. (45) My brother works there, (46) and he gave them to me, but I have to go out of town this weekend. Why don't you put them to good use?
**M:** Really? That's very nice of you. I really appreciate it.

**中文对照：**
> **W：**我无意中听到你跟销售经理说你和妻子喜欢看电影。你们这周末要去看吗？
> **M：**是的，我正想着查一下第六帝国电影院星期天的日场安排。那儿本周末正在上映《欢乐满人间》。你知道，我是古典电影的超级影迷。
> **W：**哦，太好了。我有两张你们可以在那个电影院用的赠票。我的弟弟在那儿工作，是他给我的，不过我这周末要去外地。你们好好利用一下这两张票吧。
> **M：**真的吗？你太好了。非常感谢。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **overhear**：无意中听说
- **by any chance**：正好，碰巧
- **matinée**：日场
- **you see**：你瞧，你知道
- **classical flick**：古典电影
- **complimentary**：免费的，赠送的
- **go out of**：离开
- **appreciate**：感激
- **theatrical**：剧院的，戏剧的
- **check out**：〈口〉试试，看看

#### Q44 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What will the man do this weekend? (男士这周末会做什么？)
- (A) Go to his brother's place. (去他弟弟那里。)
- (B) Watch a theatrical play. (看一部舞台剧。)
- (C) Check out a film. (看一部电影。)
- (D) Attend a musical performance. (参加一个音乐演出。)

#### Q45 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the woman offer the man? (女士给了男士什么东西？)
- (A) Free tickets. (免费电影票。)
- (B) A videotape. (一盘录影带。)
- (C) Some popcorn. (一些爆米花。)
- (D) A classical book. (一本古典作品。)

#### Q46 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Where does the woman's brother work? (女士的弟弟在哪儿工作？)
- (A) At a theater. (电影院。)
- (B) At a bookstore. (书店。)
- (C) At a travel agency. (旅行社。)
- (D) At a hotel. (宾馆。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I overheard you mentioning ~ = I couldn't help but hear you say ~ = I heard you talking to someone about ~** (我无意中听你提起…)
  - *例句：I overheard you mentioning to Ralph about the apartment you are trying to rent.* (我无意中听到你向拉尔夫提起你要租的房子。)
- **be into watching movies = like going to the movies = be movie buffs** (喜欢看电影)
  - *例句：Jeff is into watching classical films.* (杰夫喜欢看古典电影。)
- **complimentary tickets = free tickets = tickets at no charge** (赠票)
  - *例句：I got two complimentary tickets to the play.* (我有这场表演的两张赠票。)

### Questions 47 - 49

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Hello, Ms. Wilson. This is Mark Daniels. I regret to inform you that I'll be a few minutes late for our meeting.
**W:** What's the problem? Are you stuck in traffic?
**M:** No, but I missed the exit for your office, so I had to drive for ten minutes until I could turn around. (47) I should be there in fifteen minutes.
**W:** Okay, but please be aware that I have to leave by 2:30. I'm meeting with the CEO of my firm then. (48) Will you have enough time for the demonstration? (49)
**M:** More than enough. (49) You'll be able to see everything our new laptop can do.
**W:** Great. I'm looking forward to it.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**您好，威尔逊女士。我是马克·丹尼尔斯。很遗憾告知您，我们的会议我可能要晚几分钟。
> **W：**遇到了什么问题？您堵车了吗？
> **M：**没有。但是我错过了去你办公室的出口，所以不得不再开十分钟才能转弯。我十五分钟内到。
> **W：**好的，但是要知道我必须在2点半前离开。我要去见我们公司的首席执行官。你有足够的时间来演示吗？
> **M：**足够了。您可以看到我们的新笔记本电脑的一切功能。
> **W：**太好了。我很期待。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **regret to inform**：很遗憾的告知
- **stuck in**：陷入
- **exit**：出口；通道
- **more than enough**：远远多于；富裕的
- **be able to**：能；会
- **laptop**：笔记本电脑
- **look forward to do sth**：期待着做

#### Q47 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What is the man's problem? (男士遇到了什么问题？)
- (A) He left his office late. (他离开办公室有点晚。)
- (B) He did not bring a map. (他没有带地图来。)
- (C) He went the wrong way. (他走错路了。)
- (D) He got caught in traffic. (他遇到了交通拥堵。)

#### Q48 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What will the woman do later in the afternoon? (下午晚些时候女士要做什么事？)
- (A) Negotiate a price. (商谈价格。)
- (B) Meet an executive. (会见一位高管。)
- (C) Make an offer. (报价。)
- (D) Sign a contract. (签合同。)

#### Q49 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the man most likely mean when he says, “More than enough”? (当男人说 “ 足够了 ” 时，最有可能是什么意思？)
- (A) The woman's counteroffer is acceptable. (女士的还价是可以接受的。)
- (B) He brought several products with him. (他带了好几件产品。)
- (C) He can finish the demonstration by 2:30. (他可以在 2 点半之前完成演示。)
- (D) The room he will use is the right size. (他需要用的房间大小合适。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **a few = a little** (一点，一些)
  - *例句：He has a few friends.* (他有一些朋友。)
- **I'm meeting ~ = I'm going to meet ~** (我要去见…)
  - *例句：I am meeting Peter tonight and he is bringing me to see a movie.* (今晚我要见彼得，他带我去看电影。)

### Questions 50 - 52

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** I completely forgot that today is Rick's housewarming party. (50) I forgot to get him a gift, and I don't think I'll have enough time after work to go shopping. I'm going to run over to the mall during lunch. (51) Do you want to go together?
**M:** Sorry, Jean, but I am meeting someone for lunch today. Plus, I already picked up something a couple of nights ago.
**W:** I see. I guess I have no choice but to go alone then. Anyway, will you be taking your car to the party tonight?
**M:** No, I'm getting a lift with Eric. My car conked out on me last night, and it is in the garage today. (52) I had to take the bus to work this morning.

**中文对照：**
> **W：**我把里克今天的乔迁聚会忘得干干净净。我忘记给他买礼物了，我想下班后我也没有足够的时间去商店了。我只能午饭时跑去商场看一下。你想和我一起去吗？
> **M：**抱歉，琼，我今天要和别人一起吃午饭。另外，我几天前已经买好礼物了。
> **W：**我明白了。我想除了自己去我没有其他选择了。对了，你今晚会开车去聚会吗？
> **M：**不会，我要搭埃里克的车去。我的车昨晚突然出故障了，今天被送去修车厂了。我今早不得不乘公交车来上班。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **housewarming**：乔迁庆宴
- **run over**：（跑）过去
- **get a lift**：搭车
- **conk out**：突然出故障，失灵
- **garage**：车库；修车厂
- **publicize**：公布
- **auto repair shop**：修车厂
- **afford**：买得起，支付得起

#### Q50 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Why is Rick having a party? (里克为什么要办聚会？)
- (A) To celebrate his birthday. (为了庆祝他的生日。)
- (B) To welcome people to his new place. (为了欢迎大家去他的新家。)
- (C) To publicize his recent promotion. (为了公布他最近升迁的消息。)
- (D) To entertain an important client. (为了招待一位重要的客户。)

#### Q51 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What will the woman be doing during lunch? (女士在午饭时会做什么？)
- (A) Meet with Eric. (见埃里克。)
- (B) Shop for a gift. (去买一个礼物。)
- (C) Attend a party. (参加一个聚会。)
- (D) Pick up her car. (取她的车。)

#### Q52 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Why does the man say, “I'm getting a lift with Eric”? (男士为什么说 “ 我要搭埃里克的车去 ” ？)
- (A) His car is in the auto repair shop. (他的车在汽车修理厂。)
- (B) He can't afford the price of gas anymore. (他再也付不起汽油费了。)
- (C) His usual ride was not available. (他平时搭的车今天不能用。)
- (D) He got rid of his car. (他把车扔掉了。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I completely forgot it. = It completely slipped my mind. = I didn't remember it at all.** (我把它彻底忘记了。)
- **run over = head over = go over** (到…去)
  - *例句：I think I will run over to the store now.* (我想我现在要去商店了。)
- **pick up = buy = get** (买)
  - *例句：I picked up the drinks.* (我买了饮料。)
- **get a lift = get a ride = ask someone to drive me** (搭车)
  - *例句：I'm getting a lift with a co-worker.* (我在搭一个同事的车。)
- **My car conked out on me. = My car broke down on me. = My car stopped running.** (我的车突然出故障了。)
- **It is in the garage today. = It is in the auto repair shop today.** (它今天在修车厂里。)

### Questions 53 - 55

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** I know that you've worked very hard the last couple of weeks preparing for the presentation, and I am sure that you will do an excellent job today. (53) I just wanted to wish you good luck.
**M:** Thanks. I am a bit nervous right now, but at the same time I am quite confident. (54) I have worked very hard, and I really know my material inside out. So, don't worry. I will do my best.
**W:** Actually, I feel very relieved to hear that from you. I was a bit worried that you might not be ready. Anyway, where is Mark? The traffic is quite bad at this time of the day, and I don't want to take any chances of being late.
**M:** Don't worry, Ms. Wang. It usually only takes about fifteen minutes to get there from here. If worst comes to worst, I can always get off and run there. (55)

**中文对照：**
> **W：**我知道你这几周一直在很努力地准备这次演讲，我相信你今天一定会表现得特别好。我只想祝你好运。
> **M：**谢谢。我现在有点儿紧张，但是我也很自信。我非常努力地准备，对要讲的内容了如指掌。所以别担心，我会尽力的。
> **W：**听你这么说我真的很欣慰。我原来还有点儿担心你可能没准备好。对了，马克在哪儿？每天的这个时候交通都很糟糕，我可不想迟到。
> **M：**别担心，王女士。从这里到那里一般只需要15分钟。如果遇到最坏的情况，我也能下车，跑着过去。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **excellent**：非常好
- **a bit**：一点儿
- **nervous**：紧张的
- **at the same time**：同时
- **quite**：非常
- **confident**：自信
- **inside out**：彻底地
- **relieve**：放心，宽慰
- **get off**：下车
- **self-assured**：自信的
- **self-conscious**：害羞的
- **get caught in traffic**：遇到交通堵塞

#### Q53 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What will the man do today? (男士今天会做什么？)
- (A) Prepare for a presentation. (准备演讲。)
- (B) Make a speech. (发表演讲。)
- (C) Look for a job. (找工作。)
- (D) Compete in a race. (参加赛跑。)

#### Q54 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** How does the man feel? (男士的感觉如何？)
- (A) Self-assured. (自信。)
- (B) Self-conscious. (害羞。)
- (C) Fortunate. (幸运。)
- (D) Terrible. (害怕。)

#### Q55 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the man say he will do if they get caught in traffic? (男士说如果遇到交通堵塞他会怎么做？)
- (A) Take another road. (走另外一条路。)
- (B) Run to the meeting place. (跑到会场。)
- (C) Call and delay the meeting. (打电话，推迟会议。)
- (D) Have someone else attend the meeting. (让别人参加会议。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I really know my material inside out. = I really know my work well. = I really have the material memorized.** (我确实对我的材料了如指掌。)
- **If worst comes to worst ~ = If I have no options left ~ = If I am backed in a corner ~** (如果遇到最坏的情况…)
  - *例句：If worst comes to worst, I will just ask my parents for help.* (如果遇到最坏的情况，我会让父母帮忙的。)

### Questions 56 - 58

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M1:** What was your impression of the first candidate we met? (56)
**W:** You're talking about Leslie Wheeler, right? I thought she was extremely competent and would make a great addition to the company. (57) How about you, Joe?
**M2:** I agree with you completely.
**M1:** Honestly, I wasn't very impressed with her. But if you both disagree, I suppose we can invite her back for a second interview.
**W:** In my opinion, that would be the best thing to do. Shall I give her a call before lunch? (58)
**M1:** I don't think we should do that. Let's wait a couple of days until the interviews are all over.

**中文对照：**
> **M1：**你们对我们见到的第一位申请人的印象如何？
> **W：**你是说莱利斯·惠勒吗？我认为她非常能干，将会是公司一个很好的新生力量。乔，你觉得呢？
> **M2：**我完全赞同。
> **M1：**老实说，我对她不是很满意。但是，如果你们都不同意，我想可以邀请她参加第二次面试。
> **W：**在我看来，那将是最好的办法了。我要不要午饭前给她打个电话？
> **M1：**我认为我们不应该那样做。让我们再等几天，直到面试全部结束。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **impression**：印象
- **candidate**：申请人，候选者
- **competent**：能干的，胜任的
- **completely**：完全地
- **interview**：面试
- **a couple of**：几，一些

#### Q56 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What are the speakers mainly discussing? (讲话者们主要在谈论什么？)
- (A) A job applicant. (一位求职者。)
- (B) Upcoming interviews. (即将到来的面试。)
- (C) Their job duties. (他们的工作职责。)
- (D) A new hire. (一名新员工。)

#### Q57 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does Joe mean when he says, “I agree with you completely”? (当乔说 “ 我完全赞同 ” 时，是在暗示什么？)
- (A) He is in favor of speaking with more candidates. (他赞同与更多的申请者交谈。)
- (B) The applicants have been very impressive. (申请者们给人留下非常深刻的印象。)
- (C) Leslie Wheeler would be a good worker. (莱利斯 · 惠勒将会是一位好员工。)
- (D) The woman ought to apply for a transfer. (这位女士应申请工作调动。)

#### Q58 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the woman suggest doing? (这位女士建议做什么？)
- (A) Waiting for a while. (再等一等。)
- (B) Going to lunch early. (早点去吃午饭。)
- (C) Calling Leslie Wheeler. (给莱利斯)
- (D) Sending out invitations.

**延伸表达与补充：**
  - *例句：D* (）发出邀请函。)
- **would make a great addition to the company** (将会是公司一个很好的新生力量)
- **I agree with you completely. = I agree with you entirely./I totally agree with you.** (我完全同意。)
  - *例句：I completely forget that it's her birthday today.* (我完全忘记了今天是她生日。)
- **Honestly, I wasn't very impressed with her. = Honestly, I wasn't very satisfied with her.** (说实话，我对她不是很满意。)
  - *例句：I think the chief exec was favorably impressed by your presentation.* (我认为总经理对你的汇报相当满意。)

### Questions 59 - 61

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** There seems to be some mistakes on this bill. You charged me for a movie I didn't watch. And this charge here...what is it? (60)
**W:** That's for the room service you had this morning, sir. (59)
**M:** Room service? What room service? You'd better check your computer again because I think you're mistaking me for someone else. I met a client for breakfast at a restaurant this morning. (61)
**W:** Oh, is that right? Let me straighten this mistake out right away.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**这个账单上好像有些错误。我并没有看的一场电影，你们却向我收费了。还有这项收费…这是什么？
> **W：**这是您今天早上的房间服务费，先生。
> **M：**房间服务费？什么房间服务？你最好再查一下你的电脑，因为我认为你把我和别人弄混了。我今天早上在饭店和客户一起吃的早餐。
> **W：**哦，是吗？我马上纠正这个错误。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **mistake**：错误
- **charge**：收费
- **straighten out**：改正；澄清

#### Q59 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Where is the conversation taking place? (对话发生在哪里？)
- (A) At a movie theater. (电影院。)
- (B) At a hotel front desk. (宾馆的前台。)
- (C) In a computer store. (电脑商店。)
- (D) In a restaurant. (饭店。)

#### Q60 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What seems to be the problem? (出了什么问题？)
- (A) A mistake has occurred in the bill. (账单上出现了错误。)
- (B) The service at the restaurant was slow. (饭店的服务太慢了。)
- (C) The food was delivered to the wrong room. (饭菜被送错了房间。)
- (D) The computer is not working properly. (电脑不能正常工作。)

#### Q61 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What did the man do in the morning? (男士早上做了什么？)
- (A) He met a client. (他见了一个客户。)
- (B) He watched a movie. (他看了一场电影。)
- (C) He stayed in his room. (他待在自己的房间里。)
- (D) He was taking care of a problem. (他那时正在解决问题。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **You charged me for a movie I didn't watch. = I was charged for a movie I didn't see. = I have been billed for a movie I did not watch.** (我并没有看的一场电影，你们却向我收费了。)
- **I think you're mistaking me for someone else. = You must be confusing me with someone else. = I am not the person you think I am.** (我认为你把我和别人弄混了。)
- **Let me straighten this mistake out right away. = Let me correct the mistakes for you right now.** (我马上纠正这个错误。)

### Questions 62 - 64

![Page 86](images/listen_page_86.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Lars, would you mind listening to me rehearse my presentation for this afternoon's meeting. (62) I want to make sure I get everything right.
**M:** Can you wait a few minutes? I have to write an e-mail to my boss about the department's budget.
**W:** Sure, it's fine for me to wait.
**M:** What are you going to be talking about anyway? I wasn't even aware there's a meeting later today. (64)
**W:** It was called last night after almost everyone had gone home for the day. (64) I'll be talking about the effects of the new marketing campaign. (63)
**M:** Oh, I heard things are going well. I trust you have good news for everyone. Meeting Agenda

**中文对照：**
> **W：**拉尔斯，你介意听我排练一下今天下午的会议报告吗？我想确保一切顺利。
> **M：**稍等几分钟可以吗？我得给老板写一封关于部门预算的电子邮件。
> **W：**没问题，我可以等。
> **M：**对了，你要谈什么内容？我都不知道今天晚些时候有个会议。
> **W：**昨天晚上，几乎所有人都回家了，才有人打电话通知。我要谈一下新的营销活动的效果。
> **M：**噢，我听说一切都很顺利。我相信你会给大家带来好消息。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **rehearse**：排练；预演
- **presentation**：描述，陈述
- **budget**：预算，预算费
- **effect**：影响；效果；作用
- **campaign**：运动；活动会议议程

#### Q62 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the woman want the man to do? (对话中的女士想要男士做什么？)
- (A) Help her practice. (帮她排练。)
- (B) Talk to his boss on her behalf. (代表她去和上司谈话。)
- (C) Add some graphics to her presentation. (给她的报告加一些图表。)
- (D) Proofread her report. (检查她的报告。)

#### Q63 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. What time will the woman give her presentation? (请看图表。对话中的女士几点作报告？)
- (A) At 3:00. (3 点。)
- (B) At 3:15. (3 点 15 分。)
- (C) At 3:30. (3 点 30 分。)
- (D) At 3:45. (3 点 45 分。)

#### Q64 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What happened last night? (昨晚发生了什么？)
- (A) Some results were released. (公布了一些结果。)
- (B) New workers were hired. (雇用了新员工。)
- (C) A meeting was scheduled. (安排了一次会议。)
- (D) A presentation was given. (作了一个报告。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **get everything right = get everything ready** (把一切准备好)
  - *例句：Get everything right before it's too late.* (把一切准备好，免得太迟来不及。)

### Questions 65 - 67

![Page 87](images/listen_page_87.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Ms. Collins is considering restructuring the manner in which we acquire books for the library.
**W:** Why is that? Is there a problem?
**M:** Sort of. Take a look at this graph. The section with the least number of books is also the busiest because patrons are checking them out so much. (65)
**W:** Hmm...We should definitely be spending more money in that case. How soon can we start purchasing more books?
**M:** We've almost spent the money allocated for acquisitions for the year, (66) so we should wait two more months before buying anything new.
**W:** Well, meanwhile, let's compile a list of which books we want to acquire. (67)

**中文对照：**
> **M：**科林斯女士正在考虑调整我们为图书馆采购书的策略。
> **W：**这是为什么呢？有什么问题吗？
> **M：**有点问题。看一下这张图表。图书数量最少的区域却是最忙碌的，这是因为顾客经常去那里借书。
> **W：**嗯…那样的话，我们确实应该花更多的钱。我们多久之后开始购买新书？
> **M：**我们几乎用光了今年分配给我们购买图书的资金，所以我们应该再等两个月才能去买新书。
> **W：**好吧。与此同时，我们整理一张想要购买的图书的清单吧。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **restructure**：调整；重组
- **patron**：顾客
- **check out**：查看
- **purchase**：购买
- **allocate**：拨给
- **compile**：编写

#### Q65 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Which section has the most books borrowed? (请看图表。借书最多的是哪一个区域？)
- (A) Children's Books. (童书。)
- (B) Novels. (小说。)
- (C) Nonfiction. (非虚构类图书。)
- (D) Reference Books. (参考书。)

#### Q66 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the man say about the budget? (关于预算，男士说了什么？)
- (A) There is little money left in it. (预算没剩多少钱了。)
- (B) It was decreased this year. (今年的预算减少了。)
- (C) It will be increased next year. (明年的预算将会增加。)
- (D) There is enough money to buy more books. (有足够的钱买更多的书。)

#### Q67 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the woman propose doing? (女士建议做什么？)
- (A) Rearranging the books in the library. (重新整理图书馆的书籍。)
- (B) Thinking of which books to buy. (考虑买什么书。)
- (C) Giving a list of books to Ms. Collins. (给科林斯女士一张书单。)
- (D) Looking for cheap books to purchase. (寻找廉价书。各区域图书的数量)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **sort of = a little bit** (有点)
  - *例句：Excuse me, I seem to be a little bit lost.* (对不起，我似乎有点迷路了。)
- **take a look at = have a look at** (看一看)
  - *例句：Can you take a look at my paper?* (你能看一下我的论文吗？)
- **two more months = another two months** (再两个月)
  - *例句：We need two more months to complete the task.* (我们还需两个月才能完成任务。)

### Questions 68 - 70

![Page 88](images/listen_page_88.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Dennis, I'm taking the train to Piedmont tomorrow. Do you happen to know where the taxi stand at the station is?
**M:** It used to be in front of the exit on the northern side of the building, but it's being renovated. (68) So head to the eastern side instead. (69)
**W:** Thanks for the information. I need to catch a cab to get to my client's office.
**M:** Will you spend the night there or take the train back after your meeting's done?
**W:** I'll probably stay there for the night. You wouldn't happen to know any good places to eat there, would you? (70)
**M:** I know some. I'll e-mail you the details when I get back to my office.

**中文对照：**
> **W：**丹尼斯，我明天要乘火车去皮埃蒙特。你知道火车站的出租车站点在哪里吗？
> **M：**以前在火车站北出口的前面，但是现在正在整修。所以还是去东出口吧。
> **W：**谢谢你提供的信息。我需要乘出租车去见一个客户。
> **M：**你在那过夜还是在会议结束后乘火车回来？
> **W：**我有可能在那里过夜。你不会碰巧知道那里有哪些美食吧？
> **M：**我知道一些。我到办公室后发邮件给你详细的信息。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **taxi stand**：出租车站点
- **renovate**：修整，修复
- **head to**：前往
- **catch a cab**：乘出租车
- **client**：客户
- **detail**：细节

#### Q68 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the man say about the train station in Piedmont? (关于皮埃蒙特火车站，男士说了什么？)
- (A) It is in the center of the city. (它在市中心。)
- (B) Passengers think it is convenient. (乘客认为它很便利。)
- (C) Some work is being done on it. (它现在正在施工中。)
- (D) The subway station is located near it. (地铁站就在它附近。)

#### Q69 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Where is the taxi stand? (请看图表。出租车车站在哪里？)
- (A) Exit 1. (出口 1 。)
- (B) Exit 2. (出口 2 。)
- (C) Exit 3. (出口 3 。)
- (D) Exit 4. (出口 4 。)

#### Q70 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the woman ask the man about? (女士问了男士关于什么的问题？)
- (A) Hotels. (旅店。)
- (B) Restaurants. (餐厅。)
- (C) Parks. (公园。)
- (D) Entertainment centers. (娱乐中心。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **take the train = by train** (乘火车)
  - *例句：I'd like to take the train to go to Beijing.* (我想乘火车去北京。)
- **catch a cab = take a taxi** (乘出租车)
  - *例句：It is very hard to catch a cab in the rush hour.* (很难在高峰期搭上出租车。)
- **get to = arrive at = reach** (到达)
  - *例句：I'll give you a call as soon as get to Beijing.* (我一到北京就给你打电话。)

## Part 4: 简短独白 (Q71 - Q100)

### Questions 71 - 73

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Hi. It's nice to see you all. Before we begin the cooking course, let me tell you who I am. Luke Paget is my name. For the past 3 years I've been the leader of a team of innovative chefs working for Holiday Time Resorts. (71) As my main role is to develop new meals, (72) it's a great pleasure to be here and have the opportunity to meet people, especially those who are passionate about food and cooking. Please watch and listen carefully. Should you have any questions, make a note, and then ask them later during the discussion period. (73)

**中文对照：**
> 嗨，很高兴见到大家。在我们开始烹饪课之前，让我先自我介绍一下。我是卢克·佩吉特。过去的三年里我一直在假日时光度假村领导创意厨师团队。因为我的主要职责是开发新菜肴，所以我很高兴有机会在这里见到大家，尤其是热衷于美食和烹饪的朋友们。请大家仔细地看、仔细地听。如果有什么问题，请记录下来，然后在后面的讨论时间里提问。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **cooking course**：烹饪课
- **innovative**：创新的，有革新精神的
- **chef**：厨师
- **role**：作用，任务
- **develop**：开发
- **opportunity**：机会
- **passionate**：热情的
- **make a note**：做记录
- **think up**：想出
- **conduct**：指导
- **ingredient**：调味品
- **jot down**：草草记下

#### Q71 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Who is Mr. Paget? (佩吉特先生是谁？)
- (A) A chef. (厨师。)
- (B) A hotel manager. (酒店经理。)
- (C) A teacher. (教师。)
- (D) A grocery store clerk. (杂货店店员。)

#### Q72 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the speaker imply when he says, “As my main role is to develop new meals”? (讲话者说 “ 因为我的主要职责是开发新菜品 ” ，他在暗示什么？)
- (A) His main job is to greet the customers. (他的主要工作是迎接顾客。)
- (B) His main job is to think up new dishes. (他的主要工作是想出新菜品。)
- (C) His main job is to conduct cooking lessons. (他的主要工作是指导烹饪课。)
- (D) His main job is to stock fresh ingredients. (他的主要工作是贮备新鲜调味品。)

#### Q73 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the speaker ask those who have questions to do? (讲话者让有问题要问的人做什么？)
- (A) Jot them down and ask later. (记下问题，过一会儿再提问。)
- (B) Talk to Mr. Paget right away. (立刻和佩吉特先生探讨。)
- (C) E-mail them to him after the talk. (讲座结束后把问题用邮件发给他。)
- (D) Approach him before the talk. (讲座开始之前来找他。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **the leader of a team = the head of a team = the person who is in charge in a team** (团队的负责人)
  - *例句：You will one day become a leader of a team.* (你有一天会成为团队的领导的。)
- **main role = main job = main duty** (主要任务)
  - *例句：My main role is to make sales.* (我的主要任务是推销商品。)
- **make a note = write down** (做记录扩展表达：)
  - *例句：jot down Did you make a note of that?* (草草记下；匆匆记下你把它记录下来了吗？)

### Questions 74 - 76

**听力独白/对话原文：**
This brings us to the final stage of our tour and a most welcome one: it's the company café. (74) We hope that you will be pleasantly surprised by the quality and range of food and coffee on offer here. Why don't we all sit down and sample the coffee and cakes while I explain to you how the system works? The café opens at eight for hot drinks and light snacks. (75) Full food service is offered from midday until one thirty. On our right, you can see the cafeteria section, where you can choose your main meal at lunchtime. Sandwiches and cakes may be purchased at all times from the cafe section on your left. (76) In order to take advantage of this excellent service, simply show your employee identity card to the cashier. Are there any questions?

**中文对照：**
> 现在我们来到了本次参观的最后一站，也是最受欢迎的一个地方：公司的餐厅。我们希望这里供应的各种美食和咖啡能给大家带来惊喜。我们都坐下来品尝一下咖啡和糕点吧，同时，我可以给大家讲讲餐厅的营业情况。餐厅8点开始营业，供应热饮和简单的快餐。全面的食品供应是从中午12点到1点半。我们的右手边是自助餐厅区，大家在午餐时可以在这儿选择主餐。三明治和糕点在我们左手边的咖啡厅区域全天供应。如果想享受这里优良的服务，只需向收款台出示工作证即可。还有什么问题吗？

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **final stage**：最后阶段
- **welcome**：受欢迎的
- **pleasantly**：愉快地
- **range**：一系列
- **sample**：品尝；体验
- **snack**：快餐
- **midday**：中午，正午
- **cafeteria**：自助餐厅
- **section**：区域
- **at all times**：任何时候，一直
- **take advantage of**：利用
- **employee identify card**：工作证
- **cashier**：收银台；收银员

#### Q74 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** Who most likely is giving the talk? (讲这段话的人最有可能是谁？)
- (A) A tour guide. (导游。)
- (B) A cafeteria worker. (自助餐厅工作人员。)
- (C) A waiter. (服务生。)
- (D) A company employee. (公司员工。)

#### Q75 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What time does the place open? (这里几点开始营业？)
- (A) At ten. (10 点。)
- (B) At nine. (9 点。)
- (C) At eight. (8 点。)
- (D) At seven. (7 点。)

#### Q76 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What is available throughout the day? (什么是全天供应的？)
- (A) Sandwiches. (三明治。)
- (B) Hot meals. (热菜。)
- (C) Hot coffee. (热咖啡。)
- (D) Light snacks. (简单的快餐。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **This brings us to the final stage of our tour. = This brings us to the end of our tour. = This brings us to the last part of the tour.** (现在我们来到了本次参观的最后一站。)
- **In order to take advantage of this excellent service ~ = In order to make the best use of this service ~ = In order to make full use of this service ~** (为了好好利用这里优良的服务…)

### Questions 77 - 79

![Page 89](images/listen_page_89.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Hello to all our listeners out there. This is Rachel Lee from your number one weekly investment advice program “Investment Matters”. （ 77, 78 ） Don't miss tomorrow's program. We're going to give you all the information you need to choose the best deals in banking. Be sure to have your pens and notebooks ready— you could save thousands with just a little common sense and good advice, of course. This will be followed by our regular panel session but this time with an extra special guest—it's investment superstar Morris Stevenson, a freelance financial consultant and multi-millionaire, and of course, the author of the best- selling book You Can Be Rich! Call our hotline number if you want to speak to Morris. (79) Until tomorrow, everybody, goodbye from Rachel.

**中文对照：**
> 听众朋友们，大家好。这里是最棒的每周投资指南节目《投资要点》，我是雷切尔·李。明天的节目千万不要错过。我们将会向您提供关于如何在银行业务中选择最佳交易的全部信息。注意准备好纸和笔——靠一点常识，当然还有好的建议，你就能节省几千块钱。在这之后是我们例行的专家讨论环节，不过这次的专家是一位特别嘉宾——投资明星莫里斯·史蒂文森，他从事自由职业的财务顾问，也是一位千万富翁，当然他还是畅销书《你能成为富翁！》的作者。假如你想和莫里斯对话，请拨打我们的热线电话吧。我是雷切尔，听众朋友们，明天见。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **weekly**：每周一次的
- **investment**：投资
- **miss**：错过
- **deal**：交易
- **banking**：银行业务
- **common sense**：常识
- **follow**：跟随
- **panel**：专家
- **session**：会议
- **freelance**：自由职业（者）的
- **multi-millionaire**：千万富翁
- **best-selling**：畅销的
- **hotline**：热线
- **collateral**：抵押
- **station**：电台

#### Q77 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** How often does the show air? (这个节目多久播出一次？)
- (A) Everyday. (每天。)
- (B) Once a week. (一周一次。)
- (C) On weekends. (每个周末。)
- (D) Twice a week. (一周两次。)

#### Q78 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Who might be interested in listening to the show? (谁可能会对这个节目感兴趣？)
- (A) Those who want to borrow money without collateral. (不想通过抵押来贷款的人。)
- (B) People who wish to start their own businesses. (想自己开办公司的人。)
- (C) People who want to make wise investments. (想要明智地投资的人。)
- (D) Those who are seeking careers as consultants. (想以顾问为职业的人。)

#### Q79 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** How can the listeners ask Morris questions? (听众如何向莫里斯提问？)
- (A) By coming to the show. (参与到节目中来。)
- (B) By sending e-mails. (发送电子邮件。)
- (C) By calling the station. (给电台打电话。)
- (D) By talking to him in person. (当面和他对话。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **Don't miss tomorrow's program.** (不要错过明天的节目。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：Please tune in again tomorrow. We will be back again tomorrow.* (欢迎明天继续收听。明天再见。)
- **You could save thousands.** (你能节省几千块钱。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：You can save a lot of money. You can cut costs.* (你能节省不少钱。你可以削减成本。)

### Questions 80 - 82

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Hello, Mr. Duvall. This is Tony from the Reservations Department at the National Opera. I received your message, and I want to answer your queries regarding the performance tomorrow. (80) As you know, Thursday is a popular night, so I suggest that you book immediately and pay for your tickets before 5 p.m. this evening. (81) As for a group booking, at present, there are fifteen seats available to your group, but unfortunately they are not all together. I am hoping that this will be okay. Anyway, if you do decide to take these tickets, I can offer you a generous group discount of 20 percent. All you need to do is call me to confirm (82) and then come in to the reservations office to pick up your tickets. I hope you have a nice evening.

**中文对照：**
> 您好，杜瓦尔先生。我是国家剧院预订部的托尼。我收到了您的留言，想解答一下您关于明晚演出的疑问。您也知道，周四晚上很火，所以我建议您马上预订，并且在今晚5点之前支付票款。关于团体预订，目前有15个座位可以提供给您的团体，不过很不巧它们不都在一块儿。我希望这没有大碍。总之，如果您决定买这些票，我可以给您八折的团队优惠折扣。您需要做的就是打电话给我确认并来预订办公室取票。希望您度过一个愉快的夜晚。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **reservation**：预订
- **query**：询问，疑问
- **regarding**：关于
- **performance**：演出
- **suggest**：建议
- **book**：预订
- **immediately**：立刻，马上
- **generous**：优惠的
- **show up**：出席，露面
- **in cash**：用现金

#### Q80 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Why is the caller leaving a message? (打电话的人为什么留言？)
- (A) He is returning a phone call. (他在回复一个来电。)
- (B) He wants to books tickets to the opera. (他想预订该剧院的票。)
- (C) He hopes to get a discount on future tickets. (他希望以后买票能拿到折扣。)
- (D) He can't attend the performance tomorrow. (他不能参加明天的演出。)

#### Q81 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** According to the speaker, what should Mr. Duvall do by 5 p.m.? (根据讲话者所说，杜瓦尔先生在 5 点之前应该做什么？)
- (A) Pay for the tickets. (支付票款。)
- (B) Reserve seats. (预订座位。)
- (C) Join a group. (加入一个团体。)
- (D) Show up at the theater. (到剧院去。)

#### Q82 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** How can Mr. Duvall get the discount? (杜瓦尔先生怎样能拿到折扣？)
- (A) By showing up at the theater early. (早点儿到剧院。)
- (B) By paying for the tickets in cash. (用现金支付票款。)
- (C) By making a phone call. (打一个电话。)
- (D) By becoming a member. (成为会员。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **Thursday is a popular night. = Thursday is a busy night. = Thursday night will be crowded.** (周四晚上的演出很火。)
- **I suggest that you book immediately. = I recommend you reserve it right away. = I advise you to book now.** (我建议您马上预订。)

### Questions 83 - 85

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Good evening, everybody. I'd just like to say a few words before officially opening the exhibition. (83) I'm very pleased to see so many faces here tonight. It seems that many people share my interest in the history of the Old Town. And it is a fascinating history! These documents, photographs, artworks, and other historical items vividly reflect the life of the Old Town, (84) from its Roman beginnings until modern times. My special thanks to the local library and museum for all their work and also to our many private contributors. (85)

**中文对照：**
> 大家晚上好。我想在展览正式开幕之前讲几句话。很高兴今晚在这里见到了这么多来宾。看起来很多人都和我一样对老城的历史有着浓厚的兴趣，而且它的历史又是这样引人入胜！这些文件、照片、工艺品和其他历史文物生动地展现了老城从罗马开创时期到现代的生活面貌。我要特别感谢地方图书馆和博物馆所做的工作，并感谢众多的个人捐赠者。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **officially**：正式地
- **exhibition**：展览
- **share**：分享
- **fascinating**：引人入胜的
- **vividly**：生动地
- **artwork**：艺术品
- **historical**：历史的
- **reflect**：再现，反映
- **beginning**：开始
- **contributor**：捐赠者
- **community**：社区
- **mayor**：市长

#### Q83 (正确答案：D)

- (B) In a library. (在图书馆里。)
- (C) At a museum. (在博物馆。)
- (D) At an exhibition. (在展览会上。)

#### Q84 (正确答案：D)

- (B) Papers. (文件。)

**延伸表达与补充：**

### Questions 86 - 88

Hello, Mr. Jackson, this is Jane Erickson from the Port Project Committee at N.P.U. Architectural Services. I hope you remember me. Anyway, the committee was very impressed by your presentation today, and we'd like to encourage you to submit a formal quote as soon as possible. (86) I know that the closing date is in six weeks, (87) but would it be possible for you to submit your documents in three weeks? The committee needs as much time as possible to evaluate each proposal and make a recommendation. Should you have any inquiries at all, please don't hesitate to call me at 781-2213. (88)

**中文对照：**

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **architectural**：建筑的
- **impress**：给留下印象
- **encourage**：鼓励
- **formal**：正式的
- **quote**：报价
- **closing date**：截止日期
- **evaluate**：评估
- **make a recommendation**：提出建议
- **inquiry**：询问
- **hesitate**：犹豫
- **make a presentation**：发言
- **architect**：建筑师，设计师

- (B) To respond back to a call made earlier. (为了回复之前的一个电话。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **a formal quote = an official quote** (一份正式的报价)
  - *例句：Please submit a formal quote by this Friday.* (请在本周五之前提交一份正式的报价。)
- **The closing date is in six weeks. = The due date is in six weeks.** (截止日期是六周之后。)
- **Should you have any inquiries... = If you have any questions... = If you have anything you want to know...** (如果您有任何疑问…)
  - *例句：Should you have any inquiries, please don't hesitate to call me at my office.* (如果您有任何疑问，请随时打我的办公电话。)

### Questions 89 - 91

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Well, as you can see, I am surprised and overwhelmed by this award. (89) I'd especially like to dedicate the “Young Entrepreneur of the Year” trophy to my mother, who has always supported me. Actually, it was in my mother's garage that I developed my hobby into a successful business. I started as a child, building the electronic project kits that she bought me. (90) I soon began making modifications, and from there I moved on to design. Now I provide secure computer networks for large corporations all over North America. Well, I'm one of those lucky people who have become rich doing what they love! (91) Thanks again to everybody who has made it possible. (89)

**中文对照：**
> 哦，大家都看到了，我得到这个奖特别惊喜，都有些不知所措了。我特别想把这个“年度青年企业家”奖杯献给一直以来都在支持我的母亲，实际上，我就是在母亲的车库里把兴趣发展成了成功的事业。我从小便开始装配她给我买的电气工程套件。后来我开始进行改进，然后又开始设计。现在我给遍布北美的大型公司提供安全的电脑网络服务。是的，我是一个幸运的人，靠做自己喜欢的事致富！再次感谢所有让这一切成为可能的人。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **overwhelm**：使不知所措，使吃惊
- **dedicate**：献给
- **trophy**：奖品，奖杯
- **support**：支持
- **garage**：车库
- **electronic**：电子的
- **kit**：成套部件
- **modification**：修改，改变
- **secure**：安全的，可靠的
- **all over**：遍及，到处
- **achieve**：达到
- **launch**：发布
- **gadget**：装置
- **reveal**：泄露，透露

#### Q89 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What is the purpose of the speech? (这篇讲话的目的是什么？)
- (A) To congratulate his mother on achieving her goal. (祝贺他母亲实现她的目标。)
- (B) To thank those who helped him win the award. (感谢那些帮助他获奖的人。)
- (C) To launch a new electronic gadget. (发布一种新的电子装置。)
- (D) To reveal the secret to making money. (透露赚钱的秘密。)

#### Q90 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** How did the speaker first become interested in his field of work? (讲话者最初是如何对他所从事的行业产生兴趣的？)
- (A) He took a class in school. (他在学校上了一门课。)
- (B) His mother introduced him to it. (他的母亲向他介绍的。)
- (C) His friend got him a job. (他的朋友给他找了一份工作。)
- (D) He read about it in a magazine. (他在杂志上读到的。)

#### Q91 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Why does the speaker say, “I'm one of those lucky people who have become rich doing what they love”? (讲话者为什么说 “ 我是一个幸运的人，靠做自己喜欢做的事致富 ” ？)
- (A) He makes a living doing what he likes. (他以自己的爱好为生。)
- (B) He has a very wealthy mother. (他有一个非常富有的母亲。)
- (C) He travels all over America. (他到美国各处旅游。)
- (D) He has enough time for his hobbies. (他有足够的时间留给自己的兴趣爱好。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **who has always supported me = who has always been with me** (一向支持我的人扩展表达：)
  - *例句：who has always believed in me I'd like to thank those who have always supported me through thick and thin.* (一向信任我的人我要感谢一直以来不管艰难困苦都在支持我的人。)
- **move on to = go forward** (开始做（别的事）)
  - *例句：I moved on to design to better my career opportunities.* (我开始做设计，使自己有更好的职业机遇。)

### Questions 92 - 94

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Welcome, everybody, to the “City at Night” tour. My name's Barbara, and I'll be your guide (92) and host this evening. I know that many of you know Blackburn well, but I hope that you are going to enjoy seeing a different side of this city. First, we'll be visiting Blackburn's medieval fortress. And I should warn you that we will be visiting the dungeons and torture chamber. Then we'll go to historic Wetherby Mansion. There are rumors that it is haunted by the ghost of Lady Wetherby, (93) who disappeared mysteriously five hundred years ago. And finally, to finish on a happier note, there will be a champagne supper in Blackburn Tower Park, which has a splendid view of the sparkling city lights and the surrounding hills. (94)

**中文对照：**
> 欢迎大家参加“城市之夜”的旅行。我叫芭芭拉，是今晚的导游和接待员。我知道你们中有很多人已经非常了解布莱克本，不过，我希望大家可以愉快地领略这个城市的另一面。首先，我们将会参观布莱克本的中世纪城堡。我要提醒大家的是我们还会参观地牢和刑讯室。然后我们会去历史上著名的韦瑟比庄园。有传闻说那里有韦瑟比夫人的鬼魂出没，五百年前她在那儿神秘地消失了。最后，我们可以高兴一点儿，在布莱克本的塔楼公园里将举行一场香槟晚宴，在那里我们可以观赏城市璀璨的灯火和环绕的群山。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **host**：接待员
- **medieval**：中世纪的
- **fortress**：堡垒，城堡
- **warn**：警告，忠告
- **dungeon**：地牢
- **torture**：折磨
- **chamber**：室，房间
- **mansion**：大宅，庄园
- **haunt**：（鬼魂等）出没于
- **mysteriously**：神秘地
- **supper**：晚餐
- **splendid**：美妙的

#### Q92 (正确答案：A)

- (B) Mr. Blackburn. (布莱克本先生。)
- (C) A history teacher. (历史教师。)
- (D) A restaurant host. (饭店老板。)

- (B) It is very old. (它很古老。)

- (A) It is located on the outskirts of the city. (它位于市郊。)
- (B) The place has become a landmark of the city. (这里已经成为该市的标志性建筑。)
- (C) There are hills near the place. (这里周围有山。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I hope that you are going to enjoy seeing a different side of this city. = I hope that you will be looking forward to experiencing a different side of the city. = I expect that you will appreciate a different part of the city.** (希望大家可以愉快地领略这个城市的另一面。)
- **There are rumors that ~ = There are false beliefs that ~ = There are misconceptions that ~** (有传闻说…)
  - *例句：There are rumors that our company is in financial trouble.* (有传闻说，我们公司陷入了财务危机。)

  - *例句：The concert will take place the day after tomorrow.* (音乐会将于后天举行。)

  - *例句：There are a wide variety of flowers in Uncle Wang's garden.* (王叔叔的花园里有各种各样的花。)

### Questions 98 - 100

![Page 93](images/listen_page_93.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Hello, Jason. This is Steve Meyers. I'd like to inform you that I'm getting close to where you are right now. I just passed a sign indicating that I need to get off the interstate in six kilometers. (98) I know the restaurant we're meeting at is close to the exit, so I estimate that I'll be there in about ten minutes. (99) If you want to go ahead and order drinks and appetizers, please be my guest. You know what I like. I hope you brought your laptop with you. (100) I need to show you some files, but mine is in the shop, so I wasn't able to bring it.

**中文对照：**
> 你好，杰森。我是史蒂夫·迈耶斯。我想告知你，我正在接近你目前所在的位置。我刚通过一个指示牌，表明我需要在六公里后驶离州际公路。我了解到我们约见的餐厅离公路出口很近，所以我估计十分钟之内就能到达那里。如果你想提前去并点上饮料和开胃菜，那么请别客气。你知道我喜欢什么。我希望你带着笔记本电脑，因为我需要给你展示一些文件，我的落在店里了，所以我没法带。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **sign**：指示牌；记号
- **indicate**：表明；预示
- **get off**：从下来；脱下
- **interstate**：州际公路
- **exit**：出口；通道
- **estimate**：估计，估价
- **go ahead**：先走；前进
- **appetizer**：开胃菜；前菜
- **be my guest**：别客气，请便
- **laptop**：笔记本电脑
- **file**：文件；档案

#### Q98 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Where will the speaker get off the interstate? (请看图表。讲话者会在哪里驶离州际公路？)
- (A) At Gatlinburg. (在加特林堡。)
- (B) At Shelbyville. (在谢尔比维尔。)
- (C) At Lake Simon. (在西蒙湖。)
- (D) At Portsmouth. (在朴茨茅斯。)

#### Q99 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** Where is the speaker's final destination? (讲话者的最终目的地是哪里？)
- (A) An office building. (一栋办公大楼。)
- (B) A coffee shop. (一间咖啡馆。)
- (C) A park. (一座公园。)
- (D) A restaurant. (一家餐馆。)

#### Q100 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the speaker request? (讲话者要求什么？)
- (A) A file folder. (一个文件夹。)
- (B) A laptop. (一台笔记本电脑。)
- (C) A map. (一张地图。)
- (D) A contract. (一份合同。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **would like to do ~ = want to do~** (想要做…)
  - *例句：I would like to practice my oral English with native speakers.* (我想和母语人士一起练习英语口语。)
- **close to = next to** (接近，在附近)
  - *例句：The office building is right close to a big shopping mall.* (那栋办公大楼正好在一家大型购物中心附近。)
