## Part 1: 照片描述 (Q1 - Q6)

### Q1 (正确答案：C)

![Page 95](images/listen_page_95.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) They're waiting for their bags. (他们在等自己的行李。)
- (B) They're about to board the plane. (他们即将登机。)
- (C) They're relaxing in a waiting area. (他们正在等候区休息。)
- (D) They're sitting in a conference hall. (他们正坐在会议厅内。)

**其他可能表达：**
- The people are sitting in a waiting area. (他们坐在等候区内。)
- Many of the seats are occupied. (很多座位都有人。)
- Most of the people have taken seats. (大多数人都有座位。)


### Q2 (正确答案：A)

![Page 95](images/listen_page_95.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) They have gathered in a small group. (他们聚集成一小群。)
- (B) They are taking a break from work. (他们暂停工作，正在休息。)
- (C) The people are getting ready to leave for the day. (人们正准备下班了。)
- (D) They are waiting to be seated in a restaurant. (他们在餐厅等位。)

**其他可能表达：**
- They are talking in a group. (他们正聚集在一起谈话。)
- The place is bright and spacious. (这里明亮而宽敞。)
- The room is brightly lit. (房间的灯光很明亮。)


### Q3 (正确答案：D)

![Page 95](images/listen_page_95.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) She's fixing the wheel of the cart. (她正在修理手推车的轮子。)
- (B) She's pushing the cart toward the construction area. (她正在推手推车去工地。)
- (C) She's pouring cement onto the ground. (她正朝地上浇水泥。)
- (D) She's moving some construction materials. (她正在运送一些建筑材料。)

**其他可能表达：**
- The woman is pushing a wheelbarrow. (女士正在推独轮车。)
- She is transporting some dirt. (她正在运一些土。)
- The wheelbarrow is full of dirt. (独轮车装满了土。)


### Q4 (正确答案：C)

![Page 96](images/listen_page_96.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) The boat has stopped at sea. (船停在海上。)
- (B) The sailboat is being pushed into the water. (帆船正被推进水中。)
- (C) The boat is resting under the trees. (船正停在树下。)
- (D) The trees are being cut down at the moment. (树木现在正在被砍倒。)

**其他可能表达：**
- The boat is shaded by the trees. (船在树荫下。)
- A boat has been left under the trees. (一艘船被留在树下。)
- The boat has been taken out of the water. (船被人从水里拉出来了。)


### Q5 (正确答案：D)

![Page 96](images/listen_page_96.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) The bed is being made right now. (有人正在铺床。)
- (B) The window blinds have been drawn to keep the lights out. (窗帘被拉下来了，以便遮挡阳光。)
- (C) The television has been placed in the middle of the room. (电视机被放在房间的中间。)
- (D) The windows have been left unclosed. (窗户一直没关。)

**其他可能表达：**
- All the windows are open. (所有的窗户都开着。)
- Light is shining through the windows. (阳光透过窗户照进来。)
- The television has been placed in the corner of the room. (电视在房间的角落里。)


### Q6 (正确答案：D)

![Page 97](images/listen_page_97.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) She's preparing dinner for her family. (她在为家人准备晚餐。)
- (B) She's wiping off the kitchen counter. (她在擦洗厨房的操作台。)
- (C) She's washing some vegetables. (她在洗一些蔬菜。)
- (D) She's standing near the sink. (她站在水槽旁边。)

**其他可能表达：**
- She's working in the kitchen. (她正在厨房里干活。)
- She's standing at the kitchen sink. (她正站在厨房的水槽旁边。)
- She's washing her hands. (她正在洗手。)
- 注：在Part 1中，每道试题都添加了3种可能的正确表达方式，考生可
- 以了解对于同样的照片可能出现的不同表达。


## Part 2: 应答测试 (Q7 - Q31)

### Q7 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Do you know the person who was standing next to Mr. Thomson at the conference? (你认识会上站在汤普森先生旁边的那个人吗？)
- **A:** She's the new receptionist. (她是新来的接待员。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Who was that talking to Mr. Thompson at the conference? (会上和汤普森先生说话的人是谁？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) In an hour. (一个小时之后。)
  - (B) I'll go with you. (我会和你一起去。)
  - (C) Our new receptionist. (我们的新接待员。)


### Q8 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Where do I go to catch the bus that's coming in from Detroit? (我应该在哪儿等从底特律来的公交车？)
- **A:** Line up at Platform 7. (在7号站台排队。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Where does the bus to Detroit stop? (开往底特律的公交车停在哪里？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) At Platform 7. (在 7 号站台。)
  - (B) In ten minutes. (10 分钟后。)
  - (C) On a business trip. (出公差。)


### Q9 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** What type of car do you want to get? (你想买哪种汽车？)
- **A:** Something that's good on gas. (省油的汽车。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** What kind of car are you thinking of getting? (你想买哪种汽车？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I want something with good mileage. (我想买油耗低的车。)
  - (B) I didn't drive today. (我今天没开车。)
  - (C) No, I take the bus to work. (不，我乘公交车去上班的。)


### Q10 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Do you think I need to take my umbrella with me? (你觉得我需要带上雨伞吗？)
- **A:** You should. It's going to pour today. (你应该带。今天会下大雨。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Do you think I should pack my umbrella? (你认为我应该带上雨伞吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, I think he will do it. (是的，我认为他会这么做。)
  - (B) It is scheduled to stop soon. (按计划它就要停止了。)
  - (C) Yes, I heard rain is in the forecast. (是的，我听天气预报说有雨。)


### Q11 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Should we continue working until we finish this or get some lunch first? (我们应该继续把工作做完还是先吃午饭？)
- **A:** Why don't we finish what we are doing first? (我们为什么不先把手头的事做完呢？注：在Part 2中，为帮助考生提高听懂题目的能力，添加了和试题相同或相似的表达方法。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Should we finish what we're doing or go for lunch first? (我们是应该先做完手头的事，还是先去吃午饭？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) They're doing it now. (他们正在做这个。)
  - (B) Let's get this over with first. (让我们先做完这个吧。)
  - (C) Some sandwiches and drinks. (几块三明治，几杯饮料。)


### Q12 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** When do you think the delivery trucks will take off? (你认为送货车几点会出发？)
- **A:** Just after 9 o'clock. (—9点以后。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** When do you suppose the delivery trucks will leave? (你觉得送货车什么时候会出发？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) He's coming by bus. (他乘公交车来。)
  - (B) Probably before ten. (很可能在 10 点之前。)
  - (C) Sure, I will take it there. (当然，我会把它带到那儿。)


### Q13 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Let's just take my car to the Chinese place on Spadina Road. (咱们就坐我的车去斯帕迪纳路的中国饭店吧。)
- **A:** Sure, that sounds like a good idea. (好啊，这个主意听上去不错。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Why don't we drive to the new Chinese restaurant on Spadina Road? (我们为什么不开车去斯帕迪纳路上新开的那家中餐馆呢？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Sure, I've been craving Chinese food lately. (当然，我最近一直盼着吃中国菜呢。)
  - (B) Lunch with the rest of the staff members. (和其他同事一起吃午饭。)
  - (C) He lived in Hong Kong for a while. (他在香港住过一段时间。)


### Q14 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Where do I line up for tickets? (我在哪儿排队买票？)
- **A:** Window Number 5. (—5号窗口。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Where do I go to pick up the tickets? (我去哪儿取票？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Try that window over there. (去那边的窗口试试看。)
  - (B) Sure, I will pick you up at seven. (当然，我 7 点钟来接你。)
  - (C) You need to get up a little earlier. (你需要早一点儿起床。)


### Q15 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Aren't you in the mood to go to the art gallery after work today? (你今天下班后想去美术馆吗？)
- **A:** Sorry, I have to work overtime this evening. (抱歉，我今晚得加班。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Don't you feel like going over to the art gallery after work? (难道你不想下班后去美术馆吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, he teaches art for a living. (是的，他靠教美术谋生。)
  - (B) Yes, but I don't think I can tonight. (想去，但是我今晚去不了。)
  - (C) Okay, I could hang the picture in my room. (好的，我可以把这幅画挂在我的房间里。)


### Q16 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Who didn't attend this morning's meeting? (谁没来参加今天上午的会议？)
- **A:** Lynn is sick at home. (林恩生病在家。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Who didn't show up to this morning's meeting? (谁没来参加今天上午的会议？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Lynn called in sick this morning. (林恩今天一早打电话请病假了。)
  - (B) To show it to the client. (把它拿给客户看。)
  - (C) Yes, we signed the contract. (是的，我们签了合同。)


### Q17 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Your house is walking distance from the office, isn't it? (你家离单位只有几步路的距离，是吗？)
- **A:** Yes, I live a block away from here. (是的，我家离这儿只有一条街的距离。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** You walk to the office every morning, don't you? (你每天步行去上班，是吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Sorry, but he has not shown up to work yet. (抱歉，可是他还没来上班。)
  - (B) Yes, I live five minutes away from here. (是的，从这里到我住的地方只要 5 分钟。)
  - (C) Did you try calling him at home? (你试过给他家里打电话了吗？)


### Q18 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** I don't know why the phone is not ringing much today. (我不知道为什么今天的电话不多。)
- **A:** Let's wait and see. The ad we took out should take effect soon. (咱们等等看。我们发布的广告应该会很快见效的。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** I don't understand why we are not getting many calls today. (我不明白为什么今天电话不多。)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I didn't call him either. (我也没有给他打电话。)
  - (B) Give it some time. The ad only went out this morning. (等等看。广告今天早上才发布。)
  - (C) Why don't you study a little more? (你为什么不多学习一点儿？)


### Q19 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How about asking Mr. Harris to take us around the factory site? (让哈里斯先生带我们参观一下厂房好吗？)
- **A:** I'll call and ask him. (我会打电话问他的。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Why don't you ask Mr. Harris to give us a tour of the plant floor? (你为何不请哈里斯先生带我们参观一下厂房？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I'll make the necessary arrangements. (必要的话，我会安排的。)
  - (B) Yes, he gave me the ticket this morning. (是的，他今天上午把票给我了。)
  - (C) The factory supervisor is here now. (工厂的主管现在在这儿。)


### Q20 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Did you get a chance to meet the new designer? (你见到新来的设计师了吗？)
- **A:** Not yet. I've been too busy. (还没有。我一直特别忙。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Have you had a chance to say hello to our new designer? (你和我们的新设计师打过招呼了吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) She was recruited from another company. (她是从另一个公司招聘来的。)
  - (B) That's great. Thank you very much. (太好了。非常感谢。)
  - (C) No, but I would like to meet her. (没有，不过我很愿意见见她。)


### Q21 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Are you going to the picnic this weekend? (这周末你去野餐吗？)
- **A:** I don't have a way to get there. (我搭不到车。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** You are planning on going to the weekend picnic, aren't you? (你正计划周末去野餐，是吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) No, I will be going with Sarah instead. (不，我要和萨拉一起去。)
  - (B) That depends on if I can get a ride. (那要看我能不能搭到车。)
  - (C) Well, I could pick you up at ten. (哦，我可以 10 点去接你。)


### Q22 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** When are you coming? (你什么时候来？)
- **A:** I'll be there this Friday. (我这周五到那儿。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** When should I be expecting you? (你什么时候来？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) How's Friday for you? (星期五怎么样？)
  - (B) I should be there. (我会到那儿。)
  - (C) Yes, he is expecting you. (是的，他在等你。)


### Q23 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Ask the manager to draft a letter of recommendation for you. (请老板给你起草一封推荐信吧。)
- **A:** I already asked him. (我已经请他写了。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Why don't you ask the boss to write a letter of recommendation for you? (你为什么不让老板给你写一封推荐信？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) At the post office. (在邮局。)
  - (B) I already did. (我已经这么做了。)
  - (C) From a college friend. (从一个大学的朋友那里。)


### Q24 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Did you by chance see a bank machine near the hotel? (你有没有在宾馆附近见到银行取款机？)
- **A:** Yes, there is one at the corner. (见到了，拐角那儿有一个。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** You didn't happen to see a bank machine near this hotel, did you? (你没在这家宾馆附近看到银行取款机，是吧？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) There is one on the corner. (拐角处有一个。)
  - (B) No, it didn't happen that way. (不，事情不是那样的。)
  - (C) The machine is out of order. (机器出故障了。)


### Q25 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** When does the ticket expire? (票什么时候到期？)
- **A:** Take a look on the back of the ticket. (看一看票的背面。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** How long is the ticket valid for? (票的有效期到什么时候？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Check the expiration date. (查一下到期日。)
  - (B) It's valued at two dollars. (它的估价是两美元。)
  - (C) Not too much longer, I hope. (我希望不会太久。)


### Q26 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Do you have any idea why Ms. O'Brien booked her appointment on Monday? (你知道为什么欧布赖恩女士把见面日期定在周一吗？)
- **A:** She's planning to go away on Tuesday. (她计划周二走。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Do you know why Ms. O'Brien made her appointment for Monday? (你知道欧布赖恩女士为什么把会面定在周一吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I'll call to make a reservation. (我会打电话预约的。)
  - (B) She's leaving town on Tuesday. (她周二要去外地。)
  - (C) For three o'clock this afternoon. (今天下午 3 点。)


### Q27 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** There are many errors on this paper. (这份材料里有很多错误。)
- **A:** I'll ask John to proofread it again. (我会让约翰再校对一遍。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** There are far too many errors on this draft. (这份草案里的错误太多了。)
- **选项：**
  - (A) He mistakenly put it there. (他错把它放在那儿了。)
  - (B) Yes, it is a bit too far. (是的，有点儿太远了。)
  - (C) Let me get John to edit it again. (我让约翰把它再校订一遍吧。)


### Q28 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How would you like to join me for a cup of coffee after the meeting? (你想不想会后和我们一起喝杯咖啡？)
- **A:** Sure, I would like that very much. (当然，我非常愿意。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Would you care for a cup of coffee after the meeting? (你想在会后喝杯咖啡吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) No, I didn't meet him today. (不，我今天没见到他。)
  - (B) Yes, she does care about it. (是的，她确实关心这个。)
  - (C) Sure, that would be very nice. (当然，那太好了。)


### Q29 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Didn't she appear on the show before? (她以前没在这个演出中出场吗？)
- **A:** Yes, she came on the show last year. (出过场，她去年演过这个节目。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Hasn't she been on the show before? (她以前没参加过这个演出吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, about a year ago. (参加过，大约一年前。)
  - (B) Okay, I will show it to you later. (好的，我过一会儿拿给你看。)
  - (C) It will air this Tuesday. (这周二播出。)


### Q30 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** What's your number of vacation days this year? (今年你的假期有几天？)
- **A:** I believe it's two weeks. (我想是两周。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** How many paid vacation days do you get this year? (你今年有几天带薪假期？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) As far as I know, it's two weeks. (据我所知，有两周。)
  - (B) I will be going to Mexico for two weeks. (我会去墨西哥待两周。)
  - (C) Yes, I am thinking of doing that as well. (是的，我也正在考虑那样做。)


### Q31 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Today is the grand opening of our new branch office, isn't it? (今天是我们新的分公司盛大开业的日子，是吗？)
- **A:** Yes, and I have to be there soon. (是的，我一会儿得到那儿去。Questions 32 through 34 refer to the following conversation.W:Tom， isn't it about time that you should have heard something aboutyour promotion？（)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** The new branch office is scheduled to have its grand opening today, isn't it? (新的分公司定在今天盛大开业，是吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, and I have to leave soon to get there. (是的，我得马上到那儿去。)
  - (B) You shouldn't worry too much. It'll be all right. (你不应该太担心了。不会有事的。)
  - (C) They are not as big as we had hoped. (它们不像我们希望的那么大。)


## Part 3: 简短对话 (Q32 - Q70)

### Questions 32 - 34

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Tom, isn't it about time that you should have heard something about your promotion? (32) It's been a couple of weeks since the boss first mentioned it to you, hasn't it?
**M:** The announcement will be posted on the company notice board after lunch today. (33) I am starting to feel a bit nervous.
**W:** Yeah, I guess you would. But you know what? Don't worry too much. I am certain that you will get the position. I mean, realistically speaking, there isn't anyone in our office who can do the job that you do. (34)
**M:** You are too kind. Let's just hope that management feels the same way as you do.

**中文对照：**
> **W：**汤姆，到现在你应该已经听说你升职的消息了吧？自从经理第一次向你提起这件事，到现在已经有几周了，对吗？
> **M：**通知会在今天午饭后张贴在公司的公告栏上。我开始觉得有些紧张了。
> **W：**是的，我猜你也会紧张。但是你知道吗，别太担心了。我肯定你会得到这个职位的。我的意思是，实事求是地说，咱们办公室里没有谁能做得了你这份工作。
> **M：**你太好了。希望管理层和你想的一样。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **promotion**：升职
- **post**：张贴
- **notice board**：公告栏
- **nervous**：紧张的
- **position**：职位
- **realistically**：实际地，现实地
- **management**：管理人员
- **slack off**：松懈，偷懒

#### Q32 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What is the man waiting to hear? (男士在等着听什么消息？)
- (A) The result of his promotion. (他升职的结果。)
- (B) The date of his next business trip. (他下一次出差的日期。)
- (C) The announcement of his next job. (他下一份工作的通知。)
- (D) The location of his new office. (他新办公室的位置。)

#### Q33 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** How will the man hear about the news? (男士会从哪里得到消息？)
- (A) From his boss. (从他的老板那里。)
- (B) From a display board. (从公告栏。)
- (C) From the company newsletter. (从公司的通讯。)
- (D) From a phone call from his manager. (从他经理的电话那里。)

#### Q34 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What does the woman think of the man? (女士怎么看男士？)
- (A) He should get along with his boss better. (他应该更好地和他的老板相处。)
- (B) He has been slacking off lately. (他最近偷懒了。)
- (C) He is an excellent speaker. (他是一个出色的演讲者。)
- (D) He is good at what he does. (他很擅长他的工作。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **It's been a couple of weeks since ~ = It's been a few weeks since ~ = It's been several weeks since ~** (自从…已经有几个星期了。)
  - *例句：It's been a couple of weeks since you started working here.* (自从你来这儿工作已经有几个星期了。)
- **I am certain that you will get the position. = I am confident that you will get the job.** (我肯定你会得到这个职位。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：I am sure that you are going to be promoted.* (我确信你会升职的。)

### Questions 35 - 37

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Do you know why Ms. Sato called a meeting for 11? (36) I thought she was leaving for Chicago this morning.
**W:** She was, but she delayed her trip a couple of days. She apparently is not happy with the proposal we put together, and she said she couldn't possibly present that in Chicago today. (35) So, she called a meeting this morning to talk to us about it. Anyway, we'd better get going, or we are going to be late. It's almost eleven o'clock.
**M:** I hope the meeting will be short. I have to meet a client at 12:00 for lunch on the other side of town, and I have to leave the office by 11:30 at the latest. (37)
**W:** Well, I am sure that Ms. Sato will let you go early if you tell her about the situation before the meeting starts. (37)

**中文对照：**
> **M：**你知道佐藤女士为什么召集大家在11点开会吗？我原以为她今天上午要出发去芝加哥呢。
> **W：**她本来要去，但是她把行程推迟了几天。她显然对我们整理出来的提案不满意，还说她不可能今天去芝加哥提交这份提案。所以她今天上午召集开会，要和我们讨论这个提案。不管怎样，我们得走了，不然要迟到了。马上就11点了。
> **M：**我希望这个会议不会太长。我12点得到城那边和一个客户吃午饭，最晚11点半就得从办公室出发。
> **W：**哦，我肯定如果你开会前对佐藤女士讲明情况的话，她会让你早点儿走的。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **call a meeting**：举行会议，召集会议
- **delay**：推迟
- **apparently**：显然地
- **put together**：整理
- **present**：提交
- **get going**：出发，开始行动
- **at the latest**：最晚，最迟

#### Q35 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Why did Ms. Sato postpone her trip? (佐藤女士为什么推迟了出行？)
- (A) She was not satisfied with her presentation material. (她对提案材料不满意。)
- (B) She suddenly had to attend to other business. (她突然必须处理别的事情。)
- (C) She woke up late and missed her early flight. (她起晚了，错过了早班飞机。)
- (D) She could not get a plane ticket to Chicago. (她买不到去芝加哥的机票。)

#### Q36 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** When will the speakers attend the meeting? (讲话者将于几点参加会议？)
- (A) 10:00. (10 点。)
- (B) 11:00. (11 点。)
- (C) 11:30. (11 点半。)
- (D) 12:00. (12 点。)

#### Q37 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What will the man most likely do before the meeting? (开会前男士最有可能做什么？)
- (A) Call his client. (给他的客户打电话。)
- (B) Make a plane reservation. (预订机票。)
- (C) Speak to Ms. Sato. (和佐藤女士谈话。)
- (D) Make copies of the proposal. (复印提案。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **leave for Chicago = take off to Chicago = go to Chicago** (动身去芝加哥)
  - *例句：Our team members will be leaving for Chicago to attend a conference.* (我们团队成员将要去芝加哥参加一个会议。)
- **She delayed her trip a couple of days. = She put off her trip for a few days. = She postponed her trip a couple of days.** (她把出行推迟了几天。)
- **is not happy with ~ = is not satisfied with ~ = is not content with ~** (对…不满意)
  - *例句：She is not happy with her job.* (她对自己的工作不满意。)
- **I hope the meeting will be short. = I hope the meeting will end early. = I hope the meeting will not last long.** (我希望会议不会太长。)

### Questions 38 - 40

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Hi, my name is Sarah Ferguson, and I made a reservation for a non- smoking room with a view of the river for two nights. (38)
**M:** I'm terribly sorry, Ms. Ferguson, but our staff must have made a mistake (39) , because according to the information in the computer, your room is facing the park, not the river.
**W:** That's terrible. I was hoping to have a nice view of the river from my room. Oh well, I guess mistakes happen. I'll just take the room facing the park then.
**M:** Thank you. And to make up for our mistake, we would like to offer you a free dinner coupon for two at our hotel restaurant located on the basement floor. (40)

**中文对照：**
> **W：**你好，我是萨拉·弗格森，我预订了两晚无烟河景房。
> **M：**非常抱歉，弗格森女士，我们的工作人员一定是弄错了，因为根据电脑里的信息，您的房间是朝向公园的，不是河畔。
> **W：**那太糟糕了。我本来希望能从我的房间看到河畔的好景色。唉，好吧，应该是哪儿出错了吧。那我就要朝公园的房间吧。
> **M：**谢谢。为了弥补我们的过错，我们想向您提供一张我们宾馆餐厅的免费双人晚餐券，餐厅在地下一层。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **make a reservation**：预订
- **non-smoking room**：无烟房间
- **view**：景色
- **make a mistake**：出错
- **according to**：根据，按照
- **face**：面向，面对
- **make up for**：补偿，弥补
- **basement floor**：地下一层
- **riverside**：河畔

#### Q38 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Where are they? (他们在哪里？)
- (A) At a riverside. (在河畔。)
- (B) At a hotel. (在宾馆。)
- (C) At a restaurant. (在饭店。)
- (D) At a park. (在公园。)

#### Q39 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Why is the man apologizing to the woman? (男士为什么向女士道歉？)
- (A) He forgot to make a reservation. (他忘记预订了。)
- (B) One of his staff members made a mistake. (他的一个员工出了一点儿差错。)
- (C) He does not know how to use the computer. (他不知道怎么使用电脑。)
- (D) The restaurant is closed for business today. (餐厅今天停业。)

#### Q40 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the man offer the woman? (男士向女士提供了什么？)
- (A) A free meal coupon. (一张免费的餐券。)
- (B) A discount on the room. (房价打折。)
- (C) A walk in the park. (到公园散步。)
- (D) Internet access. (互联网接入。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I made a reservation for a non-smoking room. = I booked a non-smoking room. = I called in advance for a non-smoking room.** (我预订了一个无烟房间。)
- **make up for our mistake = compensate you for our mistake** (弥补我们的过错)
  - *例句：We are going to give you a 25% discount on your meal to make up for our mistake.* (为了弥补我们的过错，我们将给您的餐费打75折。)
- **a free dinner coupon for two = a complimentary dinner coupon for two people** (一张免费的双人晚餐券)
  - *例句：The room comes with a free dinner coupon for two at our hotel restaurant.* (这个房间附送一张我们饭店餐厅的免费两人晚餐券。)

### Questions 41 - 43

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Hey, David, I just dropped off my car to get an oil change at George's Garage, (41) and I didn't see your car there. Didn't you say that you were going to take your car in to get your winter tires put on this morning?
**M:** Oh, I didn't take my car there. I ended up taking it to another place.
**W:** Really? Why did you do that? I thought you said you were happy with the work they did to your car the last time you took it in.
**M:** I know, but I found a better and cheaper place near my apartment. (42) Plus, the mechanic that used to take care of my car at George's Garage doesn't work there anymore. He apparently started his own shop downtown somewhere. (43)

**中文对照：**
> **W：**嘿，戴维，我刚刚把车开到乔治修车行去换油了，我没在那儿看到你的车。你不是说要今天上午开车去装冬季轮胎吗？
> **M：**哦，我没把车开到那儿。我后来开到另一个地方了。
> **W：**是吗？为什么？我以为你说过你上次到那儿对他们的工作满意呢。
> **M：**我知道，但是我在我家附近发现一个更好更便宜的地方。另外，乔治修车行那个过去经常给我修车的机修工不在那儿干了。他显然是在城里某个地方自己开店了。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **garage**：修车行
- **end up**：结果
- **be happy with**：对满意
- **mechanic**：机修工，技工
- **take care of**：处理
- **apparently**：显然地，明显地

#### Q41 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** Why did the woman drop by George's Garage? (女士为什么去乔治修车行？)
- (A) To put on some new tires. (去装一些新轮胎。)
- (B) To talk to George. (去和乔治聊天。)
- (C) To take care of a bill. (去付账单。)
- (D) To get an oil change. (去换油。)

#### Q42 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Why did the man take his car somewhere else? (为什么男士把车送到别的地方去了？)
- (A) He was not happy with the service at George's Garage. (他对乔治修车行的服务不满意。)
- (B) He found a cheaper place close to his apartment. (他发现他家附近有一个更便宜的地方。)
- (C) The mechanic who took care of his car did a terrible job. (给他修车的机修工干得很糟糕。)
- (D) The woman had recommended another place to him. (女士向他推荐了另一个地方。)

#### Q43 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** According to the man, what happened to the mechanic he knows at George's Garage? (根据男士所说，他认识的那个乔治修车行的机修工后来怎么了？)
- (A) He got fired. (他被开除了。)
- (B) He was promoted. (他升职了。)
- (C) He started his own business. (他自己开店了。)
- (D) He went to work for another shop. (他去另一家店工作了。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I just dropped off my car. = I just left my car.** (我刚刚从我的车上下来。)
  - *例句：I just dropped off my car at my mom's place.* (我刚刚把车停在妈妈那儿了。)
- **He apparently started his own shop. = He apparently started his own business. = He apparently opened up his own place.** (他显然自己开店了。)

### Questions 44 - 46

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Marcia, would you be interested in switching shifts with me tomorrow?
**W:** Not particularly. I specifically requested the morning shift so that I could attend a concert in the evening. (44)
**M:** That's too bad. I need to finish by four to take my wife to the airport.
**W:** I'd love to help you out, but I've already got tickets, and they aren't refundable. You know, Tina mentioned that she's not busy tomorrow.
**M:** Really? I ought to talk to her in that case. (45) Do you happen to know where she is? (46)
**W:** She ran out to get a drink from the café downstairs. She should return here in twenty minutes. (46)

**中文对照：**
> **M：**玛西亚，你明天有兴趣和我换班吗？
> **W：**并不是特别想。我专门要求上早班，就是为了晚上去听音乐会。
> **M：**那太糟了。我需要在四点之前下班，然后送我妻子去机场。
> **W：**我很乐意帮你，但是我已经买了票，而且不能退。你知道，蒂娜说她明天不忙。
> **M：**真的吗？那样的话我应该和她谈谈。你知道她在哪儿吗？
> **W：**她跑到楼下的咖啡馆去喝东西了。应该会在二十分钟内回来。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **be interested in**：对感兴趣
- **switch shifts with sb**：与某人交换轮班
- **particularly**：特别，尤其
- **specifically**：特别地；明确地
- **request**：要求；请求
- **attend a concert**：听音乐会
- **refundable**：可退费的；可偿还的
- **mention**：提到；说起

#### Q44 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the woman say she is going to do tomorrow evening? (女士说她明天晚上要做什么？)
- (A) Going to the airport. (去机场。)
- (B) Meeting a family member. (去见家人。)
- (C) Going to see a concert. (去听音乐会。)
- (D) Working in the evening. (去工作。)

#### Q45 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the woman imply when she says, “Tina mentioned that she's not busy tomorrow”? (当女士说 “ 蒂娜说她明天不忙 ” 时暗含的是什么意思？)
- (A) Tina needs a new work assignment. (蒂娜需要一项新的工作任务。)
- (B) She has been working on a project with Tina. (她一直在和蒂娜一起做项目。)
- (C) The man should ask Tina for help. (男士应该向蒂娜寻求帮助。)
- (D) The office will be closed tomorrow. (明天办公室会关门。)

#### Q46 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What will the man most likely do next? (男士下一步很可能会做什么？)
- (A) Wait for a colleague to return. (等待一位同事回来。)
- (B) Call Tina on his phone. (给蒂娜打电话。)
- (C) Go to a café with the woman. (和女士一起去咖啡馆。)
- (D) Take a short break. (休息一小会儿。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **take sb. to the airport = accompany sb. to the airport** (送某人去机场)
  - *例句：John took us to the airport.* (约翰把我们送到飞机场。)
- **I'd love to do sth. = I'd like to do sth.** (我很乐意做…)
  - *例句：I'd love to buy some apples.* (我想买一些苹果。)
- **ought to do sth. = should do sth.** (应该做某事)
  - *例句：You ought to work harder.* (你工作应该再努力一些。)

### Questions 47 - 49

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** The copier has been on the blink for a few days. （ 48,49 ） I called you guys last week to come and take a look. (47) What took you so long?
**M:** I'm terribly sorry, but some of our technicians have suddenly come down with terrible colds, and I have been terribly busy running around. (48) Anyway, did you check and see if any paper is jammed inside? (49)
**W:** Yes, that's the first thing I did, and that's not the problem. And it's not the toner either. I'm afraid the problem may be more serious. (49)
**M:** All right. Let me take a look and see what the problem is.

**中文对照：**
> **W：**这个复印机坏了好几天了。我上周给你们打过电话，叫你们来看一下。怎么现在才来？
> **M：**非常抱歉，我们有几个技术员突然得重感冒病倒了，我一直忙着东奔西跑。不管怎样，你检查过吗？是不是有纸卡在里面了？
> **W：**是的，我首先检查的就是这个，但是问题不在这儿。也不是墨粉的问题。我觉得问题可能更严重。
> **M：**好吧，我看一看是什么问题。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **on the blink**：（机器）出毛病，坏了
- **technician**：技术员
- **come down with**：因为病倒了
- **cold**：感冒
- **jam**：卡住
- **serious**：严重的
- **take a look**：看一看

#### Q47 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** When did the woman first make the call? (女士最早是在什么时候打的电话？)
- (A) Last week. (上周。)
- (B) A few days ago. (几天前。)
- (C) Yesterday. (昨天。)
- (D) Today. (今天。)

#### Q48 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Who most likely is the man? (男士最有可能是谁？)
- (A) A doctor. (医生。)
- (B) A weather reporter. (天气预报员。)
- (C) A photocopier technician. (复印机维修员。)
- (D) A newspaper employee. (报社员工。)

#### Q49 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What is the problem? (问题是什么？)
- (A) The weather has suddenly gotten very cold. (天气突然变得特别冷。)
- (B) The man has come down with a cold. (男士因为感冒病倒了。)
- (C) Some important papers are missing. (几份重要的文件丢了。)
- (D) The copier is not working properly. (复印机不能正常工作了。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **The copier has been on the blink. = The photocopy machine is broken. = The copy machine is not working.** (复印机坏了。)
- **come down with terrible colds = catch bad colds** (患感冒病倒了)
  - *例句：Many of the guys didn't show up because they have suddenly come down with terrible colds.* (好几个人没来，因为他们突然得重感冒病倒了。)
- **run around = go around** (奔忙)
  - *例句：I'm going to be busy running around tomorrow.* (我明天要东奔西跑了。)
- **be jammed = be stuck = be clogged** (堵住，卡住)
  - *例句：The water pipe is jammed right now.* (水管现在堵住了。)

### Questions 50 - 52

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Jason, what are you planning to do this evening? Some of us are going to see a movie together. (50)
**M:** I've got tickets to see a baseball game tonight. (50)
**W:** Oh, that sounds like a lot of fun. I hope you enjoy it. By the way, have you finished the report yet?
**M:** I've written everything and checked it for mistakes, but I need to insert a couple of graphs. I should be done with that in ten minutes. (51)
**W:** Great. Would you e-mail me a copy when you're finished, please? (52)
**M:** Of course. That's not a problem at all.

**中文对照：**
> **W：**杰森，你今晚打算做什么？我们几个人打算一起去看电影。
> **M：**我有今晚棒球赛的票。
> **W：**哦，听起来很有趣。希望你玩得愉快。顺便问一下，你的报告完成了吗？
> **M：**我写好了所有东西并检查了错误，但是我需要插入一些图表，应该十分钟内就能做完。
> **W：**太好了。你写完后发到我邮箱一份好吗？
> **M：**当然可以。完全没问题。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **plan to do sth**：计划做某事
- **be going to**：将要；打算
- **baseball game**：棒球比赛
- **by the way**：顺便问一下
- **check**：检查；选中
- **yet**：仍然；然而
- **insert**：插入；嵌入
- **not ... at all**：一点也不；别客气
- **a couple of**：三两个；一对

#### Q50 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Why does the man say, “I've got tickets to see a baseball game tonight”? (男士为什么说 “ 我有今晚棒球赛的票 ” ？)
- (A) To request some time off from work. (要求休息一段时间。)
- (B) To turn down an invitation. (拒绝邀请。)
- (C) To ask the woman to go with him. (邀请女士和他一起去。)
- (D) To explain why he is leaving early. (解释他为什么要提前离开。)

#### Q51 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the man suggest about the report? (关于这份报告男士有什么暗示？)
- (A) It is nearly finished. (快完成了。)
- (B) He wrote it with a co-worker. (他和一位同事一起写的。)
- (C) It is several pages long. (它有好几页。)
- (D) He needs some help with it. (他需要一些帮助。)

#### Q52 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What does the woman ask the man to do? (女士让男士做什么？)
- (A) E-mail her the updated budget. (把更新后的预算发到她邮箱。)
- (B) Begin working on a new project. (开始做一个新项目。)
- (C) Speak to someone in the Graphics Department. (与制图部门的人交谈。)
- (D) Send her a copy of a completed assignment. (把完成后的作业发一份到她邮箱。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **be going to = will** (将要)
  - *例句：We are going to the cinema tonight.* (我们今晚打算去看电影。)
- **That sounds like a lot of fun. = That sounds like so much fun.** (听起来很有趣。)
  - *例句：Wow! That sounds like a lot of fun. I'm sorry I missed it.* (哇，听起来很有趣。真是遗憾，我错过了。)

### Questions 53 - 55

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** I noticed you walking out of the subway station this morning (53) when I was driving to work. Where is your car?
**M:** Oh, I left it at home. I've decided to take the subway to work from today (53) because I can't afford to drive it every day.
**W:** I know what you mean. The prices of gas and parking are way too high these days. And insurance, that's another story. In fact, it's so bad that I have been seriously thinking of selling my car. (54)
**M:** Well, you should think about taking the subway to work too (55) then, because it's not as bad as you think it is. In fact, I kind of enjoy reading the paper and not having to worry about driving.

**中文对照：**
> **W：**今天早晨我开车上班时看到你从地铁站出来。你的车呢？
> **M：**噢，我把它放家里了。我已经决定从今天开始乘地铁上班了，因为每天开车我负担不起了。
> **W：**我明白你的意思。最近油价和停车费都太贵了，而且保险也是个问题。实际上，情况太糟了，我一直在认真地考虑要不要把车卖了。
> **M：**那么，你应该也考虑一下乘地铁上班，因为乘地铁并不像你想像的那么糟糕。其实，我有点儿喜欢上在地铁里读报纸的感觉了，而且不用为开车担心。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **notice**：注意到
- **drive to work**：开车上班
- **take the subway**：乘地铁
- **afford**：买得起
- **insurance**：保险
- **seriously**：认真地，严肃地
- **get rid of**：摆脱

#### Q53 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** How did the man get to work this morning? (男士今天早上怎么去上班的？)
- (A) He drove his car. (他开车去的。)
- (B) He took public transportation. (他乘坐公共交通工具去的。)
- (C) He got a ride with a co-worker. (他搭同事的车去的。)
- (D) He walked. (他步行去的。)

#### Q54 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What has the woman been thinking of doing? (女士一直在考虑什么？)
- (A) Taking the bus to work. (乘公交车上班。)
- (B) Getting rid of her car. (把她的车处理掉。)
- (C) Catch up on her reading. (把落下的书读完。)
- (D) Changing her insurance company. (换一家保险公司。)

#### Q55 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the man mean when he says, “because it's not as bad as you think it is”? (男士说 “ 因为乘地铁并不像你想象的那么糟糕 ” ，是想表达什么意思？)
- (A) The woman should sell her car. (女士应该卖掉她的车。)
- (B) The woman should take the subway. (女士应该乘坐地铁。)
- (C) The woman should read more books. (女士应该读更多的书。)
- (D) The woman should buy more insurance. (女士应该买更多的保险。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I noticed you walking out of the subway station. = I saw you walking out of the subway station.** (我看到你从地铁站走出来。)
- **I can't afford to drive it every day. = It costs too much to drive my car every day. = It is too expensive to bring my car every day.** (每天开车我负担不起。)
- **I know what you mean. = I understand you.** (我明白你的意思。)

### Questions 56 - 58

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Mr. Sanchez is coming in to take a look around our factory (57) to see if it's big enough to suit his demands. If he is satisfied, there is a good chance that he will sign a deal with us today. (56)
**W:** I really hope that will happen. The business this deal will bring is huge. Let's just keep our fingers crossed.
**M:** Don't worry too much. I'm sure we will get it. After all, we have everything he requested over the phone. Anyway, let's take off a bit early to pick him up at the airport. (58)
**W:** That sounds like a good idea. We don't want to get stuck in rush hour traffic and be late for his arrival. (58)

**中文对照：**
> **M：**桑切斯先生要来参观我们的工厂，看一看工厂的规模是不是符合他的需求。如果他满意，今天我们就有机会和他签下一份合同。
> **W：**真希望能那样。这次交易是一笔大生意，但愿我们能成功。
> **M：**别太担心了，我们肯定会得到的。毕竟他在电话中要求的一切我们都有。不管怎样，我们还是早点儿出发去机场接他吧。
> **W：**听起来是个好主意。我们别赶上高峰时间堵车，免得迟到。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **take a look**：看一看，参观
- **suit one's demands**：符合某人的需求
- **demand**：需要，需求
- **be satisfied**：满意
- **keep one's fingers crossed**：祝好运，祝成功
- **pick up**：接（机）
- **get stuck in traffic**：堵车
- **rush hour**：交通的高峰时间

#### Q56 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What are they discussing? (他们在讨论什么？)
- (A) Problems at their factory. (他们工厂的问题。)
- (B) One of their loyal customers. (他们的一位忠实客户。)
- (C) The possibility of a big deal. (一笔大生意的可能性。)
- (D) Their upcoming business trip. (他们近期的一次商务旅行。)

#### Q57 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Why is Mr. Sanchez coming? (桑切斯先生为什么要来？)
- (A) To check out the plant. (查看工厂。)
- (B) To present a deal. (谈合作。)
- (C) To make a sale. (出售商品。)
- (D) To give a speech. (做演讲。)

#### Q58 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Why does the man want to take off early? (为什么男士要早走？)
- (A) To avoid heavy traffic. (避开拥挤的交通。)
- (B) To catch an early flight. (赶一趟早班飞机。)
- (C) To meet a client at the factory. (到工厂见一个客户。)
- (D) To close a deal. (完成一笔交易。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **if he is satisfied = if he is content = if he is happy with it** (如果他满意的话)
  - *例句：If he is satisfied, he will come back again.* (如果他满意，他会再回来的。)
- **He will sign a deal. = He will agree to a deal. = He will consent to a deal.** (他会签下一份合同。)
- **Let's just keep our fingers crossed. = Let's just hope for the best. = Let's just wait and hope that everything will be okay.** (但愿我们能成功。)

### Questions 59 - 61

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W1:** Have you submitted your nomination for the employee of the quarter? (59) It's due by 5:00 today.
**M:** Thanks for the reminder. I've been so busy these days. Who did you nominate? (60)
**W1:** I thought Kevin Schroeder did a great job during the past couple of months. (59)
**W2:** You can say that again, Lisa. He managed to bring in several new clients, four of whom are from Europe. (61)
**M:** I had no idea he was doing such a great job. Isn't he relatively new?
**W1:** Not really. He's been employed here for three years, but he's rarely in the office, so that's why you don't see him too often.

**中文对照：**
> **W1：**你提交本季度的员工推荐表了吗？截止时间到今天5点。
> **M：**谢谢提醒。这些天我实在是太忙了。你推荐的是谁？
> **W1：**我认为在过去的几个月，凯文·施罗德工作很出色。
> **W2：**你说的没错，丽萨。他成功地引进了几位新客户，其中有四位来自欧洲。
> **M：**没想到他工作这么出色。他不是刚来不久吗？
> **W1：**其实不算是。他在这里已经工作三年了。但是他很少在办公室，所以你才没有经常见到他。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **submit**：提交，呈递
- **nomination**：推荐，提名
- **quarter**：季度
- **reminder**：提醒
- **relatively**：相对地
- **rarely**：很少

#### Q59 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What are the speakers mainly discussing? (讲话者们主要在讨论什么？)
- (A) An award winner. (一位获奖者。)
- (B) A new contract. (一份新合同。)
- (C) One of their co-workers. (他们的一位同事。)
- (D) Their European branch. (他们的欧洲分部。)

#### Q60 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What does the man imply when he says, “Thanks for the reminder”? (当这位男士说 “ 谢谢提醒 ” 时，是在暗指什么？)
- (A) He forgot about an upcoming meeting. (他忘记了即将召开的会议。)
- (B) He has not asked Lisa a question yet. (他还没有问丽萨一个问题。)
- (C) He needs to speak with his boss soon. (他需要尽快和老板谈一谈。)
- (D) He has not nominated anyone for an award. (他还没有提名任何一位获奖人员。)

#### Q61 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What is suggested about Kevin Schroeder? (关于凯文)
- (A) He is planning to resign from his job.
- (B) He works in the Sales Department.
- (C) He is the man's supervisor.
- (D) He is transferring to a branch in Europe.

**延伸表达与补充：**
  - *例句：A B C D* (）他计划从他的工作岗位辞职。（）他在销售部门工作。（）他是这位男士的主管。（）他将调任到欧洲分部。)
- **You can say that again, Lisa. = You are right, Lisa.** (你说得没错，丽萨。)
- **manage to do sth.** (设法做成，努力完成（困难的事）)
  - *例句：I finally managed to push the huge animal away.* (我们最后终于把这个庞大的动物推走了。)
- **bring in** (吸引（顾客）)
  - *例句：We've got to bring in more business if we want the restaurant to survive.* (餐馆若要生存下去，我们必须招徕更多的生意。)

### Questions 62 - 64

![Page 103](images/listen_page_103.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** That workshop conducted by Matthew Carter was outstanding. I'm glad we decided to attend it.
**W:** I couldn't agree more. So what are your plans for the remainder of the day?
**M:** The only other event I'm interested in attending starts at 1:30. (62) It should be pretty interesting.
**W:** You're not staying for the speech being given at 4:00?
**M:** I'd love to listen to Andrea Warner talk, but I've got to catch a plane to Dublin this evening. (63) Anyway, why don't we have lunch together and then return to the convention center?
**W:** Sounds good. We can discuss a couple of those ideas for projects you mentioned on the phone last week. (64) Afternoon Events

**中文对照：**
> **M：**马修·卡特主持的研讨会非常出色。我很高兴我们来参加了。
> **W：**我非常同意。那么你今天剩下的时间有什么计划？
> **M：**我唯一感兴趣的另一个活动是在1点半开始。这个活动应该很有趣。
> **W：**你不准备留下来听4点的演讲吗？
> **M：**我很想去听安德里亚·华纳的演讲，但是我今晚要赶飞机去都柏林。不管怎样，我们一起吃午饭，然后再回会议中心怎么样？
> **W：**听起来不错。我们可以讨论一下你上周在电话里提到的几个想法。下午活动

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **workshop**：研讨会
- **conduct**：组织并实施
- **outstanding**：出色的
- **remainder**：剩余部分
- **pretty**：相当地
- **convention center**：会议中心
- **project**：项目

#### Q62 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Which speaker's talk will the man attend? (请看图表。男士将参加哪位发言人的演讲？)
- (A) Sam Popov's. (山姆 · 波波夫的演讲。)
- (B) Irene Chang's. (艾琳 · 常的演讲。)
- (C) Rusty Meadows's. (鲁斯蒂 · 梅多斯的演讲。)
- (D) Andrea Warner's. (安德烈亚 · 沃纳的演讲。)

#### Q63 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What will the man do in the evening? (男士晚上将要做什么？)
- (A) Take a flight. (乘飞机。)
- (B) Return to his home. (回家。)
- (C) Ride on a train. (乘火车。)
- (D) Meet a potential client. (会见潜在客户。)

#### Q64 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the woman suggest doing? (女士建议做什么？)
- (A) Ordering food for lunch. (订午餐。)
- (B) Talking to a guest speaker. (与客座发言人交谈。)
- (C) Discussing some work matters. (讨论一些工作事项。)
- (D) Sharing the notes they took. (分享他们的笔记。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **be interested in = take an interest in** (对…感兴趣)
  - *例句：I'm interested in playing football.* (我喜欢踢足球。)
- **catch a cab = take a taxi** (乘出租车)
  - *例句：It is very hard to catch a cab in the rush hour in this city.* (这座城市在高峰时间很难打到出租车。)
- **Why don't you do = Why not do** (为什么不做…？)
  - *例句：Why don't you do some exercise to lose weight?* (你为什么不通过锻炼减肥呢？)
- **a couple of = several** (几个)
  - *例句：I've got a couple of questions to ask you.* (我有几个问题想要问你。)

### Questions 65 - 67

![Page 104](images/listen_page_104.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Before we board our plane, do you mind if we do some shopping at the duty-free stores? I need to buy some souvenirs for my friends. (65)
**M:** Be my guest. But I've got to head to the gate to speak with somebody there. Take a look at my boarding pass.
**W:** Oh, I can't believe one of the letters in Thomas is missing. (66)
**M:** Yeah, I want to make sure there aren't any problems when it's time to board. Where shall we meet when I'm done?
**W:** How about at that coffee shop over there? After I finish shopping, I'd like something to drink. (67)
**M:** Great. I'll see you in a few minutes. Boarding Pass

**中文对照：**
> **W：**在登机前，你介意我们去免税店买点东西吗？我需要给我的朋友买一些纪念品。
> **M：**请自便。但是我需要去登机口跟那里的人谈谈。你看一下我的登机牌。
> **W：**哦，我简直不敢相信“Thomas”竟然丢了一个字母。
> **M：**是的，我想确保登机时没有任何问题。我完事之后我们在哪里见面呢？
> **W：**在那边的咖啡店如何？我买完东西之后想喝些东西。
> **M：**好的。几分钟之后见。登机牌

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **board the plane**：登机
- **duty-free store**：免税店
- **souvenir**：纪念品
- **be my guest**：请自便
- **boarding pass**：登机牌

#### Q65 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the woman want to do next? (女士接下来想做什么？)
- (A) Get her boarding pass. (取登机牌。)
- (B) Check her luggage. (检查行李。)
- (C) Purchase some items. (买一些东西。)
- (D) Speak with a gate attendant. (和登机口的服务员谈谈。)

#### Q66 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Which information is incorrect? (请看图表。下列哪项信息是不正确的？)
- (A) Name. (姓名。)
- (B) Flight number. (航班号。)
- (C) Departure time. (出发时间。)
- (D) Gate. (登机口。)

#### Q67 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Where will the speakers meet? (说话人要在哪里见面？)
- (A) At a gate. (在登机口。)
- (B) At a coffee shop. (在咖啡店。)
- (C) At a duty-free store. (在免税店。)
- (D) At a restaurant. (在餐厅。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **buy sth. for sb. = buy sb. sth.** (给某人买某物)
  - *例句：I want to buy a coat for my mother as her birthday present.* (我想给我妈妈买一件大衣作为她的生日礼物。)
- **Be my guest. = Help yourself.** (请自便。)
  - *例句：If anyone wants to use my apartment during the summer, be my guest.* (如果有人想在暑假住我的公寓，请自便吧。)
- **How about doing = What about doing** (做某事如何？)
  - *例句：How about having lunch after the meeting is over?* (会议结束后一起吃午饭如何？)
- **in a few minutes = a few minutes later** (几分钟之后)
  - *例句：I'll be back in a few minutes.* (我几分钟之后就回来。)

### Questions 68 - 70

![Page 105](images/listen_page_105.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Have we made arrangements to reschedule last week's outdoor concert which was canceled due to rain? (68)
**W:** I was informed by Travis Donovan that it will be held next Tuesday at 6:00 in the evening.
**M:** Are you positive? I want to print some posters to advertise it and don't want to get the date wrong. (69)
**W:** Why don't you call Mr. Donovan at extension 584 and confirm it with him?
**M:** Thanks for the number. But I have to wait to call him because I just saw him leave the office with a client. (70)
**W:** Oh, I wasn't aware he had any meetings scheduled for today. Last Week's Weather Forecast

**中文对照：**
> **M：**上周由于下雨而取消的户外演唱会是否已经重新做了安排？
> **W：**特拉维斯·多诺万通知我说演唱会将于下周二晚上6点举行。
> **M：**你确定吗？我想印一些海报来做宣传，所以我不想弄错时间。
> **W：**你为什么不打多诺万先生的分机号584去和他确认一下呢？
> **M：**谢谢你告诉我他的号码。但是我必须得等一会才能给他打电话，因为我刚看见他和一位客户离开了办公室。
> **W：**哦，我还没注意到他今天有什么会议安排。上周的天气预报

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **arrangement**：安排
- **cancel**：取消
- **inform**：通知
- **positive**：确定的
- **poster**：海报
- **extension**：电话分机
- **confirm**：确认
- **aware**：知道的

#### Q68 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. When was the concert originally scheduled for? (请看图表，音乐会原计划什么时候举办？)
- (A) Monday. (星期一。)
- (B) Tuesday. (星期二。)
- (C) Wednesday. (星期三。)
- (D) Thursday. (星期四。)

#### Q69 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Why does the man want to know the new date of the concert? (为什么男士想要知道演唱会新的日期？)
- (A) To inform the ticket holders. (为了通知观众。)
- (B) To update an Internet advertisement. (为了更新网络广告。)
- (C) To make some posters. (为了制作一些海报。)
- (D) To confirm with the venue owner. (为了与场馆业主确认。)

#### Q70 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the man say about Mr. Donovan? (关于多诺万先生，男士说了什么？)
- (A) He will perform at the concert. (他将在演唱会演出。)
- (B) He is out of the office. (他现在不在办公室。)
- (C) He is on the phone with a client. (他正在和一位客户打电话。)
- (D) He is in his office. (他在办公室。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **due to = because of** (因为，由于)
  - *例句：I asked a leave due to illness.* (我因为生病请假了。)
- **be aware = know** (知道)
  - *例句：Everyone is aware that smoking is harmful to health.* (每个人都知道吸烟有害健康。)

## Part 4: 简短独白 (Q71 - Q100)

### Questions 71 - 73

![Page 105](images/listen_page_105.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Attention, all warehouse staff. This is an important notice, so please listen carefully. As you all know, Friday is the day of the big move. (71) Packing will begin on Thursday morning, and the movers will arrive at eight o'clock Friday morning. We strongly advise you to remove your personal belongings no later than Wednesday night. (72) If you don't, there is a good chance they will be lost or damaged in the move. Please arrive by seven o'clock tomorrow morning, dressed in comfortable clothes. I know Thursday and Friday will be long and busy days, but an excellent lunch will be provided for all of you, (73) and there will be a special “housewarming” party on the following Monday night.

**中文对照：**
> 库房全体工作人员请注意，现在宣布一条重要通知，请仔细听。大家都知道，周五那天要搬家。打包工作从周四上午开始，搬运工人会在周五早上8点到。我们强烈建议大家在周三晚上之前取走个人物品，否则物品很可能在搬家过程中丢失或损坏。请大家明天早上7点之前到库房，穿上舒适的衣服。我知道周四和周五会漫长而繁忙，不过我们会给大家提供丰盛的午餐，而且在下周一晚上还会专门举行一个乔迁晚宴。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **warehouse**：库房，仓库
- **notice**：通知
- **carefully**：仔细地
- **move**：搬家
- **mover**：搬运工人
- **personal**：个人的，私人的
- **belongings**：所有物，财产
- **no later than**：不迟于
- **damage**：损坏
- **comfortable**：舒适的
- **housewarming**：乔迁庆宴
- **following**：接着的
- **formally**：正式地
- **occasion**：场合

#### Q71 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** When will the move take place? (搬家安排在什么时候？)
- (A) Wednesday. (周三。)
- (B) Thursday. (周四。)
- (C) Friday. (周五。)
- (D) Monday. (周一。)

#### Q72 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the speaker recommend the listeners do? (讲话者建议听众做什么？)
- (A) Show up an hour earlier than the movers. (比搬运工人早一个小时到。)
- (B) Pack away their personal goods. (把个人物品打包拿走。)
- (C) Help look for some lost items. (帮忙寻找几件丢失的物品。)
- (D) Dress formally for the occasion. (穿正装。)

#### Q73 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What will be provided to the listeners on the day of the move? (搬家那天会向听众提供什么？)
- (A) A free meal. (免费餐食。)
- (B) Extra pay. (额外的报酬。)
- (C) A ride home. (开车送他们回家。)
- (D) A party. (宴会。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **Friday is the day of the big move. = We will move on Friday. = The moving date is Friday.** (搬家的日子是在周五。)
- **no later than Wednesday night = before Wednesday night = Wednesday night is the deadline** (周三晚上之前)
  - *例句：You have to finish this report no later than Wednesday night.* (你必须在周三晚上之前完成这个报告。)
- **dressed in comfortable clothes** (穿上舒适的衣服扩展表达：)
  - *例句：dressed in casual wear dressed in your normal, everyday wear Mr. King was dressed in comfortable clothes at the company picnic.* (穿上便装穿日常的普通服装金先生参加公司的野餐时穿了舒适的衣服。)

### Questions 74 - 76

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Hi, this is Sharon Star calling. I tried several times to get through to you at the cell number you gave me, but it has been busy for the last twenty minutes. Anyway, Mr. Trent, I hope you get this message. I'd like to say I'm sorry, but I won't be able to get to the interview on time. We'll have to make it some other time. (74) Unfortunately, there's been a major accident on St. Kilda Road, and traffic is at a complete standstill. There is absolutely no chance of me making it this afternoon. (75) I hope this won't be a major inconvenience to you. I'm available for an interview any time tomorrow or even this evening if you have the time. (76) Let me give you my mobile phone number again. It's 777-0045. Thanks.

**中文对照：**
> 您好，我是莎伦·斯塔尔。我按照您给我的号码给您打了几次电话，但是打了20分钟一直占线。不管怎样，特伦特先生，希望您能收到这条留言。我想说很抱歉，我不能按时参加面试了。我们得换个时间。很遗憾，希尔达路上发生了一起重大交通事故，交通完全瘫痪了。我今天下午根本不可能到那儿。希望这不会给您造成很大的不便。如果您有时间的话，明天的任何时间或者即使今天晚上我都可以参加面试。我把我的手机号码再告诉您一遍，是777-0045。谢谢。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **get through to**：与联系，通电话
- **on time**：按时
- **unfortunately**：不走运地，不巧地
- **major**：重要的
- **standstill**：停滞
- **absolutely**：完全地
- **inconvenience**：不便
- **available**：有空的
- **report**：报告

#### Q74 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Why is the speaker leaving the message? (讲话者为什么留言？)
- (A) To postpone her appointment. (推迟会面。)
- (B) To set up a job interview. (约定一个工作面试。)
- (C) To report an accident on the road. (报告路上的一起交通事故。)
- (D) To get the number of a co-worker. (要一位同事的电话号码。)

#### Q75 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** Where most likely is the caller now? (打电话的人现在最有可能在哪儿？)
- (A) At her office. (在她的办公室。)
- (B) On the subway. (在地铁里。)
- (C) At a hospital. (在医院。)
- (D) In her car. (在她的汽车里。)

#### Q76 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** When does the caller say that she will be available? (打电话的人说她什么时间有空？)
- (A) Right now. (现在。)
- (B) This evening. (今天晚上。)
- (C) Next week. (下周。)
- (D) This weekend. (这周末。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I tried several times to get through to you. = I called you many times. = I tried phoning you a few times.** (我给您打了几次电话。)
  - *例句：I tried several times to get through to you the other night, but you didn't answer your phone.* (我前几天晚上给您打了几次电话，但是您都没有接。)
- **We'll have to make it some other time.** (我们得换个时间。)
  - *例句：I'm going to have to put it off for another day. I have no choice but to see you another time.* (我不得不将其推迟到其他时间。扩展表达：我只好换个时间再跟您见面了。)
- **Traffic is at a complete standstill. = Traffic is not moving at all. = Traffic is backed up for miles.** (交通完全瘫痪了。)

### Questions 77 - 79

**听力独白/对话原文：**
You have called Academic Enterprises, Australia's leading providers of school and home-based educational programs and materials. (77) Unfortunately, all of our operators are occupied at the present. We value your call, so please wait, and one of our staff members will speak to you shortly. If your inquiry has to do with Academic Enterprises' after-school or vacation educational programs, please press “1”; if you have an inquiry regarding the availability of textbooks or other educational materials, please press “2”. For packaging, dispatch, or billing inquiries, please press “3”. (78) For franchising inquiries, please press “4”. Or simply hold, and one of our operators will be with you as soon as possible. (79)

**中文对照：**
> 欢迎致电澳大利亚一流的学校和家庭教育课程和教材供应商学术公司。很不巧，我们所有的接线员都在通话中。您的来电对我们来说很重要，请稍候，我们的工作人员很快会和您通话。如果您想咨询我公司的课外或假期教育课程，请按“1”；如果您想咨询课本或其他教材的供应情况，请按“2”；关于包装、送货或付款的咨询，请按“3”；关于特许经营的咨询，请按“4”。或者您可以稍候，我们的接线员会尽快和您通话。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **leading**：领导的，主要的
- **provider**：供应商
- **home-based**：基于家庭的，在家的
- **educational**：教育的
- **operator**：接线员
- **occupy**：使从事，使忙碌
- **value**：重视
- **shortly**：很快地
- **inquiry**：询问，打听
- **after-school**：课后的
- **textbook**：课本
- **dispatch**：派送
- **franchise**：特许经营

#### Q77 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does Academic Enterprises provide? (学术公司提供什么？)
- (A) Educational books. (教育类图书。)
- (B) Free consultations. (免费咨询。)
- (C) Free delivery services. (免费送货服务。)
- (D) Training classes. (培训课程。)

#### Q78 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What should a caller with a question about a delivery do? (如果想打电话咨询送货方面的问题，问询人应该怎么做？)
- (A) Press 1. (按 1 。)
- (B) Press 2. (按 2 。)
- (C) Press 3. (按 3 。)
- (D) Press 4. (按 4 。)

#### Q79 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Who should wait on the line? (谁应该在线等待？)
- (A) Those who are already customers. (那些已经成为顾客的人。)
- (B) Those who do not want to deal with a machine. (那些不想和机器打交道的人。)
- (C) Those who don't have touch-tone phones. (那些没有按键式电话的人。)
- (D) Those who do not know the extension number. (那些不知道分机号的人。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **All of our operators are occupied at the present. = All of our operators are on the phone now. = Every one of our operators is on the line at the moment.** (我们所有的接线员现在都在通话中。)
- **We value your call. = Your call is important to us.** (您的来电对我们来说很重要。)
- **Our staff member will speak to you shortly. = Our staff will talk to you as soon as possible. = Our staff will be right with you.** (我们的工作人员很快会和您通话。)

### Questions 80 - 82

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Good evening. Perhaps some of you don't know me. I'm Dr. Cummins, the principal of St. Michael's Elementary School. （ 80, 81 ） It's a great pleasure to welcome you to tonight's special performance. I hope that you, like me, will be overwhelmed by the sheer talent and enthusiasm of our young break dancers. I have personally attended three of the rehearsals, so I can assure you that they have sacrificed hours of personal time and buckets of sweat to bring you this exciting production. (82) This is a group production, choreographed by the performers themselves, with the help of our wonderful musical arts teacher, Ms. Wang. So, without further ado, sit back, and enjoy our fabulous young dancers.

**中文对照：**
> 晚上好。也许你们中有些人不认识我，我是卡明斯博士，圣米歇尔小学的校长。欢迎大家观看今晚的特别演出。希望你们能像我一样，被我们年轻的霹雳舞演员的才华和热情征服。我本人已经参加过三次彩排，所以我可以向你们保证，他们为了带给大家精彩的节目，牺牲了很多个人时间，洒下无数辛勤的汗水。这是一个集体表演，舞蹈设计由他们自己完成，我们出色的音乐美术教师王女士在一旁协助。那么，闲话少说，让我们坐好，开始欣赏年轻舞蹈演员们的精彩表演吧。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **principal**：校长
- **performance**：表演
- **overwhelm**：倾倒，征服
- **sheer**：真正的，纯粹的
- **enthusiasm**：热情
- **assure**：保证
- **sacrifice**：牺牲
- **bucket**：大量
- **sweat**：汗水
- **choreograph**：设计舞蹈动作
- **without further ado**：不费周折地，干脆痛快地
- **sit back**：放松，坐好
- **fabulous**：极好的

#### Q80 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Where is the talk most likely taking place? (讲话最有可能发生在哪儿？)
- (A) At a hospital. (在医院。)
- (B) At a public school. (在公办学校。)
- (C) At a theater. (在剧院。)
- (D) At an art gallery. (在美术馆。)

#### Q81 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Who is Dr. Cummins? (卡明斯博士是谁？)
- (A) A dancer. (舞蹈演员。)
- (B) An artist. (艺术家。)
- (C) The headmaster. (校长。)
- (D) The producer. (制作人。)

#### Q82 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Which of the following was mentioned by the speaker? (下面哪一项被讲话者提到过？)
- (A) The performers spent hours putting together the show. (演员们花了很多时间排练节目。)
- (B) Ms. Wang is the leading dancer of tonight's performance. (王女士是今晚表演的领舞。)
- (C) The theater is a full house for the first time since its opening. (自开业以来，剧院第一次全场坐满。)
- (D) All of the dancers are up-and-coming professionals. (所有舞蹈演员都是很有前途的专业演员。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **sheer talent = pure talent** (高超的才能)
  - *例句：He has a sheer talent for making sales.* (他拥有极高的销售才能。)
- **without further ado = without further delay = without further trouble** (干脆痛快地)
  - *例句：Now, without further ado, let's bring on the next speaker, Mr. Steve Shaw.* (现在，闲话少说，让我们有请下一位演讲人，史蒂夫)

### Questions 83 - 85

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Well, everybody, the History Society Functions Committee welcomes you all. I must say that I am surprised. There are so many people here tonight and so many new faces! (83) Let me say that I believe you have made an excellent decision to attend this meeting. Our speaker tonight will be one of the world's leading experts on Anglo-Saxon issues. He's Professor Michael Sutherland, who has kindly consented to come all the way from the University of Essex to speak to us. Professor Sutherland is not only an expert on the Anglo-Saxon period but also one of the most interesting speakers I have ever met. (84) So please welcome Professor Michael Sutherland. (85)

**中文对照：**
> 大家好，历史社会功能委员会欢迎大家的到来。我不得不说我非常惊讶。今晚有这么多人，这么多新面孔！我相信大家来参加这次会议是一个很棒的决定。我们今晚的发言人是世界领先的盎格鲁—撒克逊问题专家之一，米歇尔·萨瑟兰教授。他欣然同意从艾塞克斯大学远道赶来，为我们作演讲。萨瑟兰教授不仅是盎格鲁—撒克逊时代的研究专家，还是我见过的最风趣的演讲人之一。所以，请大家欢迎米歇尔·萨瑟兰教授。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **make a decision**：做决定
- **excellent**：极好的
- **leading**：主要的，领先的
- **expert**：专家
- **consent**：同意
- **all the way**：从远道
- **anticipate**：预料，期待
- **put on**：举办，举行

#### Q83 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What is implied about today's event? (关于今天的活动，以上讲话中有何暗示？)
- (A) There are more people in the audience than anticipated. (听众比预期的多。)
- (B) Today's event is one of the best events ever put on. (今天的活动是举办过的最好的一次。)
- (C) The audience members have waited a long time for it. (听众已经等待很久了。)
- (D) It was very difficult to get tonight's guest speaker. (很难见到今晚的特邀演讲者。)

#### Q84 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the speaker mention about today's guest speaker? (关于今晚的特邀演讲者，讲话者提到了什么？)
- (A) He is a university student. (他是大学学生。)
- (B) He is a history teacher. (他是历史教师。)
- (C) He is a very good talker. (他是很棒的演讲者。)
- (D) He is very famous worldwide. (他在国际上都很知名。)

#### Q85 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What will happen next? (下面要发生什么？)
- (A) The audience members will take an intermission break. (听众将中场休息。)
- (B) The guest speaker will take the stand. (特邀演讲人上台讲话。)
- (C) The speaker will give a brief introduction of the day's event. (讲话者对今天的活动做简要介绍。)
- (D) The day's event will come to an end. (今天的活动会结束。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **who has kindly consented to do = who has kindly given permission to do = who has kindly agreed to do** (（他）欣然同意…)
  - *例句：I'd like to thank Ms. Harris, who has kindly consented us to use her house for our next meeting.* (我想感谢哈里斯女士，她欣然同意我们用她的房子举办下一次会议。)
- **one of the most interesting speakers** (最风趣的演讲者之一扩展表达：)
  - *例句：one of the best speakers one of the most striking speakers Susan Davis is one of the most interesting speakers I have ever met.* (最优秀的演讲者之一最吸引人的演讲者之一苏珊)

### Questions 86 - 88

![Page 108](images/listen_page_108.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Could everybody please stop working for a minute and listen carefully? As you know, there are only four days until Christmas. Our company has been approached by the St. Vincent de Paul Society with an urgent request. St. Vincent's Christmas Appeal aims to provide blankets and hot meals to all of the city's homeless on Christmas Day. (86) However, this year they have not received a sufficient number of blankets. Could all of you please check your cupboards to see if you have any warm blankets to spare? Please only bring clean blankets in good condition. (87) Collectors from St. Vincent's will be calling tomorrow and Friday, (88) so I hope you all can help out.

**中文对照：**
> 请大家把工作停一会儿，听仔细了。大家都知道，离圣诞节只有4天了。圣文森特·保罗教会找到我们公司商量一个紧急请求。圣文森特的圣诞倡议是要在圣诞节当天为全城无家可归的人提供毯子和热的饭菜。可是，今年他们没有收到足够数量的毯子。请大家查看一下你们的衣柜，看看有没有多余的、暖和的毯子腾出来。请把干净、完好的毯子带来。圣文森特收毯子的人会在明天和周五打电话来，所以我希望大家都能帮忙。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **approach**：接洽，找商量
- **society**：协会，团体；教会
- **urgent**：紧急的
- **aim to**：目标是
- **blanket**：毯子
- **homeless**：无家可归的人
- **sufficient**：足够的，充分的
- **cupboard**：橱柜，衣柜
- **spare**：拨出；腾出
- **orphanage**：孤儿
- **unemployed**：失业者
- **donate**：捐献
- **volunteer**：志愿者
- **charity**：慈善机构
- **function**：盛大的集会，宴会

#### Q86 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** According to the speaker, who are in need of their help? (根据讲话者所说，谁需要他们的帮助？)
- (A) People without homes. (无家可归者。)
- (B) Runaway teenagers. (离家出走的青少年。)
- (C) Local orphanages. (当地的孤儿。)
- (D) Unemployed members of society. (社会失业者。)

#### Q87 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What is the speaker asking the listeners to do? (讲话者要求听众做什么？)
- (A) Donate some money. (捐款。)
- (B) Volunteer time at a charity function. (在一个慈善活动上做志愿者。)
- (C) Give unused blankets. (提供闲置的毯子。)
- (D) Prepare a Christmas present. (准备一份圣诞礼物。)

#### Q88 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** When will they be contacted by the charitable organization? (慈善组织什么时候联系他们？)
- (A) Before the end of today. (今天下班前。)
- (B) Toward the end of this week. (这周末。)
- (C) Early next week. (下周早些时候。)
- (D) On Christmas Day. (圣诞节当天。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **If you have any warm blankets to spare** (如果你有多余的、暖和的毯子腾出来扩展表达：)
  - *例句：If you have any extra blankets If you have any blankets you are not using at the moment If you have any warm blankets to spare, please bring them in tomorrow.* (如果你有多余的毯子如果你有暂时不用的毯子如果你有多余的、暖和的毯子腾出来，请明天带来。)
- **I hope you all can help out. = I hope all of you can lend a hand. = I hope all of you can contribute.** (我希望你们都能帮上忙。)

### Questions 89 - 91

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Attention, all shoppers! (89) Rush now to Tim Holton's for a very special offer. Yes, shoppers, from now until noon you can enjoy the special taste of Tim's many varieties of donuts or a delicious sandwich or one of their aromatic coffees at very special prices. (90) Why don't you sit down, and rest your weary legs? Your choice of coffee and donut will cost you only two dollars. The sandwich and donut set is only three dollars. Yes, shoppers, up until twelve o'clock, (90) a delicious cup of the best-brewed coffee and a donut set will cost you only two dollars, and a sandwich set will cost only three dollars. That's half the original price, shoppers. (91) Don't miss out!

**中文对照：**
> 全体顾客请注意！现在赶快到蒂姆·霍尔顿店吧，那里有特价优惠商品。是的，顾客们，从现在开始到中午，你能以特价享受到蒂姆店各种各样的炸面包圈或美味三明治或香浓咖啡。为什么不坐下来让疲惫的双腿休息一下呢？咖啡和炸面包圈只需2美元。三明治和炸面包圈套餐只需3美元。是的，顾客们，12点之前，一杯美味的煮咖啡加一个炸面包圈的套餐只卖2美元，一份三明治套餐只卖3美元。这是原价的一半，顾客们。千万不要错过！

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **rush**：冲，奔，赶紧
- **a variety of**：各种各样的
- **aromatic**：香浓的；芬芳的
- **weary**：疲惫的，劳累的
- **brewed coffee**：煮好的咖啡
- **original price**：原价

#### Q89 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Where is the announcement most likely taking place? (这条广播最有可能在哪儿播放？)
- (A) At a mall. (在商场。)
- (B) At a coffee shop. (在咖啡厅。)
- (C) At a sandwich store. (在三明治店。)
- (D) At a doctor's office. (在医生办公室。)

#### Q90 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** When will the special offer end? (特价供应到什么时候结束？)
- (A) At noon. (中午。)
- (B) This evening. (今天晚上。)
- (C) Tomorrow. (明天。)
- (D) This weekend. (本周末。)

#### Q91 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What is the original cost of a sandwich set? (一份三明治套餐的原价是多少？)
- (A) Two dollars. (2 美元。)
- (B) Three dollars. (3 美元。)
- (C) Four dollars. (4 美元。)
- (D) Six dollars. (6 美元。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **up until twelve o'clock = right through to noon = just before twelve o'clock** (直到12点)
  - *例句：The sale will last up until twelve o'clock today.* (特价销售会持续到今天12点。)
- **half the original price = 50% off the regular price** (半价)
  - *例句：That shirt is half the original price today only.* (那件衬衫半价销售，仅限今日。)

### Questions 92 - 94

![Page 109](images/listen_page_109.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Now that you've checked in, I'd like to let you know about some of the hotel's facilities. (92) First, on the second floor, there are separate gentlemen's and ladies' saunas. These are provided free to our guests (93) and are open from seven o'clock in the morning until ten in the evening. They are a wonderful way of relaxing after a long day. Second, the basement sports center offers a lap swimming pool, two squash courts, a weight room, and a relaxation center where you can enjoy yoga, massages, and aromatherapy. You can buy daily discount entry cards at the reception desk. (94) And finally, on behalf of the hotel, I'd like to offer you a free drink coupon, which can be used at the hotel restaurant. We hope you enjoy your stay!

**中文对照：**
> 既然大家已经登记入住了，我想给大家介绍宾馆的一些设施。首先，在二层有男女桑拿浴室各一间，免费向客人开放，时间是早上7点到晚上10点。漫长的一天结束后，可以到那里好好放松一下。第二，地下室的运动中心提供一个及膝深的游泳池、两个壁球场、一个举重房和一个放松中心，在那里你可以做瑜伽、接受按摩和芳香疗法。在前台可以买到每日优惠入场卡。最后，我想代表宾馆给大家发放一张免费饮品券，本券可以在宾馆的餐厅使用。希望大家入住愉快！

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **facility**：设施
- **separate**：单独的，分开的
- **wonderful**：非常好的
- **basement**：地下室
- **lap**：膝盖
- **weight room**：举重房
- **aromatherapy**：芳香疗法
- **entry card**：入场卡
- **on behalf of**：代表
- **stylish**：时髦的，漂亮的
- **bathing suit**：泳衣
- **rubdown**：按摩
- **outfit**：全套用品；全套装备

#### Q92 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Who is listening to the talk? (谁在听这段讲话？)
- (A) Hotel employees. (宾馆的员工。)
- (B) Guests. (客人。)
- (C) Fitness instructors. (健身教练。)
- (D) Restaurant staff. (餐厅工作人员。)

#### Q93 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Which of the following is offered for free? (下面哪一项是免费提供的？)
- (A) Men's and women's spas. (男女桑拿浴室。)
- (B) A stylish bathing suit. (时髦的泳衣。)
- (C) A muscle rubdown. (肌肉按摩。)
- (D) A workout training lesson. (健身训练课程。)

#### Q94 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What is available at the reception desk? (前台提供什么？)
- (A) A discount coupon. (打折券。)
- (B) A day's pass. (每日入场卡。)
- (C) Workout outfits. (健身的全套装备。)
- (D) Squash rackets. (壁球球拍。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **after a long day** (漫长的一天结束后扩展表达：)
  - *例句：after a hard day after a tiring day I went straight to bed after a long day at the office.* (艰苦的一天结束后疲惫的一天结束后在办公室度过漫长的一天之后，我直接上床睡觉了。)
- **and finally = and lastly = in conclusion** (最后)
  - *例句：And finally, we will end the meeting.* (最后，我们将结束会议。)
- **on behalf of the hotel = as a representative of the hotel = to speak for the hotel** (代表宾馆)
  - *例句：I'd like to make this very important announcement on behalf of the hotel.* (我想代表宾馆发布这则重要通知。)

### Questions 95 - 97

![Page 109](images/listen_page_109.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Welcome, shoppers, to the Landmark Department Store's special year- end sale. (95) Nearly every item here is being offered at a discount. However, if you want to find the best deals in the entire store, drop by the jewelry department, where you can get savings of up to fifty percent. (96) Make sure you sign up for a special shopper's card before you check out, too. (97) Doing that will give you ten percent off on future purchases and make you eligible for all kinds of special offers throughout the year. If you need assistance, speak to one of our customer service representatives. You can find them on every floor. Landmark Department Store

**中文对照：**
> 各位顾客，欢迎大家参加地标百货公司的年终特别促销活动。这里几乎每一件商品都有折扣。然而，如果您想在商场找到最优的价格，那么请去珠宝柜台看看吧，在那里您可以节省将近百分之五十的花费。在您结账之前也请确保已经注册了特别折扣卡。注册这张卡之后您将在未来的购物中享受九折优惠并且可以参与全年各式特别优惠活动。如果您需要帮助，请联系任何一位客服代表即可。这些代表您在每层都可找到。地标百货公司

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **landmark**：地标；里程碑
- **year-end sale**：年终促销
- **discount**：（打）折扣
- **best deal**：最优价格
- **entire**：全部的；整个的
- **drop by**：顺道拜访
- **jewelry**：珠宝
- **sign up**：注册；登记
- **check out**：结账；检验
- **assistance**：帮助；援助
- **representative**：代表；典型

#### Q95 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Why is the store having a sale? (这家商场为什么促销？)
- (A) It is celebrating its grand opening. (为了庆祝它的正式营业。)
- (B) The year is coming to an end. (一年行将结束。)
- (C) Students are going back to school. (学生们正在返校。)
- (D) It is going out of business. (它面临倒闭。)

#### Q96 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Where can shoppers get the biggest discounts? (请看图表。顾客们可以在哪里获得最高折扣？)
- (A) On the first floor. (在一层。)
- (B) On the second floor. (在二层。)
- (C) On the third floor. (在三层。)
- (D) On the fourth floor. (在四层。)

#### Q97 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the speaker recommend listeners do? (讲话者建议听众们做什么？)
- (A) Use the coupons they were given. (使用他们领的优惠券。)
- (B) Try on items before buying them. (购买货品之前先试戴。)
- (C) Apply for a special discount card. (申请一张特别折扣卡。)
- (D) Check out before the store closes. (在商场打烊之前结账。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **up to = no less than = as many as** (多达；相当于)
  - *例句：The Olympic Stadium will hold up to 80,000 spectators.* (奥林匹克将可容纳多达80 000名观众。)
- **eligible for = qualify for** (有资格；能胜任)
  - *例句：He is eligible for this position.* (他能够胜任这一职位。)

### Questions 98 - 100

![Page 110](images/listen_page_110.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Welcome, everyone, to the thirteenth annual conference being hosted by the International Society of Electrical Engineers. My name is Kate Daniels, and I'm the current president of the society. (98) Before we get started with the keynote speech by Dr. Lyndon Schafer, I should inform you of a couple of things. First, Sarah West will be a bit late, so she'll be changing speaking times with Meredith Trudeau. (99) In addition, we'll be holding the election for a new president today at 5:00 in the evening. (100) Only current members of the society are eligible to vote. You must show your membership card prior to receiving a ballot.

**中文对照：**
> 欢迎大家参加由电机工程学国际社团主办的第十三届年度会议。我叫凯特·丹尼尔斯，目前担任本社团的主席。在林登·莎菲尔博士开始主题演讲之前，我宣布几件事情。首先，萨拉·韦斯特会晚些到场，因此她将和梅雷德斯·特鲁多交换出场演讲的顺序。另外，今晚5点我们将会选举新的主席。只有社团的现任成员可以参选。请务必于收到选票之前出示您的会员卡。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **host**：主持（人）
- **international**：国际的，世界的
- **society**：社团；社会
- **engineer**：工程师
- **current**：现在的，最近的
- **president**：主席；校长；董事长
- **keynote speech**：主题演讲；专题报告
- **inform**：通知，告知
- **election**：选举；当选
- **ballot**：选票；投票

#### Q98 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Who is the speaker? (这位讲话是谁？)
- (A) A college professor. (一名大学教授。)
- (B) A group executive. (一名团队管理者。)
- (C) A local politician. (一名当地的政治家。)
- (D) A business owner. (一名企业负责人。)

#### Q99 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. What time will Sarah West give her talk? (请看图表。萨拉 · 韦斯特将于什么时间开始她的演讲？)
- (A) At 10:00 a.m. (上午 10 点。)
- (B) At 11:00 a.m. (上午 11 点。)
- (C) At 1:00 p.m. (下午 1 点。)
- (D) At 2:00 p.m. (下午 2 点。)

#### Q100 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the speaker say will happen at 5:00 p.m.? (讲话者说下午 5 点将会发生什么？)
- (A) An election will take place. (将会举行一场选举。)
- (B) New members will be inducted. (会有新成员入会。)
- (C) Awards will be presented. (会有人致闭幕词。)
- (D) A person will give the closing speech.

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **a couple of = several = some = a number of** (几个；一些)
  - *例句：There are a couple of things to be finished before this weekend.* (在这周末之前有几件事情要完成。)
- **prior to = before = precede = ahead of** (在…之前)
  - *例句：All the plans should be completed prior to our departure.* (我们出发之前所有计划都应完成。)

## Part 1: 照片描述 (Q1 - Q6)

### Q1 (正确答案：D)

![Page 112](images/listen_page_112.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) He's clearing off the desk. (他在清理桌子。)
- (B) He's e-mailing a friend. (他在给朋友发邮件。)
- (C) He's putting up notices on the wall. (他正把通知贴到墙上去。)
- (D) He's sitting in front of the fax machine. (他坐在传真机前面。)

**其他可能表达：**
- He is sitting at the desk. (他坐在书桌旁。)
- He is working at the keyboard. (他正在使用键盘。)
- He is working with a computer. (他正在使用电脑。)


### Q2 (正确答案：C)

![Page 112](images/listen_page_112.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) One man is giving a speech in a conference hall. (一位男士正在会议厅里做演讲。)
- (B) All of the men are watching television. (所有的人都在看电视。)
- (C) One of the men is talking into the microphone. (其中一个人在对着话筒讲话。)
- (D) They are holding a conversation over coffee. (他们一边交谈一边喝咖啡。)

**其他可能表达：**
- One man is being interviewed. (一位男士正在被采访。)
- An interview is taking place at the moment. (现在正在进行一场采访。)
- The man being interviewed is speaking into a microphone. (被采访的男士正对着话筒讲话。)


### Q3 (正确答案：D)

![Page 112](images/listen_page_112.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) The women are waiting for the bus to arrive. (女士们正在等公交车。)
- (B) They're lining up to board the bus. (她们正在排队上公交车。)
- (C) Some of them are walking toward the bus. (她们中的一些人正走向公交车。)
- (D) The people have already gotten off the bus. (人们已经下了公交车。)

**其他可能表达：**
- They are walking away from the bus. (她们正从公交车那里走开。)
- The women are dressed for warm weather. (女士们都穿着暖和天气里穿的衣服。)
- Some of them are carrying bags. (她们中的一些人拿着包。)


### Q4 (正确答案：B)

![Page 113](images/listen_page_113.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) The man is leaning over the long table. (男士正靠在长桌上。)
- (B) The man is sorting through the pile of books. (男士正在整理一堆书。)
- (C) The man is stacking the books on the shelves. (男士正把书堆放到书架上。)
- (D) The man is looking to make a purchase. (男士正在浏览，打算购买。)

**其他可能表达：**
- Some books have been stacked up in front of the man. (一些书已经堆放在男士面前。)
- The man is holding a book in front of him. (男士在他面前举着一本书。)
- He has picked up a book from the pile. (他从一堆书中拿起一本。)


### Q5 (正确答案：A)

![Page 113](images/listen_page_113.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) One of the women has a hat on. (其中一位女士戴着帽子。)
- (B) The women are riding their bicycles. (女士们在骑自行车。)
- (C) The bicyclists are locking up their bikes. (骑自行车的人正在锁车。)
- (D) They have stopped to get something from the store. (她们停下来到商店买东西。)

**其他可能表达：**
- The women have gotten off their bicycles. (女士们已经从自行车上下来了。)
- They are standing next to the bicycles. (她们正站在自行车旁边。)
- The bicycles are loaded with some goods. (自行车上载着一些货物。)


### Q6 (正确答案：C)

![Page 113](images/listen_page_113.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) Some customers are entering the store. (一些顾客正往商店里走。)
- (B) The store clerk is cleaning the store with a broom. (店员正在用扫帚清扫商店。)
- (C) Some goods have been hung on a rack outside of the store. (一些商品被挂在商店外面的架子上了。)
- (D) The floor of the store is being mopped. (有人正在拖商店的地板。)

**其他可能表达：**
- Some items are on display outside the store. (商店外面展示了一些物品。)
- The brooms have been put on a rack. (扫帚被放到架子上了。)
- There is a rack full of goods. (有一个装满货物的架子。)
- 注：在Part 1中，每道试题都添加了3种可能的正确表达方式，考生可
- 以了解对于同样的照片可能出现的不同表达。


## Part 2: 应答测试 (Q7 - Q31)

### Q7 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How much will it cost me to get to the airport by bus? (坐大巴去机场要花多少钱？)
- **A:** It's five dollars one way. (单程是5美元。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** How much is the bus ride to the airport? (坐大巴到机场需要多少钱？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Thirty minutes from here. (从这里走 30 分钟。)
  - (B) One will be leaving soon. (一辆车马上要出发了。)
  - (C) Five dollars for adults. (成人票 5 美元。)


### Q8 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Is there a place you regularly go to get your hair done? (你定期到某个地方做头发吗？)
- **A:** Yes, to a hair salon near my house. (是的，到我家附近的一个美发店。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Where do you usually get your hair done? (你通常在哪里做头发？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) From a hairstylist I know. (在一个我认识的发型师那里。)
  - (B) I don't like my hair long. (我不喜欢留长发。)
  - (C) Usually once a month. (一般是一个月一次。)


### Q9 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** When are you thinking of returning to work? (你想什么时候回去上班？)
- **A:** I should recover in a couple of weeks. (我应该过几周就会康复。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** When do you plan to go back to work? (你计划什么时候回去工作？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I'll go back with you. (我会和你一起回去。)
  - (B) My doctor says in two weeks. (我的医生说两周之后。)
  - (C) I get off at five o'clock today. (我今天 5 点下车的。)


### Q10 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Where is Michelle's birthplace? (米歇尔的出生地是哪里？)
- **A:** She was born in Paris. (她出生在巴黎。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Where did Michelle say she was born? (米歇尔说她是在哪里出生的？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) She doesn't know it yet. (她还不知道。)
  - (B) Yes, she grew up there. (是的，她在那儿长大。)
  - (C) I think she is French. (我想她是法国人。)


### Q11 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Who is going to show up to the party this evening? (谁会出现在今晚的聚会上？)
- **A:** Everyone should be coming. (每个人都会来。注：在Part 2中，为帮助考生提高听懂题目的能力，添加了和试题相同或相似的表达方法。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Who is going to be at the party tonight? (今晚谁要去参加聚会？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Everyone will be there. (每个人都会到那儿。)
  - (B) The party is going to be great. (聚会将会非常棒。)
  - (C) To celebrate our tenth anniversary. (为了庆祝我们的十周年纪念日。)


### Q12 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** When are you going to finish the report? (你什么时候能完成这个报告？)
- **A:** I'll get it to you before lunch. (我会在午饭前拿给你。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** When will you have the report ready? (你什么时候能把报告准备好？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I report directly to Mr. Singh. (我直接向辛格先生报告。)
  - (B) Yes, you can give it to me. (是的，你可以把它给我。)
  - (C) I'll have it on your desk by noon. (我会在中午之前把它放到你桌上。)


### Q13 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Can you work the Saturday shift, or do you want me to ask John to come in instead? (你能上周六的班吗，还是你想要我让约翰来替你？)
- **A:** I can come in. (我可以来。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Do you want to work this Saturday, or should I get John to fill in for you? (你想这周六上班，还是我让约翰代替你？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) The work is not too bad. (这份工作不错。)
  - (B) This weekend is perfect. (这周末就很好。)
  - (C) I'll come in if you'd like. (如果你想要我来，我就来。)


### Q14 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Who dropped in to see me while I was on the road? (我在路上的时候谁来拜访过我？)
- **A:** Your insurance rep, Julie. (你的保险代理人，朱莉。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Who came by while I was out? (我出去的时候谁来过？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I'll take it for you. (我会替你拿着它。)
  - (B) Julie, your insurance agent. (朱莉，你的保险经纪人。)
  - (C) I am expecting him today. (我今天在等他。)


### Q15 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Could you please shut the window a bit? (你能把窗户关上一点儿吗？)
- **A:** Yes, of course. (好的，当然可以。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Could you do me a favor and close the window a little? (你能帮我个忙把窗户关上一点儿吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Next to the window, thanks. (窗户旁边，谢谢。)
  - (B) Sure, I can do that. (当然，我可以这么做。)
  - (C) Yes, they are very close. (好的，它们离得很近。)


### Q16 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Did Bill come in to the office today? (比尔今天来办公室了吗？)
- **A:** He is at home in bed. (他今天卧床在家。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Has anyone seen Bill today? (今天有人看见比尔吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) He called in sick. (他打电话请病假了。)
  - (B) I saw it many times. (我看见它许多次了。)
  - (C) Today is not a good day. (今天是糟糕的一天。)


### Q17 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How do you feel about our new receptionist? (你觉得咱们新来的接待员怎么样？)
- **A:** I didn' t get a chance to talk to her yet. (我还没有机会和她说话呢。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** What do you think of our new receptionist? (你觉得咱们的新接待员怎么样？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) At the reception desk. (在前台。)
  - (B) I'll think it over tonight. (我今晚会仔细考虑。)
  - (C) I have not met her yet. (我还没有见过她。)


### Q18 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Did your meeting with your client go okay? (你和客户的会面进行得顺利吗？)
- **A:** Yes, it went very smoothly. (是的，进行得很顺利。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** How did your meeting with your client go? (你和客户的会面进行得如何？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, let's take off. (是的，咱们出发吧。)
  - (B) It went better than I expected. (进行得比我预计的要好。)
  - (C) He left an hour ago. (他一个小时前走的。)


### Q19 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** I spoke to the manager at last. (我终于和经理谈话了。)
- **A:** How did you manage that? (你怎么做到的？)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** I finally got a hold of the manager. (我最后找到经理了。)
- **选项：**
  - (A) How did you pull that off? (你怎么做到的？)
  - (B) They hold it for a month. (他们将其保存了一个月。)
  - (C) He doesn't work there anymore. (他再也不在那儿工作了。)


### Q20 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**

- **A:** As soon as the rain stops. (雨一停就开始。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** When is the game supposed to start? (比赛什么时候开始？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) When the rain lets up a little. (雨小一点儿的时候。)
  - (B) The game is going to be great. (比赛将会很精彩。)
  - (C) Between Boston and New York. (在波士顿队和纽约队之间。)


### Q21 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Weren't you a little worried about Jack not showing up to work today? (杰克今天没来上班，你一点儿也不担心吗？)
- **A:** No, he phoned me this morning. (不担心，他今天早上给我打电话了。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Weren't you a bit concerned about Jack being absent today? (杰克今天没来，你一点儿也不担心吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) That's too bad. (那太糟糕了。)
  - (B) He is worried. (他很担心。)
  - (C) No, he called in. (不担心，他打过电话了。)


### Q22 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Would you be willing to go to Mexico if the company paid for your trip? (如果公司出钱，你愿意去墨西哥出差吗？)
- **A:** Sure, but why do you want me to take the trip? (当然，但是你为什么想让我出差呢？)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Would you be willing to take a trip to Mexico on company expense? (公司出钱的话，你愿意出差去一趟墨西哥吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Was it that expensive? (会花很多钱吗？)
  - (B) What's the occasion? (是什么事情呢？)
  - (C) He is well trained. (他受了很好的训练。)


### Q23 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Where can I get this authorized? (我到哪儿能获得授权呢？)
- **A:** John is the person you are looking for. (约翰是你要找的人。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Where should I go to get this approved? (我应该到哪儿去获得批准呢？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Your best bet is to speak to John. (你最好去和约翰谈谈。)
  - (B) You have to prove it first. (你必须先证明它。)
  - (C) I could get it for you. (我可以为你拿到它。)


### Q24 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**

- **A:** Yes, he's very nice to me. (是的，他对我很好。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** How do you get along with your boss? (你和老板相处得怎么样？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I will bring it along tomorrow. (我明天会把它带来。)
  - (B) He is very kind to me. (他对我非常好。)
  - (C) Yes, he's my manager. (是的，他是我的经理。)


### Q25 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**

- **A:** When Terry shows up to take over. (特里来接替我的时候。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** What time are you thinking of taking off? (你想几点出发？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) As soon as Terry comes to replace me. (特里一来接替我，我就出发。)
  - (B) It's five after six right now. (现在是 6:05 。)
  - (C) I still need a little more time. (我还需要一点儿时间。)


### Q26 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**

- **A:** He's not here right now. (他现在不在这儿。)

  - (B) He stepped out for a moment. (他暂时出去了。)
  - (C) I will get it for you in a second. (我马上把它拿来给你。)


### Q27 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**

- **A:** I'm a bit busy with work, so I'm thinking of doing the same thing. (我工作有点儿忙，所以我也想这么办。)
