### Q6 (正确答案：A)

![Page 147](images/listen_page_147.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) People are looking into the aquarium. (人们在朝水族馆里看。)
- (B) People are waiting to go into the pool. (人们在等着进入游泳池。)
- (C) People are swimming in a pool. (人们在游泳池里游泳。)
- (D) People are watching a movie. (人们在看电影。)

**其他可能表达：**
- They are looking at the same thing. (他们在看同样的东西。)
- The people are standing next to the aquarium. (人们正站在水族馆旁边。)
- A couple of the women are carrying bags on their shoulders. (一些女士肩上背着包。)
- 注：在Part 1中，每道试题都添加了3种可能的正确表达方式，考生可
- 以了解对于同样的照片可能出现的不同表达。


## Part 2: 应答测试 (Q7 - Q31)

### Q7 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Where does the train for Chicago stop? (开往芝加哥的火车停在哪里？)
- **A:** Go line up at Gate 6. (到6号站台去排队。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Where can I catch the train for Chicago? (我在哪里能搭到开往芝加哥的火车？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) In one hour. (在一小时内。)
  - (B) At Stop 6. (在 6 号站台。)
  - (C) Yes, you can. (是的，你可以。)


### Q8 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Have the boxes been shipped out yet? (那些箱子已经用船运走了吗？)
- **A:** Yes, they went out this morning. (是的，它们是今早发走的。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Have the boxes been sent out yet? (那些箱子发送出去了吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Once a day. (一天一次。)
  - (B) Yes, they've been delivered. (是的，它们已经被运走了。)
  - (C) In the storage room. (在储物间里。)


### Q9 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Who is due to give a speech now? (现在应该谁演讲？)
- **A:** Linda Evans is scheduled to go up. (按计划琳达·埃文斯应该上去。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Who is scheduled to speak first? (按计划谁应该先发言？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) He is the keynote speaker. (他是主讲人。)
  - (B) Linda Evans is the first on the list. (琳达 · 埃文斯是名单上的第一个人。)
  - (C) They are scheduled to arrive soon. (按计划他们很快就会到了。)


### Q10 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Where do these dishes go? (这些菜放在哪里？)
- **A:** Put them here beside me. (把它们放在我旁边。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Where do you want me to put these dishes? (你想让我把这些菜放在哪儿？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Just place them next to me. (把它们放我旁边就行。)
  - (B) Yes, it is my favorite. (是的，它是我最喜欢的。)
  - (C) We're going to the restaurant. (我们打算去餐馆。)


### Q11 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Is sales tax included in this bill? (这个账单里包括营业税吗？)
- **A:** Yes, it's included in the total. (是的，它包含在总额中了。注：在Part 2中，为帮助考生提高听懂题目的能力，添加了和试题相同或相似的表达方法。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Does this total include sales tax? (这个总额包括营业税吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, we're taking a taxi. (是的，我们打算打车。)
  - (B) No, they don't sell it there. (不，他们不在那里出售它。)
  - (C) Yes, I believe it does. (是的，我认为是这样的。)


### Q12 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** When will you leave? (你将在什么时候离开？)
- **A:** At the end of this week. (这周末。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** When do you plan on taking off? (你打算什么时候动身？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) This Friday. (这周五。)
  - (B) Yes, of course. (好的，当然可以。)
  - (C) No, turn it on. (不，把它打开。)


### Q13 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Could you lend me a hand with something in the meeting room, or are you tied up at the moment? (你现在时间紧吗？可以到会议室帮我个忙吗？)
- **A:** I'm free until ten o'clock. (我10点以前都有空。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Can you come into the meeting room to give us a hand, or are you too busy right now? (如果你不是太忙的话，可以到会议室来给我们帮下忙吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I could spare a few minutes. (我可以腾出几分钟。)
  - (B) I think there is plenty of room. (我觉得有足够的空间。)
  - (C) Yes, I can lend you one. (好的，我可以借给你一个。)


### Q14 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Caroline did accept the offer she got from New York, didn't she? (卡罗琳确实接受了纽约那份工作，是吗？)
- **A:** She is still thinking it over. (她仍在仔细考虑。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Caroline is planning to take the job in New York, isn't she? (卡罗琳打算接受纽约的那份工作，是吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I think she's still considering her options. (我认为她现在仍在考虑她的选择。)
  - (B) It was not planned properly to begin with. (还没有合理地计划好来实施它。)
  - (C) They're yours, aren't they? (它们是你的，不是吗？)


### Q15 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** What is happening with the food we ordered? (我们点的食物怎么样了？)
- **A:** It's probably on its way now. (也许正被送过来。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Why is it taking such a long time for the food to get here? (为什么这么久才把食物送过来？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) We only ordered ten minutes ago. (我们 10 分钟前才点的餐。)
  - (B) The chicken is their best dish. (鸡肉是他们最好的菜。)
  - (C) Let's just eat here and go. (我们就在这里吃完再走吧。)


### Q16 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** We do know each other, don't we? (我们的确认识彼此，不是吗？)
- **A:** Yes, I'm quite sure we've met somewhere before. (是的，我非常确定我们以前在哪里见过。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** I'm quite certain that we've met somewhere, haven't we? (我很确信我们在什么地方见过，对吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I know where it is, too. (我也知道它在哪里。)
  - (B) Yes, you do look familiar. (是的，你确实看起来面熟。)
  - (C) He is sure about it. (他对此很确信。)


### Q17 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Do you know why the big boss postponed the meeting? (你知道大老板为什么将会议推迟了吗？)
- **A:** He was needed elsewhere. (其他地方需要他。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Why did the president put off the meeting for another day? (为什么总裁把会议推迟到了另一天？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) No, I have not met with him yet. (不，我还没有见到他。)
  - (B) The conference room is on this floor. (会议室在这一层。)
  - (C) He had to attend to something urgent. (他不得不处理紧急事件。)


### Q18 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Would you like more food, or are you okay? (你吃饱了吗？还需要更多食物吗？)
- **A:** I can't eat another bite, thanks. (我已经吃得很饱了，谢谢。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Are you full, or would you like seconds? (你吃饱了吗，要不要再来一些？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) No, I'll take the first one. (不，我要吃第一个。)
  - (B) That would be all right. (那将很好。)
  - (C) Thanks, but I'm full. (谢谢，我已经吃饱了。)


### Q19 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** When are we expecting Paul? (保罗什么时候过来？)
- **A:** I'll phone and ask him. (我会打电话问他的。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** When is Paul due to arrive here? (保罗应该什么时候到这里？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) No, he has not handed it in yet. (不，他还没有把它交上来。)
  - (B) Next month is the deadline. (下个月是最后期限。)
  - (C) Let me call him to find out. (让我给他打电话问清楚吧。)


### Q20 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Could you please hold this door open? (你可以帮我扶下门让它开着吗？)
- **A:** Yes, of course. (好的，当然可以。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Would you mind holding the door open for me? (你介意帮我扶下门让它开着吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Of course. Here you go. (当然可以，您这边请。)
  - (B) Oh, it's probably closed. (噢，它可能关了。)
  - (C) No, it's being held another time. (不，它将在其他时间举行。)


### Q21 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** There is rain in the forecast for this weekend, isn't there? (天气预报说这周末会下雨，是吗？)
- **A:** Yes, but I am going away. (是的，不过我要离开了。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** The rain is expected to come down hard this weekend, isn't it? (这周末会下大雨，是吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, he is waiting for it now. (是的，他现在正在等它。)
  - (B) Yes, but I won't be here. (是的，不过到时我不在这里。)
  - (C) To get away for a while. (离开一会儿。)


### Q22 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Could you please repeat that again, Mr. Carlson? (卡尔森先生，您可以重复一遍吗？)
- **A:** Mail a check to his address. (往他的地址邮寄一张支票。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** What was that you said again, Mr. Carlson? (卡尔森先生，您刚才又说了一遍什么？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Sorry, I am not sure where Mr. Carlson is. (抱歉，我不清楚卡尔森先生在哪里。)
  - (B) Yes, she said it several times already. (是的，她已经说过几遍了。)
  - (C) I said you should send them a check. (我说你应该给他们寄一张支票。)


### Q23 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How did your staff do in the game at the company picnic? (你的员工在公司野餐时举行的比赛中表现如何？)
- **A:** We didn't play because it rained. (下雨了，我们就没玩。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Did your staff win the game at the company picnic? (你的员工在公司野餐时赢得比赛了吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) We have been doing fine. (我们一直做得很好。)
  - (B) It got rained out. (那时外面下雨了。)
  - (C) That's what he said. (那正是他所说的。)


### Q24 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Didn't you think the movie was very emotional? (难道你不认为这部电影很感人吗？)
- **A:** Yes, I nearly cried. (是啊，我都快哭了。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** I thought the movie was very moving, didn't you? (我觉得这部电影很感人，你不这么认为吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, it was very touching. (是的，电影非常感人。)
  - (B) Let's go to the theater later. (咱们待会儿一起去电影院吧。)
  - (C) We're moving out next week. (我们下周搬家。)


### Q25 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** I heard that you have old comic books in stock here. (我听说你们这里有旧连环画的存货。)
- **A:** Yes, the clerk over there will help you find them. (是的，那边的店员会帮你找到它们。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** I was told by a friend of mine that you carry old comic books here. (我的一个朋友告诉我，你这里有旧的连环漫画册出售。)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Go and speak to that man wearing the cap. (去和那位戴帽子的男士说吧。)
  - (B) I'm sorry, but those are too heavy to be carried. (我很抱歉，那些东西太重了，搬不动。)
  - (C) Yes, the bookstore is across the road. (是的，书店在马路对面。)


### Q26 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How do you get to work every morning? (你每天早晨怎么去上班？)
- **A:** I bought a car recently. (我最近买了一部车。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** How do you commute to work from your place? (你怎么从住处去上班？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, I am doing great. (是的，我做得很棒。)
  - (B) I'm not familiar with the area. (我对这个地方不熟悉。)
  - (C) I usually drive my car. (我通常自己开车去。)


### Q27 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Should we study the map before taking off? (我们在出发前应该研究一下地图吧？)
- **A:** It's okay. I've been there many times before. (没问题。我已经去过那里很多次了。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Don't you think you should study the map before we leave? (难道你不认为你应该在我们离开之前研究一下地图吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Don't worry, I know the area well. (不用担心，我对该地区很熟悉。)
  - (B) I've already studied for the test. (我已经为这次考试学习过了。)
  - (C) Why don't we take off soon? (为什么我们不尽快离开？)


### Q28 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Could you ask John to step in here when he shows up? (约翰露面的时候你可以让他来这里吗？)
- **A:** He is not coming back to the office today. (他今天不会回办公室了。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Can you tell John to come and see me when he steps into the office? (约翰到办公室的时候你让他过来找我好吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, he stepped out a minute ago. (是的，他刚刚出去。)
  - (B) I think he went to see his doctor. (我想他是去看医生了。)
  - (C) I don't think he's coming back today. (我想他今天不会回来了。)


### Q29 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Who is the head of our Hong Kong branch office? (谁是我们香港分公司的负责人呢？)
- **A:** I'll look into it for you. (我会帮你查一下。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Who is the person in charge of our Hong Kong branch? (谁主管我们香港分公司呢？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, Ms. Wong was born there. (是的，翁女士出生在那里。)
  - (B) To learn how to speak Chinese. (学习如何讲汉语。)
  - (C) Let me find out for you. (我帮你查一下。)


### Q30 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Maybe we should make reservations before heading down. (也许我们应该在过去之前先预订。)
- **A:** Yes, it would be safer that way. (是的，那样会更保险。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Perhaps we should call to reserve the tables for this evening. (也许我们应该打电话预订今晚的席位。)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Thank you. It was a delicious meal. (谢谢你，这顿饭真可口啊。)
  - (B) I think that may be a wise thing to do. (我想那样做可能是明智的。)
  - (C) That would be a table for a party of six. (那会是一张六人桌。)


### Q31 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Don't you need to confirm your flight? (你不需要确认你的航班吗？)
- **A:** I already called the airport earlier. (我早些时候已经给机场打过电话了。Questions 32 through 34 refer to the following conversation.M:Susan， I need you to make a dozen copies of these reports fortomorrow's meeting with the board members before you take off today.（32，33）W: I'm sorry， Mr. Brown， but we are completely out of paper right now. Icalled our supplier and made the order last night， but it has not arrived yet.M: Okay， I will call and find out what's happening.In the meanwhile， sendPeter down to the stationery store to buy some paper right away.（34）Thereare a lot of pages to copy， so you'd better get started if you don't want to stay latetonight.W: All right. I will take care of the matter right away.M：苏珊，我需要你在今天下班前把报告复印几十份，为明天的董事会用。W：很抱歉，布朗先生，我们的纸现在都已经用光了。我昨晚就给供货商打过电话订货，但纸还没有送来。M：好吧，我会打电话看看是怎么回事。同时，让彼得现在去文具店买一些纸。需要复印的文件有很多页，所以你如果不想加班的话就赶紧行动吧。W：好的。我会立刻着手处理的。dozen几十，许多board委员会，董事会take off离开completely完全地，彻底地supplier供货商make an order下订单in the meanwhile与此同时，在此期间stationery文具店take care of处理)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Don't you have to call the airport to confirm your flight today? (你今天不用给机场打电话确认你的航班吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I already took care of it this morning. (我今早已经确认过了。)
  - (B) We are still considering which firm to go with. (我们仍在考虑与哪家公司合作。)
  - (C) I am taking the seven o'clock flight out. (我将乘 7 点的飞机过去。)


## Part 3: 简短对话 (Q32 - Q70)

### Questions 32 - 34

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Susan, I need you to make a dozen copies of these reports for tomorrow's meeting with the board members before you take off today. （ 32, 33 ）
**W:** I'm sorry, Mr. Brown, but we are completely out of paper right now. I called our supplier and made the order last night, but it has not arrived yet.
**M:** Okay, I will call and find out what's happening. In the meanwhile, send Peter down to the stationery store to buy some paper right away. (34) There are a lot of pages to copy, so you'd better get started if you don't want to stay late tonight.
**W:** All right. I will take care of the matter right away.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**苏珊，我需要你在今天下班前把报告复印几十份，为明天的董事会用。
> **W：**很抱歉，布朗先生，我们的纸现在都已经用光了。我昨晚就给供货商打过电话订货，但纸还没有送来。
> **M：**好吧，我会打电话看看是怎么回事。同时，让彼得现在去文具店买一些纸。需要复印的文件有很多页，所以你如果不想加班的话就赶紧行动吧。
> **W：**好的。我会立刻着手处理的。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **dozen**：几十，许多
- **board**：委员会，董事会
- **take off**：离开
- **completely**：完全地，彻底地
- **supplier**：供货商
- **make an order**：下订单
- **in the meanwhile**：与此同时，在此期间
- **stationery**：文具店
- **take care of**：处理

#### Q32 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the man ask the woman to do? (男士要求女士做什么？)
- (A) Pick up today's newspaper at the store. (到商店去取今天的报纸。)
- (B) Place an order with the supplier. (向供货商下订单。)
- (C) Make duplicates of some documents. (复印一些文件。)
- (D) Get Peter to come into his office. (让彼得到他的办公室来。)

#### Q33 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** When will the man meet with the board members? (男士什么时候与董事会成员见面？)
- (A) Right away. (马上。)
- (B) This evening. (今天晚上。)
- (C) Tomorrow morning. (明天上午。)
- (D) Later this week. (本周晚些时候。)

#### Q34 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What will the woman do first? (女士会先做什么？)
- (A) Use the photocopier. (使用复印机。)
- (B) Run down to the stationery store. (跑去文具店。)
- (C) Talk to a co-worker. (与一位同事交谈。)
- (D) Call their supplier. (打电话给供货商。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I will call and find out what's happening. = I will phone and see what the problem is. = I will call and look into the problem.** (我会打电话看看是怎么回事。)
- **If you don't want to stay late tonight. = If you want to leave early today. = If you don't want to work overtime today.** (如果你今天不想加班的话)
- **I will take care of the matter right away. = I will handle the situation right now. = I will look after the matter right now.** (我会立刻着手处理的。)

### Questions 35 - 37

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Hello, Ms. Maxwell. You wanted me to visit to talk about something?
**W:** That's correct. I need to talk about the tenants upstairs in the unit above me. They keep making too much noise late at night. (35)
**M:** I see. Have you spoken with them in person to request that they be quieter?
**W:** I have, but that didn't work. They still listen to music and play the guitar at all hours of the day and night. (36)
**M:** Okay, I'd better pay a visit to 4C and have a talk with them. (37) When I'm done, I'll come back down here.
**W:** Thanks. I really appreciate your assistance.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**您好，马克斯韦尔女士。您是想让我过去谈点事情吗？
> **W：**是的。我需要和你谈谈住在我楼上的这户租客。他们在深夜不停地制造噪音。
> **M：**我明白了。您有没有亲自跟他们谈过，要求他们安静一些呢？
> **W：**我谈过，但是没有用。他们依旧昼夜不停地听歌、弹吉他。
> **M：**好的，我最好去4C和他们谈谈。谈完回来告诉您。
> **W：**谢谢。我真的很感激你的帮助。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **visit**：参观；拜访
- **talk about**：谈论
- **tenant**：房客；居住者
- **in person**：亲自
- **request**：要求；请求
- **play the guitar**：弹吉他
- **pay a visit to sb**：拜访某人；去看望某人
- **come back**：回来；记起

#### Q35 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Who most likely is the man? (男士很可能是做什么的？)
- (A) An office supervisor. (办公室主管。)
- (B) A real estate agent. (房产经纪人。)
- (C) An apartment manager. (公寓管理者。)
- (D) A building repairperson. (大楼修理工。)

#### Q36 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the woman mean when she says, “That didn't work”? (女士说 “ 没有用 ” 是什么意思？)
- (A) Her neighbors did not become quieter. (她的邻居并没有变得更安静。)
- (B) Her kitchen sink did not stop leaking. (她的厨房水槽并没有停止漏水。)
- (C) She could not get her rent reduced. (她的租金并没有减少。)
- (D) She was unable to repair a broken window. (她不能修好坏了的窗户。)

#### Q37 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What will the man most likely do next? (男士下一步很可能会做什么？)
- (A) Go upstairs. (去楼上。)
- (B) Listen to some music. (听音乐。)
- (C) Make a phone call. (打电话。)
- (D) Examine the woman's kitchen. (检查女士的厨房。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I see. = I understand.** (我明白了。)
  - *例句：I see what you mean.* (我明白你的意思。)
- **At all hours of the day and night. = All the day and night.** (不分昼夜)
  - *例句：She thinks she can call me at all hours of the day and night.* (她以为她可以不分昼夜随时给我打电话。)
- **I really appreciate ~ = I am very grateful for ~** (我很感激…)
  - *例句：I really appreciate your dedication to this project.* (我非常感激你对这一项目的付出。)

### Questions 38 - 40

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** I'm terribly sorry, but I won't be able to show you the house you mentioned over the phone this morning. The owner went away for the weekend and was supposed to be back this morning, but he just called and said he won't be back until tomorrow because his flight got canceled. （ 38,39 ）
**W:** That's terrible. I got off work an hour early and drove all the way across town to see this house. Isn't there any possible chance that I could at least take a look around the yard? (40)
**M:** Well, I am sure that the owner won't mind if we checked out the house. Give me a second. I will call his hotel and ask for his permission. In the meantime, would you like some coffee?
**W:** Yes, that would be nice. I take mine black, please.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**非常抱歉，我不能带你参观今天早晨你在电话里提到的房子了。房主出去度周末了，本来是要今天早晨回来的，但是他刚刚打来电话说因为航班取消了，他要到明天才能回来。
> **W：**那太糟了。我提前一小时下班，然后开车穿越了整个城镇来看他的房子。有没有可能让我至少看看院子呢？
> **M：**嗯，我确定房主一定不会介意我们看看房子的。请等我一下。我去给他住的宾馆打个电话征得他的同意。在此期间，你想喝点咖啡吗？
> **W：**嗯，好的。我喝清咖啡。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **be supposed to**：应该，被期待
- **get off work**：下班
- **at least**：至少
- **take a look**：看一下
- **mind**：介意
- **permission**：许可
- **in the meantime**：在此期间

#### Q38 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Who most likely is the man? (男士最有可能是谁？)
- (A) A real estate agent. (房地产代理人。)
- (B) The owner of the house. (房子的主人。)
- (C) A coffee shop attendant. (咖啡店服务员。)
- (D) A hotel worker. (旅店工作人员。)

#### Q39 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What does the man imply when he says, “he won't be back until tomorrow because his flight got canceled”? (男士说 “ 因为航班取消了，他要到明天才回来 ” ，他在暗示什么？)
- (A) The woman does not have an appointment. (女士没有预约。)
- (B) The man cannot get on the next flight. (男士赶不上下一班飞机。)
- (C) The owner of the house cannot be reached. (联系不上房主。)
- (D) The woman's appointment got canceled. (女士的预约被取消了。)

#### Q40 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the woman request? (女士请求什么？)
- (A) To go for a drive. (去开车兜风。)
- (B) To see the house. (去看房子。)
- (C) To travel by plane. (去乘飞机旅行。)
- (D) To drink some coffee. (去喝咖啡。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I won't be able to show you the house. = I won't be able to take you around the house. = I won't be able to take you to the house.** (我不能带你参观房子了。)
- **Isn't there any possible chance ~? = Isn't there a possible way ~? = Couldn't we somehow ~?** (还有没有可能…？)
  - *例句：Isn't there any possible chance that I can come and see the doctor today?* (今天还有没有可能让医生给我看病呢？)
- **Would you like some coffee? = Would you care for some coffee? = How about some coffee?** (你想喝点咖啡吗？)

### Questions 41 - 43

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Do you know if enough people have registered for the computer class? I have to let Mr. Terrance know whether the class is going to open or not. (42)
**M:** I checked the list earlier, and there were many who had already registered. I think it's safe to tell Mr. Terrance that the class is going to be held. In fact, ask him if he would be interested in opening an extra class? (41) Registration lasts until this Friday, and I think there is a good chance that we could fill another class. (43)
**W:** I think he would be happy to hear that. I will call him right away to see what he says.
**M:** Thanks, and could you also do me a favor and see how many people have registered for the cooking class?

**中文对照：**
> **W：**是否有足够多的人注册了计算机课，你知道吗？我需要让特伦斯先生知道这门课是否要开。
> **M：**我之前查看过名单，已经有不少人注册了。我认为可以告诉特伦斯先生这门课要开。事实上，问问他是否乐意再额外开一个班？注册到本周五才结束，我认为我们很有可能再招满一个班。
> **W：**我想他听到这个消息一定会高兴的。我会立刻给他打电话看他怎么说。
> **M：**谢谢，你可否也帮我查查有多少人注册了烹饪课？

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **register**：注册
- **safe**：安全的，保险的
- **extra**：额外的，另外的
- **fill**：完成，填满

#### Q41 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Who is Mr. Terrance? (特伦斯先生是谁？)
- (A) A computer technician. (电脑技术员。)
- (B) A student. (学生。)
- (C) An instructor. (讲师。)
- (D) A chef. (厨师。)

#### Q42 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does Mr. Terrance want to know? (特伦斯先生想知道什么？)
- (A) If enough students have enrolled. (是否招收了足够多的学生。)
- (B) How fast the computers will be set up. (电脑多快能装好。)
- (C) How good the food is. (这些食物有多好。)
- (D) When the registration ends. (注册什么时候结束。)

#### Q43 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What will happen this Friday? (这周五将发生什么事情？)
- (A) The man will buy a new computer. (男士将买一台新电脑。)
- (B) The registration period will come to an end. (注册期将截止。)
- (C) The woman will receive her diploma. (女士将取得学位证书。)
- (D) They will dine in a fine restaurant. (他们将在一个很好的餐馆用餐。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I think it's safe to tell Mr. Terrance ~ = I think it's all right to tell Mr. Terrance ~ = I don't think anyone would mind if you told Mr. Terrance ~** (我认为我们可以告诉特伦斯先生…)
  - *例句：I think it's safe to tell Mr. Terrance about the deal.* (我认为我们可以告诉特伦斯先生这笔交易。)
- **opening an extra class = opening an additional class = having another class become available** (另外开一个班)
  - *例句：We are planning on opening another class next week.* (我们正计划下星期再开一个班。)
- **Registration lasts until this Friday. = The registration period ends this Friday. = Registration ends this Friday.** (注册持续到本周五。)

### Questions 44 - 46

![Page 151](images/listen_page_151.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** There is a person here by the name of Steven Harris to see Mr. Williams, John. He says he is a school friend from college. (44) Could you do me a favor and see if he is in his office?
**M:** Mr. Williams stepped out a minute ago, Lisa. He said he was going to talk to Dan about next week's seminar. Do you want me to go and check for you? (45) I was just about to go and make copies of this report anyway.
**W:** Yes, could you do that for me? If he is not there, try the second floor conference room. He is scheduled to give a talk to the sales staff about next week's seminar after lunch today. (46) He might have gone there early to test the equipment he will be using.
**M:** Okay, I will find him for you.

**中文对照：**
> **W：**约翰，这儿有一位叫史蒂文·哈里斯的人想见威廉姆斯先生。他说是威廉姆斯先生的大学校友。你能不能帮我看一下他在不在办公室？
> **M：**丽莎，威廉姆斯先生刚出去。他说他打算和丹商谈下周的研讨会。你想让我去帮你看看吗？反正我也正打算出去复印这份报告呢。
> **W：**好的，那你能帮我去看一下吗？如果他不在那里，去二层的会议室看看。他定在今天午饭后去就下周的研讨会给销售人员讲话。也许他会提前到那里测试将用到的设备。
> **M：**好的，我会帮你找他。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **step out**：出去
- **make a copy**：复印
- **give a talk**：讲话
- **equipment**：设备

#### Q44 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** How does Mr. Williams know Mr. Harris? (威廉姆斯先生是怎样认识哈里斯先生的？)
- (A) They work together. (他们一起工作。)
- (B) They went to school together. (他们曾经一起上过学。)
- (C) They are related. (他们是亲戚。)
- (D) They live in the same building. (他们住在一座楼里。)

#### Q45 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the man say he will do for the woman? (男士说他将为女士做什么？)
- (A) Make some copies. (复印几份文件。)
- (B) Find Mr. Williams. (找到威廉姆斯先生。)
- (C) Talk to Dan about the seminar. (与丹商谈研讨会。)
- (D) Set up the equipment. (安装设备。)

#### Q46 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** When is Mr. Williams scheduled to give a speech to the salespeople? (按计划，威廉姆斯先生应该什么时候给销售人员讲话？)
- (A) In a few minutes. (几分钟后。)
- (B) Before lunch. (午饭前。)
- (C) This afternoon. (今天下午。)
- (D) This evening. (今天晚上。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **a school friend from college = a college buddy = a friend I went to college with** (一位大学校友)
  - *例句：I know John because he is a school friend from college.* (我认识约翰，因为他是我大学时期的校友。)
- **try the second floor conference room** (试一下二层的会议室扩展表达：)
  - *例句：go to the second floor conference room take a look at the conference room on the second floor* (去二层的会议室看看二层的会议室)
- **test the equipment = try out the equipment = inspect the equipment** (测试设备)
  - *例句：We have to test the equipment before the guests arrive.* (我们必须在客人们到达之前测试一下设备。)

### Questions 47 - 49

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Ms. Lee, I'm calling to let you know about the results of the interview you had with us on Monday. I've gotten the word from my boss that the position is yours if you're still interested. (47)
**W:** Are you kidding? I mean, of course I am still interested.
**M:** That's great. When do you think you will be able to start your new position? Is next Monday okay?
**W:** I'm sorry, but I have not had a chance to inform my current boss about my quitting here, and I think I have to give him two-week's notice to find a replacement. (48) How about the first of June? (49)

**中文对照：**
> **M：**李女士，我打电话是要通知您周一参加我们面试的结果。我得到了老板的确认，如果您还对这个职位感兴趣的话，那它就是您的了。
> **W：**您不是在开玩笑吧？我的意思是，我当然还对它感兴趣。
> **M：**太好了。您认为您什么时候能够开始这项新工作呢？下周一可以吗？
> **W：**很抱歉，我一直还没找到机会将辞职的事通知我的现任经理，而且我觉得我应该给他两周的时间去物色替代的人选。6月1日怎么样？

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **quit**：离开
- **notice**：通知
- **replacement**：替代者，接替者
- **candidate**：候选人

#### Q47 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What is the purpose of the man's call? (男士打电话的目的是什么？)
- (A) To notify the woman of a test result. (告知女士一项考核的结果。)
- (B) To see if the woman would be interested in the job. (确认女士是否对这项工作感兴趣。)
- (C) To ask the woman some questions about work. (询问女士一些关于工作的问题。)
- (D) To tell the woman that he might be leaving his job. (告诉女士他可能要离职了。)

#### Q48 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the woman say she has to do? (女士说她必须做什么？)
- (A) Notify her manager about her quitting her job. (通知她的经理她要辞职。)
- (B) Inform the candidate about the results of his job interview. (通知应聘者的面试结果。)
- (C) Ask the candidate how soon he can start his new position. (询问应聘者什么时候可以开始这项新工作。)
- (D) Tell her boss about the interview set for the day. (告诉她的老板今天的面试安排情况。)

#### Q49 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** When does Ms. Lee say she will be available to start? (李女士说她什么时候可以开始新工作呢？)
- (A) Today. (今天。)
- (B) This week. (本周。)
- (C) In two weeks. (两周后。)
- (D) Next month. (下个月。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I've gotten the word from my boss. = I received the confirmation from my boss. = I got the go-ahead sign from my boss.** (我得到了老板的确认。)
- **Are you kidding?** (不会是在开玩笑吧？扩展表达：)
  - *例句：No way! Get out of here!* (没门！滚出去)
- **the first of June = June 1st = at the beginning of June 6** (月1日)
  - *例句：The new accountant will join us from the first of June.* (新会计6月1日就会加入我们了。)

### Questions 50 - 52

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** As you can see, Ms. Bright, the Emerald Room has space for fifty people, so that should be large enough for the seminar you're hosting. (50)
**W:** Actually, we've had more than seventy people sign up so far. It appears as though we may have more than 100 attendees.
**M:** The Diamond Room has a capacity of 150. It's our biggest room, but it's rented out on December 11.
**W:** How about on the tenth?
**M:** It's available the entire day. Perhaps it would be better to book it on an alternative date. (51)
**W:** I pretty much have to, don't I? But I need to speak with my supervisor first to get confirmation. (52)

**中文对照：**
> **M：**正如您所看到的，布赖特女士，翡翠厅可容纳

#### Q50 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** 人，场地大小应该适 合您将主办的研讨会。 W: 实际上，到目前为止，我们已经有 70 多个人报名了。看来我们可能 有 100 多名参会者。 M: 钻石厅可以容纳 150 人，是我们这最大的厅，但在 12 月 11 号租出去 了。 W: 可以预订 10 号吗？ M: 那天一整天都可以。可能更改预订日期比较好。 W: 我确实只能这样做了，是吧？但是我得先和我的主管沟通确认一 下。 seminar 研讨会 sign up 报名 appear 似乎，出现 as though 好像 attendee 出 席者 capacity 容量 rent out 租出 available 可用的 alternative 供选择的 supervisor 主管人 confirmation 确认 50 What does the man say about the Emerald Room? (关于翡翠厅，男士说了什么？)
- (A) It is available on the tenth. (可预订十号的。)
- (B) It costs more than the Diamond Room. (它比钻石厅更贵。)
- (C) It has already been rented out. (它已经租出去了。)
- (D) It can hold up to fifty people. (它可以容纳 50 人。)

#### Q51 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the man suggest doing? (男士建议如何做？)
- (A) Booking the Emerald Room. (预订翡翠厅。)
- (B) Changing the date of an event. (更改研讨会日期。)
- (C) Visiting a different venue. (去另一个会场。)
- (D) Restricting the number of attendees. (限制参会者人数。)

#### Q52 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What will the woman most likely do next? (接下来女士最有可能做什么？)
- (A) Sign a contract. (签合同。)
- (B) Contact the attendees. (联系参会者。)
- (C) Pay a deposit. (付订金。)
- (D) Talk to her boss. (和她的上司谈谈。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **It appears as though = It appears as if** (看起来，似乎，好像)
  - *例句：It appears as if you are very tired.* (你看起来好像很累。)
- **It would be better to book it on an alternative date. = You had better book it on another day.** (更改预订日期比较好。)
  - *例句：It would be better to make a decision now.* (最好现在做决定。)

### Questions 53 - 55

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Jonathan, if you have not reserved your flight tickets yet, you'd better do it soon. (53) I was just told by Sarah that it was going to be difficult to get seats from next week. (54)
**M:** Oh? Why is that?
**W:** Well, the International Film Festival is being held in New York during the same week as our conference. This event apparently attracts thousands of people from all walks of life into the city, and all the flights and hotel rooms get booked. (55)
**M:** Is that right? In that case, I'd better call right now and book a seat. I don't want to miss the conference.

**中文对照：**
> **W：**乔纳森，如果你还没有预订机票，那你得赶紧了。萨拉刚刚告诉我，从下周开始将会很难订到座位。
> **M：**喔？为什么会那样呢？
> **W：**哦，国际电影节和我们的会议都是下周在纽约举行。这一活动肯定会吸引成千上万各行各业的人到这个城市去，所有的航班和宾馆房间都会被预订。
> **M：**是那样吗？如果那样的话，我最好现在就打电话订个座位。我不想错过这次会议。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **reserve**：预订
- **apparently**：明显地
- **attract**：吸引
- **all walks of life**：各行各业

#### Q53 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the woman advise the man to do? (女士建议男士做什么？)
- (A) Book airline tickets. (订机票。)
- (B) Postpone the trip. (推迟旅行。)
- (C) Attend the film festival. (参加电影节。)
- (D) Skip the conference. (不去参加会议。)

#### Q54 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What did Sarah say to the woman? (萨拉对女士说过什么？)
- (A) She finished booking the hotel rooms. (她预订了宾馆房间。)
- (B) The staff will attend the film festival. (员工们将参加电影节。)
- (C) It might be hard to get a seat on the plane. (飞机座位可能很难订到。)
- (D) They will make a speech at the conference. (他们将会在会议上发言。)

#### Q55 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What will happen in New York during the week the speakers are there? (说话人在纽约的那一周将会发生什么事情？)
- (A) A big crowd from all over the world will gather. (来自世界各地的人都会聚在那里。)
- (B) The closing ceremony of the Film Festival will be held. (将举行电影节的闭幕式。)
- (C) Many hotels will be offering discounts. (许多宾馆将提供折扣。)
- (D) The company will hold its annual conference. (公司将举行年度会议。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **It is going to be difficult to get seats. = It is not going to be easy to get seats. = It is going to be next to impossible to get seats.** (将很难订到座位了。)
  - *例句：It is going to be difficult to get seats to the play.* (将很难订到这场演出的座位了。)
- **Why is that?** (为什么会那样呢？扩展表达：)
  - *例句：Why do you say that? = Is there any reason why you are saying that?* (你为什么那么说呢？)
- **people from all walks of life** (来自各行各业的人扩展表达：)
  - *例句：people from everywhere people from different backgrounds There will be people from all walks of life at the event.* (来自各地的人有着不同背景的人将会有来自各行各业的人参与这一活动。)

### Questions 56 - 58

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** I was just reading over the sales report and realized that our numbers have taken quite a dip compared to this time last year. (56) What do you think the problem is?
**W:** Well, there are several reasons, but one of the main reasons is that we have lost some of our main players to our competitors. (57) I brought the issue up at our last meeting, but no one really thought that it was all that important. I, on the other hand, feel that we really need to focus our attention on keeping those talented people here.
**M:** In your opinion, what is the main reason people are leaving us?
**W:** It's obvious. We need to compensate them with higher pay and benefits. (58)

**中文对照：**
> **M：**我刚刚读了一遍销售报告，发觉我们的数字与去年同期相比下降幅度很大。你认为问题出在哪里？
> **W：**哦，有几个原因，但主要原因之一是我们的一些主要成员跳槽到了竞争对手那里。我在上次会议上曾提出过这个问题，但是没有人认为这有多么重要。另一方面，我觉得我们真的需要集中精力把那些人才留下。
> **M：**在你看来，人才离开我们公司的主要原因是什么？
> **W：**原因显而易见。我们需要提供更高的薪水和更好的福利作为他们的报酬。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **read over ~**：把读一遍
- **realize**：意识到，发觉
- **number**：数字
- **dip**：下降
- **compared to ~**：与相比
- **main player**：主力
- **competitor**：竞争者，对手
- **on the other hand**：在另一方面
- **focus**：集中
- **attention**：注意力
- **talented**：有才华的
- **obvious**：明显的
- **compensate**：付报酬

#### Q56 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the man imply when he says, “our numbers have taken quite a dip compared to this time last year”? (男士说 “ 我们的数字与去年同期相比下降幅度很大 ” ，他在暗示什么？)
- (A) The company's sales have slightly increased. (公司的销售额稍微增长了。)
- (B) The company's sales took a big dive. (公司的销售额大幅下降。)
- (C) The company's sales remain unchanged. (公司的销售额没有什么变化。)
- (D) The company's sales have broken all the sales record. (公司的销售额打破了所有的销售纪录。)

#### Q57 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the woman think is the main reason for the problem mentioned? (女士认为导致提到的问题的主要原因是什么？)
- (A) The loss of their best staff. (最优秀的员工的流失。)
- (B) The increased price of the products. (产品价格的上涨。)
- (C) The stress of working long hours. (长时间工作造成的压力。)
- (D) The lack of talented people. (人才的缺乏。)

#### Q58 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** According to the woman, how can the problem be solved? (根据女士所说，这一问题将如何解决？)
- (A) By offering more pay. (通过提供更高的工资。)
- (B) By providing a better working environment. (通过提供更好的工作环境。)
- (C) By reducing the employee's work hours. (通过缩短员工的工作时间。)
- (D) By offering incentives. (通过提供奖励。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **take quite a dip = take a big plunge = take a big fall** (急剧下降)
  - *例句：The temperature has taken quite a dip in the last few days.* (在过去几天里气温急剧下降。)
- **It's obvious. = It's clear. = It's right there.** (这很明显。)
- **We need to compensate them with higher pay and benefits. = We need to provide them with higher pay and benefits. = We need to satisfy them with higher pay and benefits.** (我们需要提供更高的薪水和更好的福利作为他们的报酬。)

### Questions 59 - 61

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W1:** Mr. Sullivan is going to take everyone in the department out to dinner tonight to celebrate our highly profitable month. (59)
**M:** That's great news. Where will we be dining?
**W1:** He wants us to choose between Tino's and the Roadhouse. Personally, I prefer Tino's. (60)
**W2:** You can't go wrong with it. What do you think, Josh?
**M:** That's fine with me, Stacy. (60) Would you like me to call and book a table, Amy? (61)
**W1:** Yes, please. (61) We need a table for twenty at six thirty. I'm pretty sure private rooms are available, so why don't you request one of those, Josh?

**中文对照：**
> **W1：**沙利文先生今晚要请我们部门所有人吃饭，来庆祝本月盈利丰厚。
> **M：**这是个好消息。我们在哪里吃饭？
> **W1：**他想让我们在Tino's餐厅和Roadhouse餐厅之间做选择。就我个人而言，我更喜欢Tino's餐厅。
> **W2：**你的选择不错。乔希，你觉得呢？
> **M：**我没问题，史黛西。艾米，你想让我电话预订餐位吗？
> **W1：**好的，谢谢。我们需要预订六点半的一张20人的餐位。乔希，我确信肯定是有包间的，所以你为何不申请一间呢？

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **personally**：就个人而言
- **prefer**：更喜欢
- **book**：预定，预约
- **private room**：包间，包房
- **available**：可用的，可获得的
- **pretty**：相当，十分

#### Q59 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Why will the speakers go out to dinner? (讲话者们为什么要出去吃饭？)
- (A) They will meet some foreign clients. (他们将要见一些外国客户。)
- (B) They just hired some new employees. (他们刚刚雇用了一些新员工。)
- (C) They made a lot of money recently. (他们最近赚了很多钱。)
- (D) They have a business project to discuss. (他们有一个商业项目要讨论。)

#### Q60 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Why does Stacy say, “You can't go wrong with it”? (史黛西为什么说 “ 你的选择不错 ” ？)
- (A) To agree with the day they will go out. (同意他们那天外出。)
- (B) To state her preference for a dish. (说出她喜爱的一道菜。)
- (C) To indicate she likes the restaurant. (表明她喜欢这家餐厅。)
- (D) To admit that she agrees with the man. (承认她同意男士的观点。)

#### Q61 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What will the man probably do next? (男士接下来将要做什么？)
- (A) Contact a restaurant. (联系一家餐厅。)
- (B) E-mail Mr. Sullivan. (给沙利文先生发邮件。)
- (C) Speak with his coworkers. (和他的同事们讲话。)
- (D) Visit a client. (拜访一位顾客。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **You can't go wrong with it. = Your choice is good.** (你的选择不错。)
  - *例句：You can not go wrong with black trousers.* (黑色裤子不错。)

### Questions 62 - 64

![Page 154](images/listen_page_154.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Craig, I'm driving to Carter Pharmaceuticals to give a product demonstration today. (62) I know you've been there before. Do you happen to know where I can park?
**M:** You'd be better off taking the bus. Parking in that area is hard to find.
**W:** I know, but I'll be bringing a couple of boxes with me, so there's no way I can take them on the bus. (63)
**M:** In that case, you'd better park in the pay lot on Wilson Avenue. It's across from the Murray Building. (64)
**W:** That's sort of far from Carter Pharmaceuticals, isn't it?
**M:** It's two blocks away, but it's the closest lot to where you're heading.

**中文对照：**
> **W：**克雷格，我今天要开车去卡特药业公司做产品展示。我知道你之前去过。你知不知道我可以把车停在哪里？
> **M：**你最好乘坐公交车。那块区域很难找到停车的地方。
> **W：**我知道，但是我要带上几个箱子，所以我没法把它们带上公交车。
> **M：**那样的话，你最好把车停在威尔逊大道的收费停车场。它就在穆瑞大厦对面。
> **W：**那儿离卡特药业公司有些远，是不是？
> **M：**隔着两个街区，但那是离你的目的地最近的停车场了。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **pharmaceutical**：药物
- **demonstration**：演示，展示
- **a couple of**：几个
- **pay lot**：付费停车场
- **sort of**：有点儿，有些
- **block**：街区
- **head**：朝某方向行进

#### Q62 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Why is the woman going to Carter Pharmaceutical? (女士为什么要去卡特药业公司？)
- (A) To negotiate a contract. (谈判合同。)
- (B) To show how a product works. (演示产品。)
- (C) To apply for a position. (应聘职位。)
- (D) To submit some documents. (提交一些文件。)

#### Q63 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** According to the woman, why is she unable to take the bus? (根据女士所说，她为什么不能够乘坐公交车？)
- (A) She lost her bus pass. (她弄丢了公交车卡。)
- (B) No buses go close to Carter Pharmaceuticals. (没有公交车距离卡特药业公司很近。)
- (C) She will be carrying some items. (她要带些物品。)
- (D) The bus will take a long time to arrive. (公交车需要很长时间抵达。)

#### Q64 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Where does the man tell the woman to park? (请看图表，男士告诉女士在哪里停车？)
- (A) Site 1. (地点 1 。)
- (B) Site 2. (地点 2 。)
- (C) Site 3. (地点 3 。)
- (D) Site 4. (地点 4 。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **be better off (doing sth.) = be wiser (to do sth.)** (（对于做某事来说）是较为明智的)
  - *例句：You'd be better off going there by air.* (你最好乘飞机去那里。)

### Questions 65 - 67

![Page 155](images/listen_page_155.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** I heard an alarming report from Mr. Davis a few minutes ago. He mentioned that Gordon, Inc. has made a bid for one of our competitors.
**W:** So the rumors that Gordon is thinking of getting involved in our industry are true. （ 65, 66 ）
**M:** It appears that way. We've known for a long time that Gordon wants to own a publishing company. (65)
**W:** Anyway, which company is it bidding on? Is it bigger or smaller than us?
**M:** It's the second-largest company in the region according to market share. (67)
**W:** Oh, that will make it just a bit larger than us since we're the third-largest company. Market Share of Local Companies

**中文对照：**
> **M：**几分钟前我听到了戴维斯先生的一份惊人的报告。他提到，戈登公司已经出价要收购我们的一个竞争对手了。
> **W：**所以，戈登公司正在考虑涉足我们行业的小道消息已经坐实了。
> **M：**看起来是这样的。我们很早就知道戈登公司想要拥有一个出版公司。
> **W：**不管怎么说，它正在收购的是哪家公司呢？比我们公司大还是小？
> **M：**依据市场份额来看，它是本地区第二大公司。
> **W：**哦，那它比我们公司大一点儿，因为我们是第三大的公司。本地公司市场份额

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **alarming**：惊人的，令人恐怖的
- **mention**：提到
- **make a bid for**：出价购买，收购
- **get involved in**：涉足，涉入
- **anyway**：不管怎么说
- **region**：地区
- **market share**：市场份额

#### Q65 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What industry do the speakers most likely work in? (讲话人最有可能从事哪一行业？)
- (A) Logistics. (物流。)
- (B) Manufacturing. (制造业。)
- (C) Food Service. (餐饮业。)
- (D) Publishing. (出版业。)

#### Q66 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What does the man indicate about Gordon, Inc.? (关于戈登集团，男士暗示了什么？)
- (A) It is owned by a foreign conglomerate. (它归属于国外一家大企业集团。)
- (B) It is his company's main competitor. (它是男士所在公司主要的竞争对手。)
- (C) It has a branch office in the downtown area. (它在市中心拥有一家分公司。)
- (D) It is not currently involved in his industry. (它目前尚未涉足男士所在的行业。)

#### Q67 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Which company did Gordon, Inc. attempt to buy? (请看图表，戈登公司试图购买哪家公司？)
- (A) Duncan, Inc. (邓肯集团。)
- (B) Percival. (珀西瓦尔公司。)
- (C) Fordham Corp. (福德姆集团。)
- (D) Bellevue. (贝尔维公司。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **It appears that ~ = It seems that ~** (似乎…)
  - *例句：It appears that it is going to rain because there is thick black cloud over the sky.* (看起来要下雨了，因为天空乌云密布。)

### Questions 68 - 70

![Page 156](images/listen_page_156.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** What are all of these boxes doing here in the office?
**M:** I was at lunch when they arrived, so I'm not sure, but it appears as if the computer monitors the Accounting Department ordered have arrived. (68)
**W:** Well, we have some clients coming momentarily, so they have to be removed at once.
**M:** Okay, I'll call the secretary there and make sure someone comes here to take them away. (69)
**W:** Thanks, Fred. After doing that, would you mind straightening up the conference room? I noticed it was a bit messy. (70)
**M:** No problem. I'll get right on it as soon as I make the call.

**中文对照：**
> **W：**办公室里的这些箱子都是干什么的？
> **M：**它们送来的时候，我在吃午餐，所以我也不清楚，但是看起来是会计部门订购的电脑显示器到了。
> **W：**哦，我们的一些客户马上就要来了，所以现在必须把这些显示器挪走。
> **M：**好的，我给那儿的秘书打个电话，确保有人来把它们搬走。
> **W：**谢谢，弗雷德。做完这件事后，你介意把会议室收拾一下吗？我注意到它有些乱。
> **M：**没问题。我打完电话后就立刻去收拾。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **at lunch**：吃午餐
- **monitor**：显示器
- **accounting**：会计
- **client**：客户
- **momentarily**：立刻，一会儿，随时
- **remove**：移动，搬开
- **straighten up**：使整洁，收拾
- **conference room**：会议室
- **messy**：凌乱的

#### Q68 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the man say about the boxes? (关于那些箱子，男士说了什么？)
- (A) They were delivered by him. (它们是由他派送的。)
- (B) They contain computer monitors. (它们装的是电脑显示器。)
- (C) They need to be removed. (它们需要被搬走。)
- (D) They are from his department. (它们来自他所在的部门。)

#### Q69 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Who will the man call? (请看图表，男士将会给谁打电话？)
- (A) Anne Cleburne. (安娜 · 克利伯恩。)
- (B) Ronald Wilson. (罗纳德 · 威尔逊。)
- (C) Ozzie Martin. (奥齐 · 马丁。)
- (D) Elizabeth Yost. (伊丽莎白 · 约斯特。)

#### Q70 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the woman ask the man to do? (女士要求男士做什么？)
- (A) Clean a room. (清洁房屋。)
- (B) Contact a client. (联系客户。)
- (C) Send an e-mail. (发送电子邮件。)
- (D) Arrange some books. (整理一些书。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **make sure = make certain** (确保，确定)
  - *例句：First, make sure the printer has enough paper in it.* (首先，要确保打印机里面的纸张充足。)
- **Would you mind doing sth.? = Do you mind if ~** (您介意做…吗？)
  - *例句：Would you mind lending me your car tomorrow?* (您介意明天把车借我一下吗？)

## Part 4: 简短独白 (Q71 - Q100)

### Questions 71 - 73

![Page 157](images/listen_page_157.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Hi, Susan. This is Steve from the Accounting Department. (71) I heard from the receptionist that you are very busy today because of job interviews, but I have to bring some urgent, outstanding financial matters to your attention. Would it be possible for us to get together in my office, say, tomorrow morning at ten? (72) The particular items I would like to discuss with you relate to claims for travel expenses made by members of the Personnel Department after the conference last September. There are no serious problems with these claims, but in many cases the claims forms haven't been completed satisfactorily. (73) I'm sure we can clear this up quickly. Let me know if you can't make it tomorrow.

**中文对照：**
> 苏珊，你好，我是会计部门的史蒂夫。接待员告诉我因为面试的事情你今天会很忙，但我必须提醒你注意一些紧急的、还未解决的财务问题。明天上午10点钟你能到我办公室来吗？我想与你讨论的具体事情是关于一项旅行费用报销的，旅行费是人事部门成员参加去年九月份的会议后产生的。关于这些报销并没有严重的问题，但在许多情况下，报销表格填写得并不令人满意。我相信我们可以很快就把这件事解决好。如果你明天不能过来的话，请告诉我。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **accounting**：会计
- **receptionist**：接待员，前台
- **urgent**：紧急的
- **outstanding**：还未解决的
- **financial**：财务的
- **matter**：问题
- **attention**：注意
- **get together**：在一起
- **particular**：细致的，详细的
- **relate to ~**：与有关
- **claim**：报销
- **travel expense**：旅行费用
- **in many cases**：在许多情况下
- **complete**：使完整
- **satisfactorily**：令人满意地
- **clear up**：解决，消除

#### Q71 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Who most likely is Steve? (史蒂夫最有可能是什么人？)
- (A) An accountant. (会计。)
- (B) The receptionist. (接待员。)
- (C) The personnel manager. (人事经理。)
- (D) Travel agent. (旅行代理商。)

#### Q72 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** When does the speaker want to meet with Susan? (讲话人想什么时候和苏珊见面？)
- (A) This afternoon. (今天下午。)
- (B) Tomorrow. (明天。)
- (C) This week. (本周。)
- (D) Next week. (下周。)

#### Q73 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the speaker wish to address the listener about? (讲话人想和听话人谈论什么？)
- (A) Some forms that were not filled out satisfactorily. (一些填写得不太令人满意的表格。)
- (B) The money spent during the last business trip. (上次差旅的花费情况。)
- (C) The traveling arrangements of an upcoming business trip. (即将开始的差旅的行程安排。)
- (D) The request of a larger expense budget. (一项金额更大的支出预算请求。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **Would it be possible to ~? = Do you think it's possible to ~? = Could it be possible to ~?** (可以…吗？)
  - *例句：Would it be possible to take your car?* (可以搭你的车吗？)
- **in many cases = in many situations = in many incidents** (在许多情况下)
  - *例句：The company bus is available, but in many cases the workers do not make use of it.* (公司的车可以用，但在许多情况下，工人们都不用。)
- **I'm sure we can clear this up quickly. = I'm sure we can straighten this up quickly. = I'm quite certain that we can smooth this thing over quickly.** (我确信我们可以很快解决这件事。)

### Questions 74 - 76

**听力独白/对话原文：**
In sports news today, Blackburn United announced their intention to recruit new players and expand their facilities after their historic Cup Final win on Friday night. （ 74, 75 ） Their win has attracted the attention of major new sponsors and investors from the corporate world. (76) There are rumors that two star strikers now playing with European teams have signed or are close to signing. New coaching staff members will also be recruited, and training facilities and clubrooms will be upgraded, a club spokesperson announced today.

**中文对照：**
> 在今天的体育新闻中，周五晚上历史性地赢得决赛冠军的布莱克本联队宣布，他们打算招募新球员并增加设施。他们的胜利吸引了商业界新兴的大赞助商和投资商的注意。有传言说，目前正在欧洲球队效力的两位明星前锋已经或将要与其签约。一位俱乐部发言人今天表示，他们还将招募新的教练组成员，并升级训练设备和俱乐部聚会室。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **intention**：意图
- **recruit**：招募，吸收（新成员）
- **expand**：扩充
- **facility**：设施
- **Cup Final**：决赛杯
- **attract**：吸引
- **attention**：注意力
- **major**：大的，主要的
- **corporate**：公司的
- **striker**：前锋
- **clubroom**：俱乐部聚会室
- **upgrade**：更新，升级

#### Q74 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What is the report mainly about? (这则报道主要是关于什么的？)
- (A) The corporate decision to sponsor a sports team. (公司赞助一个运动队的决定。)
- (B) The multi-million dollar trade of a star player. (一位球星几百万美元的转会交易。)
- (C) The hiring of a new member of the coaching staff. (聘用一位新的教练组成员。)
- (D) The team's decision to recruit more players. (球队招募更多球员的决定。)

#### Q75 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What happened on Friday? (周五发生了什么事情？)
- (A) The team hired a new coach. (球队聘用了一位新教练。)
- (B) They got a new sponsor. (他们有了一个新的赞助商。)
- (C) The team won a cup. (球队赢得了一个奖杯。)
- (D) They scouted new players. (他们物色到了新球员。)

#### Q76 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What did the spokesperson announce? (发言人宣布了什么？)
- (A) The team has already signed a star player from Europe. (球队已经和一名欧洲球星签约。)
- (B) A few investors are interested in the club. (一些投资商对俱乐部感兴趣。)
- (C) A new head coach has joined the team. (一位新的主教练加入了球队。)
- (D) The team has purchased new fitness equipment. (球队购买了新的健身器材。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **recruit new players = gather new players = find new players** (招募新球员)
  - *例句：The team has decided to recruit new players from the minor league.* (球队已决定从小联盟中招募新球员。)
- **will be upgraded = will be improved = will be advanced** (将被升级)
  - *例句：Most of the equipment we use will be upgraded by the end of this year.* (我们使用的绝大多数设备将在今年年底之前升级。)

### Questions 77 - 79

**听力独白/对话原文：**
I'd like to welcome you all to this creative writing seminar. We have some wonderful activities for you this evening. The program tonight has been developed by our special guest, John Walkley, (77) the author of that wonderful novel The Smiths and the winner of the Franklin Award for Literature last year. (78) Before John begins the session, I'd like to say a few words about his life. Born in a small, country town in the southwest, he had difficulty finding friends. He began writing at an early age and was soon winning prizes for his poetry and short stories. I can't think of a better person to speak to us tonight about creativity. (79) So please welcome John Walkley.

**中文对照：**
> 欢迎大家来参加这次创意写作研讨会。今晚我们为大家准备了许多精彩的活动。今晚的节目是由我们的特别来宾约翰·沃克利策划的，他就是那部精彩小说《史密斯一家》的作者，也是去年富兰克林文学奖的获得者。在约翰开始这次会议之前，我想先介绍一下他的生平。他出生在西南部的一个乡村小镇，在那里他很难找到朋友。他很早就开始写作了，并且他的诗歌和短篇小说很快就为他赢得不少奖项。我想不出今晚还有谁能比他更适合给我们讲创意。那么让我们欢迎约翰·沃克利。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **creative**：创造性的
- **develop**：策划
- **session**：会议
- **poetry**：诗歌
- **creativity**：创造性，创意

#### Q77 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Who most likely put the evening's event together? (谁最有可能组织晚上的活动？)
- (A) The speaker. (讲话人。)
- (B) Mr. Smith. (史密斯先生。)
- (C) Mr. Walkley. (沃克利先生。)
- (D) Mr. Franklin. (富兰克林先生。)

#### Q78 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What did John Walkley achieve last year? (约翰 · 沃克利去年取得了什么成就？)
- (A) He published his first novel. (他出版了自己的第一部小说。)
- (B) He won a literary award. (他获得了一项文学奖。)
- (C) He wrote a poem for his mother. (他为自己的母亲写了一首诗。)
- (D) He developed a computer program. (他开发了一个电脑程序。)

#### Q79 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the speaker mean when he says, “I can't think of a better person to speak to us tonight about creativity”? (讲话者说 “ 我想不出今晚还有谁能比他更适合给我们讲创意 ” ，是想表达什么意思？)
- (A) John is an imaginative person. (约翰是一个富有想象力的人。)
- (B) John is not a very sociable person. (约翰不是一个很喜欢社交的人。)
- (C) John recently moved to a small country town. (约翰最近搬到了一个乡村小镇。)
- (D) John began writing right after college. (约翰大学毕业后就开始写作。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I'd like to say a few words about his life. = I'd like to express a few words in regards to his life. = I'd like to tell you a bit about his life.** (我想先介绍一下他的生平。)
- **I can't think of ~ = I can't come up with ~ = I can't imagine ~** (我想不出…)
  - *例句：I can't imagine anyone who can replace Mr. King after he retires.* (我想不出在金先生退休后有谁能替代他。)
- **So please welcome John Walkley. = So, let's all put our hands together for John Walkley. = So, let's all give a big round of applause for John Walkely.** (那么让我们欢迎约翰)
  - *例句：So please welcome John Walkley to the stage.* (那么让我们欢迎约翰)

### Questions 80 - 82

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Hello, everyone. I have been invited to your organization to advise you about increasing your sales. (80) I have observed your operations with a great deal of care, and I must say that I have enjoyed my time here. I should also say that I've been impressed with the dedication and enthusiasm I've seen here. Your organization provides a valuable service and performs very well. And the staff is effective and efficient and clearly likes working here. It is possible, however, to improve your service and your sales. (81) One of the ways we are going to start doing that is by encouraging staff participation and creativity. So let's break into small groups and think about ways that we can improve the store. (82)

**中文对照：**
> 各位好！我被邀请到贵公司来，就提高销售量的问题提供咨询。我非常认真地考察了你们的经营状况，我得说我很喜欢待在这里，而且我还要说，这里的奉献精神和热情给我留下了深刻的印象。你们公司提供了有价值的服务，并且经营出色。另外，员工很得力、很高效，看得出他们很喜欢在这里工作。但是，继续提升你们的服务和销售量还是有可能的。要做到这些，我们将开始采用的方法之一是激发员工的参与度和创造性。那么就让我们分成若干小组，然后想想怎样才能让店铺变得更好。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **organization**：组织，公司
- **observe**：观察
- **a great deal of**：大量的，许多
- **be impressed with ~**：对有深刻印象
- **dedication**：奉献
- **enthusiasm**：热情
- **valuable**：有用的，有价值的
- **perform**：执行
- **effective**：有效的，得力的
- **efficient**：有效率的
- **clearly**：显然地，无疑地
- **improve**：提高
- **encourage**：鼓励，促进
- **participation**：参与
- **creativity**：创造性
- **break into**：化整为零

#### Q80 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What is the main role of the speaker? (讲话人的主要任务是什么？)
- (A) To make operations run smoother. (让工作进行得更顺畅。)
- (B) To think of ways to improve employee job satisfaction. (想办法提高员工的工作满意度。)
- (C) To help increase sales. (帮助提高销售量。)
- (D) To upgrade the skills of the workers. (提高工人的技能。)

#### Q81 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the speaker say could be improved? (讲话人说可以提高什么？)
- (A) The attitude of the employees. (员工的态度。)
- (B) The service they provide. (他们提供的服务。)
- (C) The flow of their operations. (他们的工作流程。)
- (D) The working conditions. (工作条件。)

#### Q82 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What will they do next? (他们接下来将做什么？)
- (A) Gather into small groups. (组成若干小组。)
- (B) Talk about the upcoming sales. (谈论接下来的销售量。)
- (C) Walk around the operations area. (绕着工作区转一转。)
- (D) Take a break for lunch. (休息一下吃午餐。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I have observed your operations. = I have looked at your operations. = I have checked out your operations.** (我已经考察了你们的经营状况。)
- **So let's break into small groups. = So let's divide ourselves into small groups. = So let's all get into small groups.** (那么就让我们分成若干小组。)

### Questions 83 - 85

![Page 158](images/listen_page_158.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Attention, all passengers. The City Hall Subway Station is now closed due to flooding. (83) All subway trains on north- and south-bound routes have been halted. Passengers who are in City Hall Station are at present being assisted in leaving the building by emergency teams. We advise all commuters to take buses that will be running along both routes at approximately ten-minute intervals. (84) We estimate that normal operations at City Hall Station will resume in two hours. (85) We apologize for any inconvenience.

**中文对照：**
> 所有乘客请注意。由于洪水的缘故，地铁市政厅站现在已经关闭。所有南北双向行驶的地铁列车均已停驶。在地铁市政厅站的乘客现在正在紧急救援队的协助下离开地铁站。我们建议所有通勤者乘坐公交车，公交车大约每隔10分钟发一趟，两条路线均有车辆运行。我们估计地铁市政厅站将在两小时后恢复正常运行。由此带来的不便，我们深表歉意。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **flooding**：洪水
- **halt**：停止，终止
- **assist**：协助
- **emergency**：紧急情况，紧急事件
- **commuter**：通勤者
- **approximately**：大约
- **interval**：间隔
- **estimate**：估计
- **resume**：恢复
- **apologize**：道歉
- **inconvenience**：不便
- **subside**：退落；消退

#### Q83 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What is the announcement mainly about? (这则通告主要是关于什么的？)
- (A) The stoppage of the train service. (列车服务停止。)
- (B) The opening of a new subway station. (新开了一个地铁站。)
- (C) The weekend weather forecast. (周末天气预报。)
- (D) The bus routes in the city. (城市内的公交车线路。)

#### Q84 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the speaker suggest the listeners do? (讲话人建议听众做什么？)
- (A) Stay home this weekend. (本周末待在家里。)
- (B) Take alternative transportation. (选择其他的交通工具。)
- (C) Check out the new station. (看看新站。)
- (D) Wait until the rain subsides. (等到雨变小。)

#### Q85 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** According to the speaker, when will the situation be resolved? (根据讲话人所说，这一情况什么时候能得以解决？)
- (A) In an hour. (1 小时后。)
- (B) In two hours. (2 小时后。)
- (C) In three hours. (3 小时后。)
- (D) In four hours. (4 小时后。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **have been halted = have been stopped = have been terminated** (已经被停止了)
  - *例句：All operations have been halted after the workers walked off their jobs.* (工人们罢工后，所有的运营都被停止了。)
- **We advise all commuters to take buses. = We ask all commuters to take buses.** (我们建议所有通勤者乘坐公交车。)
  - *例句：We advise all travelers to take public transportation.* (我们建议所有的旅行者使用公共交通工具。)
- **We estimate that ~ = We predict that ~ = We guess that ~** (我们估计…)
  - *例句：We estimate that many of the workers will be happy to hear the news.* (我们估计许多工人听到这则消息都会感到高兴。)

### Questions 86 - 88

**听力独白/对话原文：**
This is Francis Kelly live from Collins Street with an update on the annual St. Patrick's Day parade. Right now I can see the first floats of the parade proceeding down Collins Street (86) between George and Pitt Street. The warm and sunny conditions today have drawn out the crowds in record numbers. (87) Police have estimated the crowd to be more than 100,000. Police have warned that anyone coming to the parade should not approach via either George or Pitt Streets. These roads are now completely blocked, and the police are no longer letting anybody pass the barriers. Police advise that any spectators arriving now should proceed towards Federation Square, (88) which is not yet completely filled.

**中文对照：**
> 这是弗朗西斯·凯利从柯林斯街发回的有关年度圣帕特里克节游行的最新现场报道。现在我可以看到游行的第一批花车沿着柯林斯街在乔治街和皮特街之间行进。今天阳光充足且温暖，这种天气吸引的游行人数创下了历史纪录。警方估计游行人数超过了10万人。警方警告参加游行的人不要经由乔治街或皮特街到达那里。这些街道现在已经完全堵塞，警方也不再让任何人通过路障。他们建议现在到达的观众朝联盟广场行进，这个广场现在还没有爆满。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **live**：现场的
- **update**：最新报道
- **annual**：年度的，每年的
- **parade**：游行
- **float**：花车
- **proceed**：行进
- **draw out**：吸引，使来
- **crowd**：人群
- **estimate**：估计
- **warn**：警告
- **approach**：靠近
- **via**：经由，通过
- **completely**：完全地；彻底地
- **block**：阻塞
- **barrier**：路障，障碍物
- **spectator**：（观看比赛或表演的）观众

#### Q86 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Where is the parade now? (游行队伍现在在哪里？)
- (A) On Collins Street. (在柯林斯街。)
- (B) On George Street. (在乔治街。)
- (C) On Pitt Street. (在皮特街。)
- (D) At Federation Square. (在联盟广场。)

#### Q87 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What is attracting people to the parade in record-breaking numbers? (是什么吸引了数量上创历史纪录的游行者？)
- (A) The television exposure. (电视报道。)
- (B) The beautiful weather. (宜人的天气。)
- (C) The convenient location. (方便的地点。)
- (D) The size of the parade. (游行的规模。)

#### Q88 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** According to the police, what should those coming to the parade do? (根据警方的要求，那些即将参加游行的人应该怎么做？)
- (A) Enter through George Street. (由乔治街进入。)
- (B) Head toward Federation Square. (朝联盟广场前进。)
- (C) Take the subway to Pitt Street. (乘坐地铁去皮特街。)
- (D) Park their cars on Collins Street. (将他们的车停在柯林斯街。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **have drawn out the crowds = have brought out many people = have attracted many people** (吸引了很多人)
  - *例句：The shows at the film festival have drawn out the crowds we did not expect.* (电影节的表演吸引的观众之多超出了我们的想象。)
- **These roads are now completely blocked. = These roads are not accessible at the moment. = These roads are unapproachable now.** (这些道路现在已经完全堵塞了。)

### Questions 89 - 91

**听力独白/对话原文：**
We'd like to start our evening news bulletin with a special report. The weather bureau has issued a special warning regarding an approaching dust storm. The unusually dry weather which we've been experiencing over the last three months has combined with strong northeasterly winds to produce a massive dust storm, which is moving steadily towards our city. The thick clouds should hit the northwestern suburbs by about 9:00 a.m. tomorrow morning (89) and then gradually move across the city in a southeasterly direction. The weather bureau advises all residents to make no unnecessary trips tomorrow, as visibility will be extremely reduced. (90) Schools and government offices will, however, be open tomorrow. Anyone with asthma or any other breathing disorder should remain indoors (91) and keep doors and windows tightly closed.

**中文对照：**
> 我们想以一则特别报道来开始晚间新闻快报。气象局对即将到来的沙尘暴发布了特别警告。过去三个月来，我们一直经历的不寻常的干燥天气与强劲的东北风一同形成了一场巨大的沙尘暴，这场沙尘暴现在正在平稳地朝我市移动。乌云将在明天上午9点到达西北部郊区，然后会逐步向东南方向移动并穿过城市。因为空气能见度将大大降低，所以气象局建议所有居民取消不必要的出行。但学校和政府部门仍将开放。有哮喘及其他呼吸系统疾病的人应该待在室内，并且将门窗紧闭。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **bulletin**：新闻快报
- **weather bureau**：气象局
- **warning**：警告
- **approach**：接近
- **dust storm**：沙尘暴
- **unusually**：不同寻常地
- **combine**：结合
- **massive**：巨大的
- **steadily**：平稳地
- **thick**：浓的，浓厚的
- **suburb**：郊区
- **gradually**：逐步地
- **unnecessary**：不必要的
- **visibility**：能见度
- **extremely**：极度地
- **asthma**：哮喘
- **disorder**：病症，紊乱
- **tightly**：紧紧地

#### Q89 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** When is the dust storm expected to hit the city? (预计沙尘暴将在何时袭击这座城市？)
- (A) This afternoon. (今天下午。)
- (B) This evening. (今天晚上。)
- (C) Tomorrow morning. (明天上午。)
- (D) Tomorrow afternoon. (明天下午。)

#### Q90 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Why does the speaker say, “The weather bureau advises all residents to make no unnecessary trips tomorrow”? (讲话者为什么说 “ 气象局建议所有居民取消不必要的出行 ” ？)
- (A) Many of the roads will be closed to traffic. (许多道路将禁止车辆通行。)
- (B) The drivers will have a hard time seeing the roads. (司机将很难看清道路。)
- (C) There is the possibility of a tornado coming. (可能会有龙卷风来袭。)
- (D) Some of the roads will be very slippery. (一些街道将会很滑。)

#### Q91 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** According to the speaker, who should stay indoors tomorrow? (根据讲话者所说，什么样的人明天应该待在室内呢？)
- (A) People with respiratory problems. (有呼吸系统疾病的人。)
- (B) School children under the age of 12. (不满 12 岁的在校学生。)
- (C) Seniors with heart problems. (有心脏病的老年人。)
- (D) Those who live in the southern part of the city. (那些生活在城市南部的人们。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **move steadily = move gradually = move step by step** (平稳地移动)
  - *例句：The newly released book by Stephenie Meyer is moving steadily up the best seller's list.* (斯蒂芬妮)
- **should hit the northwestern suburbs** (将袭击西北部郊区扩展表达：)
  - *例句：should reach the northwestern suburbs = should arrive at the northwestern suburbs The storm should hit the northwestern suburbs by late this afternoon.* (将到达西北部郊区风暴将在今天下午晚些时候袭击西北部郊区。)

### Questions 92 - 94

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Welcome, everybody, to this staff meeting. (92) I have to add a new item to the agenda since I received several complaints yesterday about the state of the lunchroom. I'm not going to name anybody at this meeting, but I have to say that I, too, am also disappointed by the behavior of certain staff members. (94) The lunchroom is a shared facility and one which provides all of us with a valuable service. Let's keep it clean! (93) If you make a mess, clean it up. If you read the newspaper, return it to the table folded neatly when you have finished with it. If you use the sink, make sure you leave it clean. This is a question of basic good manners, and I hope I never have to speak to anybody here again about it! (94)

**中文对照：**
> 欢迎大家来参加这次员工会议。昨天我收到了几份关于餐厅状况的投诉，所以我必须在议程中增加一项新内容。在这次会议上我不会点任何人的名字，但是我也不得不说，我本人也对某些员工的表现感到失望。餐厅是一个公用设施，它为我们所有人提供了重要的服务。让我们保持餐厅的清洁吧！如果你把它弄脏了，那就应该打扫干净。如果你阅读了报纸，读完之后你应该将它叠整齐放回到桌上。如果你用了水槽，要保证用完时它也是干净的。这是一个基本的礼貌问题，我希望以后再也不用和在座的诸位谈这件事情！

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **add**：增加
- **agenda**：议程
- **state**：状况
- **lunchroom**：餐厅
- **disappointed**：失望的
- **behavior**：表现
- **certain**：某些
- **valuable**：重要的，有价值的
- **make a mess**：弄脏，弄乱
- **neatly**：整洁地
- **manner**：礼貌；礼仪

#### Q92 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Who most likely is the speaker addressing? (讲话人最有可能在向什么人发言？)
- (A) Cafeteria workers. (餐厅工人。)
- (B) Staff members. (员工。)
- (C) The cleaning staff. (清洁工。)
- (D) The facility manager. (设备经理。)

#### Q93 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What is the talk mainly about? (这则讲话主要是关于什么的？)
- (A) To welcome people to the meeting. (欢迎人们参加会议。)
- (B) To notify a new regulation at the company. (宣布公司的一项新规定。)
- (C) To ask the staff to deal with customers' complaints. (让员工处理顾客投诉。)
- (D) To ask the employees to better take care of the eating area. (让雇员们更好地维护就餐区。)

#### Q94 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What is implied about some of the workers at the company? (关于公司的某些员工可以推断出什么？)
- (A) They are inconsiderate of others. (他们不为别人着想。)
- (B) They seldom make any complaints. (他们很少抱怨。)
- (C) They usually eat in the cafeteria. (他们通常在餐厅吃饭。)
- (D) They don't talk to one another very much. (他们不怎么和别人说话。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I'm not going to name anybody.** (我不会点任何人的名字。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：I'm not going to point any fingers at anyone. I'm not going to blame anyone in particular.* (我不想指出任何人。我不想特别批评任何人。)

### Questions 95 - 97

![Page 161](images/listen_page_161.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
It's time for an update on the local economy. Thanks to the efforts of Mayor Crawford, several companies have opened branches in Richmond during the past year. That's been great for the economy as unemployment is at a record low. (95) However, there's a housing shortage now, so the average price of a house has risen by more than twenty percent this year. This morning, Carter Construction announced it's building an apartment complex on the eastern side of the Mohawk River. It will be adjacent to the Danforth Bridge. (96) Construction won't be complete until eighteen months from now, (97) but when it's done, more than 600 family-sized units will be available for rent or purchase.

**中文对照：**
> 是时候给当地经济注入新动力了。得益于克劳福德市长的努力，过去一年来，很多企业都在里士满开设了分支机构。这对于经济来说意义重大，因为失业率创下历史最低点。然而，由于当下住房紧张，今年的房价平均上涨了20%以上。就在今天早上，卡特建设公司宣布要在莫华克河东岸建一栋公寓大楼。大楼将与丹福斯大桥毗邻。整个建设工期将历时18个月，且大楼一经建成，将有多套家庭住宅可供租赁或购买。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **unemployment**：失业
- **at a record low**：创历史新低
- **housing shortage**：住房紧张
- **announce**：宣布
- **apartment complex**：公寓大楼
- **be available for**：有效；对有用
- **purchase**：购买

#### Q95 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the speaker say about the local economy? (关于当地经济，讲话者说了什么？)
- (A) It should start to improve next month. (当地经济状况预计下个月会有所改善。)
- (B) High local taxes are hurting it. (当地经济因税收过高而遭到损害。)
- (C) The unemployment rate is very low. (失业率非常低。)
- (D) There are jobs available in the construction industry. (建筑行业有工作机会。)

#### Q96 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Where is the apartment complex being constructed? (请看图表，公寓大楼将被建立在哪个地点？)
- (A) Site 1. (地点 1 。)
- (B) Site 2. (地点 2 。)
- (C) Site 3. (地点 3 。)
- (D) Site 4. (地点 4 。)

#### Q97 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** When will construction on the apartment complex be completed? (公寓大楼的建设什么时候可以竣工？)
- (A) In half a year. (半年后。)
- (B) In a year. (一年后。)
- (C) In a year and a half. (一年半以后。)
- (D) In two years. (两年后。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **It's time for ~ = It's high time that ~ It's time for you to be boarding.** (你是时候登机了。)
- **Thanks to the efforts of ~ = Due to the efforts of ~ = Given the efforts of ~** (得益于…的努力)
  - *例句：Thanks to the efforts of note-taking, we learned a lot.* (由于努力记笔记，我们学到了很多。)

### Questions 98 - 100

![Page 161](images/listen_page_161.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
I've got a quick update on the luncheon—we're going to be having to celebrate the successful completion of the Dumont project. (98) I reserved a room at the restaurant at the Greenbrier Hotel, but I was informed by Ms. Anderson that CEO Richards and ten members of his staff intend to be at the luncheon. I'll be calling the hotel back to arrange a private room big enough for forty-five people. (99) We'll also be increasing the budget since we'll have so many more people there. As soon as I make the necessary arrangements, I'll send an e-mail to each of you to provide you with the relevant data. (100) Greenbrier Hotel Restaurant Private Rooms

**中文对照：**
> 我收到了午宴的最新消息——午宴是为了庆祝杜蒙特工程成功竣工而举办的。我之前在绿蔷薇酒店预订好了一间包间，可后来安德森女士通知我说理查德总裁会带十名员工出席宴会。现在我要给酒店打电话，让他们安排一个能容纳45人的大包间。我们也会增加预算，毕竟现在人数增多了。待我一切安排妥当后，会给每个人发一封邮件告知具体细节。绿蔷薇酒店餐厅包间名录

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **update**：最新消息
- **luncheon**：午宴
- **reserve**：预定
- **be informed by**：被告知
- **intend to**：打算
- **call back**：回电
- **make the necessary arrangements**：一切安排妥当
- **private room**：包间

#### Q98 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What is the speaker mainly discussing? (讲话者主要在讨论什么？)
- (A) The Dumont project. (杜蒙特项目。)
- (B) A conference with the CEO. (和总裁的会议。)
- (C) Last week's luncheon. (上周的午宴。)
- (D) Plans for a special event. (一项特殊活动计划。)

#### Q99 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Which room will the speaker most likely reserve? (请看图表，讲话者最有可能预订哪个房间？)
- (A) Silk. (丝绸厅。)
- (B) Gold. (黄金厅。)
- (C) Platinum. (铂金厅。)
- (D) Diamond. (钻石厅。)

#### Q100 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the speaker say he will do? (讲话者说他将要做什么？)
- (A) Send some information. (发送一些信息。)
- (B) Cancel a reservation. (取消预定。)
- (C) Request more money. (申请增加预算。)
- (D) Read his e-mail. (查阅他的邮件。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **be informed by = be told = be brought in on** (被…告知拓展表达：)
  - *例句：inform sb. of sth. inform on sb. I have been reliably informed that the couple will marry next year.* (告知某人某事告发某人我得到可靠消息说他俩明年会再婚。)
