| **7** | A | **17** | A | **27** | C | **37** | A | **47** | B | **57** | A | **67** | A | **77** | B | **87** | A | **97** | C |
| **8** | A | **18** | A | **28** | B | **38** | D | **48** | C | **58** | B | **68** | A | **78** | A | **88** | A | **98** | B |
| **9** | A | **19** | B | **29** | C | **39** | B | **49** | D | **59** | C | **69** | B | **79** | B | **89** | A | **99** | C |
| **10** | A | **20** | A | **30** | A | **40** | B | **50** | C | **60** | A | **70** | C | **80** | A | **90** | D | **100** | C |


## Part 1: 照片描述 (Q1 - Q6)

### Q1 (正确答案：D)

![Page 164](images/listen_page_164.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) He's drinking some water. (他正在喝水。)
- (B) He's checking his reflection in the mirror. (他正在查看自己在镜中的影像。)
- (C) He's enjoying a meal at the table. (他正在餐桌旁吃饭。)
- (D) He's reading a paper in a dining area. (他正在就餐区读报纸。)

**其他可能表达：**
- He is looking over the paper. (他正在查看报纸。)
- He is studying the newspaper. (他正在研究报纸。)
- He is leafing through the paper. (他正在浏览报纸。)


### Q2 (正确答案：A)

![Page 164](images/listen_page_164.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) The woman is picking out an item. (女士正在挑选商品。)
- (B) The woman is cleaning the floor. (女士正在扫地。)
- (C) The woman is helping a customer. (女士正在为顾客服务。)
- (D) The woman is trying on a jacket. (女士正在试穿夹克。)

**其他可能表达：**
- The woman is choosing an item. (女士正在挑选商品。)
- The woman is about to select an item on the rack. (女士正打算从货架上挑选一件商品。)
- She has reached out to pick out an item from the rack. (她已经伸出手去从货架上拿商品。)


### Q3 (正确答案：D)

![Page 164](images/listen_page_164.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) The aircraft is about to land at the airport. (这架飞机正要在机场着陆。)
- (B) The people are boarding the plane. (人们正在登机。)
- (C) The cargo is being loaded onto the plane. (货物正在被装上飞机。)
- (D) The plane landed a short while ago. (飞机刚着陆一小会儿。)

**其他可能表达：**
- The woman is stepping down from the plane. (女士正在走下飞机。)
- An exit ramp extends up to the door of the plane. (出舱舷梯伸到了飞机门口。)
- The passengers are walking away from the plane. (乘客们正在离开飞机。)


### Q4 (正确答案：C)

![Page 165](images/listen_page_165.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) One man is standing at the door. (一位男士正站在门口。)
- (B) The men are walking up the stairs. (男士正在上楼梯。)
- (C) One man is filming the other. (一位男士正在给另一位男士拍照。)
- (D) The men are being interviewed. (男士正在接受采访。)

**其他可能表达：**
- One man has crouched down. (一位男士已经蹲下了。)
- One man is holding a camera on his shoulder. (一位男士肩上正扛着摄像机。)
- The man being filmed is wearing a safety helmet. (正被拍摄的男士戴着安全头盔。)


### Q5 (正确答案：C)

![Page 165](images/listen_page_165.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) The tables have been set up indoors. (餐桌已经在室内摆好了。)
- (B) A waiter is serving the customers. (一位服务员正在为顾客服务。)
- (C) Some people are seated outside. (一些人在室外就座了。)
- (D) The area is entirely shaded. (整块区域都是阴凉地。)

**其他可能表达：**
- There are tables and chairs set up outdoors. (室外摆放着餐桌和椅子。)
- There are buildings on both sides of the street. (街道两边都有建筑。)
- There are still seats available. (还有座位空着。)


### Q6 (正确答案：B)

![Page 165](images/listen_page_165.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) The cars are parked on the road. (汽车停在路上。)
- (B) There are vehicles in the driveway. (车道上有车辆。)
- (C) The windows are being cleaned. (有人正在擦窗户。)
- (D) A man is getting into the car. (一位男士正在上车。)

**其他可能表达：**
- There are trees growing around the house. (房子周围种着树。)
- The vehicles are parked next to each other. (这些车辆并排停放着。)
- The cars are parked facing the same direction. (这些汽车都朝一个方向停放。)
- 注：在Part 1中，每道试题都添加了3种可能的正确表达方式，考生可
- 以了解对于同样的照片可能出现的不同表达。


## Part 2: 应答测试 (Q7 - Q31)

### Q7 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** When are you going? (你什么时候走呢？)
- **A:** When I get this work done. (当我把这项工作做完的时候。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** When are you thinking of taking off? (你想什么时候动身呢？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) As soon as I get this done. (我一把这个做完（就动身）。)
  - (B) He took it with him. (他把它带在身上。)
  - (C) At around 3 last night. (昨天夜里 3 点左右。)


### Q8 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** What part of Canada do you come from? (你是加拿大哪个地方的人？)
- **A:** I grew up in Kingston. (我在金士顿长大。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Where in Canada are you from? (你是加拿大哪个地方的人呢？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I was born in Kingston. (我出生在金士顿。)
  - (B) Early tomorrow morning. (明天一大早。)
  - (C) No, I don't feel like it. (不，我不喜欢它。)


### Q9 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Excuse me, but may I use your phone? (打扰一下，我可以用你的电话吗？)
- **A:** Be my guest. (请不要客气。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Pardon me, but would it be possible for me to use your phone? (不好意思，我可以用你的电话吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Sure, but you have to dial 9 to call out. (可以，不过你打电话前要先拨 9 。)
  - (B) The phone directory is on the lower shelf. (电话姓名簿在下面的架子上。)
  - (C) There is one on the first floor of this building. (这栋楼的一层有一个。)


### Q10 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How much is the entrance fee? (入场费是多少？)
- **A:** It's ten dollars. (—10美元。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** How much is it to get into the place? (进那里要多少钱？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) There is a ten-dollar cover charge. (需要 10 美元的服务费。)
  - (B) Sure, we can go there if you'd like. (好的，如果你乐意的话，我们可以去那里。)
  - (C) How about going this Saturday? (这周六去怎么样？)


### Q11 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Why don't we grab a cab? (我们为什么不打车呢？)
- **A:** I'd rather walk. (我更想走路。注：在Part 2中，为帮助考生提高听懂题目的能力，添加了和试题相同或相似的表达方法。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Why don't we flag down a cab? (我们为什么不乘出租车？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Let's just go for a walk instead. (我们还是散散步吧。)
  - (B) It's about an hour from here. (从这里过去要一个小时左右。)
  - (C) Because it's a national holiday. (因为是全国性的假日。)


### Q12 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How are you planning to get to Chicago? (你打算怎么去芝加哥？)
- **A:** I'll be taking my car. (我打算自己开车去。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Are you going to take the bus to Chicago? (你打算乘坐巴士去芝加哥吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) The boss told me to. (老板让我去做。)
  - (B) To pick up someone. (去接某人。)
  - (C) No, I am going to drive. (不，我打算开车去。)


### Q13 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Who's planning to come to the party? (谁打算来参加这次派对？)
- **A:** As far as I know, everyone will be there. (据我所知，每个人都会过去。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Who is supposed to show up at the party? (谁应该在派对上露面呢？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Everyone said they'll be there. (每个人都说要来。)
  - (B) He's holding it at a banquet hall. (他正在宴会厅举行派对。)
  - (C) Yes, I had a great time there. (是的，我在那里度过了愉快的时光。)


### Q14 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How long are you planning to be away? (你计划离开多久？)
- **A:** I'm thinking of spending a year abroad. (我在考虑在国外待一年。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** How long are you thinking of going? (你想离开多久？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) For about a year or so. (大约一年。)
  - (B) What's with the long face? (为什么愁容满面？)
  - (C) Yes, I will be going with John. (是的，我将和约翰一起去。)


### Q15 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Why don't we have lunch together? (我们一起吃午饭怎么样？)
- **A:** Can we do it another time instead? (我们可以改天吗？)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Would you like to go for lunch together? (你想一起去吃午饭吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) At the company cafeteria. (在公司食堂。)
  - (B) There are four people in our group. (我们组有四个人。)
  - (C) Thank you, but I am too busy today. (谢谢，不过我今天太忙了。)


### Q16 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Would you like to meet in my office or at a coffee shop somewhere? (你想在我的办公室碰面呢，还是在什么地方的咖啡店呢？)
- **A:** The coffee shop on Main Street sounds good. (主街的咖啡店听起来不错。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Where do you feel like meeting, here in my office or somewhere outside? (你想在什么地方见面，是我办公室这里，还是外面什么地方？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Okay, that sounds like a good place to meet. (可以，那听起来是个不错的见面地点。)
  - (B) How about the little coffee shop on Main Street? (主街的小咖啡店怎么样？)
  - (C) Yes, I think I can spare the time to see you. (是的，我想我可以抽时间见见你。)


### Q17 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** When is your first day at the main office? (你什么时候开始在总公司上班？)
- **A:** I'll start going there from next month. (我下个月开始去那里上班。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** When will you start your new position at the head office? (你什么时候开始到总公司的新岗位上班呢？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) The first of next month. (下个月的 1 号。)
  - (B) At the downtown office. (在位于市中心的办公室。)
  - (C) I'm heading this one. (我正负责这个。)


### Q18 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Wasn't Peter's presentation impressive? (彼得的演讲难道不令人难忘吗？)
- **A:** Yes, it was quite inspiring. (是的，确实很鼓舞人心。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Didn't you think Peter gave a great presentation? (你难道不认为彼得的演讲很棒吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, he was very impressive. (是的，他给人留下了很深刻的印象。)
  - (B) Yes, for three hours. (是的，三个小时。)
  - (C) I already got the present. (我已经收到礼物了。)


### Q19 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How about having Greek food this evening? (今晚吃希腊餐如何？)
- **A:** That sounds very delicious. (听起来很好吃。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Should we try Greek food tonight? (今晚我们尝尝希腊菜怎么样？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, he is from Greece. (是的，他是从希腊来的。)
  - (B) Sure, I'd love to try it. (好的，我乐意去试试。)
  - (C) I didn't go there tonight. (我今晚没有去那里。)


### Q20 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How did Mr. Smith respond to the project? (史密斯先生是如何回应这个项目的？)
- **A:** He seemed very positive about it. (他似乎对它很有信心。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** What did Mr. Smith say about the new project? (史密斯先生对于新项目说了些什么？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) He made some great comments. (他给予了很高的评价。)
  - (B) The projector is in the meeting room. (投影仪在会议室。)
  - (C) Yes, he mentioned it to me. (是的，他向我提起过。)


### Q21 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** How would you like to go for a stroll? (你觉得出去遛个弯怎么样？)
- **A:** Sure, let me put on my jacket first. (好的，让我先穿上夹克。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Would you rather stay here or go for a walk with me? (你是想待在这里，还是想和我出去散散步呢？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I've been waiting for an hour. (我已经等了一个小时了。)
  - (B) Let me get my jacket. (让我去拿夹克。)
  - (C) Yes, I think so. (是的，我认为是这样。)


### Q22 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Who's responsible for putting together the event? (谁负责组织这次活动？)
- **A:** Larry is heading this one. (拉里负责本次活动。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Who put the event together? (谁组织了这次活动？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Larry's the one in charge. (拉里是负责人。)
  - (B) I will put it there later. (我一会儿会把它放到那里。)
  - (C) Sorry, I can't go today. (抱歉，我今天不能去。)


### Q23 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Do you think it'd be better to drive or take the bus? (你觉得是开车还是坐公交车更好呢？)
- **A:** It's probably faster to take a cab. (可能打车会快一点。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Should I take my car, or do you think it would be wiser to take the bus? (我应该自己开车吗，或者你觉得乘公交车是不是更明智一点？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) The boss is a wise man. (老板是个精明人。)
  - (B) Let's just hop in a cab instead. (我们还是打车吧。)
  - (C) It shouldn't take over an hour. (不会超过一小时的。)


### Q24 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Did you not drive to work today? (你今天没有开车来上班吗？)
- **A:** No, I left my car at home. (没有，我把车放在家里了。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Didn't you bring your car to work this morning? (你今天早晨不是开车来上班的吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) No, I took the bus today. (不，我今天是坐公交车来的。)
  - (B) Yes, I will drive you there. (是的，我会开车把你送到那里。)
  - (C) She might be working today. (她今天也许在工作。)


### Q25 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Should I let John know that you came by? (我可以告诉约翰你过来了吗？)
- **A:** Yes, could you? (好的，有劳了。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Can I tell John that you are here? (我可以告诉约翰你在这里吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Sure, that would be okay. (好的，没问题。)
  - (B) Yes, he is here today. (是的，他今天在这里。)
  - (C) No, we are not leaving yet. (不，我们现在还不走。)


### Q26 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** This is great weather to just wander around the beach. (今天天气不错，适合去海边散步。)
- **A:** Yes, I agree with you. (是的，我同意你的说法。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Today is a great day to go for a walk by the beach. (今天是去海边散步的好日子。)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, it is a beautiful day. (是的，今天天气很好。)
  - (B) I didn't know it was raining. (我不知道在下雨。)
  - (C) I went swimming the other day. (我前几天去游泳了。)


### Q27 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Where do you take your car to get it repaired? (你在哪里修的车？)
- **A:** What's wrong with it? (它出了什么毛病？)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Where do you get your car fixed? (你的车是在哪里修的？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I park my car in the underground garage. (我把我的车停在地下车库了。)
  - (B) From a grocery store near my house. (从我家附近的一家杂货店。)
  - (C) Why? Are you having car problems? (怎么了？你的车出毛病了吗？)


### Q28 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Are you going to make the speech today, or will Mr. Smith do it? (今天是你还是史密斯先生要作报告呢？)
- **A:** He's away on a business trip. (他出差了。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Are you making the presentation today, or is Mr. Smith going to do it? (今天是你还是史密斯先生要作报告呢？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) He is going to be here any minute now. (他现在随时都可能到这里。)
  - (B) He told me to take care of it today. (他让我今天负责这次报告。)
  - (C) It is supposed to last until three. (它应该会持续到 3 点。)


### Q29 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** What part of the design do you not like? (这个设计的哪个部分您不喜欢？)
- **A:** The color is not right. (颜色不合适。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** What is it about the design that you don't like? (您不喜欢这个设计的什么地方？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, I need your signature. (是的，我需要您的签名。)
  - (B) That's very kind of you. (您真是太好了。)
  - (C) The color seems to be a bit off. (好像有点掉色。)


### Q30 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Is Peter aware of the fact that Mr. Kim knows why he was late to the meeting? (彼得知道金先生了解他开会迟到的原因吗？)
- **A:** Yes, I told him. (知道，我告诉他了。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Does Peter know that Mr. Kim knows why he was late to the meeting? (彼得知道金先生了解他开会迟到的原因吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) He's been informed. (他已经被告知了。)
  - (B) I was five minutes late. (我迟到了五分钟。)
  - (C) He was stuck in traffic. (他被堵在路上了。)


### Q31 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Did you speak to Cindy today or yesterday? (你是今天还是昨天和辛迪谈的？)
- **A:** She called this morning, but I wasn't here. (她今天上午打电话了，但我当时不在这儿。Questions 32 through 34 refer to the following conversation.M:I can't believe this， but I managed to book a ticket to Singapore.（)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Did you talk to Cindy this morning or last night? (你是今天上午还是昨天晚上和辛迪谈的？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I'm thinking of taking off today. (我想今天请假。)
  - (B) She left a message on my machine. (她在我的电话答录机上留言了。)
  - (C) It may not last that long. (也许不会持续那么久。)


## Part 3: 简短对话 (Q32 - Q70)

### Questions 32 - 34

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** I can't believe this, but I managed to book a ticket to Singapore. (32) I will be on the seven o'clock flight tomorrow morning.
**W:** That's great. Does that mean that you will get to see your friend who moved out there a few years back after you are finished meeting with Mr. Wang? (33)
**M:** I am not sure because Mr. Wang will probably want to take me around the plant site on the day I arrive there. I am hoping that I will be able to see my friend the day after, but he mentioned that he might have to leave town that day. He said he would try to rearrange his trip, but I have not spoken to him for a few days. I will call him tonight to see if he is able to do that.
**W:** You should just take your vacation early and spend a week there after you take care of your business. (34) It's not like you get to travel to the Far East all the time, you know.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**真是难以置信，我成功地订了一张去新加坡的机票。我将乘坐明天早上7点的飞机。
> **W：**太好了。那是不是意味着你与王先生会面后就会去拜访你几年前搬到那儿的朋友？
> **M：**我还不能确定，因为我到达的当天王先生很可能会带我去看厂址。我希望第二天能去拜访我的朋友，但是我的朋友说过他那天也许得离开新加坡。他说他会尽量重新安排旅程，但是我已经几天没和他联系了。我今晚给他打电话，看看他能否重新安排。
> **W：**你处理完事情后应该早点儿去度假，在那儿待上一个星期。你知道，你不是一直可以去远东旅行的。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **manage to do**：成功做（某事）
- **rearrange**：重新安排
- **Far East**：远东
- **overseas**：国外的
- **attend to**：处理
- **matter**：事情，事务

#### Q32 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What will the man do tomorrow? (男士明天将会做什么？)
- (A) Help his friend move into a new place. (帮他的朋友搬到新家。)
- (B) Leave on an overseas business trip. (出发到国外出差。)
- (C) Take Mr. Wang to the factory site. (带王先生去工厂。)
- (D) Prepare for his vacation to the Far East. (为去远东度假做准备。)

#### Q33 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the woman want to know? (女士想知道什么？)
- (A) Whether the man will have enough time to attend to personal matters. (男士是否有足够的时间来处理个人事务。)
- (B) If the man is going to make the sale. (男士是否能做成这笔买卖。)
- (C) How much the new business is going to cost. (新生意将花费多少钱。)
- (D) How long he has known Mr. Wang. (他认识王先生多久了。)

#### Q34 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the woman suggest the man do? (女士建议男士做什么？)
- (A) Go on the trip another time. (改天再去旅行。)
- (B) Take his vacation early. (早点儿去度假。)
- (C) Talk to Mr. Wang right away. (立刻和王先生谈话。)
- (D) Book his ticket early. (早点儿订票。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I managed to book a ticket.** (我成功地订了一张票。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：I was able to reserve a ticket. I reserved a seat on the plane.* (我订到了一张票。我订了一张飞机票。)
- **I have not spoken to him for a few days.** (我已经几天没和他讲话了。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：I have not seen him for a couple of days. I have not talked to him for a while.* (我已经几天没看到他了。我有好一会儿没跟他讲话了。)
- **take care of your business = look after your matters = tend to your affairs** (管好你自己的事情)
  - *例句：John will go with you to Seattle to help take care of your business.* (约翰将与你一起去西雅图，帮你照看生意。)

### Questions 35 - 37

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Welcome back to the office, Greg. How was your trip to Milan?
**M:** It didn't go quite as well as I had expected. I had been hoping the client would sign a contract, but he wants to negotiate more. (35)
**W:** It sounds like you'll be returning there soon.
**M:** Yeah, I'm scheduled to meet Mr. Roberts next Thursday. But I've got to visit Frankfurt before I go back to Milan. (36)
**W:** Good luck. If there's anything I can do to help, all you have to do is ask.
**M:** I'll probably take you up on that offer. I've got two other international customers who need to be visited, but I don't have time. (37)

**中文对照：**
> **W：**欢迎回到办公室，格雷格。你的米兰之行怎么样？
> **M：**没有我预期的那么顺利。我本来希望那位客户能签合同，但是他想要进一步谈判。
> **W：**听起来你很快还会再去米兰。
> **W：**是的。我定好了下个星期四和罗伯茨先生会面。但是去米兰之前我得先去趟法兰克福。
> **W：**祝你好运。如果有什么我能帮忙的，尽管开口。
> **M：**我可能需要你的帮助。我还需要拜访另外两位国际客户，但是我没有时间。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **client**：客户
- **sign a contract**：签订合同
- **negotiate**：谈判
- **schedule**：安排，预定
- **take sb. up on sth**：接受或采纳某人的
- **international**：国际的

#### Q35 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What is the conversation mainly about? (这段对话主要是关于什么的？)
- (A) The woman's assignment. (女士的任务。)
- (B) The branch in Milan. (米兰的分店。)
- (C) The man's client. (男士的客户。)
- (D) A complete negotiation. (一次完整的谈判。)

#### Q36 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What will the man do before visiting Milan? (在去米兰前，男士会做什么？)
- (A) Sign a contract. (签合同。)
- (B) Travel to Frankfurt. (去法兰克福。)
- (C) Negotiate with Mr. Roberts. (和罗伯茨先生谈判。)
- (D) Train the woman. (培训女士。)

#### Q37 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the man suggest about the woman? (从男士的话语中可以推断出女士的什么信息？)
- (A) She will take a trip abroad soon. (她很快将要去国外出差。)
- (B) She needs more work experience. (她需要更多的工作经验。)
- (C) She knows Mr. Roberts personally. (她认识罗伯茨先生本人。)
- (D) She lived in Milan in the past. (她过去住在米兰。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I'm scheduled to meet Mr. Roberts next Thursday. = I plan to meet Mr. Roberts next Thursday.** (我定好了下个星期四和罗伯茨先生会面。)
  - *例句：The abandoned building is scheduled to be torn down this afternoon.* (这栋废弃大楼计划好了今天下午被拆除。)
- **I'll probably take you up on that offer. = I'll probably accept your offer.** (我可能需要你的帮助。)
  - *例句：We will take you up on your invitation.* (我们会接受你的邀请。)

### Questions 38 - 40

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** When do you think you will be able to wrap up the deal with the retail shop owners? (38) I hope it will be soon because we have to start the construction work as soon as possible.
**W:** Well, I had a meeting with them this morning, and things went quite smoothly. If everything goes as planned, I should have all of their signatures by the end of this week. (39)
**M:** Well, I hope so. Otherwise, we will not be able to start the construction work on time, and there is a good chance that we will not be able to have the building ready for the exposition next January.
**W:** Don't worry. I will get the approval this week. And I will make sure the construction work gets underway by next Monday. (40)

**中文对照：**
> **M：**你觉得什么时候可以和零售店的店主们签订协议呢？我希望能快点儿，因为我们得尽快开始施工。
> **W：**我今天上午和他们开了一个会，事情进展得很顺利。如果一切按计划进行，到这个周末我就会拿到他们所有人的签字。
> **M：**嗯，我希望如此。否则，我们就不能按时开始施工，而且很可能我们无法为明年1月份的博览会准备好这栋楼。
> **W：**不要担心。这个周末我会拿到批准，而且我保证下星期一之前工程就会开始。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **wrap up**：最终或成功地解决
- **retail shop**：零售店
- **construction work**：施工
- **smoothly**：顺利地
- **otherwise**：否则
- **on time**：按时
- **exposition**：博览会
- **approval**：同意，批准
- **underway**：在进行中
- **grand opening**：隆重开张
- **let go**：解雇；开除

#### Q38 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What does the man want to know? (男士想知道什么？)
- (A) When the exposition is going to start. (博览会将于什么时候开始。)
- (B) How long the construction will take. (工程将花费多长时间。)
- (C) Where the stores are located. (商店位于哪里。)
- (D) How soon the woman will close the deal. (女士多快能签订合同。)

#### Q39 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** According to the woman, what might happen by the end of this week? (根据女士所说，这周末前可能会有什么事情发生？)
- (A) The shop will have its grand opening. (商店将隆重开张。)
- (B) All of the signatures will be collected. (将收集完所有的签字。)
- (C) Some of the workers will be let go. (一些工人将被解雇。)
- (D) The exposition will open to the general public. (博览会将对大众开放。)

#### Q40 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** According to the woman, when will the construction most likely begin? (根据女士所说，工程最有可能何时开工？)
- (A) This week. (这星期。)
- (B) Next week. (下星期。)
- (C) Before the winter. (在冬季之前。)
- (D) Next year. (明年。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **wrap up the deal = close the deal = finalize the deal** (签订协议)
  - *例句：We really need to wrap up the deal today.* (我们确实需要在今天签订协议。)
- **Things went quite smoothly. = Things went without any problems. = Things went very well.** (事情进展得很顺利。)
  - *例句：I was told that things went quite smoothly last night.* (我被告知昨晚事情进展得很顺利。)
- **if everything goes as planned = if all things go as scheduled** (如果一切按计划进行扩展表达：)
  - *例句：if the entire thing goes as we had anticipated We could be sitting at a beach this time next week if everything goes as planned.* (如果一切按我们预期的进行如果一切按计划进行，下星期的这个时候我们应该会坐在海滩上。)

### Questions 41 - 43

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Jack, I'm sorry to tell you this, but you and I are going to have to work late this evening. The brochures we ordered came in this morning, but there is a problem. Can you believe they forgot to attach our company logo to them? (41)
**M:** You've got to be kidding me. How many brochures are there?
**W:** Well, there are 12 boxes that need to go out first thing tomorrow morning, (43) so you and I are going to have to get them done tonight. （ 41, 42 ）
**M:** Are you kidding me? Couldn't we just send them back and have the printing company do the work?

**中文对照：**
> **W：**杰克，很抱歉地告诉你，今天晚上我们俩得加班了。我们订购的小册子今天早上已经到了，但是有一个问题。你能相信吗，他们居然忘记把我们公司的新商标贴在小册子上了。
> **M：**你在开玩笑吧。一共有多少本小册子？
> **W：**嗯，一共有12箱小册子明天一早就需要发出去。所以我们俩今天晚上得把它们弄好。
> **M：**你在开玩笑吧？难道我们不能直接把它们退回去让印刷公司来做吗？

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **work late**：加班
- **brochure**：小册子
- **attach**：贴上
- **send back**：退回
- **immediate**：立即的，即刻的
- **attention**：注意
- **extra**：额外的

#### Q41 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the woman say to the man? (女士对男士说什么？)
- (A) An error needs their immediate attention. (有个错误需要他们立刻注意。)
- (B) They have been working too hard lately. (他们最近工作太辛苦了。)
- (C) The design of their new company logo is bad. (他们公司的新商标设计得很差。)
- (D) An order they placed has not arrived yet. (他们下的一个订单还没有送到。)

#### Q42 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** How will they solve the problem? (他们将如何解决这个问题？)
- (A) By ordering extra boxes. (订购额外的箱子。)
- (B) By returning the products. (退还商品。)
- (C) By doing the work themselves. (他们自己做这项工作。)
- (D) By finding another company. (找另一家公司。)

#### Q43 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What will happen tomorrow morning? (明天早晨会发生什么事？)
- (A) A new shipment will arrive. (一批新的货物将到达。)
- (B) Some goods will be sent out. (一些商品将被发出。)
- (C) The boxes will be sent back. (箱子将被退回。)
- (D) They will find a new printing company. (他们将找到一家新的印刷公司。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **There are 12 boxes that need to go out first thing tomorrow morning. = There are a dozen boxes that must be sent out first thing tomorrow morning. = There are 12 boxes that have to go out first thing tomorrow morning.** (一共有12箱小册子明天一早就需要发出去。)
- **get them done tonight = finish them this evening = complete them by the end of the day** (今天晚上把它们弄好)
  - *例句：It is crucial that we get them done tonight.* (今天晚上我们要把它们弄好，这一点很重要。)
- **Couldn't we just send them back? = Can't we just return them? = Couldn't we just have them taken back?** (难道我们不能直接把它们退回去吗？)

### Questions 44 - 46

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** I just received a call from Larry from our head office, and he said Mr. Wang can't give the presentation tomorrow at our company's annual conference being held at the Prince Hotel because of a sudden illness in his family. (44) He asked me to take his place at the conference. (45) Would you happen to know if there is a bus or subway that goes directly from here?
**W:** I didn't know that you were going to give a speech there. In fact, Mr. Singh and I are going to be in attendance, and we are planning to drive. If you'd like, you can ride along with us. (46)
**M:** That sounds wonderful. What time will you be taking off?
**W:** We will meet here at 7 since it only takes about an hour to get there. We might even have time for breakfast once we get there.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**我刚刚接到总部的拉里打来的电话，他说王先生因为家人突然生病，明天不能在我公司于王子宾馆举办的年会上作报告了。王先生让我替他在会上作报告。你知道有从这儿直达那里的公交车或地铁吗？
> **W：**我不知道你要去那里作报告。事实上，辛格先生和我也将出席，我们打算开车去。如果你愿意的话，可以坐我们的车一起去。
> **M：**太棒了。你们什么时候出发？
> **W：**因为开车到那里一个小时左右，所以我们打算7点在这儿集合。我们到了那儿甚至还有时间吃早饭呢。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **give a presentation**：做演讲
- **annual**：每年的
- **sudden**：突然的
- **take one's place**：代替某人
- **give a speech**：发言，作报告
- **come down with**：得，染上（病）
- **unexpected**：没有料到的

#### Q44 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Why won't Mr. Wang be able to give the speech? (王先生为什么不能去做报告？)
- (A) He suddenly came down with an illness. (他突然病倒了。)
- (B) He does not have a way to get to the hotel. (他没法到宾馆。)
- (C) He has to attend to a family member. (他必须去照顾一位家庭成员。)
- (D) He has to make an unexpected trip. (他必须参加一次意料之外的旅行。)

#### Q45 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the man imply when he says, “He asked me to take his place at the conference”? (男士说 “ 王先生让我替他在会上作报告 ” ，他在暗示什么？)
- (A) He will drive the woman to the conference. (他会开车把女士送到会场。)
- (B) He will visit Mr. Wang at the hospital. (他会到医院探望王先生。)
- (C) He will fill in for Mr. Wang. (他会代替王先生（作报告）。)
- (D) He will make breakfast for the guests. (他会为客人们做早餐。)

#### Q46 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** How will the man get to the conference? (男士将如何到达会场？)
- (A) By car. (乘小汽车。)
- (B) By train. (乘火车。)
- (C) By bus. (乘公交车。)
- (D) By airplane. (乘飞机。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **He asked me to take his place. = He asked me to fill in for him. = He asked me to do it instead.** (他让我代替他。)
  - *例句：He asked me to take his place at the meeting because something urgent has come up.* (因为有紧急的事情发生，他让我代替他参加会议。)
- **be going to be in attendance = will be present = be going to be there** (将出席)
  - *例句：Most of the people I know are going to be in attendance.* (我认识的大部分人都将出席。)
- **You can ride along with us.** (你可以坐我们的车一起去。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：You can come with us. = You can tag along with us. If you don't have a way to get there, you can ride along with us.* (你可以和我们一起来。如果你没法去那里，可以坐我们的车一起去。)

### Questions 47 - 49

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** We are short of staff today. Why don't you call up some of the part-time workers and see if they can work today? We are expecting a massive crowd to swarm us tonight since a great review got printed in today's local paper.
**M:** Is that why we are getting so many calls? I couldn't figure out why the phone was ringing off the hook.
**W:** I didn't know about it either, but one of the customers told me that he came after reading the review. (48) He also complimented us on the great food we serve here. (47)
**M:** That's good to hear. All the renovation work we did here and hiring the new chef we scouted from France are really paying off. (49)

**中文对照：**
> **W：**我们今天缺人手。你为什么不打电话通知一些兼职员工，看看他们能不能今天来工作？因为今天的地方报纸上有一篇很棒的评论，所以我们预计今晚会有大量顾客蜂拥而来。
> **M：**那就是我们接到这么多电话的原因吗？我想不通为什么电话总是响个不停。
> **W：**我也不知道为什么。但是其中有一位顾客告诉我他是读完这篇评论后过来的。他也称赞了我们所提供的美味食物。
> **M：**听起来不错。我们在这儿做的所有整修以及聘请从法国找来的新厨师真是物有所值啊。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **be short of staff**：缺人手
- **call up**：打电话
- **massive**：大量的
- **swarm**：蜂拥
- **review**：评论
- **figure out**：想明白
- **ring off the hook**：电话响个不停
- **compliment**：称赞
- **renovation**：整修
- **scout**：寻找
- **pay off**：物有所值，取得成功

#### Q47 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Where do they most likely work? (他们最有可能在哪里工作？)
- (A) A newspaper company. (报社。)
- (B) A restaurant. (餐馆。)
- (C) A phone company. (电话公司。)
- (D) A travel agency. (旅行社。)

#### Q48 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** How did the woman learn about the news? (女士是怎么知道消息的？)
- (A) By reading it in a paper. (在报纸上读到的。)
- (B) From a co-worker. (从同事那里获知的。)
- (C) One of the customers told her. (一位顾客告诉她的。)
- (D) She overheard the chef talking. (她无意中从厨师那里听说的。)

#### Q49 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What have they done to improve their business? (他们做了什么来改善他们的生意？)
- (A) They took out an ad in the local paper. (他们在当地报纸上登了广告。)
- (B) They contacted their existing customers. (他们联系了已有的顾客。)
- (C) They provided food samples to their guests. (他们向客人们提供了食物样品。)
- (D) They hired a new professional cook. (他们雇了一位新的专业厨师。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **We are short of staff today. = We don't have enough people today. = We are lacking staff today.** (我们今天缺人手。)
- **We are expecting a massive crowd to swarm us tonight. = We are anticipating a lot of people to come tonight. = We are predicting a large number of people to turn out this evening.** (我们预计今晚会有大量顾客蜂拥而来。)
- **I couldn't figure out why the phone was ringing off the hook. = I couldn't understand why there were so many calls. = I couldn't make out the reason why the phone was ringing so much.** (我想不通为什么电话总是响个不停。)

### Questions 50 - 52

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Will you be making the trip out to Los Angeles next Monday?
**W:** I was planning to, but something has come up, (50) so I was contemplating whether or not I should delay my trip to the week after. Why do you ask?
**M:** My brother who moved to France five years ago is coming to LA next week on a business trip, so I was thinking of going out there to see him. (51) And since I heard you are going, I thought maybe we could drive down together.
**W:** That sounds like a good idea. I do have to make a trip there, and it would be nice to have some company. Hmm...tell you what, I will see what I can do to take the trip next week after all. (52) Let me give you a shout with the details after lunch today.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**下星期一你要去洛杉矶旅行吗？
> **W：**原本打算去的，但发生了一些事情，所以我正在考虑是否应该将旅行推迟到一周以后。你为什么这么问呢？
> **M：**我有个五年前移居法国的哥哥下星期出差去洛杉矶，所以我想去那儿看望他。因为听说你要去，所以我原想我们可以一起开车去。
> **W：**这个主意听起来不错。我是得去那儿旅行，而且能有同伴一起去很好。嗯…我说，我看看能做些什么以便下个星期能出发。今天午饭后我再和你细谈吧。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **come up**：发生
- **contemplate**：考虑
- **drive down**：开车过去
- **company**：同伴
- **tell you what**：（用以提出建议）我说
- **keep ~ company**：与相伴，陪
- **accompany**：陪伴

#### Q50 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Why is the woman thinking of postponing her trip? (为什么女士在考虑推迟她的旅行？)
- (A) She is not feeling well. (她觉得不舒服。)
- (B) Her car is in need of repairs. (她的汽车需要修理。)
- (C) She has something else to attend to. (她需要处理其他事情。)
- (D) Her brother is coming to see her. (她哥哥要来看她。)

#### Q51 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Why will the man take the trip? (男士为什么要去旅行？)
- (A) To meet his brother. (去看望他的哥哥。)
- (B) To attend an important meeting. (去参加一次重要的会议。)
- (C) To keep the woman company. (去陪伴女士。)
- (D) To meet his client. (去会见他的客户。)

#### Q52 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the woman say she will let the man know about? (女士说她会告诉男士什么？)
- (A) If she can go away with the man or not. (她是否可以和男士一起去。)
- (B) When she will be able to get back from LA. (她什么时候可以从洛杉矶回来。)
- (C) How many people she will be going on the trip with. (她将和多少人一起去旅行。)
- (D) Who will be accompanying her on the trip. (谁将陪伴她一起去旅行。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I was planning to do = I was thinking to do = I was meaning to do** (我原本打算做)
  - *例句：I was planning to drive there.* (我原本打算开车到那里。)
- **I was contemplating ~ = I was thinking about ~ = I was pondering about ~** (我正在考虑…)
  - *例句：I was contemplating the situation, and I think I have figured out the answer.* (我正在考虑这个情况，并觉得我已经想出答案了。)
- **It would be nice to have some company. = It would be nice to have someone beside me.** (能有同伴一起去很好。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：It would be nice to have somebody to talk to. It would be nice to have some company for a change.* (能有人一起聊聊天很好。改变一下，有同伴一起去很好。)

### Questions 53 - 55

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Wilma, are you planning to e-mail me those documents anytime soon? The staff meeting is thirty minutes from now. (54)
**W:** I sent them to you more than two hours ago. Didn't you get them?
**M:** Apparently not. I just checked my e-mail, and nothing has arrived all morning. (53)
**W:** We could be having problems with the company-wide computer server. I'll give someone in the Maintenance Department a call right now.
**M:** Okay, but before you do that, how about printing the documents and then bringing them to me? (55) I need to look over them at once.
**W:** No problem. You'll have them in two minutes.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**威尔玛，你会尽快将那些文件发到我电子邮箱吗？三十分钟后员工会议就开始了。
> **W：**我两个多小时前就发给你了。你没收到吗？
> **M：**显然没有收到。我刚查看了邮箱，整个早上没收到任何邮件。
> **W：**我们公司内部的计算机服务器可能出问题了。我马上给维修部的工作人员打个电话。
> **M：**好的，但是在你打电话前，你先把文件打印了拿给我怎么样？我需要马上看一下。
> **W：**没问题。两分钟之后给你。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **document**：文件
- **staff meeting**：员工会议
- **apparently**：显然地
- **server**：服务器
- **Maintenance Department**：维修部
- **look over**：检查

#### Q53 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What is the man's problem? (男士的问题是什么？)
- (A) He cannot log on to his computer. (他无法登录他的电脑。)
- (B) An e-mail has not arrived. (一封电子邮件尚未收到。)
- (C) An appointment was just canceled. (刚刚取消了一个预约。)
- (D) He forgot about a staff meeting. (他忘记了员工会议。)

#### Q54 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Why does the man need some documents? (为什么男士需要一些文件？)
- (A) He has a meeting to attend. (他将要参加一个会议。)
- (B) He needs to check them for mistakes. (他需要检查文件是否有错。)
- (C) He has to mail them to a customer. (他必须把文件邮寄给客户。)
- (D) He needs to sign them. (他需要在文件上签字。)

#### Q55 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the man request the woman to do first? (男士请女士先做什么？)
- (A) Repair some machinery. (修理一些机器。)
- (B) Contact a technician. (联系一位技术人员。)
- (C) Print some papers. (打印一些文件。)
- (D) Schedule a meeting. (安排一场会议。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **How about ~ = What about ~ …** (怎么样)
  - *例句：How about going out for a walk?* (出去散步怎么样？)
- **I need to look over them at once. = I need to examine them at once.** (我需要马上看一下。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：look through* (浏览)

### Questions 56 - 58

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** You didn't forget to call the Maintenance Department to take a look at our machine, did you? (56)
**W:** I made the call to Jack as soon as I got into work at 9 this morning, (56) but he said he had many rounds to make today. (57) According to him, the earliest he can come is around 4.
**M:** That's a bit late. I have an appointment with Mr. Smith at 5, and it will take me at least an hour to get there. (58) We need someone here to explain the problem to him.
**W:** My meeting with my client got canceled. I'll stick around and tell Jack about the problem. You go right ahead and meet Mr. Smith.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**你没忘记给维修部打电话让他们来检查我们的机器吧？
> **W：**我今天早上9点钟一上班的时候就给杰克打了电话，但是他说他今天要去巡查很多地方。按他的意思，他最早下午4点左右能来。
> **M：**那有点儿晚了。我和史密斯先生约好5点钟碰面，去那儿路上至少要花一个小时。我们需要找人留在这里把问题解释给杰克听。
> **W：**我和客户的会面取消了。我会待在这儿和杰克谈这个问题。你去见史密斯先生吧。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **maintenance**：维护，维修
- **take a look at ~**：检查
- **at least**：至少
- **stick around**：逗留
- **go right ahead**：请便
- **drop by**：顺道拜访
- **take care of**：处理

#### Q56 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Who most likely is Jack? (杰克最有可能是谁？)
- (A) A co-worker. (一位同事。)
- (B) A client. (一位客户。)
- (C) The mechanic. (机械师。)
- (D) The department head. (部门领导。)

#### Q57 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Why will Jack come late? (杰克为什么会迟到？)
- (A) He has many places to visit. (他得去很多地方。)
- (B) He has a long way to drive to get there. (他到那里要开很久的车。)
- (C) He has to drop by a client's office first. (他得先顺道去一位客户的办公室。)
- (D) He has a personal problem to take care of. (他有件私事需要处理。)

#### Q58 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** When will the man most likely leave for his appointment? (男士最有可能在什么时候动身赴约？)
- (A) At 1. (1 点。)
- (B) At 4. (4 点。)
- (C) At 5. (5 点。)
- (D) At 9. (9 点。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **You didn't forget to call ~ = You remembered to call ~** (你没忘记给…打电话)
  - *例句：You didn't forget to call the client about the order, did you?* (你没忘记给客户打电话说定单的事，对吧？)
- **has many rounds to make today** (今天要去巡查很多地方扩展表达：)
  - *例句：has many places to go has many deliveries to make Jack is out because he has many rounds to make today.* (有许多地方要去有许多货物要投递杰克出去了，因为他今天要去巡查很多地方。)
- **I'll stick around. = I'll hang around. = I'll wait around.** (我会待在这里。)
  - *例句：I'll stick around here until Ms. Taylor shows up.* (我会待在这儿直到泰勒女士露面。)

### Questions 59 - 61

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M1:** Wendy, are you still planning to order some items from the office supply store? (59)
**W:** That's correct. Do you need me to add anything to the list? You'd better do it by three.
**M1:** Okay. I noticed we're out of file folders and could use some ink for the printer, too. I'll e-mail the details to you. (59)
**W:** Thanks, Brian. I'll check my inbox before I submit the order form.
**M2:** Oh, I could use a few things as well, (59) but I've got to attend a meeting. It's not going to finish until four. (60)
**W:** I suppose I can wait until then, Mr. Lopez. Just get me the list as quickly as you can. (61)

**中文对照：**
> **M1：**温迪，你还在计划从办公用品店订购一些东西吗？
> **W：**是的。你还有什么需要添加到清单上吗？你最好三点之前完成。
> **M1：**好的。我注意到我们的文件夹用完了，还需要一些打印机的墨水。我会把具体信息用邮件发给你。
> **W：**谢谢，布瑞恩。在提交订单之前，我会查看我的收件箱。
> **M2：**哎呀，我也想要一些东西。但是我得参加一个会议，要到四点才能结束。
> **W：**我想我可以等到那时候，洛佩兹先生。只要尽快把清单给我就行。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **item**：（尤指清单上的）一项，一条
- **supply store**：供应商店
- **file folder**：文件夹
- **inbox**：收件箱
- **submit**：上交，呈交
- **attend**：出席，到场

#### Q59 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What do the men want the woman to do? (两位男士想让这位女士做什么？)
- (A) Give them some folders. (给他们一些文件夹。)
- (B) Go to a store with them. (和他们一起去商店。)
- (C) Order some items for them. (帮他们订购一些商品。)
- (D) Tell them about the budget. (告诉他们预算。)

#### Q60 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What will Mr. Lopez do at four? (洛佩兹先生要在四点做什么？)
- (A) Finish a meeting. (结束会议。)
- (B) Visit a website. (访问一个网站。)
- (C) Check his inbox. (查看他的收件箱。)
- (D) Print some copies. (打印一些副本。)

#### Q61 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** Why does the woman say, “I suppose I can wait until then”? (这位女士为何说 “ 我想我可以等到那时候 ”？)
- (A) To ask Brian to e-mail her later. (让布瑞恩稍后给她发邮件。)
- (B) To express her desire to hurry. (表达她的急切之情。)
- (C) To mention when she will leave. (提及她离开的时间。)
- (D) To tell Mr. Lopez to send her a list. (告诉洛佩兹先生给她发清单。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I could use a few things as well = I also want a few things.** (我也想要一些东西。)
  - *例句：I could use a drink.* (我先要瓶饮料。)
- **be out of sth.** (没了，用完了)
  - *例句：We're out of milk.* (我们的牛奶喝完了。)

### Questions 62 - 64

![Page 172](images/listen_page_172.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Mr. Venters has granted everyone in our department permission to attend the trade fair this Friday. (62)
**W:** That's wonderful news. I'll be out of town, so I can't make it, (62) but I'm sure many people are eager to go.
**M:** That's right. I already asked around, and seventeen people indicated they'll be going. (63) I'll be registering everyone later today.
**W:** I don't think we've ever had that many people attend a professional event.
**M:** More people are focusing on networking these days, and trade fairs are some of the best places to do that. (64)
**W:** I suppose you're right. In that case, it's a real shame I can't go. Stratford Trade Fair Registration Price List

**中文对照：**
> **M：**文特斯先生允许我们部门所有人参加本周五的商品交易会。
> **W：**这个消息太棒了。我要去趟其他城市，所以我去不了，但是我确信很多人都想去。
> **M：**对。我已经问了一圈人，17个人表示他们要去。今天晚些时候，我会为每个人报名。
> **W：**我想我们之前从来没有那么多人参加过一次专业的活动。
> **M：**如今更多人关注建立人际关系，商品交易会是建立人际关系的最佳场所之一。
> **W：**我想你是对的。那样的话，我无法去真的是个遗憾。斯特拉福德商品交易会报名价格表

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **grant**：给予，授予
- **permission**：许可，允许
- **make it**：成功做到
- **indicate**：表示，指出
- **register**：报名，注册
- **professional**：专业的，职业的
- **focus on**：专注于，关注
- **networking**：建立人际关系

#### Q62 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What will the woman do on Friday? (周五女士要做什么？)
- (A) Give a speech. (发表演讲。)
- (B) Receive professional training. (接受专业培训。)
- (C) Travel to another city. (去另外一个城市。)
- (D) Lead an orientation session. (主持岗前培训会。)

#### Q63 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. How much will it cost for each person in the department to register? (请看图表，部门每个人的报名费是多少？)
- (A) $70. (70 美元。)
- (B) $85. (85 美元。)
- (C) $95. (95 美元。)
- (D) $105. (105 美元。)

#### Q64 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** Why does the man say many people want to attend the event? (根据男士所说，为什么有许多人想要参加这次商品交易会？)
- (A) To listen to some speeches. (为了听一些演讲。)
- (B) To have a chance to get out of the office. (为了有机会离开办公室。)
- (C) To improve their skills. (为了提高技能。)
- (D) To meet other people in the industry. (为了见行业中的其他人。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **it's a shame ~ = it's a pity ~** (很遗憾…)
  - *例句：It's a shame that you missed the marvelous concert tonight.* (你错过了今天晚上精彩的音乐会，真的很可惜。)

### Questions 65 - 67

![Page 173](images/listen_page_173.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Hello. This is Cindy Wells. I've got an appointment with a dentist tomorrow at 3:30 p.m., but I'm in lots of pain. Is it possible to see someone today? (65)
**M:** I'm sorry to hear that, Ms. Wells. According to the schedule, we have one open slot today. It's at 1:00 p.m. (66) However, it won't be with your regular dentist.
**W:** That's fine. I don't believe I can wait until tomorrow.
**M:** Okay, I'll go ahead and cancel your Tuesday appointment then. (66) Oh, could you please bring your insurance card? (67)
**W:** Why do you need it? I thought you already had my records.
**M:** We're upgrading the computer system today, so we can't go online until tomorrow. Dental Clinic Schedule

**中文对照：**
> **W：**您好。我是辛迪·维尔斯。我预约了明天下午3点半看牙医，但是我现在疼得厉害，今天有可能看医生吗？
> **M：**听到这个消息，我表示很同情，维尔斯女士。根据日程安排，今天我们还有个时间段没有约满，时间是下午1点。不过，出诊的不是您平时的牙医。
> **W：**可以的。我觉得我等不到明天了。
> **M：**好的，我这就把您周二的预约取消。哦，请把您的医保卡带上。
> **W：**为什么需要医保卡？我想你们已经有我的医保记录了。
> **M：**今天我们的电脑正在升级系统，所以，我们明天才能上网。牙医诊所日程安排

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **appointment**：安排，预约
- **dentist**：牙医
- **slot**：（节目或时间表里的）时间段
- **regular**：常规的，经常的
- **cancel**：取消
- **insurance**：保险
- **upgrade**：升级

#### Q65 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What is the purpose of the woman's call? (女士打电话的目的是什么？)
- (A) To schedule a checkup. (预约体检。)
- (B) To change an appointment. (更改预约。)
- (C) To confirm the time of her appointment. (确认预约时间。)
- (D) To say she will be a bit late. (表示她要晚到一会儿。)

#### Q66 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Which dentist will the woman see? (请看图表，女士将会看哪一位牙医？)
- (A) William Norby. (威廉姆 · 诺比。)
- (B) Janet Snead. (珍妮特 · 斯尼德。)
- (C) Patricia Chang. (帕特丽夏 · 张。)
- (D) Mark Greene. (马克 · 格林尼。)

#### Q67 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the man tell the woman to bring? (男士告诉女士带上什么？)
- (A) An insurance document. (医保证件。)
- (B) Some X-rays. (一些 X 光片。)
- (C) A referral from another dentist. (另一位牙医的诊断参考。)
- (D) Her medical records. (她的就诊记录。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **make an appointment = have an appointment** (预约)
  - *例句：You should phone his secretary if you want to make an appointment.* (如果你想预约，你应当给他的秘书打电话。)

### Questions 68 - 70

![Page 173](images/listen_page_173.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Deanna, you picked up the order from the grocery store, right?
**W:** That's correct. I went in the morning before I showed up for work. Is there a problem?
**M:** Yeah, it looks like we didn't get enough flour. There were only ten kilograms in the box. (69) That's not enough to bake all the cakes and cookies which our customers ordered today. (68)
**W:** Keith told me that was how much we needed. I guess he made a mistake.
**M:** Actually, we need double that amount. (69) Would you mind going back and purchasing some more? Be sure to get a receipt so I can pay you back. (70)
**W:** All right. I should return in half an hour. Invoice

**中文对照：**
> **M：**迪安娜，你从杂货店提取了订购的货物，是吧？
> **W：**是的。我早上上班之前去了趟那里，有什么问题吗？
> **M：**对，我们的面粉好像不够了。箱子里只剩下10公斤，不够烤制今天顾客订购的所有蛋糕和饼干。
> **W：**基思跟我说我们就需要那么多。我猜他弄错了。
> **M：**其实，我们需要双倍的量。你介意回去一趟，再多买一些吗？记着要收据，我好给你报销。
> **W：**好的。我半个小时后就回来。发票

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **pick up**：取，拿
- **grocery store**：杂货店
- **show up**：露面
- **bake**：烤，烘焙
- **cookie**：饼干
- **customer**：顾客，客户
- **purchase**：购买
- **receipt**：收据

#### Q68 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Where most likely do the speakers work? (说话者们最可能在哪里工作？)
- (A) At a bakery. (面包店。)
- (B) At a grocery store. (杂货店。)
- (C) At a café. (咖啡馆。)
- (D) At a restaurant. (餐馆。)

#### Q69 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Which item does the man request more of? (对照图表，男士要求多买一些的是哪一种商品？)
- (A) TT505. (TT505 。)
- (B) RA122. (RA122 。)
- (C) OA905. (OA905 。)
- (D) FF598. (FF598 。)

#### Q70 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the man tell the woman to do? (男士告诉女士要做什么？)
- (A) Call the grocery store. (给杂货店打电话。)
- (B) Order something online. (在网上订购一些物品。)
- (C) Ask for a receipt. (要收据。)
- (D) Pay with a credit card. (用信用卡付款。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **make a mistake = make an error** (犯错，弄错)
  - *例句：It is hard not to make a mistake in any test.* (在任何考试中，不犯错是很难的。)

## Part 4: 简短独白 (Q71 - Q100)

### Questions 71 - 73

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Welcome to Yellow Submarine Apartments. We are going to give you a guided tour of this new seaside apartment complex, which incorporates many radical new architectural and lifestyle innovations. Whether you are interested in buying a retirement or holiday home, a main residence, or even an investment property, we at the Yellow Submarine Consortium can offer you some stunning properties at excellent prices. (71) Let's move into the foyer. Here and in the basement car park, friendly security staff members ensure your complete security twenty-four hours a day. (72) As you can see from the foyer, only the finest quality materials have been used in combination with the superb design. All the apartments, even on the first floor, have views over the ocean. (72) Okay, let's take the elevator to our display apartment on the eighth floor. (73)

**中文对照：**
> 欢迎来到黄色潜艇公寓。我们将带您参观一下这座新建的海滨公寓楼，它融入了许多重大的且新颖的建筑和生活方式上的创新。不管您是想买养老房还是度假房，主要居所还是投资性房产，我们黄色潜艇财团都能为您提供一些价格优惠的绝佳房产。让我们进入大厅。在这里以及地下停车场，友好的保安们会保证您一天24小时的绝对安全。您从大厅可以看得出来，我们只用最优质的材料，并使之与一流的设计相结合。所有的公寓（即使是在一楼），都可以看到海景。好的，现在让我们乘电梯去8层的样板公寓。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **guided tour**：有导游的参观
- **seaside**：海滨的
- **incorporate**：融入
- **radical**：激进的；重大的
- **architectural**：建筑的
- **innovation**：创新，革新
- **retirement home**：养老房
- **holiday home**：度假房
- **property**：房产
- **stunning**：极好的
- **foyer**：大厅
- **friendly**：友好的
- **security**：安全
- **ensure**：确保
- **combination**：结合，联合
- **superb**：极好的，一流的
- **architect**：建筑师
- **tenant**：租户
- **round-the-clock 24**：小时的，全天候的
- **breathtaking**：惊人的，心旷神怡的
- **first-rate**：一流的
- **unit**：单元

#### Q71 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** Who is the intended audience of this talk? (讲话的目标听众是谁？)
- (A) The architects. (建筑师。)
- (B) The security staff. (保安。)
- (C) The apartment tenants. (公寓的房客。)
- (D) Would-be homebuyers. (潜在的购房者。)

#### Q72 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** Which of the following is NOT part of the new apartment complex? (下列哪项不是新公寓楼的一部分？)
- (A) Round-the-clock security. (24 小时保安。)
- (B) A breathtaking view of the sea. (令人心旷神怡的海景。)
- (C) A first-rate design. (一流的设计。)
- (D) A large balcony in each unit. (每个单元的大阳台。)

#### Q73 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Where will they head next? (他们将前往哪里？)
- (A) To the ground-floor lobby. (到底层的大厅。)
- (B) To the eighth-floor apartment. (到 8 层的公寓。)
- (C) To the basement garage. (到地下车库。)
- (D) To the front yard. (到前院。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **can offer you some stunning properties at excellent prices = can provide you with some excellent properties at amazing prices = can propose some great properties at very reasonable prices** (能为您提供一些价格优惠的绝佳房产)
  - *例句：You are very lucky because we can offer you some stunning properties at excellent prices.* (您非常幸运，因为我们能为您提供一些价格优惠的绝佳房产。)
- **Only the finest quality materials have been used. = Only the best quality materials have been used. = Only the top quality materials have been used.** (只有最优质的材料才会被使用。)
  - *例句：You will be glad to know that only the finest quality materials have been used to make the products.* (你将会很高兴地得知，只有最优质的材料才会被用来制造这些产品。)

### Questions 74 - 76

**听力独白/对话原文：**
The CTV annual speech contest is a prestige competition with a tradition going back twenty-five years. (74) The winner of the first competition, held in 1981, was Brian McAdams, (75) now a well-known television journalist and anchorman for CTV. We'd like to remind you that the highest standards will be expected of all contestants at all times. However, we'd also like to say that the benefits of participating are enormous even if you don't win. A pre-competition round of selections will be held here next Monday—that's June the sixth— beginning at 8:00 p.m. So, please fill in your entry form, and we'll see you back here next Monday. (76) Thanks! CTV

**中文对照：**
> 年度演讲比赛是一个享有盛誉的比赛，有着25年的传统。布赖恩·麦克亚当斯是1981年第一届比赛的冠军，他现在是CTV著名的电视记者和新闻节目主播。我们想提醒大家，所有的参赛者在任何时候都要表现出最高的水准。不过，我们也还是想说，即使你在比赛中不能获胜，参加这项比赛的收获还是很多的。赛前选拔环节将于下星期一——也就是6月6日在这里举行，选拔从晚上8点开始。所以请填写报名表，下星期一在这里见。谢谢！

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **prestige**：威望，声望
- **competition**：比赛，竞赛
- **tradition**：传统
- **journalist**：记者
- **anchorman**：新闻节目（男）主播
- **contestant**：选手
- **at all times**：一直
- **enormous**：巨大的
- **round**：环节
- **entry form**：报名表
- **judge**：评委
- **compete in ~**：参加比赛
- **in person**：亲自

#### Q74 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** How old is the speech contest? (这项演讲比赛有多久的历史了？)
- (A) One year old. (1 年。)
- (B) Five years old. (5 年。)
- (C) Ten years old. (10 年。)
- (D) Twenty-five years old. (25 年。)

#### Q75 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the speaker imply when he says, “The winner of the first competition, held in 1981, was Brian McAdams”? (讲话者说 “ 布赖恩 · 麦克亚当斯是 1981 年第一届比赛的冠军 ” ，他在暗示什么？)
- (A) Brain's dream is to become a news anchor. (布莱恩的梦想是成为一名新闻节目主持。)
- (B) Brain will be one of the judges at the contest. (布莱恩将成为比赛的评委之一。)
- (C) Brain competed in the first ever contest. (布莱恩参加了第一届比赛。)
- (D) Brain has been the host of the contest since the first show. (从第一期节目开始，布赖恩就是这项比赛的主持人。)

#### Q76 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What should those who wish to participate in the contest do? (那些想参加比赛的人应该做什么？)
- (A) Come down to the station in person. (亲自到电视台来。)
- (B) Fill out a document. (填写一份文件。)
- (C) Call the television station. (给电视台打电话。)
- (D) Log on to the website. (登录网站。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **with a tradition going back twenty-five years = with a tradition dating back twenty-five years = with a twenty-five year tradition** (有着25年的传统)
- **a well-known television journalist and anchorman for CTV = a famous television journalist and anchorman for CTV = an acclaimed television journalist and anchorman for CTV** (中视著名的电视记者和新闻节目主播)

### Questions 77 - 79

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Hi, Mark. I've been trying to contact you by e-mail, but for some reason you have not responded. (77) This is Julie, the secretary of the Choral Society. I hope you receive this message in time. We've had to cancel tonight's rehearsal at the last minute. (78) If for some reason you don't get this message tonight, I apologize—there won't be anybody else at the hall this evening. I hope you understand that our conductor is unable to attend because of some urgent family business, (79) and we've decided to postpone the rehearsal until next week. I can't really give you any more details at the moment, but I'll let you know in the next few days. See you soon.

**中文对照：**
> 你好，马克。我一直试着通过电子邮件联系你，但是由于某种原因你还没有回复。我是合唱协会的秘书朱莉。我希望你能及时收到这条留言。在最后一刻我们不得不取消今天晚上的排练。如果出于某种原因今晚你没收到这条信息，我向你道歉——今天晚上大厅里不会有其他人的。我希望你能理解，我们的指挥因为一些紧急的家事无法来了。我们已经决定把排练推迟到下星期。现在我真的不能提供更多的详情，但是过几天我会让你知道的。再见。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **respond**：回复
- **in time**：及时
- **at the last minute**：在最后一刻
- **conductor**：指挥
- **urgent**：紧急的
- **postpone**：推迟
- **detail**：细节
- **whereabouts**：行踪，下落
- **affair**：事情

#### Q77 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** How did the woman first try to get in contact with Mark? (女士一开始试图通过什么方式联系马克？)
- (A) By phone. (通过电话。)
- (B) By e-mail. (通过电子邮件。)
- (C) By mail. (通过信件。)
- (D) By fax. (通过传真。)

#### Q78 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What is the message mainly about? (这则留言主要是关于什么的？)
- (A) The cancellation of their meeting tonight. (取消他们今晚的集会。)
- (B) A new addition to their choral group. (他们合唱团的一个新成员。)
- (C) The conductor's wish to meet more regularly. (指挥希望他们能更频繁地见面。)
- (D) The last minute details before the performance. (演出前最后的细节。)

#### Q79 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What happened to the conductor? (指挥遇到什么事情？)
- (A) No one knows his whereabouts. (没有人知道他的行踪。)
- (B) He had to attend to some personal affairs. (他必须去处理一些个人事务。)
- (C) He has been waiting in the hall for a long time. (他在大厅里等了很长时间。)
- (D) He has not attended any of the rehearsals. (他从来没有参加过任何排练。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **For some reason you have not responded. = For an unknown reason you have not provided an answer. = For a certain reason you have not gotten back to me.** (由于某种原因你还没有回复。)
  - *例句：I have left several messages on your answering machine regarding the order, but for some reason you have not responded yet.* (关于订单，我在你的电话答录机上留了几次言，但是由于某种原因你还没有回复。)
- **at the last minute = at the last second = at the last moment** (在最后一刻)
  - *例句：I changed my mind at the last minute.* (我在最后一刻改变了主意。)
- **We've decided to postpone the rehearsal.** (我们已经决定推迟排练。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：We've decided to hold off the rehearsal for a while. We've decided to put off the rehearsal until another time.* (我们已经决定暂时推迟排练。我们已经决定把排练推迟到其他时间。)

### Questions 80 - 82

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Tonight truly marks a milestone in the history of this association. When it was created 100 years ago with the intention of encouraging the conservation of English culture, (80) who would have thought that it would not only survive but also prosper until the present day? From one club with 36 members meeting in one venue in England, we have grown into a nationwide association of 50 clubs with over 600 members. (81) And the annual prize for a special contribution to English culture, which has been made possible by the generosity of our local businessmen, has become one of the nation's most prestigious awards. (82)

**中文对照：**
> 今晚的确是本协会历史上里程碑式的时刻。当100年前为鼓励保护英国文化创建本协会时，谁会想到这个协会不仅能存活到今天，而且还一直在蓬勃发展？它从最初拥有36名会员、在英格兰某处聚会的俱乐部，发展成为拥有超过600名会员、50个俱乐部的全国性协会。由我们本地商人慷慨资助的年度英国文化特别贡献奖已经成为国家最有声望的奖项之一。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **truly**：确实地，的确
- **mark**：标志
- **milestone**：里程碑
- **association**：协会
- **intention**：目的
- **encourage**：鼓励
- **conservation**：保护
- **survive**：活下来
- **prosper**：繁荣，昌盛
- **venue**：集合地
- **nationwide**：全国性的
- **contribution**：贡献
- **generosity**：慷慨
- **prestigious**：有声望的
- **preserve**：保护
- **custom**：（社会）习俗
- **playtime**：娱乐时间

#### Q80 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What was the original purpose in creating this club? (创建这个俱乐部的最初目的是什么？)
- (A) To preserve English custom. (保护英国的社会习俗。)
- (B) To provide playtime for the rich. (为富人提供娱乐。)
- (C) To encourage people to compete. (鼓励人们相互竞争。)
- (D) To introduce businessmen to each other. (介绍商人们相互认识。)

#### Q81 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** How many members does the club now have? (俱乐部现在有多少名会员？)
- (A) 36. (36 名。)
- (B) 50. (50 名。)
- (C) 100. (100 名。)
- (D) Over 600. (超过 600 名。)

#### Q82 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Who sponsors the nation's most prestigious awards? (赞助这一全国最具声望的奖项的是谁？)
- (A) Local businessmen. (当地的商人。)
- (B) The government. (政府。)
- (C) The club president. (俱乐部主席。)
- (D) The members. (会员们。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **Tonight truly marks a milestone in the history of this association.** (今晚的确是本协会历史上里程碑式的时刻。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：Tonight is really special in the association's long history. This evening clearly characterizes the achievements we have made in our association's long history.* (今晚的确是本协会悠久历史上一个特别的时刻。无疑，今晚体现了我们协会在其悠久历史中所取得的成就。)
- **with the intention of ~ = with the meaning to ~ = with the purpose of ~** (为了…，怀着…的目的)
  - *例句：I came here with the intention of winning your vote today.* (我今天来的目的是为了赢得你们的选票。)
- **Who would have thought that ~? = Who could have guessed that ~? = Who could have imagined that ~?** (谁能想到…？)
  - *例句：Who would have thought that I would be standing here talking about my achievements in front of all of you?* (谁能想到我会站在你们所有人面前谈论我的成就呢？)

### Questions 83 - 85

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Welcome to the Goldfields Tour! We have about a one-hour bus trip through beautiful rolling hills before we reach the first stop on our tour, (83) the picturesque and historic town of Daylesford. When we reach Daylesford, I suggest that we simply stroll around the old town for around thirty minutes to an hour. Daylesford was founded at the time of the first gold rush and is largely unchanged (84) since the boom period of the 1880s. Why don't you stop at one of the famous bakeries on the main street for some delicious coffee and cakes? (85) Return to the bus by 11:00 a.m., and we will proceed with the rest of the tour. Thank you.

**中文对照：**
> 欢迎参加金地之旅！旅途的第一站是风景如画、历史悠久的戴尔斯福德城，在此之前，我们要坐约一个小时的巴士，沿途可以欣赏连绵起伏的美丽丘陵。到了戴尔斯福德，我建议大家围绕这座老城逛30分钟到1小时左右。戴尔斯福德建造于第一次淘金热的时候，从19世纪80年代的繁荣时期以来大体上就没有什么变化。你们为什么不顺便去主街上一家有名的面包店品尝美味的咖啡和蛋糕呢？上午11点之前请回到巴士，我们将继续下面的旅程。谢谢。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **rolling**：连绵起伏的
- **picturesque**：风景如画的
- **stroll**：闲逛，溜达
- **gold rush**：淘金热
- **boom**：繁荣，景气
- **proceed**：继续
- **destination**：目的地，终点
- **bottom**：底部
- **resemble**：像，类似
- **seclude**：使隔离，使孤立

#### Q83 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** When will they arrive at their first destination? (他们将于什么时候到达第一个目的地？)
- (A) In ten minutes. (10 分钟后。)
- (B) In twenty minutes. (20 分钟后。)
- (C) In thirty minutes. (30 分钟后。)
- (D) In about sixty minutes. (大约 1 小时后。)

#### Q84 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the speaker mention about Daylesford? (关于戴尔斯福德，讲话人提到了什么？)
- (A) It is at the bottom of a hill. (它在一座山的山脚下。)
- (B) It still resembles the gold rush days. (它依然很像淘金热时代的样子。)
- (C) It has become a large city. (它已经变成了一座大城市。)
- (D) It is secluded from other cities. (它与其他城市隔绝。)

#### Q85 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the speaker mean when he says, “Why don't you stop at one of the famous bakeries”? (讲话者说 “ 你们为什么不顺便去一家有名的面包店呢 ” ，是想表达什么意思？)
- (A) The listeners should drop by the bakeries. (听众应该顺便去一下面包店。)
- (B) The listeners should check out the hills. (听众应该看看这里的丘陵。)
- (C) The listeners should buy some cheap gold. (听众应该买一些便宜的金子。)
- (D) The listeners should check out the historical building. (听众应该看看历史建筑。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **simply stroll around = casually walk around = freely get around** (在周围随意逛逛)
  - *例句：You will have an hour to simply stroll around the museum at your leisure.* (空闲时你有1个小时的时间在博物馆周围随意逛逛。)
- **We will proceed with the rest of the tour. = We will continue on with the rest of the tour. = We will go ahead with the rest of the tour.** (我们将继续下面的旅程。)

### Questions 86 - 88

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Excuse me, ladies and gentlemen. I hope you enjoyed your meal. Personally, I found it to be an absolute feast, and I'd like to thank the organizers for their marvelous work. It's time to move on to the more formal part of the evening, which comprises the awards for journalist and photojournalist of the year. (86) This year has been a particularly dark and dangerous one for journalists working in war zones. (87) I can only say how much I admire and respect those courageous writers and photographers who have risked death and even torture in order to bring the truth to the world. Would everyone please give a big round of applause for our chief editor? He is going to present our first award. (88)

**中文对照：**
> 女士们，先生们，打扰一下。我希望这顿饭菜能合你们的胃口。就我个人而言，我觉得这绝对是一次盛宴，我要谢谢筹办方了不起的工作。现在该进行今晚较为正式的环节了，包括为年度记者和摄影记者颁奖。今年对于在战区工作的记者们来说是极其黑暗和危险的一年。我只能说我有多么钦佩和尊重那些勇敢的记者和摄影师们，他们为了把真相告诉世人，冒着死亡甚至酷刑的危险。大家可以用热烈的掌声欢迎我们的主编吗？他将给颁发我们的第一个奖项。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **personally**：就个人而言
- **absolute**：绝对的
- **feast**：盛宴
- **organizer**：组织者
- **marvelous**：了不起的
- **formal**：正式的
- **comprise**：包含，包括
- **journalist**：记者
- **photojournalist**：摄影记者
- **particularly**：格外地
- **courageous**：勇敢的
- **torture**：酷刑，折磨

#### Q86 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What is the purpose of the talk? (这次讲话的目的是什么？)
- (A) To present awards to the best journalists. (给最优秀的记者颁奖。)
- (B) To thank the organizer for preparing the event. (感谢筹办方为这一活动所作的筹备工作。)
- (C) To welcome the listeners to a company dinner function. (欢迎听众参加公司的盛宴。)
- (D) To reveal the truth about some war secrets. (揭示一些战争机密的真相。)

#### Q87 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Why does the speaker say that this year has been particularly tough? (为什么讲话人说今年格外艰难？)
- (A) Many of the journalists had to go to war. (许多记者不得不赶赴战场。)
- (B) He lost some of his closest colleagues. (他失去了一些最亲密的同事。)
- (C) The newspaper company had a hard time. (报刊公司经历了困难时期。)
- (D) The writers could not write freely. (作者们不能自由地写作。)

#### Q88 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Who is going to make the first presentation? (谁将会颁发第一个奖项？)
- (A) The head editor. (主编。)
- (B) The speaker. (讲话人。)
- (C) The event organizer. (活动的筹办方。)
- (D) One of the journalists. (其中的一位记者。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **Excuse me, ladies and gentlemen.** (女士们，先生们，打扰一下。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：May I have your attention, ladies and gentlemen? = Attention, ladies and gentlemen.* (女士们，先生们，请注意。)
- **It's time to move on to the more formal part of the evening. = It's time to move on to the official part of the night.** (现在该进行今晚更为正式的环节了。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：It's time to get on with the night's events.* (现在该进行今晚的活动了。)

### Questions 89 - 91

![Page 177](images/listen_page_177.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Hello, this is Michael Kruger from Kruger's Family Delicatessen. We've just received a delivery from your company, (89) but on inspection we have found that an entire pallet of tinned anchovies has been damaged. (90) It looks like they fell at some time during transportation. Some of the tins have broken and are leaking oil. Many others are dented. We can't possibly accept them at the agreed price. We've already spent two hours cleaning up dripping oil. Either we can return them to you and you can deduct the costs from your next invoice, or we'll accept them at a substantial discount. Why don't you send a sales representative? (91) We need to sort this out as soon as possible. Thanks.

**中文对照：**
> 您好，我是克鲁格家庭熟食店的迈克尔·克鲁格。我们刚刚收到从贵公司发来的一批货。但是在检查时我们发现一整托盘的凤尾鱼罐头都已经坏掉了。看起来它们在运输的时候掉下来过。一些罐头盒已经摔坏了，正在漏油。许多其他的罐头盒凹了下去。我们不能按原来商定的价格接受它们。我们已经花了两个小时清洗滴下来的油。要么我们把货物寄回给你们，你们可以在下一次的发票上扣除这次的成本，要么给我们多打些折扣以便我们接受。你们为什么不派一个销售代表过来呢？我们需要尽快解决这件事情。谢谢。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **delicatessen**：熟食店
- **inspection**：检查
- **entire**：全部的
- **pallet**：（装卸、搬运货物用的）托盘，货板，集装架
- **tinned**：罐头的，听装的
- **anchovy**：凤尾鱼
- **transportation**：运输
- **leak**：泄漏
- **dent**：凹陷
- **clean up**：清理
- **drip**：滴下
- **deduct**：扣除
- **substantial**：大量的
- **sort out**：解决
- **steep**：（价格等）过高的，不合理的
- **replacement**：替代品
- **leakage**：泄漏物

#### Q89 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Who is leaving the message? (谁在留言？)
- (A) A customer. (顾客。)
- (B) A delivery staff member. (货运工。)
- (C) The food inspector. (食品检查员。)
- (D) A cleaning staff member. (清洁工。)

#### Q90 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What is the problem? (问题是什么？)
- (A) The speaker is running late with the delivery. (讲话人送货晚点了。)
- (B) The price of the goods is a bit too steep. (货物的价格有点过高了。)
- (C) The sales representative is not available now. (销售代表现在不在。)
- (D) Some damaged goods have been delivered. (一些损坏的货物被运了过来。)

#### Q91 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the caller demand the listener do? (打电话的人让听者做什么？)
- (A) Return the product. (退回商品。)
- (B) Bring replacements. (拿来替代品。)
- (C) Send someone over. (派人过来。)
- (D) Clean up the leakage. (把泄漏物清理掉。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **We've just received a delivery from your company. = We've just gotten the products delivered from your firm. = We just got the order delivered from your company.** (我们刚刚收到从贵公司发来的一批货。)
- **but on inspection = but while checking = but when we were looking over** (但是（我们）在检查时)
  - *例句：The products were delivered but on inspection we found some broken items.* (产品被送过来了，但是我们在检查时发现其中一些已经破损。)
- **We need to sort this out as soon as possible. = We need to solve this as soon as possible. = We need to find a solution for this as soon as possible.** (我们需要尽快解决这件事情。)

### Questions 92 - 94

![Page 178](images/listen_page_178.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Our Sales Department has a particularly proud record since the founding of the company in 1946. (92) Starting out just after the Second World War, our company employed three traveling salesmen and a national sales manager to expand our operations aggressively throughout North America. Of course, we couldn't have done that without top quality products to sell. On the other hand, without sales and a hungry sales staff, the company would not have been able to survive, let alone expand as it has done in the last sixty years. (93) You have been chosen from a field of sixty applicants to continue that tradition, (94) and we have faith that through your energy and positive attitude we will be able to continue our expansion to markets all over the world.

**中文对照：**
> 从公司1946年成立以来，我们销售部取得了特别值得骄傲的成绩。我们公司在二战结束不久创建的时候，雇用了三名旅行推销员和一名全国销售经理，将我们的经营范围扩张到整个北美洲。当然，没有最优质的产品出售，我们也不会取得这样的成绩。但从另外一方面来说，如果没有销售部和积极的销售人员，公司根本就不可能生存下来，更不用说在过去60年间所做的扩张了。我们从60名应聘者中挑了你们去延续这一传统。我们相信通过你们的努力和积极的态度我们一定能将市场扩大到全世界。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **particularly**：特别地
- **proud**：骄傲的
- **traveling**：旅行的
- **national**：全国的
- **operation**：经营；营运
- **aggressively**：积极地，有闯劲地
- **top quality**：一流的质量
- **on the other hand**：另一方面
- **survive**：生存
- **applicant**：应聘者
- **tradition**：传统，惯例
- **faith**：信心，信念
- **positive**：积极的
- **attitude**：态度
- **credit**：功劳
- **founder**：缔造者，创造人
- **veteran**：老兵

#### Q92 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** For about how long has the company been in business? (公司已经运营多久了？)
- (A) Over 6 years. (6 年多。)
- (B) Over 40 years. (40 多年。)
- (C) Over 60 years. (60 多年。)
- (D) Over 100 years. (100 多年。)

#### Q93 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Who does the speaker give credit for the company's success? (谁最有可能在听这个讲话？)
- (A) The sales team. (退伍军人。)
- (B) The company founder. (销售经理。)
- (C) The investors. (工厂工人。)
- (D) The operations manager. (新雇员。)

#### Q94 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** Who most likely is listening to the talk? (讲话者把公司的成功归功于谁？)
- (A) War veterans. (销售团队。)
- (B) Sales managers. (公司的创始人。)
- (C) Factory workers. (投资人。)
- (D) New employees. (运营经理。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **on the other hand** (另一方面扩展表达：)
  - *例句：on the contrary = in opposition On the other hand, we could always come back a day earlier.* (与此相反，反之另一方面，我们总是可以早一天回来。)
- **We have faith that ~ = We believe that ~ = We trust that ~** (我们相信…)
  - *例句：We have faith that you will do well at your assigned job.* (我们相信你会做好分配给你的工作。)

### Questions 95 - 97

![Page 178](images/listen_page_178.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Thank you for coming to this meeting, everyone. We need to discuss the sales data from the first quarter which was released this morning. (95) Our branches in Europe and Asia did exceptionally well. Every single one of them turned a profit in the last three months. (96) As for our American and Canadian branches, they were mostly profitable as only a couple places lost money. Now, as for our South American branches, we didn't do as well as we had hoped. Take a look at this chart here. I'd like to discuss each country individually, starting with the one which lost the greatest amount of money. (97) South American Branches First Quarter Performance

**中文对照：**
> 感谢大家来出席本次会议。下面，我们需要讨论一下今天早上公布的第一季度销售数据。集团在欧洲和亚洲的分公司做得非常出色。过去三个月以来，欧洲和亚洲的每一家分公司都处于盈利状态。同时，位于美国和加拿大的分公司基本上也处于盈利状态，仅在少数地区公司存在亏损。相比之下，我们在南美洲的分公司则表现得有些不尽人意。我们不妨来看一下下列图表。我想逐一讨论和这几个国家的情况，先从亏损最严重的开始吧。南美国家分公司第一季度销售情况

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **the first quarter**：第一季度
- **release**：公布
- **branch**：分公司
- **exceptionally**：极其，非常
- **profitable**：盈利的
- **individually**：单独地

#### Q95 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What is the speaker mostly talking about? (说话人主要在说什么？)
- (A) Expansion plans. (扩张计划。)
- (B) Financial losses. (经济损失。)
- (C) A sales report. (销售报告。)
- (D) The company's workforce. (公司的全体人员。)

#### Q96 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the speaker say about the branches in Europe? (关于欧洲的分公司，说话者说了什么？)
- (A) They were all profitable. (全部处于盈利状态。)
- (B) Some of them lost money. (有些处于亏损状态。)
- (C) Many employees transferred to them. (很多员工调到了那里。)
- (D) A few of them closed. (一些关门了。)

#### Q97 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Which country will the speaker discuss next? (请看图表，说话人接下来要讨论哪一个国家？)
- (A) Brazil. (巴西。)
- (B) Argentina. (阿根廷。)
- (C) Venezuela. (委内瑞拉。)
- (D) Ecuador. (厄瓜多尔。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **take a look at = have a look at = have a glance at = get a load of** (看一下)
  - *例句：She was greatly tempted to take a look at it.* (她非常想看一看。)

### Questions 98 - 100

![Page 179](images/listen_page_179.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Hello. My name is Richard Armstrong. You may recall that I picked up a few books at your store this afternoon. I need to report a slight problem with one. When I opened the plastic wrapper to read the book, I noticed that several pages in it were torn. (98) Since it cost me $25, (99) I'd really like to have my money refunded or receive a brand-new copy. I'll be visiting the store again tomorrow with the book, (100) but I thought that I ought to call ahead of time so that you'll be expecting me. Thanks a lot. Goodbye. Thank you for shopping at Peterman's Books

**中文对照：**
> 您好，我叫理查德·阿姆斯特朗。或许您还记得，我今天下午在您的店里挑了几本书。其中一本书有点儿小问题。我打开塑料包装想要看书的时候，注意到里面有几页破损了。毕竟这本书是我花了25美元买的，所以非常希望您能全额退款或者再给我一本全新的书。明天我会把这本书带到店里，不过在此之前，我想还是应该先给您打个电话，这样您会知道我要过去。谢谢您，明天见。感谢您光临彼得曼书店

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **recall**：回忆起
- **pick up**：买到；捡起
- **plastic wrapper**：塑料包装
- **refund**：退款
- **brand-new**：全新的
- **ahead of time**：提前

#### Q98 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What problem does the speaker mention? (说话人提到了什么问题？)
- (A) He bought the wrong book. (他买错书了。)
- (B) Some pages are ripped. (有些页撕破了。)
- (C) A cover is torn. (封皮有破损。)
- (D) There is writing in a book. (书中有字迹。)

#### Q99 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Which book has a problem? (对照图表，哪本书有问题？)
- (A) What Do They Call Her? (《他们叫她什么？》。)
- (B) The Man from the Zoo. (《这个男人来自动物园》。)
- (C) A Short History of Greece. (《希腊简史》。)
- (D) All about Geology. (《地质学大发现》。)

#### Q100 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the speaker say he will do tomorrow? (说话人说他明天会做什么？)
- (A) Make an order. (下订单。)
- (B) Call again. (再打一次电话。)
- (C) Go to the store. (去书店。)
- (D) Purchase an item. (买一件东西。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **ahead of time = in advance** (提前)
  - *例句：If there is any change about the time of the meeting, please notify us in advance.* (开会时间如有变，请提前告知我们。)

## Part 1: 照片描述 (Q1 - Q6)

### Q1 (正确答案：A)

![Page 181](images/listen_page_181.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) He is sitting near the corner. (他正坐在角落附近。)
- (B) He is wearing a long-sleeved shirt. (他穿着一件长袖衬衫。)
- (C) He is riding in his car. (他在开他的汽车。)
- (D) He is folding the paper in half. (他在将纸对折。)

**其他可能表达：**
- He is writing in his notebook. (他在他的笔记本上写字。)
- He is using a pen to jot something down. (他正用钢笔记录着什么。)
- The man is busy writing in his notepad. (男士正忙着在他的笔记本上写字。)


### Q2 (正确答案：B)

![Page 181](images/listen_page_181.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) She's fishing off the edge of the boat. (女士正在船边钓鱼。)
- (B) She's leaning against a railing. (女士正靠在栏杆上。)
- (C) She's out for a walk on a trail. (女士正在小路上散步。)
- (D) She's bending over to pick up something. (女士正在弯腰捡东西。)

**其他可能表达：**
- She is holding on to the railing. (她正抓着栏杆。)
- Some people are standing close to the railing. (一些人正站在栏杆附近。)
- The people have boarded a ship. (人们已经上了船。)


### Q3 (正确答案：D)

![Page 181](images/listen_page_181.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) One woman is reserving a room at the hotel. (一位女士正在宾馆订房间。)
- (B) The guests are checking out of their rooms. (客人们正在退房。)
- (C) The hotel clerks are standing in front of the hotel. (宾馆服务员正站在宾馆的前面。)
- (D) The lamps have been turned on. (灯已经被打开了。)

**其他可能表达：**
- The hotel clerks are helping some customers. (宾馆服务员正在为一些客人服务。)
- They're standing at the hotel front desk. (他们正站在宾馆前台旁边。)
- The room is brightly lit. (房间被照得很亮。)


### Q4 (正确答案：A)

![Page 182](images/listen_page_182.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) The man is attending to a patient. (男士正在照顾病人。)
- (B) The patient is getting up from the chair. (病人正在从椅子上起来。)
- (C) The man is putting on his gloves. (男士正在戴手套。)
- (D) The patient is looking out the window. (病人正在朝窗外看。)

**其他可能表达：**
- The dentist is treating a patient. (牙医正在为病人治疗。)
- The patient is being worked on. (病人正在接受治疗。)
- The man is seeing a patient. (男士正在为病人看病。)


### Q5 (正确答案：B)

![Page 182](images/listen_page_182.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) The workers have finished for the day. (工人们做完了一天的工作。)
- (B) The men are working outdoors. (男士们正在户外工作。)
- (C) One man is pushing the wheelbarrow. (一位男士正在推手推车。)
- (D) One man is planting trees by the hillside. (一位男士正在山坡上种树。)

**其他可能表达：**
- The men are digging the earth. (男士们正在挖土。)
- The men are using shovels. (男士们正在用铲子。)
- The men are loading dirt into the wheelbarrow. (男士们正在往手推车上装土。)


### Q6 (正确答案：C)

![Page 182](images/listen_page_182.png)

**听力原文与选项：**
- (A) They're setting the table. (他们正在布置餐桌。)
- (B) They're ready to order their meals. (他们准备好要点餐了。)
- (C) They're conversing over a meal. (他们正在边吃边聊。)
- (D) They're talking about their colleagues. (他们正在谈论他们的同事。)

**其他可能表达：**
- They are enjoying a meal together. (他们正在一起用餐。)
- The woman is gesturing with her hands. (女士正在做手势。)
- They are both wearing eyeglasses. (他们都戴着眼镜。)
- 注：在Part 1中，每道试题都添加了3种可能的正确表达方式，考生可
- 以了解对于同样的照片可能出现的不同表达。


## Part 2: 应答测试 (Q7 - Q31)

### Q7 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Would you care for something to drink while you wait? (你在等待的时候想喝点什么吗？)
- **A:** Sure, I'll have a cup of coffee, please. (当然，请给我一杯咖啡。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Would you like some coffee while you wait? (你在等待的时候想喝点咖啡吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, two copies please. (好的，请给我两份。)
  - (B) Yes, if it's not too much trouble. (好的，如果不太麻烦的话。)
  - (C) No, I only got here five minutes ago. (不，我刚到这里五分钟。)


### Q8 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Who is handling the overseas assignment? (谁负责处理海外的工作？)
- **A:** Mr. Simpson has been put in charge of it. (辛普森先生被安排负责这项工作。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Who got the overseas assignment? (谁得到了海外的工作？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Ms. Simpson did. (辛普森女士得到了。)
  - (B) That's great. (那太好了。)
  - (C) A day after tomorrow. (明天之后的某一天。)


### Q9 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** When do you want me to go? (你想让我什么时候走呢？)
- **A:** How about after lunch? (吃完午饭怎么样？)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** When should I leave? (我应该什么时候动身？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Let's say goodbye here. (我们就在这里道别吧。)
  - (B) He is on his way over. (他在过来的路上。)
  - (C) Take off right after lunch. (吃完午饭就走吧。)


### Q10 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Would you happen to have an extra key to the storage room? (你有没有多余的储藏室钥匙？)
- **A:** The caretaker should have a spare. (门房应该有备用钥匙。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Do you have a spare key to the storage room? (你有储藏室的备用钥匙吗？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) He usually keeps it there. (他通常把它放在那里。)
  - (B) There is plenty of room now. (现在有足够的空间。)
  - (C) Go and ask the caretaker. (去问问门房。)


### Q11 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Which do you think would be a quicker way to travel, the bus or the subway? (你觉得乘公交车或地铁哪个更快一点呢？)
- **A:** Probably the subway. (也许是地铁吧。注：在Part 2中，为帮助考生提高听懂题目的能力，添加了和试题相同或相似的表达方法。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Would it be faster to take the subway or bus at this time of the day? (在一天的这个时段，是乘地铁快呢，还是乘公交车快？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I know the way there. (我知道怎么去那里。)
  - (B) I'd say the subway. (我认为是地铁快。)
  - (C) He's an hour late. (他迟到了一个小时。)


### Q12 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Which bus goes to the planetarium? (哪路公交车去天文馆呢？)
- **A:** Bus Number 12. (—12路车。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Where can I catch a bus to the planetarium? (我从哪里可以坐去天文馆的公交车呢？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) It will arrive in ten minutes. (它将在 10 分钟后到达。)
  - (B) He went there yesterday. (他昨天去那里了。)
  - (C) At the stop over there. (在那边的车站。)


### Q13 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Why didn't you ask for a hand? (你为什么没找人帮忙呢？)
- **A:** I wanted to do it myself. (我曾想自己做。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Why didn't you get some help? (你为什么不让别人帮你呢？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) I thought I could handle it on my own. (我原以为自己能处理。)
  - (B) No, but I might be able to help you out. (不，不过我也许可以帮你。)
  - (C) He didn't say anything to me. (他什么都没对我说。)


### Q14 (正确答案：B)

  - (B) Yes, but I will be late. (是的，不过我可能会晚去一会儿。)
  - (C) At the big plant. (在大工厂那里。)


### Q15 (正确答案：C)

  - (B) In his big office. (在他的大办公室。)

  - (B) No, I am still working on it. (没有，我还在写呢。)

### Q27 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**

- **A:** Yes, but he moved out of the city. (是的，不过他搬到其他城市去了。)

- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, until he moved to another city. (是的，直到他搬到另一个城市。)
  - (B) He often uses it at the workplace. (他经常在工作场所使用它。)
  - (C) Yes, at the Customs Office. (是的，在海关办公室。)


### Q28 (正确答案：C)

**听力对话文本：**

- **A:** I'll take care of them now. (我现在就去办。)

**听力原文与选项：**

- **选项：**
  - (A) Sure, I'll bring you a cup. (好的，我会给你拿个杯子过来。)
  - (B) I had many opportunities. (我有很多机会。)
  - (C) I'll make them right away. (我这就去办。)


### Q29 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**

- **A:** Yes, I left the message on your desk. (打了，我把留言放到你的桌子上了。)

**听力原文与选项：**

- **选项：**
  - (A) Yes, it's on your desk. (有的，在你的桌子上。)
  - (B) He left an hour ago. (他一个小时之前走的。)
  - (C) I will pass it on to him. (我会把这个转交给他。)


### Q30 (正确答案：A)

**听力对话文本：**
