- **A:** No, we're still searching. (没有，我们还在寻找。)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** Do you know if we hired anyone to take over Mr. Peterson's job? (你知道我们是否雇人去接手彼得森先生的工作了？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) The position is still up for grabs. (这个职位现在还空缺。)
  - (B) I heard he is going into retirement. (我听说他要退休了。)
  - (C) I'll take it over to him myself. (我会亲自把这个给他送过去。)


### Q31 (正确答案：B)

**听力对话文本：**
- **Q:** Why don't we send Jenny a card to thank her for everything she has done for us? (我们为什么不送珍妮一张贺卡来感谢她为我们所做的一切呢？)
- **A:** That is very thoughtful. (你考虑得很周到。Questions 32 through 34 refer to the following conversation.M: I couldn't attend the meeting this morning.Do you know when we aresupposed to show up at the restaurant this evening？（)

**听力原文与选项：**
- **问题：** How about showing our appreciation by sending Jenny a thank-you card? (送珍妮一张感谢贺卡来表达我们的感激，怎么样？)
- **选项：**
  - (A) Thank you. I appreciate it. (谢谢你。我很感激。)
  - (B) That's a wonderful gesture. (那是一个很棒的举动。)
  - (C) The post office is not far. (邮局不太远。)


## Part 3: 简短对话 (Q32 - Q70)

### Questions 32 - 34

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** I couldn't attend the meeting this morning. Do you know when we are supposed to show up at the restaurant this evening? (32)
**W:** Well, Jack told everyone to be there by 7:00. (32) He also said for any of us to call him if we are going to be late.
**M:** Is that right? I have been asked to drop off some packages at our head office by Mr. Johnson, and I am not sure if I will be able to make it there on time. (33)
**W:** You know, if you are driving out there now, your best bet is to call Jack. (34) Highway 10 usually gets pretty jammed during the time you come back.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**我今天上午不能参加会议了。你知道今晚我们应该什么时候到达饭店吗？
> **W：**嗯，杰克说所有人应该在7∶00前到那里。他还说如果我们当中谁要晚到的话就给他打电话。
> **M：**是吗？约翰逊先生让我到总公司送些包裹，我不确定能否准时赶到饭店。
> **W：**哦，如果你要现在开车过去的话，最好还是给杰克打个电话吧。你回来的时段，10号路通常会很拥堵。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **be supposed to do**：应该
- **show up**：出现，露面
- **package**：包裹
- **on time**：准时
- **the best bet**：上策，最佳选择
- **jam**：塞满，堵塞
- **prompt**：准时的
- **errand**：差事
- **in advance**：提前

#### Q32 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What did Jack say? (杰克说什么了？)
- (A) Everyone must attend the meeting. (每个人都必须出席会议。)
- (B) Be prompt in arriving at the restaurant. (要准时到达饭店。)
- (C) Think about what they want to eat. (想想他们要吃些什么。)
- (D) Leave early to avoid terrible traffic. (早点出发以避开交通堵塞。)

#### Q33 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the man have to do? (男士得做什么？)
- (A) Run an errand. (替人跑腿。)
- (B) Buy a gift. (买件礼物。)
- (C) Call the head office. (给总公司打电话。)
- (D) Head over to the restaurant. (赶往饭店。)

#### Q34 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the woman suggest the man do? (女士建议男士做什么？)
- (A) Go to the head office another time. (换个时间再去总公司。)
- (B) Call Jack in advance. (提前给杰克打电话。)
- (C) Attend the earlier meeting. (参加再早一点的会议。)
- (D) Take public transportation. (乘坐公共交通工具。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **when we are supposed to show up = when we have to be there = when they are expecting us** (我们应该到达的时间)
- **I will be able to make it there on time. = I will most likely be there on time. = I won't be late.** (我能准时赶到那里。)
- **get pretty jammed = get pretty crowded = get quite congested** (变得非常拥堵)
  - *例句：The highway gets pretty jammed during rush hour.* (在高峰时段，公路会非常拥堵。)

### Questions 35 - 37

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Okay, let me see if I have everything straight here. Your flight is due to arrive next Tuesday on June 20 at 4:50 p. m. You will spend one night at the Hilton Hills and be on the 11 o'clock flight out to London, right?
**M:** That's correct. I will spend a night in Paris (35) to meet with Mr. Chretien the first thing Wednesday morning to settle a couple of things before I set out to London to close a deal with Mr. Charles Connery. (37) I need you to make sure you have all the documents ready for me when I get there. (36)
**W:** No problem. I've also called Mr. Chretien and told him that you would be coming to see him, and he said he would have all the necessary documents ready for you as well.
**M:** That's great. I have a gut feeling that I am going to land this contract. I feel very good about it.

**中文对照：**
> **W：**好的，让我看看我是否把一切都弄清楚了。您的航班定于下星期二，也就是6月20日下午4∶50抵达。您将在希尔顿山庄度过一晚，然后乘坐11点的航班到伦敦，是吧？
> **M：**对的。我将在巴黎度过一个晚上，周三上午第一件事情是与克雷蒂安先生解决一些事情，然后我将动身去伦敦与查尔斯·康纳里先生达成一项交易。我需要你确保在我到达那里的时候，你能够把所有文件都准备好。
> **W：**没问题。我也给克雷蒂安先生打过电话了，我告诉他您将去见他，他说他也会准备好您需要的所有文件。
> **M：**很好。我有种直觉，我将能签订这份合同。我对此感觉很好。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **due (to)**：预定的，应到的
- **correct**：正确的
- **settle**：完成，解决
- **set out**：动身
- **necessary**：必要的
- **as well**：也
- **gut feeling**：直觉，感应
- **land a contract**：得到合同，签订合同

#### Q35 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** How many nights will the man spend in France? (男士将在法国度过几个晚上？)
- (A) One. (一个。)
- (B) Two. (两个。)
- (C) Three. (三个。)
- (D) Four. (四个。)

#### Q36 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the man mean when he says, “I need you to make sure you have all the documents ready for me when I get there”? (男士说 “ 我需要你确保在我到达那里的时候，你能够把所有文件都准备好 ” ，是想表达什么意思？)
- (A) The woman should prepare all the necessary papers in advance. (女士应该提前准备所有的文件。)
- (B) The woman should call Mr. Connery to make an appointment. (女士应该给康纳里先生打电话预约。)
- (C) The woman should book a flight ticket to London. (女士应该预订去伦敦的机票。)
- (D) The woman should reserve a room at the Hilton Hills. (女士应该在希尔顿山庄预订一个房间。)

#### Q37 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Why is the man making the trip to London? (男士为什么要去伦敦？)
- (A) To meet up an old friend. (去会见一位老朋友。)
- (B) To close a deal. (去达成一项交易。)
- (C) To find his parents' land. (去找他父母的住处。)
- (D) To pick up some documents. (去取一些文件。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **settle = finalize = make things right** (完成，解决)
  - *例句：I have to settle the dispute once and for all.* (我必须彻底解决这次争执。)
- **set out to London to close a deal** (去伦敦达成一项交易扩展表达：)
  - *例句：leave for London to finalize a contract take off for London to get the agreement in writing I have to set out to London to close a deal this afternoon.* (去伦敦敲定一项合同去伦敦签订书面协议今天下午我必须去伦敦达成一项交易。)
- **I have a gut feeling that I am going to land this contract.** (我有种直觉，我将能签订这项合同。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：I am sure that I will be able to sign this contract. I have a gut feeling that ... = I have an inner feeling that ...* (我确信我能够签订这份合同。我有种直觉…)

### Questions 38 - 40

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** We're impressed with your prior experience and feel that you have a great deal of potential, so we'd like to hire you for the open position in the Research Department. (38)
**M:** Will I receive both the salary and the benefits we discussed when we met previously?
**W:** That's correct. You'll also get an annual performance bonus. We'd like you to start working on February 1.
**M:** I think that should be possible, but it depends upon my being able to find an apartment since I'll be coming from Cleveland. (39)
**W:** We have an employee who assists new workers who have to move from out of town.
**M:** Could you give me that person's telephone number, please? (40)

**中文对照：**
> **W：**我们对您以前的经验印象深刻，觉得您有很大的潜力，所以我们想聘请您去研究部门任职。
> **M：**我的薪水和福利是之前我们面谈的那样吗？
> **W：**是的。您还会有年度绩效奖金。我们希望您能于2月1日开始上班。
> **M：**我想应该没问题，但是得看我是否能找到公寓，因为我要从克利夫兰搬过来。
> **W：**我们有工作人员负责帮助从外地搬过来的新员工。
> **M：**您能给我那个人的电话号码吗？

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **be impressed with**：对印象深刻
- **prior**：先前的
- **potential**：潜力
- **open position**：空缺的职位
- **Research Department**：研究部门
- **previously**：先前地
- **annual**：年度的
- **performance bonus**：绩效奖金

#### Q38 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the woman offer the man? (女士给男士提供了什么？)
- (A) A job. (工作。)
- (B) A pay raise. (加薪。)
- (C) A subsidized home. (安家补贴。)
- (D) Improved benefits. (更好的福利。)

#### Q39 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What does the man say about Cleveland? (关于克利夫兰，男士说了什么？)
- (A) He has traveled there in the past. (他曾去过那里。)
- (B) He was born there. (他出生于那里。)
- (C) He does not mind working there. (他不介意在那里工作。)
- (D) He currently lives there. (目前他住在那里。)

#### Q40 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the man request? (男士需要什么？)
- (A) Some contact information. (一些联系信息。)
- (B) A written contract. (一份书面合同。)
- (C) Assistance finding a home. (帮助找房子。)
- (D) A performance bonus. (绩效奖金。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **a great deal of = a lot of = plenty of** (很多（修饰不可数名词）)
  - *例句：He has given me a great deal of help. a great number of* (他给了我很多帮助。扩展表达:很多（修饰可数名词）)
- **depend upon = depend on** (依赖，取决于)
  - *例句：Remember, happiness doesn't depend upon who you are or what you have; it depends solely upon what you think.* (请记住，幸福不在于你是谁或者你拥有什么，而仅仅取决于你的心态。)

### Questions 41 - 43

![Page 186](images/listen_page_186.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** I am expected to give a speech in front of all the directors in half an hour. （ 41, 42 ） I'd better go upstairs to the conference room and get all the necessary equipment ready.
**W:** Do you need any help? I could probably give you a hand setting up the projector or something.
**M:** That's very nice of you, Jan. In fact, I could use more copies of these figures. (43) Do you mind?
**W:** No, not at all. I will get them ready and bring them up to the conference room right away. (43)

**中文对照：**
> **M：**半小时后，我要在所有的主任前面作报告。我最好上楼去会议室，调试好所有必需的设备。
> **W：**你需要帮忙吗？我也许可以帮你装好投影仪或者其他设备。
> **M：**你太好了，简。实际上，我可能会用到更多份这些数据的复印件。你介意帮我复印吗？
> **W：**不，一点都不介意。我这就去准备，然后立刻把它们送到楼上会议室。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **give a speech**：作报告，发言
- **necessary**：必需的
- **equipment**：设备
- **give a hand**：帮忙
- **set up**：装配，调试
- **mind**：介意
- **not at all**：一点也不
- **upper-level**：更高级别的
- **assist**：协助
- **duplicate**：复印

#### Q41 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Who will most likely attend the meeting? (谁最有可能参加这次会议？)
- (A) Clients. (客户们。)
- (B) Upper-level managers. (更高级别的经理们。)
- (C) New employees. (新雇员们。)
- (D) Technicians. (技术人员们。)

#### Q42 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** When is the man scheduled to give his speech? (男士定于什么时间作报告？)
- (A) In thirty minutes. (30 分钟以后。)
- (B) Right away. (立刻。)
- (C) Tomorrow morning. (明天早上。)
- (D) Next week. (下星期。)

#### Q43 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** How will the woman assist the man? (女士将如何协助男士？)
- (A) By setting up the projector. (安装投影仪。)
- (B) By gathering the sales figures. (收集销售数据。)
- (C) By duplicating some documents. (复印一些文档。)
- (D) By helping to carry something to the conference room. (帮他往会议室搬些东西。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **Do you need any help? = Would you like a hand?** (你需要帮忙吗？扩展表达：)
  - *例句：Can you handle it yourself?* (你能自己处理这件事吗？)
- **I'll give you a hand. = I'll help you. = I'll assist you.** (我会帮你的。)
  - *例句：I'll give you a hand with the boxes.* (我会帮你搬这些箱子。)
- **Do you mind?** (你介意吗？扩展表达：)
  - *例句：Would it be okay? Can you?* (这样可以吗？你可以吗？)

### Questions 44 - 46

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** I'm terribly sorry, Henry, but I am going to have to cancel the meeting tonight. I just received a call from Mr. King, a very important client of mine, and he says that he is in the area and he wants to come over to the office at 6 to talk to me about something. Do you think we can get together another time?
**M:** Sure, we can always catch a flick this weekend. (45) Who is this Mr. King guy anyway?
**W:** Oh, he is the owner of a fabric manufacturing firm that I recently sold a group policy to. (44) He mentioned something about wanting to increase the size of his group policy. (46)
**M:** Wow, that's great. I wish more of my customers would come and visit me to buy extra coverage.

**中文对照：**
> **W：**亨利，我很抱歉，今晚的见面不得不取消了。我刚接到了金先生的电话，他是我的非常重要的客户，他说他现在就在附近，想在6点钟到办公室和我谈一些事情。你觉得我们可以换个时间再聚吗？
> **M：**好的，我们这周末总能抽空去看场电影的。对了，这位金先生是什么人呢？
> **W：**哦，他是一家织造厂的厂主，我最近刚卖给他一份团体保险。他提出想要增加团体保险的数额。
> **M：**哇，那很好。我希望更多的客户能来找我买其他的保险项目。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **come over**：过来
- **get together**：相聚
- **flick**：电影
- **fabric**：织物，织品
- **group policy**：团体保险
- **coverage**：投保范围，投保项目
- **critic**：批评家

#### Q44 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Who most likely are they? (他们最有可能是什么人？)
- (A) Movie critics. (电影评论家。)
- (B) Clothes designers. (服装设计师。)
- (C) Insurance agents. (保险代理人。)
- (D) Travel agents. (旅行代理人。)

#### Q45 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What did they originally plan on doing together this evening? (他们原计划今天晚上一起做什么？)
- (A) Visit a client. (拜访一位客户。)
- (B) Watch a movie. (看场电影。)
- (C) Pick up some fabric. (挑选织物。)
- (D) Get extra coverage. (获取额外的保额。)

#### Q46 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Why is Mr. King coming to see the woman? (为什么金先生来拜访女士？)
- (A) To complain about service. (来投诉服务。)
- (B) To purchase more insurance. (来购买更多的保险。)
- (C) To discuss a problem. (来讨论问题。)
- (D) To buy some clothes. (来买一些衣服。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **Do you think we can get together another time?** (你觉得我们可以换个时间再聚吗？扩展表达：)
  - *例句：Would it be okay if I postponed our meeting today? Can we meet at a later date?* (推迟一下我们今天的会议好吗？我们过些天再碰面好吗？)
- **We can always catch a flick this weekend. = We can always watch a movie this weekend. = We can always go to the theater this weekend.** (这周末我们总能抽空去看场电影的。)
- **Wow, that's great. = Wow, that's amazing. = Wow, that is wonderful.** (哇，那很好。)

### Questions 47 - 49

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Do you know how many people are going to show up this evening? (47) I need to call the restaurant to make a reservation.
**W:** There will be about 10, including me and you. (48) Why don't you check with Shirley just to make sure? She is the one who knows exactly who will be showing up.
**M:** All right, but she stepped out for a moment to mail something at the post office. (49) I will drop by her office after I come back from lunch. Do you want to join me in the cafeteria?
**W:** Sure, I will be right with you. Just give me a second to make a call to a client first.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**你知道今天晚上会有多少人到场吗？我需要给饭店打电话订餐。
> **W：**包括你和我在内大约将会有10人。你为什么不和雪莉确认一下呢？她很清楚谁将会到场。
> **M：**好的，但她出去到邮局寄东西了。我吃完午饭后会顺路到她的办公室。你想和我一起去餐厅吗？
> **W：**好的，我一会儿过去。我得先给一位客户打个电话。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **show up**：到场
- **make a reservation**：预订
- **exactly**：确切地
- **step out**：出去
- **drop by**：顺路拜访
- **turn up**：出现，到场

#### Q47 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What does the man want to know? (男士想知道什么？)
- (A) If the woman has made a reservation or not. (女士是否已经预订了。)
- (B) Where Shirley has gone. (雪莉去哪里了。)
- (C) How many people already had dinner. (多少人已经用过餐。)
- (D) Who will turn up this evening. (今天晚上谁会来。)

#### Q48 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** According to the woman, how many people are expected to show up this evening? (根据女士所说，今晚将有多少人出席？)
- (A) Six. (6 位。)
- (B) Eight. (8 位。)
- (C) Ten. (10 位。)
- (D) Twelve. (12 位。)

#### Q49 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What is Shirley most likely doing now? (雪莉现在最有可能在做什么？)
- (A) Having lunch at the company cafeteria. (在公司餐厅吃午饭。)
- (B) Booking seats at a nearby restaurant. (在附近的餐馆预订座位。)
- (C) Sending something at the post office. (在邮局寄东西。)
- (D) Talking to a client in the meeting room. (在会议室和一位客户谈话。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **Why don't you check with Shirley just to make sure? = Why don't you ask Shirley again to make sure? = You should ask Shirley to double check.** (你为什么不和雪莉确认一下呢？)
- **She stepped out for a moment. = She went out for a while.** (她出去一会儿了。)
  - *例句：Janice was here, but she just stepped out for a moment.* (贾尼丝是来过这里，但她刚出去一会儿。)
- **Just give me a second. = Just give me a moment. = Just give me a minute.** (稍等我一下。)

### Questions 50 - 52

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** I must have eaten too much last night at the buffet restaurant because my stomach still feels bloated. I'm just going to settle for coffee this morning. What are you going to have? (50)
**M:** I am starved. I am going to order the continental breakfast.
**W:** Wow, you really do have an appetite, don't you? I mean, I don't understand how you can eat as much as you do yet keep yourself so thin like that. You are so lucky. (51)
**M:** Well, I guess I have always digested my food very fast. (52) I've been thin for as long as I can remember. Actually, when I was younger, my wish was to gain some weight. In fact, I remember eating 5 meals a day during high school just to gain some weight, but I didn't have any luck.

**中文对照：**
> **W：**我昨晚在自助餐馆一定是吃多了，胃到现在还觉得胀。今天早晨我就勉强喝点咖啡吧。你打算吃点什么？
> **M：**我饿极了。我打算去点欧式早餐。
> **W：**哇，你很有胃口嘛，是吧？我是说，我不理解为什么你吃这么多，还能保持那么瘦。你真是幸运。
> **M：**嗯，我想也许是因为我总是消化得非常快。我打记事儿起就一直很瘦。实际上，当我更年轻的时候，我的愿望是增加点儿体重。事实上，我记得在高中时一天吃五顿饭来增肥，但我没那么幸运。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **bloated**：饮食过度的，胃胀的
- **settle for**：勉强接受
- **be starved**：挨饿
- **continental breakfast**：欧式早餐
- **appetite**：食欲，胃口
- **thin**：瘦的
- **digest**：消化
- **gain weight**：增肥
- **envy**：羡慕
- **metabolize**：新陈代谢

#### Q50 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Where is the conversation most likely taking place? (这则对话最有可能发生在哪里？)
- (A) At a doctor's office. (在医生的诊室。)
- (B) At a restaurant. (在饭店。)
- (C) At a health club. (在健身俱乐部。)
- (D) At a public school. (在公立学校。)

#### Q51 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Why does the woman envy the man? (为什么女士羡慕男士？)
- (A) He did very well in school. (他在学校表现很棒。)
- (B) He does not have a weight problem. (他没有体重的问题。)
- (C) He is going to eat something delicious. (他将吃一些美味的食物。)
- (D) He gets coffee at a very good price. (他以很实惠的价格买了咖啡。)

#### Q52 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What can be inferred about the man? (关于男士可以推论出什么？)
- (A) He does not like to eat much. (他不喜欢吃太多。)
- (B) He metabolizes food quickly. (他消化食物很快。)
- (C) He keeps himself in shape. (他保持着好身材。)
- (D) He recently graduated from high school. (他最近高中毕业了。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **What are you going to have? = What are you going to eat? = Have you decided what you want to eat?** (你打算吃点什么？)
- **I am starved. = I am hungry. = I could use something to eat.** (我饿极了。)
- **I've been thin for as long as I can remember. = I've been skinny since I was very young. = I've always been thin.** (我打记事儿起就一直很瘦。)

### Questions 53 - 55

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Aren't you supposed to be in Boston right now? I thought you left to attend the business conference yesterday? (53)
**W:** I did, and I came back late last night. It was only a day affair, and I took the last flight out because I have a meeting with Mr. Jones this afternoon. (54) I could have taken a flight out this morning, but I have some things to prepare before I meet with him. (55)
**M:** You know, if I had known that it was only a day affair, I would have taken the trip with you. I also have a meeting with a very important client today, and that's why I didn't make the trip.
**W:** You should've talked to me about it. We could've made the trip together.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**你现在难道不应该在波士顿吗？我以为你昨天出发去参加商务会议了啊？
> **W：**我去了，昨晚很晚回来的。会议只开一天，然后我搭了末班飞机，因为我今天下午要约见琼斯先生。我本来可以坐今天上午的飞机，但是我在见他之前需要准备一些东西。
> **M：**嗯，如果我早知道会议只开一天的话，我就和你一起去出差了。我今天也约见了一位非常重要的客户，所以就没有出差。
> **W：**你真应该和我谈谈的。我们本可以一起出差的。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **take a flight**：乘飞机

#### Q53 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Why did the woman make a trip to Boston? (为什么女士出差去波士顿？)
- (A) To participate in a meeting. (参加会议。)
- (B) To meet with a client. (会见一位客户。)
- (C) To show the city to Mr. Jones. (带琼斯先生在市里逛逛。)
- (D) To spend some time with the man. (与男士共度一段时光。)

#### Q54 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** For how many days did the woman go away? (女士离开几天了？)
- (A) One. (一天。)
- (B) Two. (两天。)
- (C) Three. (三天。)
- (D) Four. (四天。)

#### Q55 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Why did the woman come back early? (为什么女士早早回来了？)
- (A) She forgot to take some important documents. (她忘记带一些重要的文件了。)
- (B) She was not happy with the conference. (她对会议不满意。)
- (C) She needed to get ready for a meeting. (她需要为一个会议做准备。)
- (D) She couldn't convince Mr. Jones to stay longer. (她没能说服琼斯先生多待一会儿。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I came back late last night. = I returned late last night. = I got back late last night.** (我昨晚很晚回来的。)
- **It was only a day affair. = It was only a day event. = It was only for one day.** (那只是一天的事。)
- **I would have taken the trip with you. = I would have gone on the trip with you. = I would have accompanied you on the trip.** (我本可以和你一起去出差的。)

### Questions 56 - 58

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Hello. My name is Eric Farmer. I received a bill in the mail today, but that shouldn't have happened. (56) I signed up for the automatic payment system two months ago, so the bill should have already been paid.
**W:** Let me check on that, Mr. Farmer. May I have your address, please? (57)
**M:** I live at 382 Washington Avenue.
**W:** Hmm...According to the computer, the money was withdrawn from your account yesterday, so you were sent the bill in error.
**M:** I can disregard it, right?
**W:** That's correct. And thanks for bringing this to our attention. (58) We'll check the computer system for other problems like this.

**中文对照：**
> **M：**您好，我是埃里克·法默，今天我收到一张账单，但是这不应该啊。两个月前我注册了自动支付系统，所以这张账单应该已经付了。
> **W：**我来查一下，法默先生。请问您能告诉我您的地址吗？
> **M：**我住在华盛顿大街382号。
> **W：**嗯....根据电脑记录，钱昨天从您的账户扣除了，所以给您发错账单了。
> **M：**我可以忽略这封邮件，是吗？
> **W：**是的。谢谢您将此事告诉我们。我们会检查电脑系统，查找类似的问题。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **sign up for**：报名参加
- **automatic**：自动的
- **according to**：根据
- **withdraw**：取（钱）；收回
- **in error**：错误地
- **disregard**：忽视
- **bring sth to one's attention**：使某人注意某事

#### Q56 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What is the purpose of the man's call? (男士打电话的目的是什么？)
- (A) To find out if his payment was processed. (弄清楚他是否付款了。)
- (B) To say that he was charged too much. (表示他扣费太多了。)
- (C) To change his mailing address. (更改邮寄地址。)
- (D) To ask why he received a bill. (询问为什么他收到了一张账单。)

#### Q57 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the woman ask the man for? (女士需要男士提供什么？)
- (A) His name. (他的名字。)
- (B) His mailing address. (他的邮寄地址。)
- (C) His phone number. (他的电话号码。)
- (D) His e-mail address. (他的邮箱地址。)

#### Q58 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Why does the woman thank the man? (为什么女士要感谢男士？)
- (A) For not getting upset. (因为他没有生气。)
- (B) For reporting a problem. (因为他报告了一个问题。)
- (C) For paying a bill on time. (因为他及时支付账单。)
- (D) For upgrading his cable package. (因为他升级了有线电视套餐。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **The money was withdrawn from your account yesterday. = The money was taken out of your account yesterday.** (钱昨天从您的账户里扣除了。)
  - *例句：I'd like to withdraw $500 from my current account.* (我想从活期账户中取出500美元。)
- **in error = by mistake** (错误地)
  - *例句：The letter was sent to you in error.* (信被错误地寄送给了你。)
- **bring sth. to one's attention = make someone aware of sth.** (使某人注意某事)
  - *例句：She wants to bring environmental problems to the world's attention. pay attention to do sth.* (她想让环境问题引起世界的关注。扩展表达：注意做某事)

### Questions 59 - 61

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Thank you for visiting the site, Mr. Murphy. I thought you'd like to see how construction is progressing. (59)
**M1:** There aren't any problems right now, are there?
**W:** Some supplies we ordered haven't arrived yet, but they won't be needed until tomorrow.
**M1:** That's good to hear. My associate, Mr. Vernon, has a question he'd like to ask you.
**M2:** That's right. When do you anticipate finishing the work? The deadline for the project is two weeks from today. (60)
**W:** We're going to make it. There's no reason for you to be concerned.
**M2:** Okay, I'll report back to the clients to let them know what you said. (61)

**中文对照：**
> **W：**墨菲先生，感谢您来工地现场参观。我想您是想看下工程进展如何。
> **M1：**现在没有任何问题吧？
> **W：**我们订购的一些物资暂未送达，但是明天才需要这些。
> **M1：**很高兴听到这个消息。我的同事，弗农先生想问您个问题。
> **M2：**是的。您预期什么时候完成这项工作？从今天算起，该项目的截止日期是两周后。
> **W：**我们将会准时完成。您不用担心。
> **M2：**好的。我会向顾客汇报，让他们知道所说的情况。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **supply**：供给物；必需品
- **associate**：同事；伙伴
- **anticipate**：预期；预料
- **deadline**：截止日期；最后期限
- **concerned**：担忧的；关心的

#### Q59 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Where does the conversation take place? (该对话在哪发生的？)
- (A) At a shopping center. (在一个购物中心。)
- (B) In an office. (在办公室。)
- (C) At a construction site. (在一个建筑工地。)
- (D) In a restaurant. (在一家餐厅。)

#### Q60 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the woman most likely mean when she says, “We're going to make it”? (当这位女士说 “ 我们将会准时完成 ” 时，最可能意味着什么？)
- (A) A meeting will be attended. (将出席一个会议。)
- (B) A deadline will be met. (将在截止日期之前完成。)
- (C) An item will be manufactured. (将制造一个商品。)
- (D) A goal will be set. (将会设定一个目标。)

#### Q61 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What will Mr. Vernon probably do next? (接下来，弗农先生很可能做什么？)
- (A) Speak with some clients. (和一些客户交谈。)
- (B) Make a purchase. (完成一笔购买。)
- (C) Contact a delivery company. (联系快递公司。)
- (D) Work with the woman. (和那位女士一起工作。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **make it** (准时到达，赶上；获得成功；渡过难关)
  - *例句：If we run, we should make it. He came to the U.S. and not only made it but made it big. Frank was ill, and doctors didn't think he'd make it.* (如果我们跑快点的话，应该来得及。他来到美国，不仅仅成功了，而且发达了。弗兰克病的很重，医生认为他挺不过来了。)

### Questions 62 - 64

![Page 189](images/listen_page_189.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** I was impressed with the interviewee we met this morning. He has plenty of experience and should be easy to collaborate with. (62)
**M:** The only problem is that Matt Doering can't start working until two months from now. (64)
**W:** Do you think we can afford to wait that long? I suppose we could hire Harry Anderson instead, but he's not as qualified.
**M:** I'm in favor of waiting until Matt can start. (64) In the meantime, we can give extra work to Sylvia. She doesn't mind working overtime. (63)
**W:** All right, then do you want to make the call, or should I? (64)
**M:** Go ahead and do it. Let me know if our offer is accepted. (64)

**中文对照：**
> **W：**我对今天上午我们见的那位面试者印象深刻。他经验丰富，应该很容易共事。
> **M：**唯一的问题是马特·德林两个月以后才能就职。
> **W：**你觉得我们能等那么长时间吗？我认为我们应该录用哈里·安德森，但他不如马特·德林那么称职。
> **M：**我赞成等马特就职。在这期间，我们可以给西维亚额外分配工作。她不介意加班。
> **W：**好的，那么你来打这个电话还是我来打？
> **M：**你来打吧。告诉我他是否接受我们的工作邀请就好。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **be impressed with**：对印象深刻
- **interviewee**：面试者
- **collaborate with**：与共事、合作
- **afford**：负担得起
- **qualified**：称职的
- **work overtime**：加班

#### Q62 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What did the speakers do in the morning? (讲话人早上做了什么？)
- (A) Met with a client. (见了客户。)
- (B) Worked on a project together. (一起做项目。)
- (C) Interviewed an applicant. (面试了一位应聘者。)
- (D) Visited a manufacturing facility. (参观了一个生产设施。)

#### Q63 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the man suggest about Sylvia? (关于西维亚，男士暗示了什么？)
- (A) She is employed at his company. (她被他的公司聘用了。)
- (B) She stays late after work every day. (每天下班之后她都会待到很晚。)
- (C) She is working on a project for him now. (她目前在为他做项目。)
- (D) She is close friends with the woman. (她是女士的亲密朋友。)

#### Q64 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Which number will the woman call? (请看图表，女士会拨打哪个电话号码？)
- (A) 744-1292. (744-1292 。)
- (B) 847-1933. (847-1933 。)
- (C) 735-7565. (735-7565 。)
- (D) 341-6533. (341-6533 。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **be in favor of = agree with** (赞成，支持)
  - *例句：Mr. Green spoke in favour of my proposal.* (格林先生表示支持我的提议。)
- **in the meantime = meanwhile** (与此同时，在…期间)
  - *例句：The next subway will be arriving in ten minutes: in the meantime, I'll go to the man's room.* (下一班地铁十分钟后来，在这期间，我要去趟卫生间。)

### Questions 65 - 67

![Page 190](images/listen_page_190.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**M:** Thank you all for joining today's tour. As you know, there are four floors in the building, so we're going to start at the top floor and head down. (65) Are there any questions before we begin?
**W:** Yes, about how long will the tour last? (66)
**M:** If you stay for the entire tour, it will take approximately one and a half hours to see the entire museum.
**W:** Unfortunately, I have to leave for a doctor's appointment in an hour, so how much of the museum will I see? (67)
**M:** You'll be able to see everything except for the first floor.
**W:** Thank you so much for letting me know. Milton Museum Directory

**中文对照：**
> **M：**谢谢各位参加今天的观光。大家知道，这座大楼有四层，所以我们要从顶层开始参观，然后一层一层往下看。在我们参观之前，你们有问题要问吗？
> **W：**是的，这次参观会持续多长时间？
> **M：**如果全程参观，大约要用一个半小时参观完整个博物馆。
> **W：**真不巧，我一个小时后约好了看医生，所以我能参观博物馆多少部分呢？
> **M：**除了一层，其余层都可以看到。
> **W：**感谢你告诉我这么多。弥尔顿博物馆指南

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **tour**：观光，游览，参观
- **head down**：向下走
- **approximately**：大约
- **unfortunately**：不幸地是，不巧的是
- **leave for**：前往
- **appointment**：安排，预约
- **except**：除了之外

#### Q65 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. What exhibit will the tour guide show first? (请看图表，导游首先会介绍什么展品？)
- (A) Asian Art. (亚洲艺术。)
- (B) Roman History. (罗马历史。)
- (C) Renaissance Art. (文艺复兴艺术。)
- (D) Local History. (当地历史。)

#### Q66 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What does the woman ask about? (女士问了什么问题？)
- (A) The cost of the tour. (参观费用。)
- (B) The length of the tour. (参观时长。)
- (C) The number of people on the tour. (参观人数。)
- (D) The highlights of the tour. (参观重点。)

#### Q67 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What will the woman most likely do after the tour? (参观之后，女士最有可能做什么？)
- (A) Visit the gift shop. (去礼品店。)
- (B) Ask the guide some questions. (询问导游一些问题。)
- (C) Go to a health clinic. (去诊所。)
- (D) Have lunch with a friend. (和朋友吃午餐。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **It takes sb. some time to do sth. = sb. spends some time doing sth.** (某人花时间做某事)
  - *例句：It took me about two months to finish the research paper.* (我花了大约两个月的时间完成了这篇研究论文。)

### Questions 68 - 70

![Page 190](images/listen_page_190.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
**W:** Welcome to the Hatfield House. Have you had the opportunity to look over the menu?
**M:** I have, but I'm not sure what to order. It's been several months since I dined here. (68) What do you recommend?
**W:** Why don't you try our newest item? You can get a pork chop with a baked potato and sautéed vegetables. I've had it before and highly recommend it. (69)
**M:** All right, I think I'll go with your suggestion. (69)
**W:** Excellent. In the meantime, would you care for a soup or salad as an appetizer?
**M:** No thanks, but I would like some iced tea. (70)
**W:** Sure, I'll bring you a glass in a couple of minutes. (70)

**中文对照：**
> **W：**欢迎来到哈特菲尔德餐厅，您看过菜单了吗？
> **M：**我看过了，但我不太清楚应该点些什么。上次来这里吃饭已经是几个月前的事了。你推荐些什么呢？
> **W：**为什么不尝尝我们的新品？您可以来一份土豆猪排煎蔬菜，我吃过，强烈推荐它。
> **M：**好的，我觉得就按照你的建议来。
> **W：**太好了。同时，您要来一份汤或沙拉作为开胃菜吗？
> **M：**不用了，谢谢，但我想点杯冰茶。
> **W：**好的，我几分钟后就给您端来一杯。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **opportunity**：机会
- **look over**：浏览，翻阅
- **recommend**：推荐
- **chop**：排骨
- **sauté**：煎
- **go with**：顺从，听从
- **appetizer**：开胃菜

#### Q68 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the man say about the restaurant? (关于这家餐厅，男士说了什么？)
- (A) He has eaten there before. (他之前来这里吃过。)
- (B) The prices are high. (价格高。)
- (C) It has a nice atmosphere. (环境很好。)
- (D) It recently opened. (新开业。)

#### Q69 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. How much does the item the man ordered cost? (请看图表，男士点的菜的费用是多少？)
- (A) $18.00. (18 美元。)
- (B) $21.00. (21 美元。)
- (C) $22.00. (22 美元。)
- (D) $25.00. (25 美元。)

#### Q70 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What will the woman bring the man next? (女士接下来要给男士拿来什么？)
- (A) A bowl of soup. (一份汤。)
- (B) A salad. (一份沙拉。)
- (C) An appetizer. (一份开胃菜。)
- (D) A cold beverage. (一杯冷饮。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **Why don't you ~? = Why not ~?** (为什么不…？)
  - *例句：—Where should we spend our summer vacation, Mary? —Why don't we fly to Hawaii? It's a very nice place.* (玛丽，我们到哪过暑假呢？为什么不飞去夏威夷，那是个很棒的地方。)

## Part 4: 简短独白 (Q71 - Q100)

### Questions 71 - 73

![Page 191](images/listen_page_191.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Today is the first workday of the new year, and we'd like to start off with a very positive resolution, especially as we have twenty new staff members beginning today. (71) Our company has always been heavily involved in volunteer work. We have several teams of volunteers, each of which specializes in a different area. Please join one of the clubs and participate in their special activities. (73) We'd like all members to remember that service to others can be surprisingly fun and rewarding. Our receptionist, Jo Workman, (72) who is also the leader of the environmental action team, has prepared a handbook on volunteering and other social activities. Please get a copy, and don't hesitate to join. (73)

**中文对照：**
> 今天是新年的第一个工作日，我们想以一项非常积极的决定来作为开始，特别是我们将有20名新员工从今天开始工作。我们公司向来都积极参加志愿者工作。我们有几个志愿者小组，每个小组都专注于不同的领域。请加入其中一个俱乐部，并参加他们的特别活动。我们希望所有的成员都能记住为别人服务会获得惊人的乐趣和回报。我们的接待员乔·沃克曼是环境行动组的领导，她准备了一本关于志愿活动及其他社会活动的手册。请拿一本，不要犹豫，赶紧加入吧。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **positive**：积极的
- **resolution**：决定
- **especially**：特别，尤其
- **heavily**：极大地，大量地
- **involve**：参加
- **volunteer**：志愿者
- **specialize in ~**：专攻
- **participate in ~**：参与
- **surprisingly**：惊人地
- **rewarding**：有益的，有回报的
- **environmental**：环境的
- **handbook**：手册
- **hesitate**：犹豫
- **entertainer**：专业演员；表演者
- **perform**：表演
- **reward**：报答，报酬
- **guidebook**：指导手册

#### Q71 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Who is the audience of this talk? (这次讲话的听众是谁？)
- (A) Volunteers who have just joined. (刚加入的志愿者们。)
- (B) Employees of the company. (公司的雇员们。)
- (C) Special club members. (俱乐部特别会员。)
- (D) Entertainers who will perform today. (今天将进行表演的演员们。)

#### Q72 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Who is Ms. Workman? (沃克曼女士是谁？)
- (A) The company receptionist. (公司的接待员。)
- (B) A new employee. (一位新雇员。)
- (C) An author. (一位作家。)
- (D) A department head. (一位部门领导。)

#### Q73 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the speaker suggest the listeners do? (讲话者建议听众做什么？)
- (A) Pick up their rewards. (领取他们的酬金。)
- (B) Photocopy some documents. (影印一些文件。)
- (C) Join one of the teams. (加入其中的一组。)
- (D) Talk to the club leader. (与俱乐部的领导谈谈。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **heavily involved in = heavily absorbed in = deeply involved in** (积极投入，深入参与)
  - *例句：Everyone on our team is heavily involved in this project.* (我们小组的每个人都积极投身于这个项目之中。)
- **which specializes in a different area** (专攻不同的领域扩展表达：)
  - *例句：which caters to a different market which concentrates on a different market We have a team which specializes in a different area.* (适合不同的市场专注于不同的市场我们有一个小组专注于不同的领域。)
- **Don't hesitate to join. = Don't think twice about joining. = Don't even consider not joining.** (不要犹豫，赶紧加入吧。)
  - *例句：Please don't hesitate in joining us for dinner this evening.* (不要犹豫，今晚和我们一起用餐吧。)

### Questions 74 - 76

**听力独白/对话原文：**
The East York Juniors Soccer Club is launching a membership and fund- raising drive to start off the new season. (74) The club's secretary has told our local sports reporter that the club may be forced to close this year due to financial problems. (75) He would like to encourage all parents to consider the benefits to children and the community by supporting the local soccer club, which has been working in this community for the last sixty years. The annual membership fee has been raised to forty dollars in order to cover the cost of maintaining club facilities. The club is also seeking volunteers to work as officials and umpires. Anyone with first aid or coaching experience is most welcome to join the coaching team. (76)

**中文对照：**
> 东约克青少年足球俱乐部正在发展会员制和进行筹款活动来开始新的赛季。俱乐部秘书告诉我们当地的体育记者，由于财政问题，俱乐部今年也许会被迫关闭。他鼓励所有的家长考虑孩子们及社区的利益，支持这个已经在该社区服务60年的地方足球俱乐部。年会费增加了40美元，以便支付维护和保养俱乐部设施的费用。俱乐部也在寻找志愿者们来做职员和裁判员。热烈欢迎任何有急救或教练经验的人加入教练队。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **launch**：开展
- **membership**：会员制
- **fund-raising**：筹募资金
- **force**：迫使
- **encourage**：鼓励
- **community**：社区
- **support**：支持
- **membership fee**：会费
- **cover**：支付
- **maintain**：维修，保养
- **official**：职员，办公人员
- **umpire**：裁判员
- **first aid**：急救
- **close down**：关闭
- **in operation**：运行
- **to date**：到此为止
- **on the brink of ~**：在的边缘
- **shut down**：关闭

#### Q74 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What is the report mainly about? (这则报道主要是关于什么的？)
- (A) The closing down of a local sports club. (一家当地体育俱乐部的关闭。)
- (B) The need for a fund-raising drive to keep a club in operation. (需要筹募资金来维持一家俱乐部的运营。)
- (C) The amount of money they have raised to date. (迄今他们筹集的钱款总额。)
- (D) The hiring of a new coach for the team. (为球队雇一名新教练。)

#### Q75 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the speaker say about the club? (关于俱乐部，讲话人谈了些什么？)
- (A) It is on the brink of shutting down. (它正处在被关闭的边缘。)
- (B) It is only available to local residents. (它只对当地居民开放。)
- (C) It has hired a new coaching staff. (它雇了一名新教练。)
- (D) It encourages parents to join the team. (它鼓励家长加入球队。)

#### Q76 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** Who would most likely be considered for the position? (谁最有可能获得这一职位？)
- (A) A person who had played for a professional team. (曾经为专业球队踢球的人。)
- (B) Parents who have children of their own. (有孩子的家长们。)
- (C) Anyone who wishes to exercise on a regular basis. (任何想定期锻炼的人。)
- (D) Those who have knowledge of first-aid. (那些有急救知识的人。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **He would like to encourage all parents to do ~ = He would like to ask all parents to do ~ = He would like to urge all parents to do ~** (他想鼓励所有的家长去做…)
  - *例句：He would like to encourage all parents to participate in the upcoming parent- teacher meeting.* (他想鼓励所有的家长参加即将召开的家长会。)
- **The annual membership fee has been raised. = The yearly membership fee has gone up. = The cost of the yearly membership has increased.** (年会费已经增长了。)
- **cover the cost of maintaining** (支付维护的费用扩展表达：)
  - *例句：handle the cost of operating = include the cost of running We have to raise ticket prices to cover the cost of maintaining the stadium.* (支付运营所需要的费用我们需要提高票价来支付维护体育馆的费用。)

### Questions 77 - 79

![Page 192](images/listen_page_192.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Congratulations on your choice of a Xenox PDP-alpha laser fax, copier and printer. All Xenox products incorporate the latest technology into attractive, versatile, and durable office equipment. This instruction manual will demonstrate clearly how to assemble, install, and use your new Xenox-alpha. As a first step, (77) please ensure that you have a clear space that is large enough and has electrical and computer cable access. (79) Next, in the package labeled ‘A’, you will find a training video, warranty documents, and after-sales service information. (78) The video is designed for staff training. Please take the time to view it in order to get the best out of your new copier and to avoid costly damage due to incorrect use. Now, let's open package ‘B’, and begin assembly.

**中文对照：**
> 恭喜您选择了Xenox PDP-alpha激光传真机、复印机和打印机。所有Xenox产品都吸收了最新的技术，成为具有吸引力的、多功能且耐用的办公设备。这一安装手册将清楚地说明如何组装、安装及使用您的新Xenox-

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **alpha**：。第一步，请保证您有足够大的畅通空间，并有电源和电脑接线。接下来，在
- **A**：包裹里面，您将找到一盘培训录像带、保修单以及售后服务信息。录像带是为员工培训设计的。请您花点时间来观看，以便能够最有效地利用您的新打印机，并且避免由于不正确使用引起的重大损失。现在，让我们打开
- **B**：包裹，然后开始组装。
- **incorporate**：包含；吸收
- **latest**：最新的
- **attractive**：有吸引力的
- **versatile**：多功能的，万用的
- **durable**：经久的，耐用的
- **instruction manual**：安装手册
- **demonstrate**：说明
- **clearly**：清楚地
- **assemble**：组装
- **install**：安装
- **ensure**：确保
- **clear space**：畅通空间
- **access**：接入
- **warranty document**：保修单
- **after-sales service**：售后服务
- **costly**：昂贵的；重大的
- **incorrect**：不正确的
- **set up**：安装
- **read over**：通读，细读
- **manual**：手册
- **put together**：组装

#### Q77 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What is the talk mainly about? (这则谈话主要是关于什么的？)
- (A) The steps necessary in setting up the machine. (组装机器的必要步骤。)
- (B) How to send a fax overseas. (如何往国外发传真。)
- (C) Where to pick up the cheapest copier. (从哪里可以获取最便宜的复印机。)
- (D) How to make the best use of the video. (如何最有效地利用这盘录像带。)

#### Q78 (正确答案：A)

- (B) A fax machine. (一台传真机。)

- (D) Some printing paper. (一些打印纸。)

#### Q79 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What will the listeners do first? (听众将首先做什么？)
- (A) Find the right place to install the machine. (找到合适的地方安装这台机器。)
- (B) Watch the video for instruction. (观看录像以获得指导。)
- (C) Read over the manual together. (一起通读手册。)
- (D) Start putting together the equipment. (开始组装设备。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **Please take the time to view it.** (请花些时间观看它。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：Please look at it carefully. Please read it over thoroughly.* (请仔细看它。请从头至尾阅读它。)
- **get the best out of your new copier = make the best use of your new copy machine** (最有效地使用您的新复印机扩展表达：)
  - *例句：understand how to use your new copier fully Everyone should study the manual carefully to get the best out of your new copier.* (完全清楚如何使用您的新复印机每个人都应该仔细学习这本手册，以便能够最有效地利用新复印机。)
- **avoid costly damage = avoid heavy damage = avoid a lot of damage** (避免重大损失)
  - *例句：Let's think about all the possibilities to avoid costly damage.* (让我们把所有的情况都考虑到，以避免重大损失。)

### Questions 80 - 82

**听力独白/对话原文：**
In an important move today, the Board of Directors announced that their search for a new CEO has been successful. (80) We are pleased to announce that Mr. Michael Benwick, one of the most respected business leaders in Europe, has accepted the position. (81) Mr. Benwick has had a far-ranging and highly successful career in industry in South Africa and the United Kingdom. After graduating from Oxford in 1965, he took a middle management position in South Africa's mining industry. From there he has never looked back. (82) We welcome him not only for his dynamism and charisma but also for his wealth of experience.

**中文对照：**
> 在今天的一项重要提议中，董事会宣布他们成功地找到了新首席执行官。我们很高兴地宣布迈克尔·本维克先生接受了这一职位，他是欧洲最受尊敬的商业领袖之一。本维克先生在南非和英国的职业生涯涉及范围很广泛，而且非常成功。1965年从牛津毕业以后，他在南非煤矿业获得了一个中层管理职位。从那开始他一直蒸蒸日上。我们欢迎他的到来，不仅仅是因为他的干劲儿和领袖魅力，也是因为他拥有非常丰富的经验。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **move**：提议
- **successful**：成功的
- **respected**：受人尊敬的
- **accept**：接受
- **career**：职业；生涯
- **management**：管理
- **mining industry**：煤矿业
- **never look back**：一帆风顺；蒸蒸日上
- **dynamism**：干劲，活力
- **charisma**：领袖魅力
- **wealth**：丰富，大量
- **executive**：执行官
- **coalminer**：煤矿工人
- **graduate student**：研究生
- **field**：领域

#### Q80 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What is the main topic of the talk? (这则讲话的主题是什么？)
- (A) The introduction of a new company leader. (介绍公司的一位新领导。)
- (B) The success of the company in recent years. (近年来公司的成就。)
- (C) The executive's trip to the United Kingdom. (经理的英国之旅。)
- (D) The mining industry in South Africa. (南非的煤矿业。)

#### Q81 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** Who is Mr. Benwick? (本维克先生是谁？)
- (A) A coalminer. (一名煤矿工人。)
- (B) The new president. (新任总裁。)
- (C) One of the board members. (董事会的一位成员。)
- (D) A university professor. (一位大学教授。)

#### Q82 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What does the speaker imply when he says, “We welcome him not only for his dynamism and charisma but also for his wealth of experience”? (讲话人说 “ 我们欢迎他的到来，不仅仅是因为他的干劲和领袖魅力，也是因为他拥有非常丰富的经验 ” ，是在暗示什么？)
- (A) Michael is a graduate student at Oxford. (迈克尔是牛津大学的研究生。)
- (B) Michael currently works in South Africa. (迈克尔目前在南非工作。)
- (C) Michael has become a very wealthy man. (迈克尔已经成为一个非常富有的人。)
- (D) Michael is very knowledgeable in his field of work. (迈克尔在其工作领域知识非常渊博。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **We are pleased to announce that ~ = We are happy to let you know that ~ = We are excited to tell you that ~** (我们很高兴地宣布…)
  - *例句：We are pleased to announce that everyone will get a bonus this year.* (我们很高兴地宣布，每个人今年都将得到奖金。)
- **accept the position = (decide to) take the job = (make up one's mind to) come aboard** (（决定）接受这个职位)
  - *例句：I was told by the president that Mr. Lee has accepted the position we offered.* (总裁告诉我，李先生接受了我们提供的职位。)
- **From there he has never looked back. = From there he went forward.** (从那以后，他一直蒸蒸日上。扩展表达：)
  - *例句：From there he never regretted.* (从那以后，他从未后悔过。)

### Questions 83 - 85

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Welcome to Earthbeat, your top-rated, environmental radio program. (83) First, let's go to the news. We have some sad news to announce today. The federal government has decided to discontinue funding for environmental science on ABC Radio. This will mean that Earthbeat will no longer be broadcast after the last program in this series airs in November. (84) A government spokesperson said, however, that funding will be increased for pure science and business reporting. Let's move to our first special report. We have in our studio a very special guest: it's Amy McIntyre, (85) the distinguished botanist and author of several prize-winning books on the flora of New Guinea. She'll be talking to our reporter, Jim Cross.

**中文对照：**
> 欢迎收看最受大家欢迎的环境类广播节目——“地球的心跳”。首先，我们来看新闻。今天我们要播报一些令人沮丧的新闻。联邦政府决定停止资助ABC广播的环境科学类节目。这将意味着“地球的心跳”将在11月系列广播的最后一期结束之后停播。一位政府发言人说，尽管如此，对于纯理论科学和商业报道的资助将增加。让我们进入第一条特别报道。我们的演播室里来了一位非常特别的嘉宾：艾米·麦金太尔，她是著名的植物学家，也是几部关于新几内亚植物群的获奖著作的作者。她将与我们的记者吉姆·克罗斯对话。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **top-rated**：第一流的
- **environmental**：环境的
- **federal**：联邦的
- **discontinue**：停止，中断
- **funding**：提供资金
- **no longer**：不再
- **air**：广播
- **pure science**：纯理论科学
- **distinguished**：著名的
- **botanist**：植物学家
- **prize-winning**：获奖的
- **flora**：植物群
- **rating**：评级
- **take over**：接管

#### Q83 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What is Earthbeat? (地球的心跳 ” 是什么？)
- (A) A radio program. (一档广播节目。)
- (B) An environmental group. (一个环境团体。)
- (C) A ratings system. (一个评级系统。)
- (D) A science research team. “ (一个科研小组。)

#### Q84 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What is going to happen in November? (月将有什么事情发生？)
- (A) The show will receive more funding. (这个节目将获得更多的资助。)
- (B) An environmental seminar will be held. (将会举行一场环境研讨会。)
- (C) The program will air its last show. (这个节目将播出最后一期。)
- (D) A new host will take over the show. 11 (一位新主持人将接管这个节目。)

#### Q85 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Who is Ms. McIntyre? (麦金太尔女士是什么人？)
- (A) A reporter. (一名记者。)
- (B) The radio host. (一名广播主持人。)
- (C) A guest. (一位来宾。)
- (D) The show's producer. (这个节目的制作人。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **First, let's go to the news. = Let's start with (the day's) news. = Let's begin with (today's) news.** (首先，我们来看（今天的）新闻。)
- **We have some sad news to announce today. = We have some unpleasant news to tell you today. = We have some unfortunate news to announce today.** (今天我们要宣布一些令人沮丧的新闻。)
- **no longer be broadcast = no longer be aired = no longer be shown** (停播)
  - *例句：The show will no longer be broadcast next week.* (这个节目从下周起将停播。)

### Questions 86 - 88

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Hi, Jen. It's Brian calling. Could you please pass on this important message to Jack Burbery in the Dispatch Office? (86) Last night I tried to contact Jack about the return of some items from the Continental Café. The chef at the Continental is not happy about the quality of yesterday's delivery of fresh fruit and vegetables. As you know, the Continental Café has been a particularly important client of ours, so it's important that we provide it with good service. The Continental would like us to discount that delivery. (87) Could Jack send a representative to the Continental to check on the produce (88) and to arrange the details? And please tell him that this is urgent.

**中文对照：**
> 你好，珍。我是布赖恩。你可以将这条重要的信息转达给送货部的杰克·伯伯里吗？昨天晚上我试着与杰克联系，讨论从大陆咖啡厅退回的一些货物。那儿的主厨对于昨天送去的新鲜水果和蔬菜的质量很不满意。你也知道，大陆咖啡厅一直是我们特别重要的客户，所以我们为它提供优质的服务很重要。大陆咖啡厅想让我们给那次送的货打折扣。杰克能派一位代表去大陆咖啡厅核查一下货物并安排细节吗？请告诉杰克这件事非常紧急。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **dispatch**：送货，派送
- **chef**：主厨
- **delivery**：交货，交付
- **particularly**：特别地
- **representative**：代表
- **arrange**：安排
- **detail**：细节
- **urgent**：紧急的
- **convey**：传达
- **deduction**：折扣
- **replace**：更换

#### Q86 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Why is the caller leaving the message? (打电话的人为什么留言？)
- (A) To request a return on an item. (为了请求退回一件货物。)
- (B) To see if a new delivery of fresh fruit has arrived. (为了查看新送的一批新鲜水果是否送到。)
- (C) To ask the listener to convey a message. (为了让听话者转达一个信息。)
- (D) To check and see if a discount is available. (为了查看是否可以打折。)

#### Q87 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the staff from the Continental want? (大陆咖啡厅的员工想怎么样？)
- (A) Faster delivery. (送货更快一些。)
- (B) Fresher products. (货物更新鲜些。)
- (C) A deduction in price. (价格折扣。)
- (D) A return call. (回个电话。)

#### Q88 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** What is asked of Jack? (杰克被要求做什么？)
- (A) To send an apology letter right away. (立刻发一封道歉信。)
- (B) To replace the wrong items sent. (更换送错的货物。)
- (C) To thank the chef for a great meal. (谢谢主厨的盛宴。)
- (D) To send someone to check on a product. (派人去核查货物。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **pass on this important message to ~ = give this important message to ~ = hand over this important message to ~** (将这条重要的信息转达给…)
  - *例句：Could you please pass on this important message to Mr. Kim when you make your trip to the head office?* (当你去总公司出差的时候，可否将这条重要的信息转达给金先生？)
- **be not happy about ~ = be not pleased with ~ = be not too keen about ~** (对…不开心)
  - *例句：John is not happy about working the night shift.* (约翰对于值夜班很不开心。)
- **arrange the details** (安排细节扩展表达：)
  - *例句：take care of the details = set up the details I will call the restaurant and arrange the details.* (处理细节我会给饭店打电话并安排细节。)

### Questions 89 - 91

![Page 194](images/listen_page_194.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Good morning. I would like to welcome all of the 8 trainee chefs from the Food Science and Technology College this morning. (89) We hope your stay here will be profitable. I should also mention that our chain of restaurants regularly employs young graduates from your college. (90) So, we'll be watching you, and if any of you are interested in future employment with us, please let us know. You may not be aware that our chain has restaurants in all the major cities of England and Europe. We have also recently opened restaurants in India, Southeast Asia, China, and Japan. We encourage overseas work experience as a way of developing exciting cooking styles. So working with us can be a fabulous experience if you have the right attitude. So, let's get busy. Please check the notice board to find out which team you have been assigned to. (91)

**中文对照：**
> 早上好。我要欢迎今天早上从食品科学和技术学院过来的八位实习厨师。我希望你们在这里会有所收获。另外我也要提一下，我们的连锁餐馆定期雇用你们学院的年轻毕业生。所以，我们将观察你们，如果你们中的任何人对于将来受雇在此工作感兴趣的话，可以告诉我们。你们也许不知道，我们的连锁店在英国和欧洲所有的主要城市都有分布。最近我们还在印度、东南亚、中国和日本也开设了餐馆。我们鼓励大家去海外工作，以便开发令人兴奋的菜系。所以，如果你有端正的态度，和我们一起工作是一次绝佳的机会。让我们开始工作吧。请看告示牌以便确认你们被分在哪个组。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **trainee**：实习生
- **profitable**：有益的
- **regularly**：定期地
- **employ**：雇用
- **be aware that**：知道
- **encourage**：鼓励
- **overseas**：海外的，国外的
- **develop**：开发
- **fabulous**：极好的，绝妙的
- **attitude**：态度
- **notice board**：告示牌
- **find out**：找出
- **assign**：分配
- **intern**：实习生
- **greet**：会面
- **reveal**：揭示
- **latest**：最新的
- **finding**：发现

#### Q89 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What is the purpose of the talk? (这则讲话的目的是什么？)
- (A) To welcome new employees to the company. (欢迎新雇员来到公司。)
- (B) To talk to the staff about the overseas branch. (和员工谈论海外分支机构。)
- (C) To greet interns from a local college. (欢迎从当地学院来的实习生。)

#### Q91 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What will the listeners most likely do first? (听众最有可能首先做什么？)

- (B) Check the notice board. (查看告示牌。)
- (C) Fill out an application form. (填写一张申请表。)
- (D) Gather into a group. (组成一个小组。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **Please let us know. = Please talk to us. = Please speak to us.** (请告诉我们。)
  - *例句：I would appreciate it if you could please let us know what you want today.* (如果你能告诉我们你今天想要什么的话，我将会很感激。)
- **You may not be aware that ~ = You may not know that ~ = You may not have heard that ~** (你也许不知道…)
  - *例句：You may not be aware, but Larry is going to leave us soon.* (你也许不知道，拉里将很快离开我们。)
- **So, let's get busy. = So, let's get on it. = So, let's start working on it.** (那么，让我们开始工作吧。)

### Questions 92 - 94

![Page 195](images/listen_page_195.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Good afternoon, shoppers. The management here at the Maytag Department Store would like to wish everyone a very happy Christmas. (92) For your convenience, this store has extended its opening hours. We will be closing at 10:00 p. m. this evening instead of 9 like we always do. (93) This will allow all those last-minute shoppers to buy their family the presents which they so richly deserve. In fact, why don't you make an evening of it and invite your loved ones to dinner at the basement gourmet cafeteria, (94) which will be open until 8? Thank you, and merry Christmas.

**中文对照：**
> 各位顾客，大家好。美态格百货商店的经理在这里祝大家圣诞快乐。为方便各位购物，商店已经延长了营业时间。我们今晚将于10点关门，而不是以往的9点。这会让所有那些最后进来的顾客能够为他们的家人买到礼物，这些礼物是他们完全应该得到的。事实上，您为什么不花一个晚上的时间来这里逛逛，带着心爱的人在底层的美味咖啡厅用餐呢？咖啡厅将营业到8点。谢谢，圣诞快乐。

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **management**：管理
- **convenience**：方便
- **extend**：延长
- **last-minute**：最后的
- **richly**：完全地
- **deserve**：应得
- **gourmet**：美味，美食
- **normally**：通常地
- **eatery**：餐馆
- **take advantage of ~**：利用

#### Q92 (正确答案：D)
**问题：** Where is the announcement taking place? (这则通告是在哪里宣布的？)
- (A) In a family restaurant. (在家族餐馆。)
- (B) In a gift store. (在礼品店。)
- (C) In a convenience store. (在便利店。)
- (D) In a department store. (在百货商店。)

#### Q93 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** When does the business normally close? (商店通常几点关门？)
- (A) At 8. (8 点。)
- (B) At 9. (9 点。)
- (C) At 10. (10 点。)
- (D) At 11. (11 点。)

#### Q94 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** What does the speaker recommend the listeners do? (讲话人建议听众做什么？)
- (A) Shop early, and go home. (早点儿购物，然后回家。)
- (B) Spend time with their families. (与他们的家人一起分享时光。)
- (C) Try out some food at the eatery. (在餐馆尝试一些食品。)
- (D) Take advantage of their special sale. (利用他们的特别促销。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **for your convenience = for your comfort = for your pleasure** (为了方便您)
  - *例句：For your convenience, we have upgraded all the computers over the weekend.* (为了方便您，我们已经在周末将所有的电脑都升级了。)
- **We will be closing at 10:00 p. m. = We will be open until 10:00 p. m. = We will end our day at 10:00 p. m.** (我们将于晚上10点关门。)
- **This will allow ~ = This will let ~ = This will provide ~** (这将让…)
  - *例句：This will allow the visitors to park on the first floor.* (这将使参观者可以在一层停车。)

### Questions 95 - 97

![Page 195](images/listen_page_195.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
I'm pleased to report that tickets are selling rapidly, and we should sell the remaining 450 tickets by the end of the week. It appears as though everyone in town is eager to hear Jennifer Evans sing. (95) Just so you know, the posters haven't arrived yet. Eric happened to notice a mistake as the number 23 was written on the posters instead of 13. (96) So the printer had to make a change and threw away the posters which had already been printed. I've been informed that the posters will arrive tomorrow, (97) so we'll send a few of you out to post them in places around town then. See Jennifer Evans perform live!

**中文对照：**
> 很高兴能告诉大家我们的票卖得很快，预计本周结束时可将余下的450张票全部售完。好像镇上的每个人都想到现场听珍妮弗·埃文斯唱歌。正如大家所知道的，海报尚未寄到。因为艾瑞克无意中发现海报上的数字13被错写成了23。于是印刷部门那边不得不加以修改，并将已经印好的海报搁置一旁。我这边得到消息，说海报将于明天寄达。届时我们会将海报分发给各位，请大家帮忙按地点将海报贴在镇上显眼之处。观看珍妮弗·埃文斯现场表演！

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **be pleased to**：很高兴
- **remaining**：余下的
- **by the end of**：截止到
- **just so you know**：正如你所知道的那样
- **happen to**：偶然发生
- **instead of**：代替
- **throw away**：扔掉，丢弃
- **be informed that**：被告知
- **send out**：派遣；发送

#### Q95 (正确答案：B)
**问题：** What type of performance will Jennifer Evans most likely give? (珍妮弗 · 埃文斯最有可能带来什么表演？)
- (A) A comedy routine. (喜剧表演。)
- (B) A musical concert. (音乐会。)
- (C) An instrument recital. (乐器独奏会。)
- (D) A theatrical performance. (戏剧表演。)

#### Q96 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. Which section contains a mistake? (请看图表，哪个地方出现了错误？)
- (A) Date. (日期。)
- (B) Time. (时间。)
- (C) Location. (地点。)
- (D) Ticket Prices. (票价。)

#### Q97 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What will happen tomorrow? (明天会发生什么？)
- (A) An order will be delivered. (交付订单。)
- (B) A payment will be made. (付款。)
- (C) Tickets will be mailed. (邮寄票据。)
- (D) A contract will be signed. (签署合约。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **I'm pleased to = I'm glad to = I feel happy to** (很高兴…)
  - *例句：I'm pleased to know that you are coming.* (很高兴知道你要来了。)
- **It appears as though = It seems as if** (看起来好像)
  - *例句：It appears as though a new chapter has begun to take shape.* (看起来新章节好像正在慢慢成形。)

### Questions 98 - 100

![Page 196](images/listen_page_196.png)

**听力独白/对话原文：**
Thank you for attending this demonstration of my firm's newest software. (98) As I hope you noticed, the software does exactly what it's supposed to. We believe the accountants who utilize it will find they become more efficient in their work. I'd like to inform everybody of a special deal that's only for people in this room. We intend to release the software at a press conference next week. If you order it the day before, you can purchase it for fifty percent off the regular price. (99) We know everyone who's here, so simply give the operator your name when you order, and the discount will be applied. (100) 8 August

**中文对照：**
> 感谢大家出席我公司最新款软件的发布会。不知道大家是否注意到，本款软件执行指令的效果堪称完美。相信会计人员用完后会发现自己的工作效率大大提高。我在这里有个好消息要告诉大家，在座的每一位均可享受特别优惠。我们预计在下周的新闻发布会上正式公布此款软件。如若您在发布会的前一天订购，即可享受五折优惠。我们认识在座的每一位，您到时候下单时告诉客服人员您的姓名，则会自动享受该折扣。八月

**核心词汇与短语：**
- **demonstration**：演示；证明
- **accountant**：会计人员
- **utilize**：利用，使用
- **press conference**：新闻发布会
- **purchase**：购买
- **discount**：折扣
- **shareholder**：股东

#### Q98 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What type of product is being released? (正在发布的是哪类产品？)
- (A) Computer software. (计算机软件。)
- (B) An electric appliance. (家用电器。)
- (C) A book on accounting. (会计相关图书。)
- (D) A calculator. (计算器。)

#### Q99 (正确答案：C)
**问题：** Look at the graphic. When can the attendees receive a discount? (请看图表，出席人员什么时候可以享受折扣？)
- (A) On Tuesday. (星期二。)
- (B) On Wednesday. (星期三。)
- (C) On Thursday. (星期四。)
- (D) On Friday. (星期五。)

#### Q100 (正确答案：A)
**问题：** What does the speaker tell the attendees to do when they order the product? (讲话人告诉参会者，预订产品的时候要做什么？)
- (A) Provide their name. (提供姓名。)
- (B) Give a coupon code. (提供优惠券密码。)
- (C) Request a discount. (申请打折。)
- (D) Ask for free delivery. (要求免费配送。)

**延伸表达与补充：**
- **intend to = plan to = mean to = want to** (打算)
  - *例句：How do you intend to carry out this strategy?* (你打算如何将这一观念付诸实践？)
